40027006	But the chief priests took the silver pieces and said , » It is not lawful to put them into the treasury , since they are the money of blood . «
40027007	So they took counsel , and bought with them the potter’s field , to bury strangers in .
40027008	Therefore that field has been called the Field of Blood to this day .
40027009	Then was fulfilled what was spoken by Jeremiah the prophet , saying , » And they took the thirty pieces of silver , the price of him on whom a price had been set by some of the sons of Israel ,
40027010	and they gave them for the potter’s field , as the Lord directed me . «
40027011	Now Jesus stood before the governor , and the governor asked him , » Are you the king of the Jews ? « So Jesus said to him , » It is as you say . «
40027012	But when he was accused by the chief priests and elders , he made no answer .
40027013	Then Pilate said to him , » Do you not hear how many things they testify against you ? «
40027014	But he gave him no answer , not even to a single charge ; so that the governor wondered greatly .
40027015	Now at the feast the governor was accustomed to release for the crowd any one prisoner whom they wanted .
40027016	And at that time they had a notorious prisoner , called Barabbas .
40027017	So when they had gathered , Pilate said to them , » Whom do you want me to release for you , Barabbas or Jesus who is called Christ ? «
40027018	For he knew it was out of envy that they had handed him over .
40027019	While he was sitting on the judgment seat , his wife sent word to him , » Have nothing to do with that righteous man , for I have suffered greatly today in a dream because of him . «
40027020	But the chief priests and the elders persuaded the multitudes to ask for Barabbas and destroy Jesus .
40027021	The governor answered them , » Which of the two do you want me to release to you ? « They said , » Barabbas ! «
40027022	Pilate said to them , » Then what shall I do with Jesus who is called Christ ? « They all said , » Let him be crucified ! «
40027023	And he said , » Why , what evil has he done ? « But they shouted all the more , » Let him be crucified ! «
40027024	When Pilate saw that he was gaining nothing , but rather that a riot was starting , he took water and washed his hands before the crowd , saying , » I am innocent of this man’s blood . See to it yourselves . «
40027025	And all the people answered , » His blood be on us and on our children ! «
40027026	Then he released Barabbas to them ; and when he had scourged Jesus , he delivered him to be crucified .
40027027	Then the soldiers of the governor took Jesus into the Praetorium and gathered the whole garrison around him .
40027028	And they stripped him and put a scarlet robe on him ,
40027029	and when they had twisted a crown of thorns , they put it on his head , and a reed in his right hand . And they bowed the knee before him and mocked him , saying , » Hail , King of the Jews ! «
40027030	And they spat on him , and took the reed and struck him on the head .
40027031	And when they had mocked him , they took the robe off him , put his own clothes on him , and led him away to crucify him .
40027032	Now as they came out , they found a man of Cyrene , Simon by name , and they compelled him to carry his cross .
40027033	And when they came to a place called Golgotha ( which means the place of a skull ) ,
40027034	they offered him wine to drink , mingled with gall ; but when he tasted it , he would not drink it .
40027035	And when they had crucified him , they divided his garments among them by casting lots ;
40027036	and sitting down , they kept watch over him there .
40027037	And they put up over his head the charge written against him : THIS IS JESUS THE KING OF THE JEWS .
40027038	Then two robbers were crucified with him , one on the right and one on the left .
40027039	And those who passed by hurled insults at him , wagging their heads
40027040	and saying , » You who would destroy the temple and build it in three days , save yourself ! If you are the Son of God , come down from the cross . «
40027041	So also the chief priests , with the scribes and elders , mocked him , saying ,
40027042	» He saved others ; he cannot save himself . He is the King of Israel ; let him come down now from the cross , and we will believe in him .
40027043	He trusts in God ; let God deliver him now , if he desires him ; for he said , ‘ I am the Son of God . ’ «
40027044	And the robbers who were crucified with him also reviled him in the same way .
40027045	Now from the sixth hour until the ninth hour there was darkness over all the land .
40027046	And about the ninth hour Jesus cried out with a loud voice , » Eli , Eli , lama sabachthani ? « that is , » My God , my God , why have you forsaken me ? «
40027047	When some of those standing there heard this , they said , » This man is calling Elijah . «
40027048	Immediately one of them ran and took a sponge , filled it with wine vinegar and put it on a reed , and offered it to him to drink .
40027049	The rest said , » Let him alone ; let us see if Elijah will come to save him . «
40027050	And Jesus cried out again with a loud voice , and yielded up his spirit .
40027051	And behold , the curtain of the temple was torn in two , from top to bottom ; and the earth shook , and the rocks were split ;
40027052	the tombs also were opened , and many bodies of the saints who had fallen asleep were raised ,
40027053	and coming out of the tombs after his resurrection , they went into the holy city and appeared to many .
40027054	So when the centurion and those with him , who were guarding Jesus , saw the earthquake and the things that had happened , they were terrified , and said , » Truly this was the Son of God ! «
40027055	And many women were also there , looking on from afar , who had followed Jesus from Galilee , ministering to him ;
40027056	among whom were Mary Magdalene , Mary the mother of James and Joses , and the mother of Zebedee’s sons .
40027057	And when it was evening , there came a rich man from Arimathea , named Joseph , who had himself also become a disciple of Jesus .
40027058	He went to Pilate and asked for the body of Jesus . Then Pilate ordered it to be given to him .
40027059	When Joseph took the body , he wrapped it in a clean linen cloth ,
40027060	and laid it in his own new tomb , which he had hewn out of the rock ; and he rolled a great stone to the door of the tomb , and departed .
40027061	Mary Magdalene and the other Mary were sitting there opposite the tomb .
40027062	The next day , the one after the day of Preparation , the chief priests and the Pharisees gathered to Pilate
40027063	and said , » Sir , we remember how that deceiver said , while he was still alive , ‘ After three days I will rise again . ’
40027064	Therefore order that the tomb be made secure until the third day , lest his disciples come by night and steal him away , and tell the people , ‘ He has risen from the dead . ’ So the last deception will be worse than the first . «
40027065	Pilate said to them , » You have a guard ; go your way , make it as secure as you know how . «
40027066	So they went and made the tomb secure by sealing the stone and setting a guard .
40028001	Now after the Sabbath , as the first day of the week began to dawn , Mary Magdalene and the other Mary went to see the tomb .
40028002	And behold , there was a great earthquake ; for an angel of the Lord descended from heaven , and came and rolled back the stone from the door , and sat on it .
40028003	His appearance was like lightning , and his clothes were white as snow .
40028004	And the guards shook for fear of him , and became like dead men .
40028005	But the angel said to the women , » Do not be afraid , for I know that you seek Jesus who was crucified .
40028006	He is not here ; for he has risen , as he said . Come , see the place where he lay .
40028007	Then go quickly and tell his disciples that he has risen from the dead . And behold , he is going before you to Galilee ; there you will see him . Behold , I have told you . «
40028008	So they departed quickly from the tomb with fear and great joy , and ran to tell his disciples .
40028009	And behold , Jesus met them and said , » Hail ! « And they came to him and took hold of his feet and worshipped him .
40028010	Then Jesus said to them , » Do not be afraid . Go and tell my brethren to go to Galilee ; and there they will see me . «
40028011	Now while they were going , behold , some of the guard went into the city and reported to the chief priests all the things that had happened .
40028012	When they had assembled with the elders and consulted together , they gave a large sum of money to the soldiers ,
40028013	and said , » Tell them , ‘ His disciples came by night and stole him away while we were asleep . ’
40028014	And if this comes to the governor’s ears , we will satisfy him and keep you out of trouble . «
40028015	So they took the money and did as they were instructed ; and this story has been spread among the Jews to this day .
40028016	Then the eleven disciples went to Galilee , to the mountain which Jesus had appointed for them .
40028017	When they saw him , they worshipped him ; but some doubted .
40028018	And Jesus came and said to them , » All authority in heaven and on earth has been given to me .

40028020	teaching them to observe all that I have commanded you ; and behold , I am with you always , even to the end of the age . «
41001001	The beginning of the gospel of Jesus Christ , the Son of God .

41001004	John came baptizing in the wilderness , and preaching a baptism of repentance for the forgiveness of sins .
41001005	And all the land of Judea , and the people from Jerusalem , went out to him and they were all baptized by him in the Jordan River , confessing their sins .
41001006	Now John was clothed with camel's hair , and with a leather belt around his waist , and he ate locusts and wild honey .
41001007	And he preached , saying , » After me comes One who is mightier than I , the thong of whose sandals I am not worthy to stoop down and untie .
41001008	I have baptized you with water , but he will baptize you with the Holy Spirit . «
41001009	In those days Jesus came from Nazareth of Galilee and was baptized by John in the Jordan .
41001010	And immediately coming up out of the water , he saw the heavens opened and the Spirit descending upon him like a dove .
41001011	And a voice came from heaven , » You are my beloved Son , with whom I am well pleased . «
41001012	The Spirit immediately drove him out into the wilderness .
41001013	And he was in the wilderness forty days , tempted by Satan ; and he was with the wild beasts , and the angels ministered to him .
41001014	Now after John was put in prison , Jesus came to Galilee , preaching the gospel of God ,
41001015	and saying , » The time is fulfilled , and the kingdom of God is at hand ; repent , and believe in the gospel . «

41001019	When he had gone a little farther from there , he saw James the son of Zebedee , and John his brother , who also were in the boat mending their nets .

41001021	And they went into Capernaum , and immediately on the Sabbath he entered the synagogue and taught .
41001022	And they were astonished at his teaching , for he taught them as one who had authority , and not as the scribes .
41001023	Now there was a man in their synagogue with an unclean spirit . And he cried out ,
41001024	saying , » Let us alone ! What have we to do with you , Jesus of Nazareth ? Did you come to destroy us ? I know who you are — the Holy One of God ! «
41001025	But Jesus rebuked him , saying , » Be quiet , and come out of him ! «
41001026	And the unclean spirit , convulsing him and crying with a loud voice , came out of him .
41001027	And they were all amazed , so that they questioned among themselves , saying , » What is this ? A new teaching ! With authority he commands even the unclean spirits , and they obey him . «
41001028	And at once his fame spread everywhere throughout all the surrounding region of Galilee .
41001029	As soon as they left the synagogue , they went with James and John , and entered the house of Simon and Andrew .
41001030	Now Simon's mother-in-law lay sick with a fever , and immediately they told him about her .
41001031	So he came and took her by the hand and lifted her up , and immediately the fever left her . And she served them .
41001032	Now at evening , when the sun had set , they brought to him all who were sick and those who were demon-possessed .
41001033	And the whole city was gathered together at the door .
41001034	And he healed many who were sick with various diseases , and cast out many demons ; and he would not permit the demons to speak , because they knew him .
41001035	Now in the morning , a long while before daylight , he rose and went out to a solitary place , and there he prayed .
41001036	And Simon and those who were with him searched for him ,
41001037	and when they found him , they said to him , » Everyone is looking for you . «
41001038	And he said to them , » Let us go on to the next towns , so I may preach there also ; for that is why I have come . «
41001039	And he went throughout all Galilee , preaching in their synagogues and casting out demons .
41001040	Then a leper came to him , imploring him , kneeling down to him and saying to him , » If you are willing , you can make me clean . «
41001041	And Jesus , moved with compassion , put out his hand and touched him , and said to him , » I am willing ; be clean . «
41001042	And immediately the leprosy left him , and he was made clean .
41001043	And he strictly warned him and sent him away at once ,
41001044	and he said to him , » See that you say nothing to anyone ; but go , show yourself to the priest , and offer for your cleansing what Moses commanded , as a testimony to them . «
41001045	But he went out and began to talk freely about it , and to spread the news , so that Jesus could no longer openly enter a town , but was outside in the deserted places ; and people came to him from every quarter .
41002001	And when he entered Capernaum after some days , it was heard that he was home .
41002002	And many gathered together , so that there was no longer room to receive them , not even near the door . And he preached the word to them .
41002003	Then they came to him , bringing a paralytic carried by four men .
41002004	And when they could not get near him because of the crowd , they made an opening in the roof above him ; and when they had broken through , they let down the pallet on which the paralytic was lying .
41002005	When Jesus saw their faith , he said to the paralytic , » Son , your sins are forgiven . «
41002006	Now some of the scribes were sitting there , reasoning in their hearts ,
41002007	» Why does this man speak like this ? He is blaspheming ! Who can forgive sins but God alone ? «
41002008	And immediately , when Jesus perceived in his spirit that they reasoned thus within themselves , he said to them , » Why do you reason about these things in your hearts ?
41002009	Which is easier , to say to the paralytic , ‘ Your sins are forgiven , ’ or to say , ‘ Rise , take up your pallet and walk ’ ?
41002010	But that you may know that the Son of Man has authority on earth to forgive sins « — he said to the paralytic ,
41002011	» I say to you , rise , take up your pallet and go home . «
41002012	And he rose , and immediately took up the pallet and went out in the sight of them all ; so that they were all amazed and glorified God , saying , » We never saw anything like this ! «
41002013	Then he went out again beside the sea ; and all the crowd came to him , and he taught them .
41002014	As he passed by , he saw Levi the son of Alphaeus sitting at the tax office , and he said to him , » Follow me . « So he rose and followed him .
41002015	And as he sat at table in Levi's house , many tax collectors and sinners were sitting with Jesus and his disciples ; for there were many who followed him .
41002016	And the scribes of the Pharisees , when they saw him eating with sinners and tax collectors , said to his disciples , » Why does he eat with tax collectors and sinners ? «
41002017	And when Jesus heard it , he said to them , » Those who are well have no need of a physician , but those who are sick . I did not come to call the righteous , but sinners . «
41002018	Now John's disciples and the Pharisees were fasting . And people came and said to him , » Why do John’s disciples and the disciples of the Pharisees fast , but your disciples do not fast ? «
41002019	And Jesus said to them , » Can the guests of the bridegroom fast while he is with them ? As long as they have the bridegroom with them , they cannot fast .
41002020	But the days will come , when the bridegroom will be taken away from them , and then they will fast in that day .
41002021	» No one sews a patch of unshrunk cloth on an old garment ; if he does , the new piece will pull away from the old , and the tear is made worse .
41002022	And no one puts new wine into old wineskins ; if he does , the wine will burst the skins , and the wine is lost and the wineskins are ruined . But new wine must be put into new wineskins . «
41002023	One Sabbath he was going through the grainfields ; and as they made their way his disciples began to pluck heads of grain .
41002024	And the Pharisees said to him , » Look , why are they doing what is not lawful on the Sabbath ? «
41002025	But he said to them , » Have you never read what David did when he was in need and hungry , he and those who were with him :
41002026	how he entered the house of God in the days of Abiathar the high priest , and ate the consecrated bread , which is not lawful to eat , except for the priests , and also gave some to those who were with him ? «
41002027	And he said to them , » The Sabbath was made for man , not man for the Sabbath .
41002028	So the Son of Man is Lord even of the Sabbath . «
41003001	He entered the synagogue again , and a man was there who had a withered hand .
41003002	And they watched him closely , to see whether he would heal him on the Sabbath , so that they might accuse him .
41003003	And he said to the man who had the withered hand , » Come here . «
41003004	Then he said to them , » Is it lawful on the Sabbath to do good or to do evil , to save life or to kill ? « But they kept silent .
41003005	And he looked around at them with anger , grieved at the hardness of their hearts , and said to the man , » Stretch out your hand . « He stretched it out , and his hand was restored .
41003006	Then the Pharisees went out and immediately plotted with the Herodians against him , how they might destroy him .
41003007	Jesus withdrew with his disciples to the sea , and a great multitude from Galilee followed ; also from Judea
41003008	and Jerusalem and Idumea and beyond the Jordan and from around Tyre and Sidon , a great multitude , when they heard how many things he was doing , came to him .
41003009	And he told his disciples to have a small boat ready for him because of the crowd , lest they should crush him .
41003010	For he had healed many , so that all who had diseases pressed upon him to touch him .
41003011	And whenever the unclean spirits saw him , they fell down before him and cried out , » You are the Son of God . «
41003012	But he strictly ordered them not to make him known .
41003013	And he went up on the mountain , and called to him those he himself wanted . And they came to him .
41003014	Then he appointed twelve , that they might be with him and that he might send them out to preach ,
41003015	and to have authority to cast out the demons :
41003016	Simon , to whom he gave the name Peter ;
41003017	James the son of Zebedee and John the brother of James , to whom he gave the name Boanerges , that is , » Sons of Thunder « ;

41003020	Then he went home ; and the crowd came together again , so that they could not even eat .
41003021	When his family heard about this , they went to take charge of him , for they said , » He is out of his mind . «
41003022	And the scribes who came down from Jerusalem said , » He is possessed by Beelzebub , and by the prince of demons he casts out the demons . «
41003023	So he called them to himself and said to them in parables : » How can Satan cast out Satan ?
41003024	If a kingdom is divided against itself , that kingdom cannot stand .
41003025	And if a house is divided against itself , that house cannot stand .
41003026	And if Satan has risen up against himself , and is divided , he cannot stand , but is coming to an end .
41003027	No one can enter a strong man's house and plunder his goods , unless he first binds the strong man . And then he will plunder his house .
41003028	Truly , I say to you , all sins will be forgiven the sons of men , and whatever blasphemies they utter ;
41003029	but whoever blasphemes against the Holy Spirit never has forgiveness , but is guilty of an eternal sin « —
41003030	because they said , » He has an unclean spirit . «
41003031	Then his brothers and his mother came . And standing outside they sent to him , and called him .
41003032	And a crowd was sitting around him ; and they said to him , » Your mother and your brothers are outside , asking for you . «
41003033	And he replied , » Who are my mother and my brothers ? «
41003034	And he looked at those who sat in a circle around him , and said , » Here are my mother and my brothers !
41003035	Whoever does the will of God is my brother , and sister , and mother . «
41004001	Again he began to teach by the sea . and a very large crowd gathered around him , so that he got into a boat and sat in it on the sea ; and the whole crowd was beside the sea on the land .
41004002	Then he taught them many things by parables , and said to them in his teaching :
41004003	» Listen ! A sower went out to sow .
41004004	And as he sowed the seed , some fell along the path , and the birds came and devoured it .
41004005	Some fell on rocky ground , where it did not have much soil , and immediately it sprang up , because it had no depth of soil .
41004006	But when the sun came up it was scorched , and because it had no root it withered away .
41004007	Other seed fell among thorns and the thorns grew up and choked it , and it yielded no grain .
41004008	But other seed fell on good soil and yielded a crop that sprang up , increased and produced thirtyfold , sixty , and a hundred . «
41004009	And he said , » He who has ears to hear , let him hear . «
41004010	And when he was alone , those around him with the twelve asked him about the parables .
41004011	And he said to them , » To you has been given the secret of the kingdom of God , but to those outside everything is in parables ;
41004012	so that ‘ seeing they may see but not perceive , and hearing may hear but not understand ; lest they should turn again , and be forgiven . ’ «
41004013	And he said to them , » Do you not understand this parable ? How then will you understand all the parables ?
41004014	The sower sows the word .
41004015	And these are the ones along the path where the word is sown . When they hear , Satan comes immediately and takes away the word that was sown in them .
41004016	And these likewise are the ones sown on rocky ground who , when they hear the word , immediately receive it with joy ;
41004017	and they have no root in themselves , but endure for only a time . Then , when tribulation or persecution arises on account of the word , immediately they fall away .
41004018	And others are the ones sown among thorns ; they are those who hear the word ,
41004019	but the cares of this world , the deceitfulness of riches , and the desires for other things enter in and choke the word , and it becomes unfruitful .
41004020	But these are the ones sown on good soil , those who hear the word , accept it , and bear fruit thirtyfold , sixty , and a hundred . «
41004021	And he said to them , » Is a lamp brought to be put under a basket or under a bed ? Is it not to be set on a lampstand ?
41004022	For there is nothing hidden , except to be revealed ; nor is anything secret , but that it should come to light .
41004023	If anyone has ears to hear , let him hear . «
41004024	Then he said to them , » Take heed what you hear . With the measure you use , it will be measured to you ; and more will be given you .
41004025	For whoever has , to him will more be given ; and whoever does not have , from him even what he has will be taken away . «
41004026	And he said , » The kingdom of God is as if a man should scatter seed on the ground ,
41004027	and should sleep by night and rise by day , and the seed should sprout and grow , he himself does not know how .
41004028	All by itself the earth produces grain — first the blade , then the head , then the full kernel in the head .
41004029	But when the grain is ripe , at once he puts in the sickle , because the harvest has come . «
41004030	And he said , » With what shall we compare the kingdom of God , or what parable shall we use for it ?
41004031	It is like a mustard seed which , when it is sown on the ground , is the smallest of all seeds in the earth ;
41004032	yet when it is sown it grows up and becomes the greatest of all shrubs , and puts forth large branches , so that the birds of the air can make nests in its shade . «
41004033	With many such parables he spoke the word to them , as they were able to hear it .
41004034	But without a parable he did not speak to them . And when they were alone , he explained everything to his own disciples .
41004035	On that day , when evening had come , he said to them , » Let us go over to the other side . «
41004036	And leaving the crowd , they took him along , just as he was , in the boat . There were also other boats with him .
41004037	And a great storm arose , and the waves beat into the boat , so that it was already filling .
41004038	But he was in the stern , asleep on a cushion . And they woke him and said to him , » Teacher , do you not care if we perish ? «
41004039	Then he rose and rebuked the wind , and said to the sea , » Peace ! Be still ! « And the wind ceased and there was a great calm .
41004040	He said to them , » Why are you so afraid ? Have you no faith ? «
41004041	And they were filled with awe , and said to one another , » Who is this ? Even the wind and the sea obey him ! «
41005001	They came to the other side of the sea , to the country of the Gerasenes .
41005002	And when he had come out of the boat , there met him out of the tombs a man with an unclean spirit ,
41005003	who lived among the tombs ; and no one could bind him any more , not even with a chain ,
41005004	for he had often been bound with shackles and chains . But the chains he wrenched apart , and the shackles he broke in pieces ; and no one had the strength to subdue him .
41005005	Night and day among the tombs and on the mountains he was always crying out , and cutting himself with stones .
41005006	And when he saw Jesus from a distance , he ran and worshipped him .
41005007	And crying out with a loud voice , he said , » What have you to do with me , Jesus , Son of the Most High God ? I implore you by God , do not torment me . «
41005008	For he had said to him , » Come out of the man , you unclean spirit ! «
41005009	Then Jesus asked him , » What is your name ? « And he replied , » My name is Legion , for we are many . «
41005010	And he begged him eagerly not to send them out of the country .
41005011	Now a large herd of swine was feeding there on the hillside .
41005012	So all the demons begged him , » Send us to the swine , that we may enter them . «
41005013	So he gave them permission . And the unclean spirits came out , and entered the swine ; and the herd , numbering about two thousand , rushed down the steep bank into the sea , and were drowned in the sea .
41005014	So those who fed the swine fled , and told it in the city and in the country . And people went out to see what it was that had happened .
41005015	And they came to Jesus , and saw the man who had been possessed sitting there , clothed and in his right mind , the man who had had the legion ; and they were afraid .
41005016	And those who had seen it told the people what had happened to the demon-possessed man , and about the swine .
41005017	Then they began to plead with Jesus to depart from their region .
41005018	And as he was getting into the boat , the man who had been demon-possessed begged him that he might be with him .
41005019	Jesus did not let him , but said , » Go home to your friends and tell them how much the Lord has done for you , and how he has had mercy on you . «
41005020	And he went away and began to proclaim in the Decapolis how much Jesus had done for him ; and all men marveled .
41005021	And when Jesus had crossed over again by the boat to the other side , a great crowd gathered around him ; and he was by the sea .
41005022	Then came one of the rulers of the synagogue , Jairus by name . And seeing him , he fell at his feet ,
41005023	and pleaded earnestly with him , saying , » My little daughter is at the point of death . Come and lay your hands on her , so that she may be healed , and live . «
41005024	So Jesus went with him . And a great crowd followed him and thronged around him .
41005025	And there was a woman who had endured a flow of blood for twelve years ,
41005026	and she had suffered much under many physicians , and had spent all that she owned , and was no better but rather grew worse .
41005027	When she heard about Jesus , she came up behind him in the crowd and touched his garment .
41005028	For she said , » If I touch even his clothes , I shall be made well . «
41005029	And immediately the bleeding stopped ; and she felt in her body that she was healed of her disease .
41005030	And Jesus , immediately knowing in himself that power had gone out from him , turned around in the crowd and said , » Who touched my clothes ? «
41005031	And his disciples said to him , » You see the crowd pressing around you , and yet you say , ‘ Who touched me ? ’ «
41005032	And he looked around to see who had done it .
41005033	But the woman , knowing what had happened to her , came and fell down before him in fear and trembling and told him the whole truth .
41005034	And he said to her , » Daughter , your faith has made you well . Go in peace , and be healed of your disease . «
41005035	While he was still speaking , some came from the ruler of the synagogue's house who said , » Your daughter is dead . Why trouble the Teacher any further ? «
41005036	But ignoring what they said , Jesus said to the ruler of the synagogue , » Do not be afraid ; only believe . «
41005037	And he allowed no one to follow him except Peter , James , and John the brother of James .
41005038	When they came to the house of the ruler of the synagogue , he saw a tumult , and people weeping and wailing loudly .
41005039	And when he came in , he said to them , » Why make this commotion and weep ? The child is not dead , but sleeping . «
41005040	And they laughed at him . But after he put them all outside , he took the child's father and mother and those who were with him , and went in where the child was .
41005041	He took her by the hand and said to her , » Talitha cumi ! « which means , » Little girl , I say to you , arise . «
41005042	Immediately the girl stood up and walked ( she was twelve years of age ) . And they were overcome with great amazement .
41005043	He strictly charged them that no one should know this , and told them to give her something to eat .
41006001	He went away from there and came to his own country , and his disciples followed him .
41006002	And when the Sabbath had come , he began to teach in the synagogue . And many who heard him were astonished , saying , » Where did this man get these things ? And what wisdom is this which is given to him , that such mighty works are performed by his hands !
41006003	Is not this the carpenter , the son of Mary and brother of James and Joses and Judas and Simon ? Are not his sisters here with us ? « And they took offense at him .
41006004	But Jesus said to them , » A prophet is not without honor except in his own country , among his own relatives , and in his own house . «
41006005	Now he could do no mighty work there , except that he laid his hands on a few sick people and healed them .
41006006	And he marveled because of their unbelief . Then he went around the villages teaching .
41006007	And he called to him the twelve , and began to send them out two by two , and gave them authority over the unclean spirits .
41006008	He commanded them to take nothing for the journey except a staff — no bag , no bread , no money in their belts —
41006009	but to wear sandals and not put on two tunics .
41006010	And he said to them , » Where you enter a house , stay there until you leave that place .
41006011	And if any place will not receive you and they refuse to hear you , when you leave , shake off the dust that is on your feet for a testimony against them . «
41006012	So they went out and preached that people should repent .
41006013	And they cast out many demons , and anointed with oil many that were sick and healed them .
41006014	King Herod heard of it , for Jesus' name had become well known . Some said , » John the Baptist has been raised from the dead , and that is why these powers are at work in him . «
41006015	But others said , » It is Elijah . « And others said , » It is a prophet , like one of the prophets of old . «
41006016	But when Herod heard , he said , » This is John , whom I beheaded ; he has been raised from the dead ! «
41006017	For Herod himself had sent and had John arrested , and bound him in prison for the sake of Herodias , his brother Philip's wife ; because he had married her .
41006018	For John had said to Herod , » It is not lawful for you to have your brother's wife . «
41006019	And Herodias had a grudge against him , and wanted to kill him . But she could not ,
41006020	for Herod feared John and protected him , knowing that he was a righteous and holy man . When he heard him , he was much perplexed ; and yet he heard him gladly .
41006021	But an opportunity came when Herod on his birthday gave a banquet for his high officers and military commanders and the leading men of Galilee .
41006022	And when the daughter of Herodias came in and danced , she pleased Herod and his dinner guests . The king said to the girl , » Ask me for whatever you want , and I will give it to you . «
41006023	And he vowed to her , » Whatever you ask me , I will give you , up to half of my kingdom . «
41006024	So she went out and said to her mother , » What shall I ask ? « And she said , » The head of John the Baptist ! «
41006025	Immediately she came in with haste to the king and asked , saying , » I want you to give me at once the head of John the Baptist on a platter . «
41006026	And the king was exceedingly sorry ; but , because of his oaths and his guests , he did not want to refuse her .
41006027	And immediately the king sent an executioner and gave orders to bring his head . He went and beheaded him in the prison ,
41006028	and brought his head on a platter , and gave it to the girl ; and the girl gave it to her mother .
41006029	When his disciples heard of it , they came and took his body , and laid it in a tomb .
41006030	The apostles gathered to Jesus , and told him all that they had done and taught .
41006031	And he said to them , » Come away by yourselves to a lonely place and rest a while . « For there were many coming and going , and they did not even have time to eat .
41006032	So they went away in the boat to a lonely place by themselves .
41006033	But many saw them going , and knew them , and they ran there on foot from all the towns , and got there ahead of them .
41006034	When Jesus went ashore he saw a great crowd , and he had compassion on them , because they were like sheep without a shepherd . So he began to teach them many things .
41006035	When it was late in the day , his disciples came to him and said , » This is a deserted place , and already the hour is late .
41006036	Send them away , so they can go to the surrounding country and villages and buy themselves something to eat . «
41006037	But he answered them , » You give them something to eat . « And they said to him , » Shall we go and buy two hundred denarii worth of bread , and give it to them to eat ? «
41006038	But he said to them , » How many loaves do you have ? Go and see . « And when they found out they said , » Five , and two fish . «
41006039	Then he commanded them to make them all sit down in groups on the green grass .
41006040	So they sat down in groups , of hundreds and fifties .
41006041	And taking the five loaves and the two fish he looked up to heaven , and blessed , and broke the loaves , and gave them to his disciples to set before the people ; and he divided the two fish among them all .
41006042	And they all ate and were satisfied .
41006043	And they took up twelve baskets full of broken pieces and of the fish .
41006044	Now those who had eaten the loaves were about five thousand men .
41006045	Immediately he made his disciples get into the boat and go before him to the other side , to Bethsaida , while he dismissed the crowd .
41006046	And after he had left them , he went up on the mountain to pray .
41006047	When evening came , the boat was in the middle of the sea , and he was alone on land .
41006048	And he saw the disciples straining at the oars , for the wind was against them . About the fourth watch of the night he came to them , walking on the sea . He was about to pass by them ,
41006049	but when they saw him walking on the sea they thought it was a ghost , and cried out ;
41006050	for they all saw him , and were terrified . But immediately he spoke to them and said , » Take courage ! It is I ; do not be afraid . «
41006051	Then he climbed into the boat with them , and the wind ceased . And they were completely amazed ,
41006052	for they had not understood about the loaves , because their hearts were hardened .
41006053	When they had crossed over , they came to land at Gennesaret and anchored there .
41006054	And when they got out of the boat , immediately the people recognized him ,
41006055	and ran about that whole region , and began to carry those who were sick around on pallets to wherever they heard he was .
41006056	Wherever he entered , into villages , cities , or the country , they laid the sick in the marketplaces , and begged him that they might touch even the fringe of his garment . And as many as touched him were made well .
41007001	Now when the Pharisees and some of the scribes who had come from Jerusalem gathered together to him ,
41007002	they saw some of his disciples eating food with hands that were defiled , that is , unwashed .
41007003	( For the Pharisees and all the Jews do not eat unless they wash their hands in a special way , holding the tradition of the elders .
41007004	When they come from the marketplace , they do not eat unless they wash themselves . And there are many other traditions which they observe , the washing of cups and pitchers and copper vessels . )
41007005	The Pharisees and the scribes asked him , » Why do your disciples not live according to the tradition of the elders , but eat with impure hands ? «
41007006	And he said to them , » Well did Isaiah prophesy of you hypocrites ; as it is written : ‘ This people honors me with their lips , but their heart is far from me .
41007007	
41007008	You let go of the commandment of God , and hold on to the tradition of men . «
41007009	And he said to them , » You have a fine way of rejecting the commandment of God , in order to keep your tradition !
41007010	For Moses said , ‘ Honor your father and your mother ’ ; and , ‘ He who curses father or mother , let him be put to death . ’
41007011	But you say that if a man says to his father or mother , ‘ Whatever help you might otherwise have received from me is Corban ’ ( that is , a gift devoted to God ) ,
41007012	then you no longer let him do anything for his father or mother ,
41007013	thus making void the word of God through your tradition which you have handed down . And many such things you do . «
41007014	And he called all the people to him again , and said to them , » Hear me , everyone , and understand :
41007015	there is nothing outside a man which by going into him can defile him ; but the things which come out of a man are what defile him . «
41007017	When he had left the crowd and entered the house , his disciples asked him about this parable .
41007018	So he said to them , » Are you also without understanding ? Do you not see that whatever enters a man from outside cannot defile him ,
41007019	since it does not enter his heart but his stomach , and so passes on ? « ( Thus he declared all foods clean . )
41007020	And he said , » What comes out of a man is what defiles a man .
41007021	For from within , out of the heart of men , come evil thoughts , fornications , theft , murder , adultery ,
41007022	coveting , wickedness , deceit , lewdness , envy , slander , pride , foolishness .
41007023	All these evil things come from within , and they defile a man . «
41007024	From there he arose and went away to the region of Tyre and Sidon . And he entered a house , and did not want anyone to know it ; yet he could not be hidden .
41007025	But a woman whose little daughter was possessed by an unclean spirit heard about him , and she came and fell at his feet .
41007026	Now the woman was a Greek , a Syrophoenician by birth . And she begged him to cast the demon out of her daughter .
41007027	And he said to her , » Let the children first be fed , for it is not right to take the children’s bread and throw it to the dogs . «
41007028	But she answered him , » Yes , Lord , yet even the dogs under the table eat the children's crumbs . «
41007029	Then he said to her , » For this saying you may go your way ; the demon has left your daughter . «
41007030	She went home , and found her child lying on the bed , and the demon gone .
41007031	Then he departed from the region of Tyre , and went through Sidon to the Sea of Galilee , through the region of the Decapolis .
41007032	Then they brought to him a man who was deaf and had an impediment in his speech , and they begged him to put his hand on him .
41007033	And he took him aside from the multitude , and put his fingers into his ears , and he spat and touched his tongue .
41007034	And looking up to heaven he sighed and said to him , » Ephphatha , « that is , » Be opened . «
41007035	And immediately his ears were opened , and the impediment of his tongue was loosed , and he spoke plainly .
41007036	And he commanded them to tell no one ; but the more he charged them , the more widely they proclaimed it .
41007037	And they were astonished beyond measure , saying , » He has done all things well . He even makes the deaf to hear and the mute to speak . «
41008001	In those days , when again a great crowd had gathered , and they had nothing to eat , Jesus called his disciples to him , and said to them ,
41008002	» I have compassion on the multitude , because they have now been with me three days and have nothing to eat .
41008003	And if I send them away hungry to their homes , they will faint on the way ; and some of them have come a long distance . «
41008004	And his disciples answered him , » How can one feed these men with bread here in the desert ? «
41008005	And he asked them , » How many loaves do you have ? « They said , » Seven . «
41008006	So he commanded the crowd to sit down on the ground . And he took the seven loaves , and having given thanks he broke them and gave them to his disciples to set before the people ; and they set them before the crowd .
41008007	They also had a few small fish ; and having blessed them , he commanded that these also should be set before them .
41008008	They ate , and were satisfied ; and they took up seven baskets full of the broken pieces left over .
41008009	About four thousand men were present . And having sent them away ,
41008010	he immediately got into the boat with his disciples , and went to the region of Dalmanutha .
41008011	The Pharisees came and began to argue with him , seeking from him a sign from heaven , to test him .
41008012	And he sighed deeply in his spirit , and said , » Why does this generation seek a sign ? Truly , I say to you , no sign shall be given to this generation . «
41008013	And he left them , and getting into the boat again he departed to the other side .
41008014	Now the disciples had forgotten to bring bread , and they had only one loaf with them in the boat .
41008015	And he cautioned them , saying , » Take heed , beware of the leaven of the Pharisees and the leaven of Herod . «
41008016	And they discussed it with one another , saying , » It is because we have no bread . «
41008017	Being aware of it , Jesus said to them , » Why do you discuss the fact that you have no bread ? Do you not yet perceive or understand ? Are your hearts hardened ?
41008018	Having eyes do you not see , and having ears do you not hear ? And do you not remember ?
41008019	When I broke the five loaves for the five thousand , how many baskets full of broken pieces did you take up ? « They said to him , » Twelve . «
41008020	» And when I broke the seven for the four thousand , how many large baskets full of pieces did you take up ? « And they said , » Seven . «
41008021	He said to them , » Do you not yet understand ? «
41008022	And they came to Bethsaida ; and some people brought a blind man to him , and begged him to touch him .
41008023	So he took the blind man by the hand and led him out of the village . And when he had spit on his eyes and put his hands on him , he asked him » Do you see anything ? «
41008024	And he looked up and said , » I see men ; but they look like trees , walking . «
41008025	Then he put his hands on his eyes again and made him look up . And he was restored , and saw everything clearly .
41008026	And he sent him away to his home , saying , » Do not even go into the village . «
41008027	And Jesus went on with his disciples , to the villages of Caesarea Philippi ; and on the way he asked his disciples , » Who do men say that I am ? «
41008028	They replied , » Some say John the Baptist ; others say Elijah ; and still others , one of the prophets . «
41008029	And he asked them , » But who do you say that I am ? « Peter answered him , » You are the Christ . «
41008030	And he charged them to tell no one about him .
41008031	And he began to teach them that the Son of Man must suffer many things , and be rejected by the elders and the chief priests and the scribes , and be killed , and after three days rise again .
41008032	He spoke plainly about this . And Peter took him aside and began to rebuke him .
41008033	But when he had turned around and looked at his disciples , he rebuked Peter , and said , » Get behind me , Satan ! For you are not mindful of the things of God , but the things of men . «
41008034	And he called to him the multitude with his disciples , and said to them , » If anyone would come after me , let him deny himself and take up his cross and follow me .
41008035	For whoever desires to save his life will lose it , but whoever loses his life for my sake and the gospel’s will save it .
41008036	For what does it profit a man to gain the whole world , and forfeit his soul ?
41008037	Or what can a man give in exchange for his soul ?
41008038	For whoever is ashamed of me and my words in this adulterous and sinful generation , of him the Son of Man will also be ashamed when he comes in the glory of his Father with the holy angels . «
41009001	And he said to them , » Truly , I say to you that there are some standing here who will not taste death before they see the kingdom of God come with power . «
41009002	After six days Jesus took with him Peter and James and John , and led them up a high mountain apart by themselves . And he was transfigured before them ,
41009003	and his clothes became dazzling , exceedingly white , as no launderer on earth could bleach them .
41009004	And there appeared to them Elijah with Moses , and they were talking with Jesus .
41009005	And Peter said to Jesus , » Rabbi , it is good for us to be here . And let us make three tabernacles — one for you , one for Moses , and one for Elijah . «
41009006	For he did not know what to say , for they were greatly afraid .
41009007	And a cloud came and overshadowed them ; and a voice came out of the cloud , » This is my beloved Son . Listen to him ! «
41009008	Suddenly , when they looked around , they no longer saw anyone with them but Jesus only .
41009009	And as they were coming down the mountain , he charged them to tell no one what they had seen , until the Son of Man had risen from the dead .
41009010	So they kept the matter to themselves , questioning what the rising from the dead meant .
41009011	And they asked him , » Why do the scribes say that Elijah must come first ? «
41009012	Then he said to them , » Elijah does come first and restores all things . And how is it written of the Son of Man , that he must suffer many things and be treated with contempt ?
41009013	But I tell you that Elijah has come , and they did to him whatever they wished , as it is written of him . «
41009014	And when they came to the disciples , they saw a great crowd around them , and scribes arguing with them .
41009015	Immediately , when they saw him , all the people were greatly amazed , and ran to him and greeted him .
41009016	And he asked them , » What are you discussing with them ? «
41009017	And one of the crowd answered him , » Teacher , I brought my son to you , who has a mute spirit .
41009018	And wherever it seizes him , it throws him down ; he foams at the mouth , gnashes his teeth and becomes rigid . I asked your disciples to cast out the spirit , but they could not . «
41009019	He answered him , » O faithless generation , how long shall I be with you ? How long shall I bear with you ? Bring him to me . «
41009020	And they brought the boy to him . And when the spirit saw him , immediately it convulsed the boy , and he fell on the ground and rolled about , foaming at the mouth .
41009021	And Jesus asked his father , » How long has he been like this ? « And he said , » From childhood .
41009022	And it has often thrown him both into the fire and into the water to destroy him . But if you can do anything , have pity on us and help us . «
41009023	Jesus said to him , » If you can , all things are possible to him who believes . «
41009024	Immediately the father of the child cried out and said , » I believe ; help my unbelief ! «
41009025	And when Jesus saw that a crowd came running together , he rebuked the unclean spirit , saying to it , » You dumb and deaf spirit , I command you , come out of him , and never enter him again . «
41009026	And the spirit cried out , convulsed him terribly , and came out . And the boy was like a corpse ; so that many of them said , » He is dead . «
41009027	But Jesus took him by the hand and lifted him up , and he arose .
41009028	And when he had come into the house , his disciples asked him privately , » Why could we not cast it out ? «
41009029	And he said to them , » This kind can only come out by prayer . «
41009030	Then they departed from there and passed through Galilee , and he did not want anyone to know it .
41009031	For he was teaching his disciples and said to them , » The Son of Man is going to be betrayed into the hands of men . They will kill him , and when he is killed , after three days he will rise . «
41009032	But they did not understand the saying , and they were afraid to ask him .
41009033	And they came to Capernaum . When he was in the house , he asked them , » What were you discussing on the road ? «
41009034	But they kept silent ; for on the way they had discussed with one another who was the greatest .
41009035	And he sat down , called the twelve , and said to them , » If anyone desires to be first , he must be last of all and servant of all . «
41009036	And he took a little child , and put him in the midst of them . And taking him in his arms , he said to them ,
41009037	» Whoever receives one of these little children in my name receives me ; and whoever receives me , receives not me but him who sent me . «
41009038	John said to him , » Teacher , we saw a man casting out demons in your name and we forbade him , because he was not one of us . «
41009039	But Jesus said , » Do not forbid him , for no one who does a miracle in my name can soon afterward speak evil of me .
41009040	For he who is not against us is for us .
41009041	For truly , I say to you , whoever gives you a cup of water to drink in my name , because you belong to Christ , will by no means lose his reward .
41009042	» Whoever causes one of these little ones who believe in me to sin , it would be better for him if a great millstone were hung round his neck and he were thrown into the sea .
41009043	If your hand causes you to sin , cut it off . It is better for you to enter life maimed than with two hands to go into hell , to the fire that shall never be quenched .
41009045	And if your foot causes you to sin , cut it off ; it is better for you to enter life lame than with two feet to be thrown into hell .
41009047	And if your eye causes you to sin , pluck it out . It is better for you to enter the kingdom of God with one eye than to have two eyes and be thrown into hell ,
41009048	where ‘ their worm does not die , and the fire is not quenched . ’
41009049	For every one will be salted with fire .
41009050	Salt is good , but if the salt loses its flavor , how will you season it ? Have salt in yourselves , and be at peace with one another . «
41010001	Then he left there and went to the region of Judea and beyond the Jordan . And crowds gathered to him again ; and again , as his custom was , he taught them .
41010002	The Pharisees came and in order to test him asked , » Is it lawful for a man to divorce his wife ? «
41010003	He answered them , » What did Moses command you ? «
41010004	They said , » Moses permitted a man to write a certificate of divorce , and to put her away . «
41010005	But Jesus said to them , » Because of your hardness of heart he wrote you this commandment .
41010006	But from the beginning of creation God ‘ made them male and female . ’
41010007	‘ For this reason a man shall leave his father and mother and be joined to his wife ,
41010008	and the two shall become one flesh . ’ So they are no longer two , but one flesh .
41010009	Therefore what God has joined together , let not man separate . «
41010010	In the house his disciples also asked him again about this matter .
41010011	So he said to them , » Whoever divorces his wife and marries another commits adultery against her .
41010012	And if she divorces her husband and marries another man , she commits adultery . «
41010013	And they were bringing children to him , that he might touch them ; but the disciples rebuked them .
41010014	But when Jesus saw it , he was indignant and said to them , » Let the little children come to me ; and do not hinder them , for to such belongs the kingdom of God .
41010015	Truly , I say to you , whoever does not receive the kingdom of God like a little child will not enter it . «
41010016	And he took them in his arms , put his hands on them and blessed them .
41010017	And as he was setting out on his journey , a man ran up and knelt before him , and asked him , » Good Teacher , what must I do to inherit eternal life ? «
41010018	And Jesus said to him , » Why do you call me good ? No one is good but God alone .
41010019	You know the commandments : ‘ Do not murder , Do not commit adultery , Do not steal , Do not bear false witness , Do not defraud , Honor your father and mother . ’ «
41010020	And he said to him , » Teacher , all these I have observed from my youth . «
41010021	Then Jesus , looking at him , loved him , and said to him , » You lack one thing ; go and sell what you have , and give to the poor , and you will have treasure in heaven ; and come , follow me . «
41010022	But he fell sad at this word , and went away sorrowful , for he had great possessions .
41010023	Then Jesus looked around and said to his disciples , » How hard it is for those who have riches to enter the kingdom of God ! «
41010024	And the disciples were amazed at his words . But Jesus said to them again , » Children , how hard it is to enter the kingdom of God !
41010025	It is easier for a camel to go through the eye of a needle than for a rich man to enter the kingdom of God . «
41010026	And they were exceedingly astonished , and said to him , » Then who can be saved ? «
41010027	Jesus looked at them and said , » With men it is impossible , but not with God ; for all things are possible with God . «
41010028	Peter began to say to him , » See , we have left everything and followed you . «
41010029	Jesus said , » Truly , I say to you , there is no one who has left house or brothers or sisters or mother or father or children or lands , for my sake and for the gospel ,
41010030	who will not receive a hundredfold now in this time — house and brothers and sisters and mothers and children and lands , with persecutions , and in the age to come , eternal life .
41010031	But many who are first will be last , and the last first . «
41010032	They were on the road , going up to Jerusalem , and Jesus was walking ahead of them ; and they were amazed , and those who followed were afraid . And he took the twelve aside again and began to tell them what was to happen to him .
41010033	» Behold , we are going up to Jerusalem ; and the Son of Man will be betrayed to the chief priests and the scribes , and they will condemn him to death , and deliver him to the Gentiles ;
41010034	and they will mock him , and spit on him , and scourge him , and kill him . And after three days he will rise . «
41010035	Then James and John , the sons of Zebedee , came to him and said , » Teacher , we want you to do for us whatever we ask . «

41010037	And they said to him , » Grant us to sit , one at your right hand and the other at your left , in your glory . «
