41010040	but to sit at my right hand or at my left is not mine to grant , but it is for those for whom it has been prepared . «
41010041	And when the ten heard it , they began to be indignant with James and John .
41010042	But Jesus called them to himself and said to them , » You know that those who are considered rulers over the Gentiles lord it over them , and their great ones exercise authority over them .
41010043	But it shall not be so among you . But whoever wants to become great among you must be your servant ,
41010044	and whoever wants to be first among you must be slave of all .
41010045	For even the Son of Man did not come to be served , but to serve , and to give his life as a ransom for many . «
41010046	And they came to Jericho . And as he was leaving Jericho with his disciples and a great multitude , Bartimaeus , a blind man , the son of Timaeus , was sitting by the roadside begging .
41010047	And when he heard that it was Jesus of Nazareth , he began to cry out and say , » Jesus , Son of David , have mercy on me ! «
41010048	Many rebuked him and told him to be quiet , but he cried out all the more , » Son of David , have mercy on me ! «
41010049	So Jesus stopped and said , » Call him . « And they called the blind man , saying to him , » Take heart ; rise , he is calling you . «
41010050	And throwing aside his garment , he rose and came to Jesus .
41010051	And Jesus said to him , » What do you want me to do for you ? « And the blind man said to him , » Master , let me receive my sight . «
41010052	Then Jesus said to him , » Go your way ; your faith has made you well . « And immediately he received his sight and followed Jesus on the road .
41011001	And when they drew near Jerusalem , to Bethphage and Bethany , at the Mount of Olives , he sent two of his disciples ,
41011002	and said to them , » Go into the village opposite you , and immediately as you enter it you will find a colt tied , on which no one has ever sat . Untie it and bring it .
41011003	If anyone says to you , ‘ Why are you doing this ? ’ say , ‘ The Lord has need of it and will send it back here immediately . ’ «
41011004	They went away and found a colt tied at the door outside in the open street , and they untied it .
41011005	And some of those who stood there said to them , » What are you doing , untying the colt ? «
41011006	They answered as Jesus had told them to , and they let them go .
41011007	Then they brought the colt to Jesus and threw their garments on it , and he sat on it .
41011008	And many spread their garments on the road , and others spread leafy branches which they had cut from the fields .
41011009	And those who went before and those who followed cried out , » Hosanna ! Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord !
41011010	
41011011	Jesus entered Jerusalem , and went into the temple . And when he had looked round at everything , as it was already late , he went out to Bethany with the twelve .
41011012	On the next day , when they came from Bethany , he was hungry .
41011013	And seeing in the distance a fig tree in leaf , he went to see if he could find anything on it . When he came to it , he found nothing but leaves , for it was not the season for figs .
41011014	And he said to it , » May no one ever eat fruit from you again . « And his disciples heard it .
41011015	So they came to Jerusalem . And Jesus entered the temple and began to drive out those who bought and sold in the temple , and overturned the tables of the money changers and the seats of those who sold doves .
41011016	And he would not allow anyone to carry merchandise through the temple .
41011017	And as he taught them , he said , » Is it not written , ‘ My house shall be called a house of prayer for all the nations ’ ? But you have made it a den of robbers . «
41011018	And the chief priests and the scribes heard it and sought a way to destroy him ; for they feared him , because all the multitude was astonished at his teaching .
41011019	When evening came , they went out of the city .
41011020	In the morning , as they passed by , they saw the fig tree withered from the roots .
41011021	Peter remembered and said to him , » Rabbi , look ! The fig tree which you cursed has withered . «
41011022	And Jesus answered them , » Have faith in God .
41011023	Truly , I say to you , whoever says to this mountain , ‘ Be taken up and cast into the sea , ’ and does not doubt in his heart , but believes that what he says will come to pass , it will be done for him .
41011024	Therefore I tell you , whatever you ask for in prayer , believe that you have received it , and it will be yours .
41011025	And whenever you stand praying , if you have anything against anyone , forgive him , so that your Father in heaven may also forgive you your trespasses .
41011027	Then they came again to Jerusalem . And as he was walking in the temple , the chief priests , the scribes , and the elders came to him .
41011028	And they said to him , » By what authority are you doing these things ? Who gave you this authority to do them ? «
41011029	Jesus said to them , » I will ask you one question ; answer me , and I will tell you by what authority I do these things .
41011030	The baptism of John — was it from heaven or from men ? Answer me . «
41011031	And they reasoned among themselves , » If we say , ‘ From heaven , ’ He will say , ‘ Why then did you not believe him ? ’
41011032	But if we say , ‘ From men ’ « — they feared the people , for all held that John was a real prophet .
41011033	So they answered Jesus , » We do not know . « And Jesus said to them , » Neither will I tell you by what authority I do these things . «
41012001	Then he began to speak to them in parables : » A man planted a vineyard and set a hedge around it , dug a place for the wine vat and built a tower . And he leased it to vine dressers and went into a far country .
41012002	At harvest time he sent a servant to the tenants , to collect from them some of the fruit of the vineyard .
41012003	And they took him and beat him , and sent him away empty-handed .
41012004	Again he sent to them another servant , and they wounded him in the head , and treated him shamefully .
41012005	And he sent another , and him they killed ; and so with many others , some they beat and some they killed .
41012006	He still had one left to send , a beloved son . He sent him to them last , saying , ‘ They will respect my son . ’
41012007	But those tenants said to one another , ‘ This is the heir . Come , let us kill him , and the inheritance will be ours . ’
41012008	So they took him and killed him , and cast him out of the vineyard .
41012009	What will the owner of the vineyard do ? He will come and destroy the tenants , and give the vineyard to others .
41012010	Have you not read this Scripture : ‘ The stone which the builders rejected has become the chief cornerstone ;
41012011	
41012012	And they sought to arrest him , but feared the multitude , for they knew he had spoken the parable against them . So they left him and went away .
41012013	Then they sent to him some of the Pharisees and the Herodians , to catch him in his words .
41012014	When they came , they said to him , » Teacher , we know that you are true , and care about no man ; for you do not regard the person of men , but teach the way of God in truth . Is it lawful to pay taxes to Caesar , or not ?
41012015	Should we pay them , or should we not ? « But knowing their hypocrisy , he said to them , » Why do you put me to the test ? Bring me a denarius , and let me look at it . «
41012016	And they brought one . And he said to them , » Whose likeness and inscription is this ? « They said to him , » Caesar's . «
41012017	Jesus said to them , » Render to Caesar the things that are Caesar’s , and to God the things that are God’s . « And they were amazed at him .
41012018	Then some Sadducees , who say there is no resurrection , came to him ; and they asked him a question , saying :
41012019	» Teacher , Moses wrote for us that if a man’s brother dies and leaves a wife , but leaves no child , the man must take the wife , and raise up children for his brother .
41012020	Now there were seven brothers ; the first took a wife , and when he died left no children .
41012021	And the second took her , and he died ; leaving behind no children . And the third likewise .
41012022	So the seven had her and left no children . Last of all the woman died also .
41012023	In the resurrection , whose wife will she be ? For the seven had her as wife . «
41012024	Jesus said to them , » Is not this why you are wrong , that you do not know the Scriptures nor the power of God ?
41012025	For when they rise from the dead , they neither marry nor are given in marriage , but are like angels in heaven .
41012026	And as for the dead being raised , have you not read in the book of Moses , in the passage about the bush , how God said to him , ‘ I am the God of Abraham , and the God of Isaac , and the God of Jacob ’ ?
41012027	He is not the God of the dead , but of the living ; you are greatly mistaken . «
41012028	And one of the scribes came up and heard them disputing with one another , and seeing that he had answered them well , asked him , » Which commandment is the first of all ? «
41012029	Jesus answered , » The first is : ‘ Hear , O Israel , the Lord our God is one Lord .
41012030	And you shall love the Lord your God with all your heart , and with all your soul , and with all your mind , and with all your strength . ’
41012031	The second is this : ‘ You shall love your neighbor as yourself . ’ There is no other commandment greater than these . «
41012032	And the scribe said to him , » You are right , Teacher ; you have well said that God is one , and there is no other but he ;
41012033	and to love him with all the heart , and with all the understanding , and with all the strength , and to love one's neighbor as oneself , is much more than all whole burnt offerings and sacrifices . «
41012034	And when Jesus saw that he answered wisely , he said to him , » You are not far from the kingdom of God . « And after that no one dared to ask him any question .
41012035	And Jesus said , while he taught in the temple , » How is it that the scribes say that the Christ is the Son of David ?
41012036	David himself , speaking by the Holy Spirit , declared : ‘ The Lord said to my Lord : » Sit at my right hand till I put your enemies under your feet . « ’
41012037	Therefore David himself calls him ‘ Lord ’ ; how is he then his son ? « And the common people heard him gladly .
41012038	And in his teaching he said , » Beware of the scribes , who like to go around in long robes , and to have salutations in the market places
41012039	and the best seats in the synagogues and the places of honor at feasts ,
41012040	who devour widows' houses and for a pretense make long prayers . They will receive the greater condemnation . «
41012041	And Jesus sat down opposite the treasury , and watched the multitude putting money into the treasury . Many people who were rich put in large sums .
41012042	And a poor widow came , and put in two copper coins , which make a penny .
41012043	And he called his disciples to him , and said to them , » Truly , I say to you , this poor widow has put in more than all those who are contributing to the treasury .
41012044	For they all put in out of their abundance , but she out of her poverty put in everything — all she had to live on . «
41013001	And as he came out of the temple , one of his disciples said to him , » Look , Teacher , what wonderful stones and what wonderful buildings ! «
41013002	And Jesus said to him , » Do you see all these great buildings ? There will not be left here one stone upon another , that will not be thrown down . «
41013003	Now as he sat on the Mount of Olives opposite the temple , Peter , James , John , and Andrew asked him privately ,
41013004	» Tell us , when will this be ? And what will be the sign when these things are all to be fulfilled ? «
41013005	And Jesus began to say to them : » Take heed that no one deceives you .
41013006	Many will come in my name , saying , ‘ I am he , ’ and will deceive many .
41013007	When you hear of wars and rumors of wars , do not be alarmed ; such things must happen , but the end is not yet .
41013008	For nation will rise against nation , and kingdom against kingdom . And there will be earthquakes in various places , and there will be famines and troubles . These are the beginning of birth pains .
41013009	But watch out for yourselves , for they will deliver you up to councils , and you will be beaten in the synagogues . You will be brought before governors and kings for my sake , for a testimony to them .
41013010	And the gospel must first be preached to all nations .
41013011	And when they bring you to trial and deliver you up , do not worry beforehand what you are to say . But say whatever is given you in that hour ; for it is not you who speak , but the Holy Spirit .
41013012	Brother will betray brother to death , and a father his child ; and children will rise up against parents and have them put to death .
41013013	And you will be hated by all men for my name's sake . But he who endures to the end will be saved .
41013014	» When you see ‘ the abomination of desolation ’ standing where it ought not to be ( let the reader understand ) , then let those who are in Judea flee to the mountains .
41013015	Let him who is on the housetop not go down into the house , nor enter to take anything out of his house .
41013016	And let him who is in the field not go back to get his cloak .
41013017	But woe for those who are pregnant and those who are nursing babies in those days !
41013018	Pray that it may not happen in winter .
41013019	For in those days there will be tribulation , such as has not been from the beginning of the creation which God created until now , and never will be .
41013020	And if the Lord had not shortened those days , no flesh would be saved ; but for the sake of the elect , whom he chose , he shortened the days .
41013021	Then if anyone says to you , ‘ Look , here is the Christ ! ’ or , ‘ Look , he is there ! ’ do not believe it .
41013022	For false christs and false prophets will rise and show signs and wonders to deceive , if possible , even the elect .
41013023	But take heed ; see , I have told you all things beforehand .
41013024	» But in those days , after that tribulation , the sun will be darkened , and the moon will not give its light ;
41013025	
41013026	Then they will see the Son of Man coming in the clouds with great power and glory .
41013027	And then he will send out his angels , and gather his elect from the four winds , from the ends of the earth to the ends of heaven .
41013028	» Now learn this lesson from the fig tree : as soon as its branch becomes tender and puts forth its leaves , you know that summer is near .
41013029	So also , when you see these things happening , you know that it is near , right at the door .
41013030	Truly , I say to you , this generation will not pass away before all these things take place .
41013031	Heaven and earth will pass away , but my words will not pass away .
41013032	» But of that day or that hour no one knows , not even the angels in heaven , nor the Son , but only the Father .
41013033	Take heed , watch ; for you do not know when the time will come .
41013034	It is like a man going on a journey , when he leaves his house and puts his servants in charge , each with his work , and commands the doorkeeper to be on the watch .
41013035	Watch therefore — for you do not know when the master of the house will come , in the evening , or at midnight , or when the rooster crows , or in the morning —
41013036	lest , coming suddenly , he find you sleeping .
41013037	And what I say to you , I say to all : Watch ! «
41014001	It was now two days before the Passover and the feast of Unleavened Bread . And the chief priests and the scribes were seeking how to arrest him by stealth , and kill him .
41014002	But they said , » Not during the feast , lest there be an uproar of the people . «
41014003	And while he was at Bethany in the house of Simon the leper , as he sat at table , a woman came with an alabaster flask of ointment of pure nard , very costly . And she broke the flask and poured it over his head .
41014004	But there were some who said to themselves indignantly , » Why was this ointment wasted ?
41014005	For it might have been sold for more than three hundred denarii and given to the poor . « And they criticized her sharply .
41014006	But Jesus said , » Let her alone . Why do you trouble her ? She has done a beautiful thing to me .
41014007	For you always have the poor with you , and whenever you will , you can do good to them ; but you will not always have me .
41014008	She has done what she could . She has come beforehand to anoint my body for burial .
41014009	And truly , I say to you , wherever the gospel is preached in the whole world , what she has done will also be told in memory of her . «
41014010	Then Judas Iscariot , one of the twelve , went to the chief priests to betray him to them .
41014011	And when they heard it they were glad , and promised to give him money . So he sought an opportunity to betray him .
41014012	Now on the first day of Unleavened Bread , when they killed the Passover lamb , his disciples said to him , » Where do you want us to go and prepare for you to eat the Passover ? «
41014013	And he sent two of his disciples , and said to them , » Go into the city , and a man carrying a jar of water will meet you ; follow him .
41014014	And wherever he enters , say to the owner of the house , ‘ The Teacher says , where is my guest room , where I may eat the Passover with my disciples ? ’
41014015	He will show you a large upper room , furnished and ready ; make preparations for us there . «
41014016	So the disciples set out and went to the city , and found it just as he had told them ; and they prepared the Passover .
41014017	And when it was evening he came with the twelve .
41014018	And as they were at table eating , Jesus said , » Truly , I say to you , one of you will betray me , one who is eating with me . «
41014019	They began to be sorrowful , and to say to him one by one , » Is it I ? «
41014020	He said to them , » It is one of the twelve , one who dips bread into the dish with me .
41014021	For the Son of Man goes just as it is written of him , but woe to that man by whom the Son of Man is betrayed ! It would have been better for that man if he had not been born . «
41014022	And as they were eating , Jesus took bread , blessed and broke it , and gave it to them and said , » Take ; this is my body . «
41014023	Then he took the cup , and when he had given thanks he gave it to them , and they all drank from it .
41014024	And he said to them , » This is my blood of the covenant , which is poured out for many .
41014025	Truly , I say to you , I will not drink of the fruit of the vine until that day when I drink it new in the kingdom of God . «
41014026	And when they had sung a hymn , they went out to the Mount of Olives .
41014027	And Jesus said to them , » You will all fall away ; for it is written : ‘ I will strike the shepherd , and the sheep will be scattered . ’
41014028	But after I have been raised , I will go before you to Galilee . «
41014029	Peter said to him , » Even if all fall away , I will not . «
41014030	Jesus said to him , » Truly , I say to you that this very night , before the rooster crows twice , you will deny me three times . «
41014031	But he spoke more vehemently , » If I have to die with you , I will not deny you ! « And they all said the same .
41014032	They went to a place which was called Gethsemane ; and he said to his disciples , » Sit here , while I pray . «
41014033	And he took Peter , James and John with him , and he began to be deeply distressed and troubled .
41014034	And he said to them , » My soul is very sorrowful , even to death ; stay here , and watch . «
41014035	And going a little farther , he fell on the ground and prayed that , if it were possible , the hour might pass from him .
41014036	And he said , » Abba , Father , all things are possible for you . Take this cup away from me ; yet not what I will , but what you will . «
41014037	Then he came and found them sleeping , and he said to Peter , » Simon , are you asleep ? Could you not watch one hour ?
41014038	Watch and pray that you may not enter into temptation . The spirit indeed is willing , but the flesh is weak . «
41014039	And again he went away and prayed , saying the same words .
41014040	And when he came again , he found them sleeping , for their eyes were heavy ; and they did not know what to answer him .
41014041	Then he came the third time and said to them , » Are you still sleeping and resting ? It is enough ! The hour has come ; behold , the Son of Man is being betrayed into the hands of sinners .
41014042	Rise , let us go ; see , my betrayer is at hand . «
41014043	And immediately , while he was still speaking , Judas came , one of the twelve , and with him a crowd with swords and clubs , from the chief priests and the scribes and the elders .
41014044	Now the betrayer had given them a signal , saying , » The one I shall kiss is the man ; seize him and lead him away under guard . «
41014045	And when he came , he went up to him at once , and said , » Rabbi ! « and he kissed him .
41014046	And they laid hands on him and seized him .
41014047	And one of those who stood by drew his sword and struck the servant of the high priest , and cut off his ear .
41014048	And Jesus said to them , » Have you come out as against a robber , with swords and clubs to capture me ?
41014049	Every day I was with you in the temple teaching , and you did not seize me . But the scriptures must be fulfilled . «
41014050	Then they all forsook him and fled .
41014051	And a young man followed him , with nothing but a linen cloth around his body . And they seized him ,
41014052	and he left the linen cloth and fled from them naked .
41014053	And they led Jesus to the high priest ; and all the chief priests and the elders and the scribes were assembled .
41014054	But Peter followed him at a distance , right into the courtyard of the high priest . And he sat with the guards and warmed himself at the fire .
41014055	Now the chief priests and the whole council sought testimony against Jesus to put him to death , but they found none .
41014056	For many bore false witness against him , but their testimonies did not agree .
41014057	Then some stood up and bore false witness against him , saying ,
41014058	» We heard him say , ‘ I will destroy this temple that is made with hands , and in three days I will build another not made with hands . ’ «
41014059	Yet even then their testimony did not agree .
41014060	And the high priest stood up in the midst , and asked Jesus , » Have you no answer to make ? What is it that these men testify against you ? «
41014061	But he was silent and made no answer . Again the high priest asked him , » Are you the Christ , the Son of the Blessed ? «
41014062	And Jesus said , » I am . And you will see the Son of Man sitting at the right hand of the Power , and coming with the clouds of heaven . «
41014063	The high priest tore his clothes and said , » Why do we need any more witnesses ?
41014064	You have heard the blasphemy . What do you think ? « And they all condemned him as worthy of death .
41014065	Then some began to spit on him , and to blindfold him , and to beat him , and to say to him , » Prophesy ! « And the guards received him with slaps in the face .
41014066	Now as Peter was below in the courtyard , one of the servant girls of the high priest came .
41014067	And when she saw Peter warming himself , she looked at him , and said , » You also were with the Nazarene , Jesus . «
41014068	But he denied it , saying , » I neither know nor understand what you mean . « And he went out into the gateway .
41014069	And the servant girl saw him again , and began to say to those who stood by , » This is one of them . «
41014070	But again he denied it . And after a little while again those standing near said to Peter , » Surely you are one of them ; for you are a Gallilean . «
41014071	But he began to invoke a curse on himself and to swear , » I do not know this man of whom you speak . «
41014072	And immediately the rooster crowed a second time . Then Peter remembered the word Jesus had said to him , » Before the rooster crows twice , you will deny me three times . « And he broke down and wept .
41015001	Very early in the morning , the chief priests held a consultation with the elders and scribes and the whole council ; and they bound Jesus , led him away , and delivered him to Pilate .
41015002	Then Pilate asked him , » Are you the King of the Jews ? « And he answered him , » It is as you say . «
41015003	And the chief priests accused him of many things .
41015004	And Pilate again asked him , » Have you no answer to make ? See how many things they bring against you . «
41015005	But Jesus still made no answer , so that Pilate was amazed .
41015006	Now at the feast he was accustomed to release for them one prisoner whom they requested .
41015007	And with the rebels in prison , who had committed murder in the insurrection , there was a man called Barabbas .
41015008	And the crowd came up and began to ask Pilate to do as he had always done for them .
41015009	But Pilate answered them , » Do you want me to release to you the King of the Jews ? «
41015010	For he knew it was out of envy that the chief priests had handed Jesus over to him .
41015011	But the chief priests stirred up the crowd to have him release for them Barabbas instead .
41015012	And Pilate again said to them , » Then what shall I do with the man whom you call the King of the Jews ? «
41015013	And they cried out again , » Crucify him ! «
41015014	And Pilate said to them , » Why , what evil has he done ? « But they shouted all the more , » Crucify him ! «
41015015	So Pilate , wanting to satisfy the crowd , released Barabbas to them ; and he delivered Jesus , after he had scourged him , to be crucified .
41015016	The soldiers led him away into the palace ( that is , the Praetorium ) and they called together the whole battalion .
41015017	And they clothed him in a purple cloak , and they twisted a crown of thorns and put it on him .
41015018	And they began to salute him , » Hail , King of the Jews ! «
41015019	Then they struck him on the head with a reed and spat on him ; and falling on their knees , they paid homage to him .
41015020	And when they had mocked him , they took the purple robe off him , and put his own clothes on him . Then they led him out to crucify him .
41015021	Then they compelled a certain man , Simon of Cyrene , the father of Alexander and Rufus , as he was coming out of the country and passing by , to carry his cross .
41015022	And they brought him to the place called Golgotha ( which means the place of a skull ) .
41015023	Then they offered him wine mingled with myrrh , but he did not take it .
41015024	And when they crucified him , they divided his garments , casting lots for them to determine what each man should take .
41015025	And it was the third hour , when they crucified him .
41015026	And the inscription of the charge written against him read : THE KING OF THE JEWS .
41015027	And with him they crucified two robbers , one on his right and one on his left .
41015029	And those who passed by hurled insults at him , wagging their heads , and saying , » Aha ! You who would destroy the temple and build it in three days ,
41015030	save yourself , and come down from the cross ! «
41015031	So also the chief priests mocked him among themselves with the scribes , and said , » He saved others ; he cannot save himself .
41015032	Let the Christ , the King of Israel , come down now from the cross , that we may see and believe . « Those who were crucified with him also reviled him .
41015033	And when the sixth hour had come , there was darkness over the whole land until the ninth hour .
41015034	And at the ninth hour Jesus cried out with a loud voice , » Eloi , Eloi , lama sabachthani ? « — which means , » My God , my God , why have you forsaken me ? «
41015035	When some of those standing near heard this , they said , » Behold , he is calling Elijah . «
41015036	And one ran and filled a sponge full of wine vinegar , put it on a reed , and offered it to him to drink , saying , » Wait , let us see if Elijah will come to take him down . «
41015037	And with a loud cry , Jesus breathed his last .
41015038	Then the veil of the temple was torn in two from top to bottom .
41015039	So when the centurion , who stood opposite him , saw that he cried out like this and breathed his last , he said , » Truly this man was the Son of God ! «
41015040	There were also women looking on from afar , among whom were Mary Magdalene , Mary the mother of James the younger and of Joses , and Salome ,
41015041	who also followed him and ministered to him when he was in Galilee ; and many other women who came up with him to Jerusalem .
41015042	Now when evening had come , because it was the Preparation Day , that is , the day before the Sabbath ,
41015043	Joseph of Arimathea , a prominent council member , who was himself waiting for the kingdom of God , coming and taking courage , went in to Pilate and asked for the body of Jesus .
41015044	Pilate marveled that he was already dead ; and summoning the centurion , he asked him if he was already dead .
41015045	And when he learned from the centurion that he was dead , he granted the body to Joseph .
41015046	Then he bought fine linen , took him down , and wrapped him in the linen . And he laid him in a tomb which had been hewn out of the rock , and rolled a stone against the door of the tomb .
41015047	Mary Magdalene and Mary the mother of Joses saw where he was laid .
41016001	Now when the Sabbath was past , Mary Magdalene , Mary the mother of James , and Salome bought spices , so that they might go and anoint him .
41016002	And very early on the first day of the week , they came to the tomb when the sun had risen .
41016003	And they asked each other , » Who will roll away the stone from the door of the tomb for us ? «
41016004	But when they looked up , they saw that the stone , though it was very large , had been rolled away .
41016005	And entering the tomb , they saw a young man sitting on the right side , dressed in a white robe ; and they were alarmed .
41016006	But he said to them , » Do not be alarmed . You seek Jesus of Nazareth , who was crucified . He has risen ! He is not here . See the place where they laid him .
41016007	But go , tell his disciples and Peter that he is going before you to Galilee ; there you will see him , as he told you . «
41016008	So they went out quickly and fled from the tomb , for trembling and astonishment had gripped them . And they said nothing to anyone , for they were afraid .
41016009	Now when he rose early on the first day of the week , he appeared first to Mary Magdalene , out of whom he had cast seven demons .
41016010	She went and told those who had been with him , as they mourned and wept .
41016011	And when they heard that he was alive and had been seen by her , they did not believe it .
41016012	After this he appeared in another form to two of them , as they were walking into the country .
41016013	And they went and told it to the rest , but they did not believe them either .
41016014	Later he appeared to the eleven as they sat at the table ; and he rebuked them for their unbelief and hardness of heart , because they did not believe those who had seen him after he had risen .
41016015	And he said to them , » Go into all the world and preach the gospel to all creation .
41016016	He who believes and is baptized will be saved ; but he who does not believe will be condemned .
41016017	And these signs will accompany those who believe : in my name they will cast out demons ; they will speak in new tongues ;
41016018	they will pick up serpents ; and if they drink any deadly thing , it will not hurt them ; they will lay their hands on the sick , and they will recover . «
41016019	So then the Lord Jesus , after he had spoken to them , was taken up into heaven , and sat down at the right hand of God .
41016020	Then they went out and preached everywhere , and the Lord worked with them and confirmed the word by the signs that accompanied it . Amen .
42001001	Inasmuch as many have undertaken to compile a narrative of the things which have been fulfilled among us ,
42001002	just as they were delivered to us by those who from the beginning were eyewitnesses and ministers of the word ,
42001003	it seemed good to me also , having carefully investigated all things from the very first , to write to you an orderly account , most excellent Theophilus ,
42001004	so that you may know the certainty of the things which you have been taught .
42001005	In the days of Herod , king of Judea , there was a priest named Zechariah , of the division of Abijah ; and he had a wife of the daughters of Aaron , and her name was Elizabeth .
42001006	And they were both righteous before God , walking in all the commandments and ordinances of the Lord blameless .
42001007	But they had no child , because Elizabeth was barren , and they were both well advanced in years .
42001008	Now while he was serving as priest before God when his division was on duty ,
42001009	according to the custom of the priesthood , it fell to him by lot to enter the temple of the Lord and burn incense .
42001010	And the whole multitude of the people were praying outside at the hour of incense .
42001011	Then an angel of the Lord appeared to him , standing on the right side of the altar of incense .
42001012	And Zechariah was troubled when he saw him , and fear fell upon him .
42001013	But the angel said to him , » Do not be afraid , Zechariah , for your prayer is heard ; and your wife Elizabeth will bear you a son , and you shall call his name John .
42001014	And you will have joy and gladness , and many will rejoice at his birth .
42001015	For he will be great in the sight of the Lord , and shall drink neither wine nor strong drink . He will also be filled with the Holy Spirit , even from his mother’s womb .
42001016	And he will turn many of the sons of Israel to the Lord their God .
42001017	And he will go before him in the spirit and power of Elijah , ‘ to turn the hearts of the fathers to the children , ’ and the disobedient to the wisdom of the just , to make ready a people prepared for the Lord . «
42001018	And Zechariah said to the angel , » How shall I know this ? For I am an old man , and my wife is well advanced in years . «
42001019	And the angel answered him , » I am Gabriel , who stands in the presence of God ; and I was sent to speak to you , and to bring you this good news .
42001020	And behold , you will be silent and not able to speak until the day that these things come to pass , because you did not believe my words , which will be fulfilled in their time . «
42001021	And the people were waiting for Zechariah and wondering why he stayed so long in the temple .
42001022	But when he came out , he could not speak to them ; and they perceived that he had seen a vision in the temple , for he made signs to them and remained speechless .
42001023	And when his time of service was completed , he went to his home .
42001024	After these days his wife Elizabeth conceived , and for five months she hid herself , saying ,
42001025	» Thus the Lord has done to me , in the days when he looked on me , to take away my reproach among people . «
42001026	In the sixth month the angel Gabriel was sent from God to a city of Galilee named Nazareth ,
42001027	to a virgin betrothed to a man whose name was Joseph , of the house of David . The virgin’s name was Mary .
42001028	The angel went to her and said , » Hail , O highly favored one , the Lord is with you ! «
42001029	But she was greatly troubled at his saying , and considered in her mind what sort of greeting this might be .
42001030	And the angel said to her , » Do not be afraid , Mary , for you have found favor with God .
42001031	And behold , you will conceive in your womb and bear a son , and you shall call his name Jesus .
42001032	He will be great , and will be called the Son of the Most High ; and the Lord God will give him the throne of his father David .
42001033	And he will reign over the house of Jacob for ever ; and of his kingdom there will be no end . «
42001034	And Mary said to the angel , » How can this be , since I am a virgin ? «
42001035	And the angel answered her , » The Holy Spirit will come upon you , and the power of the Most High will overshadow you ; therefore the Holy One to be born will be called the Son of God .
42001036	And behold , your relative Elizabeth in her old age has also conceived a son ; and this is the sixth month with her who was called barren .
42001037	For with God nothing will be impossible . «
42001038	Then Mary said , » Behold , I am the servant of the Lord ; let it be to me according to your word . « And the angel departed from her .

42003001	Now in the fifteenth year of the reign of Tiberius Caesar , Pontius Pilate being governor of Judea , Herod being tetrarch of Galilee , his brother Philip tetrarch of Iturea and the region of Trachonitis , and Lysanias tetrarch of Abilene ,
42003002	during the high priesthood of Annas and Caiaphas , the word of God came to John son of Zechariah in the wilderness .

42003008	Therefore bear fruits worthy of repentance , and do not begin to say to yourselves , ‘ We have Abraham as our father . ’ For I tell you that God is able to raise up children to Abraham from these stones .
42003009	And even now the ax is laid at the root of the trees ; every tree therefore that does not bear good fruit is cut down and thrown into the fire . «
42003010	And the multitudes asked him , » What then shall we do ? «
42003011	And he answered them , » He who has two tunics , let him share with him who has none ; and he who has food , let him do likewise . «
42003012	Tax collectors also came to be baptized , and said to him , » Teacher , what shall we do ? «
42003013	And he said to them , » Collect no more than is appointed you . «

42003016	John answered them all , » I baptize you with water ; but one mightier than I is coming , the thong of whose sandals I am not worthy to untie . He will baptize you with the Holy Spirit and with fire .
42003017	His winnowing fork is in his hand , to clear his threshing floor , and to gather the wheat into his barn , but the chaff he will burn with unquenchable fire . «
42003018	And with many other exhortations he preached good news to the people .

42004001	Jesus , full of the Holy Spirit , returned from the Jordan and was led by the Spirit into the wilderness ,
42004002	being tempted for forty days by the devil . In those days he ate nothing , and when they had ended , he was hungry .
42004003	And the devil said to him , » If you are the Son of God , command this stone to become bread . «
42004004	But Jesus answered him , » It is written , ‘ Man shall not live by bread alone . ’ «
42004005	Then the devil took him up to a high place , and showed him all the kingdoms of the world in a moment of time .
42004006	And he said to him , » To you I will give all this authority and their glory ; for it has been delivered to me , and I give it to whom I will .
42004007	If you , then , will worship me , it shall all be yours . «
42004008	And Jesus answered him , » It is written , ‘ You shall worship the Lord your God , and him only shall you serve . ’ «

42004032	And they were astonished at his teaching , for his word was with authority .

42004034	» Ha ! What have you to do with us , Jesus of Nazareth ? Have you come to destroy us ? I know who you are — the Holy One of God ! «
42004035	But Jesus rebuked him , saying , » Be quiet , and come out of him ! « And when the demon had thrown him down in the midst , he came out of him without doing him any harm .
42004036	And they were all amazed and said to one another , » What is this word ? For with authority and power he commands the unclean spirits , and they come out ! «
42004037	And the report about him went out into every place in the surrounding region .

42004039	So he stood over her and rebuked the fever , and it left her . And immediately she rose and served them .
42004040	When the sun was setting , all those who had any that were sick with various diseases brought them to him ; and he laid his hands on every one of them and healed them .
42004041	And demons also came out of many , crying , » You are the Son of God ! « But he rebuked them , and would not allow them to speak , because they knew that he was the Christ .
42004042	Now when it was day , he departed and went into a deserted place . And the people sought him and came to him , and tried to keep him from leaving them ;
42004043	but he said to them , » I must preach the good news of the kingdom of God to the other cities also , because I was sent for this purpose . «

42005001	Now as the people pressed around him to hear the word of God , he was standing by the Lake of Gennesaret .
42005002	And he saw two boats by the lake ; but the fishermen had gone out of them and were washing their nets .
42005003	Then he got into one of the boats , which was Simon's , and asked him to put out a little from the land . And he sat down and taught the people from the boat .
42005004	When he had finished speaking , he said to Simon , » Put out into the deep , and let down your nets for a catch . «
42005005	And Simon answered , » Master , we toiled all night and caught nothing ! But at your word I will let down the nets . «
42005006	And when they had done this , they caught a great number of fish , and their nets were breaking .
42005007	So they signaled to their partners in the other boat to come and help them . And they came and filled both the boats , so that they began to sink .
42005008	When Simon Peter saw it , he fell down at Jesus' knees , saying , » Depart from me , for I am a sinful man , O Lord ! «
42005009	For he and all who were with him were astonished at the catch of fish which they had taken ;
42005010	and so also were James and John , the sons of Zebedee , who were partners with Simon . And Jesus said to Simon , » Do not be afraid . From now on you will catch men . «
42005011	So when they had brought their boats to land , they left everything and followed him .
42005012	While he was in one of the cities , a man who was full of leprosy saw Jesus ; and he fell on his face and begged him , » Lord , if you are willing , you can make me clean . «
42005013	And he stretched out his hand , and touched him , saying , » I am willing ; be clean . « And immediately the leprosy left him .
42005014	And he charged him to tell no one , » But go and show yourself to the priest , and make an offering for your cleansing as a testimony to them , just as Moses commanded . «
42005015	But the report went around concerning him all the more ; and great multitudes came together to hear and to be healed by him of their infirmities .
42005016	But he often withdrew to the wilderness and prayed .
42005017	One day as he was teaching , there were Pharisees and teachers of the law sitting by , who had come from every village of Galilee and Judea and from Jerusalem . And the power of the Lord was present for him to heal .
42005018	Then behold , men brought on a bed a man who was paralyzed , and they sought to bring him in and lay him before Jesus .
42005019	When they could not find a way to bring him in , because of the crowd , they went up on the roof and let him down with his bed through the tiles into the midst before Jesus .
42005020	When he saw their faith he said , » Man , your sins are forgiven you . «
42005021	And the scribes and the Pharisees began to reason , saying , » Who is this who speaks blasphemies ? Who can forgive sins but God alone ? «
42005022	But when Jesus perceived their thoughts , he answered them , » Why are you reasoning in your hearts ?
42005023	Which is easier , to say , ‘ Your sins are forgiven you , ’ or to say , ‘ Rise up and walk ’ ?
42005024	But that you may know that the Son of Man has authority on earth to forgive sins « — he said to the man who was paralyzed — » I say to you , rise , take up your bed and go home . «
42005025	Immediately he rose up before them , took up what he had been lying on , and went home , glorifying God .
42005026	And they were all amazed , and they glorified God and were filled with awe , saying , » We have seen strange things today . «
42005027	After this he went out , and saw a tax collector , named Levi , sitting at the tax office ; and he said to him , » Follow me . «
42005028	And he left everything , rose up and followed him .
42005029	Then Levi made him a great feast in his house ; and there were a great number of tax collectors and others sitting at table with them .
42005030	And the Pharisees and their scribes complained against his disciples , saying , » Why do you eat and drink with tax collectors and sinners ? «
42005031	And Jesus answered them , » Those who are well have no need of a physician , but those who are sick .
42005032	I have not come to call the righteous , but sinners to repentance . «
42005033	They said to him , » The disciples of John fast often and offer prayers , and so do the disciples of the Pharisees , but yours eat and drink . «
42005034	And Jesus said to them , » Can you make the guests of the bridegroom fast while he is with them ?
42005035	But the days will come when the bridegroom will be taken away from them ; then they will fast in those days . «
42005036	He told them a parable also : » No one tears a piece from a new garment and puts it on an old one ; if he does , he will tear the new garment , and the piece from the new will not match the old .
42005037	And no one puts new wine into old wineskins ; if he does , the new wine will burst the skins and it will be spilled , and the skins will be ruined .
42005038	But new wine must be put into new wineskins .
42005039	And no one after drinking old wine desires the new ; for he says , ‘ The old is better . ’ «
42006001	One Sabbath Jesus was going through the grain fields , and his disciples plucked and ate some heads of grain , rubbing them in their hands .
42006002	But some of the Pharisees said , » Why are you doing what is not lawful to do on the Sabbath ? «
42006003	Jesus answered them , » Have you not read what David did when he was hungry , he and those who were with him :
42006004	how he entered the house of God , took and ate the consecrated bread , and also gave some to those with him , which is not lawful for any but the priests to eat ? «
42006005	And he said to them , » The Son of Man is lord of the Sabbath . «
42006006	On another Sabbath he entered the synagogue and taught , and a man was there whose right hand was withered .
42006007	The scribes and the Pharisees watched him closely , to see whether he would heal on the Sabbath , so that they might find an accusation against him .
42006008	But he knew their thoughts , and said to the man who had the withered hand , » Rise and stand here . « And he rose and stood there .
42006009	Then Jesus said to them , » I ask you , which is lawful on the Sabbath : to do good or to do evil , to save life or to destroy it ? «
42006010	And he looked around at them all , and said to the man , » Stretch out your hand . « He did so , and his hand was restored .
42006011	But they were filled with fury and discussed with one another what they might do to Jesus .
42006012	In those days he went out to the mountain to pray , and all night he continued in prayer to God .
42006013	And when it was day , he called his disciples to himself ; and from them he chose twelve , whom he also named apostles :
42006014	Simon , whom he named Peter , and Andrew his brother , James and John , Philip , and Bartholomew ,
42006015	Matthew , and Thomas , James the son of Alphaeus , and Simon who was called the Zealot ,
42006016	Judas the son of James , and Judas Iscariot , who became a traitor .
42006017	And he came down with them and stood on a level place with a crowd of his disciples and a great multitude of people from all Judea and Jerusalem , and from the seacoast of Tyre and Sidon , who came to hear him and be healed of their diseases ,
42006018	and those who were troubled with unclean spirits were cured .
42006019	And all the crowd sought to touch him , for power came from him and healed them all .
42006020	He lifted up his eyes on his disciples , and said : » Blessed are you poor , for yours is the kingdom of God .
42006021	
42006022	Blessed are you when men hate you , and when they exclude you and revile you , and cast out your name as evil , because of the Son of Man .
42006023	Rejoice in that day and leap for joy , for behold , your reward is great in heaven ; for so their fathers did to the prophets .
42006024	
42006025	
42006026	Woe to you when all men speak well of you , for so did their fathers to the false prophets .
42006027	» But I say to you who hear : love your enemies , do good to those who hate you ,
42006028	bless those who curse you , pray for those who mistreat you .
42006029	To him who strikes you on the one cheek , offer the other also . And from him who takes away your cloak , do not withhold your tunic .
42006030	Give to everyone who asks of you , and from him who takes away your goods do not ask them back .
42006031	And as you wish that men would do to you , do so to them .
42006032	If you love those who love you , what credit is that to you ? For even sinners love those who love them .
42006033	And if you do good to those who do good to you , what credit is that to you ? For even sinners do the same .
42006034	And if you lend to those from whom you hope to receive back , what credit is that to you ? For even sinners lend to sinners , to receive as much back .
42006035	But love your enemies , do good , and lend , expecting nothing in return ; and your reward will be great , and you will be sons of the Most High . For he is kind to the ungrateful and evil .
42006036	Be merciful , just as your Father is merciful .
42006037	» Judge not , and you will not be judged . Condemn not , and you will not be condemned . Forgive , and you will be forgiven .
42006038	Give , and it will be given to you ; good measure , pressed down , shaken together and running over , will be put into your lap . For with the measure you use , it will be measured back to you . «
42006039	He also told them a parable : » Can a blind man lead a blind man ? Will they not both fall into a pit ?
42006040	A disciple is not above his teacher , but everyone who is fully trained will be like his teacher .
42006041	And why do you look at the speck in your brother's eye , but do not notice the plank in your own eye ?
42006042	Or how can you say to your brother , ‘ Brother , let me remove the speck that is in your eye , ’ when you yourself do not see the plank that is in your own eye ? You hypocrite ! First take the plank from out of your own eye , and then you will see clearly to take out the speck that is in your brother's eye .
42006043	» For no good tree bears bad fruit , nor does a bad tree bear good fruit .
42006044	For each tree is known by its own fruit . For men do not gather figs from thorns , nor do they pick grapes from a bramble bush .
42006045	The good man out of the good treasure of his heart brings forth good , and an evil man out of the evil treasure of his heart brings forth evil . For out of the abundance of the heart his mouth speaks .
42006046	» Why do you call me , ‘ Lord , Lord , ’ and do not do what I say ?
42006047	Every one who comes to me and hears my words and does them , I will show you what he is like :
42006048	he is like a man building a house , who dug deep and laid the foundation on the rock . And when a flood arose , the stream broke against that house and could not shake it , because it was well built .
42006049	But he who hears and does not do them is like a man who built a house on the ground without a foundation ; against which the stream broke , and immediately it fell . And the ruin of that house was great . «
42007001	When he had finished all his sayings in the hearing of the people , he entered Capernaum .
42007002	A centurion's servant , who was dear to him , was sick and ready to die .
42007003	When he heard of Jesus , he sent to him elders of the Jews , asking him to come and heal his servant .
42007004	And when they came to Jesus , they begged him earnestly , saying , » He is worthy to have you do this for him ,
42007005	for he loves our nation , and has built us our synagogue . «
42007006	And Jesus went with them . When he was not far from the house , the centurion sent friends to him , saying to him , » Lord , do not trouble yourself , for I am not worthy to have you come under my roof .
42007007	Therefore I did not even consider myself worthy to come to you . But say the word , and my servant will be healed .
42007008	For I am a man set under authority , with soldiers under me . And I say to one , ‘ Go , ’ and he goes ; and to another , ‘ Come , ’ and he comes ; and to my servant , ‘ Do this , ’ and he does it . «
42007009	When Jesus heard this , he marveled at him , and turned and said to the crowd that followed him , » I tell you , I have not found such great faith even in Israel . «
42007010	And when those who had been sent returned to the house , they found the servant well .
42007011	Soon afterward , he went to a city called Nain , and his disciples and a large crowd went along with him .
42007012	As he came near the gate of the city , behold , a dead man was being carried out , the only son of his mother ; and she was a widow . And a large crowd from the city was with her .
42007013	When the Lord saw her , he had compassion on her and said to her , » Do not weep . «
42007014	Then he came and touched the open coffin , and those who carried him stood still . And he said , » Young man , I say to you , arise . «
42007015	The dead man sat up , and began to speak . And he gave him to his mother .
42007016	Fear seized them all ; and they glorified God , saying , » A great prophet has arisen among us ; « and » God has visited his people . «
42007017	And this report about him spread throughout all Judea and all the surrounding country .
42007018	Then the disciples of John told him about all these things .
42007019	And John , calling to him two of his disciples , sent them to the Lord , saying , » Are you the One who is to come , or shall we look for another ? «
42007020	When the men had come to him , they said , » John the Baptist has sent us to you , saying , ‘ Are you the One who is to come , or shall we look for another ? ’ «
42007021	At that very hour he cured many of diseases and afflictions and evil spirits , and to many that were blind he gave sight .
42007022	He answered them , » Go and tell John what you have seen and heard : the blind receive their sight , the lame walk , the lepers are cleansed , and the deaf hear , the dead are raised up , the poor have the good news preached to them .
42007023	And blessed is he who is not offended because of me . «
42007024	When the messengers of John had departed , he began to speak to the crowds concerning John : » What did you go out into the wilderness to see ? A reed shaken by the wind ?
42007025	What then did you go out to see ? A man clothed in soft clothing ? Behold , those who are gorgeously appareled and live in luxury are in kings' courts .
42007026	But what did you go out to see ? A prophet ? Yes , I tell you , and more than a prophet .
42007027	This is he of whom it is written : ‘ Behold , I send my messenger before your face , who will prepare your way before you . ’
42007028	I tell you , among those born of women there is no one greater than John ; yet the one who is least in the kingdom of God is greater than he . «
42007029	( And when they heard him , all the people , even the tax collectors , justified God , having been baptized with the baptism of John .
42007030	But the Pharisees and the lawyers rejected the purpose of God for themselves , not having been baptized by him . )
42007031	» To what then shall I compare the men of this generation , and what are they like ?
42007032	They are like children sitting in the marketplace and calling to one another : ‘ We played the flute for you , and you did not dance ; we sang a dirge , and you did not weep . ’
42007033	For John the Baptist came neither eating bread nor drinking wine , and you say , ‘ He has a demon . ’
42007034	The Son of Man has come eating and drinking , and you say , ‘ Behold , a glutton and a drunkard , a friend of tax collectors and sinners ! ’
42007035	But wisdom is justified by all her children . «
42007036	One of the Pharisees asked him to eat with him , and he went to the Pharisee's house , and reclined at the table .
42007037	And behold , a woman of the city , who was a sinner , when she learned that Jesus was reclining at the table in the Pharisee's house , brought an alabaster flask of perfume ,
42007038	and as she stood behind him at his feet , weeping , she began to wet his feet with her tears , and wiped them with the hair of her head , and kissed his feet , and anointed them with the perfume .
42007039	Now when the Pharisee who had invited him saw it , he said to himself , » If this man were a prophet , he would have known who and what sort of woman this is who is touching him , for she is a sinner . «
42007040	And Jesus answered him , » Simon , I have something to say to you . « And he said , » Teacher , say it . «
42007041	» A certain creditor had two debtors . One owed five hundred denarii , and the other fifty .
42007042	When they had nothing with which to pay him back , he freely forgave them both . Now which of them will love him more ? «
42007043	Simon answered , » I suppose the one to whom he forgave more . « And he said to him , » You have judged rightly . «
42007044	Then he turned toward the woman and said to Simon , » Do you see this woman ? I entered your house ; you gave me no water for my feet , but she has wet my feet with her tears and wiped them with the hair of her head .
42007045	You gave me no kiss , but this woman has not ceased to kiss my feet from the time I came in .
42007046	You did not anoint my head with oil , but she has anointed my feet with perfume .
42007047	Therefore I tell you , her sins , which are many , are forgiven , for she loved much . But he who is forgiven little , loves little . «
42007048	And he said to her , » Your sins are forgiven . «
42007049	Then those who reclined at the table with him began to say among themselves , » Who is this who even forgives sins ? «
42007050	He said to the woman , » Your faith has saved you ; go in peace . «
42008001	Soon afterward , he went on through every city and village , preaching and bringing the good news of the kingdom of God . And the twelve were with him ,
42008002	and also some women who had been healed of evil spirits and infirmities : Mary , called Magdalene , from whom seven demons had come out ,
42008003	and Joanna the wife of Chuza , Herod's steward , and Susanna , and many others who provided for them out of their means .
42008004	And when a great crowd came together and people from town after town came to him , he said in a parable :
42008005	» A sower went out to sow his seed . And as he sowed , some fell along the path ; and it was trampled down , and the birds of the air devoured it .
42008006	Some fell on the rock ; and as it grew up , it withered away , because it had no moisture .
42008007	And some fell among thorns , and the thorns grew up with it and choked it .
42008008	But others fell on good soil , sprang up , and yielded a crop a hundredfold . « When he had said this he called out , » He who has ears to hear , let him hear ! «
42008009	When his disciples asked him what this parable meant ,
42008010	he said , » To you it has been given to know the secrets of the kingdom of God ; but to others it is given in parables , so that ‘ Seeing they may not see , and hearing they may not understand . ’
42008011	» Now the parable is this : The seed is the word of God .
42008012	The ones along the path are those who hear ; then the devil comes and takes away the word from their hearts , that they may not believe and be saved .
42008013	And the ones on the rock are those who , when they hear the word , receive it with joy ; but these have no root , they believe for a while and in time of temptation fall away .
42008014	And the ones that fell among the thorns , they are those who hear , but as they go on their way they are choked by the cares and riches and pleasures of life , and their fruit does not mature .
42008015	But the ones that fell on the good soil are those who , having heard the word with a noble and good heart , keep it and bear fruit with patience .
42008016	» No one , when he has lit a lamp , covers it with a vessel or puts it under a bed , but puts it on a lampstand , that those who enter may see the light .
42008017	For nothing is secret that will not be revealed , nor anything hidden that will not be known and come to light .
42008018	Therefore take heed how you hear . For whoever has , to him more will be given ; and whoever does not have , even what he thinks he has will be taken from him . «
42008019	Then his mother and his brothers came to him , but they could not reach him because of the crowd .
42008020	And it was told him , » Your mother and your brothers are standing outside , desiring to see you . «
42008021	But he said to them , » My mother and my brothers are those who hear the word of God and do it . «
42008022	One day he got into a boat with his disciples , and he said to them , » Let us go over to the other side of the lake . « So they set out .
42008023	As they sailed he fell asleep . And a windstorm came down on the lake , and they were filling with water , and were in danger .
42008024	And they went and woke him , saying , » Master , Master , we are perishing ! « Then he awoke and rebuked the wind and the raging waves ; and they ceased , and there was a calm .
42008025	He said to them , » Where is your faith ? « And they were afraid , and they marveled , saying to one another , » Who then is this , that he commands even the winds and water , and they obey him ? «
42008026	Then they sailed to the country of the Gerasenes , which is opposite Galilee .
42008027	When he stepped out on land , there met him a man from the city who had demons . For a long time he had worn no clothes , and he lived not in a house but in the tombs .
42008028	When he saw Jesus , he cried out and fell down before him , and said with a loud voice , » What have you to do with me , Jesus , Son of the Most High God ? I beg you , do not torment me ! «
42008029	For he had commanded the unclean spirit to come out of the man . For many times it had seized him , and he was kept under guard , bound with chains and shackles ; and he broke the bonds and was driven by the demon into the wilderness .
42008030	Jesus asked him , » What is your name ? « And he said , » Legion « ; because many demons had entered him .
42008031	And they begged him repeatedly not to command them to go into the Abyss .
42008032	Now a large herd of swine was feeding there on the hillside ; and they begged him to let them enter them . So he gave them permission .
42008033	Then the demons came out of the man and entered the swine , and the herd rushed down the steep bank into the lake and were drowned .
42008034	When those tending the pigs saw what had happened , they fled , and told it in the city and in the country .
42008035	Then people went out to see what had happened , and they came to Jesus , and found the man from whom the demons had gone , sitting at the feet of Jesus , clothed and in his right mind ; and they were afraid .
42008036	Those who had seen it told them how he who had been demon-possessed was healed .
42008037	Then all the people of the surrounding region of the Gerasenes asked him to depart from them , for they were seized with great fear . So he got into the boat and returned .
42008038	The man from whom the demons had gone begged that he might be with him ; but Jesus sent him away , saying ,
42008039	» Return to your home , and tell how much God has done for you . « And he went away , proclaiming throughout the whole city how much Jesus had done for him .
42008040	Now when Jesus returned , the crowd welcomed him , for they were all waiting for him .
42008041	And behold , there came a man named Jairus , who was a ruler of the synagogue ; and he fell at Jesus' feet and begged him to come to his house ,
42008042	for he had an only daughter , about twelve years of age , and she was dying . But as he went , the people pressed round him .
42008043	And a woman who had a flow of blood for twelve years and could not be healed by anyone ,
42008044	came up behind him , and touched the fringe of his garment ; and immediately her flow of blood stopped .
42008045	And Jesus said , » Who touched me ? « When all denied it , Peter said , » Master , the multitudes surround you and press upon you ! «
42008046	But Jesus said , » Someone touched me ; for I know that power has gone out from me . «
42008047	When the woman saw that she was not hidden , she came trembling , and falling down before him declared in the presence of all the people why she had touched him , and how she had been immediately healed .
42008048	And he said to her , » Daughter , your faith has made you well ; go in peace . «
42008049	While he was still speaking , someone came from the ruler of the synagogue's house and said , » Your daughter is dead ; do not trouble the Teacher any more . «
42008050	But Jesus on hearing this answered him , » Do not be afraid ; only believe , and she will be well . «
42008051	When he came into the house he permitted no one to go in with him except Peter , James , and John , and the father and mother of the girl .
42008052	Now all were wailing and mourning for her ; but he said , » Do not weep ; she is not dead , but sleeping . «
42008053	And they laughed at him , knowing that she was dead .
42008054	But he took her by the hand and called , saying , » Child , arise . «
42008055	Then her spirit returned , and she got up at once . And he directed that something should be given her to eat .
42008056	And her parents were astonished , but he charged them to tell no one what had happened .
42009001	Then he called the twelve together and gave them power and authority over all demons , and to cure diseases .
42009002	And he sent them out to preach the kingdom of God and to heal the sick .
42009003	And he said to them , » Take nothing for the journey , no staff , nor bag , nor bread , nor money ; and do not have two tunics .
42009004	Whatever house you enter , stay there , and from there depart .
42009005	And wherever they do not receive you , when you leave that town , shake off the dust from your feet as a testimony against them . «
42009006	So they departed and went through the towns , preaching the gospel and healing everywhere .
42009007	Now Herod the tetrarch heard of all that was done ; and he was perplexed , because it was said by some that John had been raised from the dead ,
42009008	by some that Elijah had appeared , and by others that one of the old prophets had risen again .
42009009	And Herod said , » John I have beheaded , but who is this about whom I hear such things ? « So he sought to see him .
42009010	And when the apostles returned , they told him what they had done . Then he took them with him and withdrew apart to a city called Bethsaida .
42009011	But when the crowds learned it , they followed him ; and he welcomed them and spoke to them about the kingdom of God , and healed those who had need of healing .
42009012	Now the day began to wear away ; and the twelve came and said to him , » Send the crowd away , to go to the surrounding villages and country , to lodge and get provisions ; for we are here in a deserted place . «
42009013	But he said to them , » You give them something to eat . « And they said , » We have no more than five loaves and two fish — unless we go and buy food for all these people . «
42009014	For there were about five thousand men . And he said to his disciples , » Make them sit down in groups of about fifty each . «
42009015	And they did so , and made them all sit down .
42009016	Taking the five loaves and the two fish and looking up to heaven , he blessed and broke them , and gave them to the disciples to set before the people .
42009017	They all ate and were satisfied , and they took up twelve baskets of broken pieces that were left over .
42009018	Now it happened that as he was praying alone his disciples were with him ; and he asked them , » Who do the crowds say that I am ? «
42009019	So they answered , » John the Baptist ; but others say Elijah ; and others say that one of the old prophets has risen again . «
42009020	And he said to them , » But who do you say that I am ? « And Peter answered , » The Christ of God . «
42009021	But he strictly warned and commanded them to tell this to no one ,
42009022	saying , » The Son of Man must suffer many things , and be rejected by the elders and chief priests and scribes , and be killed , and on the third day be raised . «
42009023	Then he said to them all , » If anyone would come after me , let him deny himself and take up his cross daily and follow me .
42009024	For whoever desires to save his life will lose it , but whoever loses his life for my sake will save it .
42009025	For what profit is it to a man if he gains the whole world , and loses or forfeits himself ?
42009026	For whoever is ashamed of me and of my words , of him will the Son of Man be ashamed when he comes in his glory and in the glory of the Father and of the holy angels .
42009027	But I tell you truly , there are some standing here who will not taste death before they see the kingdom of God . «
42009028	Now about eight days after these sayings , he took with him Peter and John and James , and went up on the mountain to pray .
42009029	And as he was praying , the appearance of his face was altered , and his robe became white and glistening .
