42009031	who appeared in glory and spoke of his departure , which he was about to accomplish at Jerusalem .
42009032	But Peter and those with him were heavy with sleep ; and when they were fully awake , they saw his glory and the two men who stood with him .
42009033	As the men were parting from him , Peter said to Jesus , » Master , it is good for us to be here ; and let us make three tabernacles : one for you , one for Moses , and one for Elijah « — not knowing what he said .
42009034	While he was saying this , a cloud came and overshadowed them ; and they were afraid as they entered the cloud .
42009035	And a voice came out of the cloud , saying , » This is my Son , my Chosen ; listen to him ! «
42009036	When the voice had spoken , Jesus was found alone . But they kept quiet , and told no one in those days any of the things they had seen .
42009037	On the next day , when they had come down from the mountain , a great crowd met him .
42009038	And behold , a man from the crowd cried out , » Teacher , I beg you to look upon my son , for he is my only child .
42009039	And behold , a spirit seizes him , and he suddenly cries out ; it convulses him so that he foams at the mouth , and will hardly leave him , bruising him .
42009040	I begged your disciples to cast it out , but they could not . «
42009041	Then Jesus answered , » O faithless and perverse generation , how long shall I be with you and bear with you ? Bring your son here . «
42009042	While he was coming , the demon threw him and convulsed him . But Jesus rebuked the unclean spirit , and healed the boy , and gave him back to his father .
42009043	And they were all amazed at the majesty of God . But while everyone was marveling at all that Jesus did , he said to his disciples ,
42009044	» Let these words sink into your ears , for the Son of Man is about to be betrayed into the hands of men . «
42009045	But they did not understand this saying , and it was hidden from them so that they did not perceive it ; and they were afraid to ask him about this saying .
42009046	And an argument arose among them as to which of them would be the greatest .
42009047	Jesus , perceiving the thought of their heart , took a little child and set him by him ,
42009048	and said to them , » Whoever receives this little child in my name receives me , and whoever receives me receives him who sent me . For he who is least among you all is the one who is great . «
42009049	Now John answered , » Master , we saw a man casting out demons in your name , and we forbade him because he does not follow with us . «
42009050	But Jesus said to him , » Do not forbid him , for he that is not against you is for you . «
42009051	When the time drew near for him to be received up , he set his face to go to Jerusalem .
42009052	And he sent messengers on ahead , who went and entered a village of the Samaritans , to make ready for him ;
42009053	but the people did not receive him , because his face was set for Jerusalem .
42009054	And when his disciples James and John saw this , they said , » Lord , do you want us to command fire to come down from heaven and consume them ? «
42009055	But he turned and rebuked them ,
42009056	and they went on to another village .
42009057	As they were going along the road , a man said to him , » I will follow you wherever you go . «
42009058	And Jesus said to him , » Foxes have holes and birds of the air have nests , but the Son of Man has nowhere to lay his head . «
42009059	To another he said , » Follow me . « But he said , » Lord , let me first go and bury my father . «
42009060	Jesus said to him , » Let the dead bury their own dead , but you go and proclaim the kingdom of God . «
42009061	Still another said , » I will follow you , Lord ; but first let me go back and say farewell to those at my home . «
42009062	Jesus said to him , » No one who puts his hand to the plow and looks back is fit for the kingdom of God . «
42010001	After this the Lord appointed seventy others , and sent them ahead of him , two by two , into every town and place where he himself was about to go .
42010002	And he said to them , » The harvest is plentiful , but the laborers are few ; pray therefore the Lord of the harvest to send out laborers into his harvest .
42010003	Go your way ; behold , I send you out as lambs among wolves .
42010004	Carry no purse , no bag , no sandals ; and greet no one on the road .
42010005	Whatever house you enter , first say , ‘ Peace to this house . ’
42010006	And if a son of peace is there , your peace will rest on him ; if not , it will return to you .
42010007	And remain in the same house , eating and drinking what they give , for the laborer deserves his wages . Do not go from house to house .
42010008	Whenever you enter a town and they receive you , eat what is set before you .
42010009	Heal the sick there and say to them , ‘ The kingdom of God has come near to you . ’
42010010	But whenever you enter a town and they do not receive you , go into its streets and say ,
42010011	‘ Even the dust of your town that clings to our feet , we wipe off against you . Nevertheless know this , that the kingdom of God has come near . ’
42010012	I tell you , it will be more tolerable on that day for Sodom than for that town .
42010013	» Woe to you , Chorazin ! Woe to you , Bethsaida ! For if the mighty works which were done in you had been done in Tyre and Sidon , they would have repented long ago , sitting in sackcloth and ashes .
42010014	But it will be more tolerable for Tyre and Sidon at the judgment than for you .
42010015	And you , Capernaum , will you be exalted to heaven ? You shall be brought down to Hades !
42010016	» He who hears you hears me , he who rejects you rejects me , and he who rejects me rejects him who sent me . «
42010017	The seventy returned with joy , saying , » Lord , even the demons are subject to us in your name . «
42010018	And he said to them , » I saw Satan fall like lightning from heaven .
42010019	Behold , I have given you authority to trample on serpents and scorpions , and over all the power of the enemy ; and nothing shall hurt you .
42010020	Nevertheless do not rejoice in this , that the spirits are subject to you , but rejoice that your names are written in heaven . «
42010021	At that hour Jesus rejoiced in the Holy Spirit and said , » I thank you , Father , Lord of heaven and earth , that you have hidden these things from the wise and prudent and revealed them to babes . Yes , Father , for so it was your good pleasure .
42010022	All things have been delivered to me by my Father , and no one knows who the Son is except the Father , and who the Father is except the Son , and the one to whom the Son chooses to reveal him . «
42010023	Then he turned to his disciples and said privately , » Blessed are the eyes which see what you see .
42010024	For I tell you that many prophets and kings desired to see what you see , and did not see it , and to hear what you hear , and did not hear it . «
42010025	And behold , a lawyer stood up to put him to the test , saying , » Teacher , what shall I do to inherit eternal life ? «
42010026	He said to him , » What is written in the law ? How do you read ? «
42010027	And he answered , » ‘ You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart , and with all your soul , and with all your strength , and with all your mind ’ ; and ‘ your neighbor as yourself . ’ «
42010028	And he said to him , » You have answered right ; do this , and you will live . «
42010029	But he , wanting to justify himself , said to Jesus , » And who is my neighbor ? «
42010030	Jesus said : » A man was going down from Jerusalem to Jericho , and he fell among robbers , who stripped him of his clothing , beat him , and departed , leaving him half dead .
42010031	Now by chance a priest was going down that road , and when he saw him he passed by on the other side .
42010032	So likewise , a Levite , when he came to the place and saw him , passed by on the other side .
42010033	But a Samaritan , as he journeyed , came where he was ; and when he saw him , he had compassion .
42010034	He went to him and bandaged his wounds , pouring on oil and wine ; then he set him on his own beast and brought him to an inn , and took care of him .
42010035	The next day he took out two denarii and gave them to the innkeeper and said , ‘ Take care of him ; and whatever more you spend , I will repay you when I come back . ’
42010036	Which of these three do you think was a neighbor to the man who fell among the robbers ? «
42010037	He said , » The one who showed mercy on him . « And Jesus said to him , » Go and do likewise . «
42010038	Now as they went on their way , he entered a village ; and a woman named Martha welcomed him into her house .
42010039	And she had a sister called Mary , who sat at the Lord's feet and listened to his word .
42010040	But Martha was distracted with much serving ; and she went to him and said , » Lord , do you not care that my sister has left me to serve alone ? Tell her then to help me . «
42010041	But the Lord answered her , » Martha , Martha , you are worried and troubled about many things ;
42010042	but only one thing is needed . And Mary has chosen that good part , which will not be taken away from her . «
42011001	He was praying in a certain place , and when he ceased , one of his disciples said to him , » Lord , teach us to pray , as John taught his disciples . «
42011002	He said to them , » When you pray , say : ‘ Father , hallowed be your name . Your kingdom come .
42011003	
42011004	
42011005	And he said to them , » Which of you who has a friend will go to him at midnight and say to him , ‘ Friend , lend me three loaves ;
42011006	for a friend of mine has come to me on a journey , and I have nothing to set before him ’ ;
42011007	and he will answer from within , ‘ Do not bother me ; the door is now shut , and my children are with me in bed ; I cannot get up and give you anything ’ ?
42011008	I tell you , though he will not get up and give to him because he is his friend , yet because of his persistence he will rise and give him as much as he needs .
42011009	So I say to you , ask , and it will be given to you ; seek , and you will find ; knock , and it will be opened to you .
42011010	For everyone who asks receives , and he who seeks finds , and to him who knocks it will be opened .
42011011	What father among you , if his son asks for a fish , will instead of a fish give him a serpent ?
42011012	Or if he asks for an egg , will give him a scorpion ?
42011013	If you then , who are evil , know how to give good gifts to your children , how much more will your heavenly Father give the Holy Spirit to those who ask him ! «
42011014	Now he was casting out a demon that was mute . So it was , when the demon had gone out , that the mute man spoke ; and the multitudes marveled .
42011015	But some of them said , » He casts out demons by Beelzebub , the prince of demons . «
42011016	Others , testing him , sought from him a sign from heaven .
42011017	But he , knowing their thoughts , said to them : » Every kingdom divided against itself is laid waste , and a house divided against itself falls .
42011018	If Satan also is divided against himself , how will his kingdom stand ? For you say that I cast out demons by Beelzebub .
42011019	And if I cast out demons by Beelzebub , by whom do your sons cast them out ? Therefore they will be your judges .
42011020	But if I cast out demons by the finger of God , then the kingdom of God has come upon you .
42011021	When a strong man , fully armed , guards his own palace , his goods are in peace .
42011022	But when one stronger than he attacks him and overpowers him , he takes away his armor in which he trusted , and divides his spoils .
42011023	He who is not with me is against me , and he who does not gather with me scatters .

42011025	And when he comes , he finds it swept and put in order .
42011026	Then he goes and takes with him seven other spirits more wicked than himself , and they enter and dwell there ; and the last state of that man is worse than the first . «
42011027	As he said these things , a woman in the crowd raised her voice and said to him , » Blessed is the womb that bore you , and the breasts that nursed you ! «
42011028	But he said , » Blessed rather are those who hear the word of God and keep it ! «
42011029	When the crowds were increasing , he began to say , » This is an evil generation . It seeks a sign , but no sign will be given to it except the sign of Jonah .
42011030	For as Jonah became a sign to the Ninevites , so also the Son of Man will be to this generation .
42011031	The queen of the South will rise at the judgment with the men of this generation and condemn them ; for she came from the ends of the earth to hear the wisdom of Solomon , and behold , something greater than Solomon is here .
42011032	The men of Nineveh will stand up at the judgment with this generation and condemn it ; for they repented at the preaching of Jonah , and behold , one greater than Jonah is here .
42011033	» No one after lighting a lamp puts it in a secret place or under a basket , but on a stand , that those who come in may see the light .
42011034	Your eye is the lamp of your body . When your eye is good , your whole body also is full of light . But when it is bad , your body also is full of darkness .
42011035	Therefore be careful that the light in you is not darkness .
42011036	If then your whole body is full of light , having no part dark , it will be completely lighted , as when the bright shining of a lamp gives you light . «
42011037	While he was speaking , a Pharisee asked him to dine with him ; so he went in and sat at table .
42011038	The Pharisee was surprised to see that he did not first wash before dinner .
42011039	But the Lord said to him , » Now you Pharisees clean the outside of the cup and dish , but inside you are full of greed and wickedness .
42011040	You foolish ones ! Did not he who made the outside make the inside also ?
42011041	But give for alms those things which are within ; and behold , everything is clean for you .

42011043	Woe to you Pharisees ! For you love the best seats in the synagogues and greetings in the marketplaces .
42011044	Woe to you ! For you are like graves which are not seen , and men walk over them without knowing it . «
42011045	One of the lawyers answered him , » Teacher , by saying these things you reproach us also . «
42011046	And he said , » Woe to you also , lawyers ! For you load men with burdens hard to bear , and you yourselves do not touch the burdens with one of your fingers .
42011047	Woe to you ! For you build the tombs of the prophets , and your fathers killed them .
42011048	So you witness that you approve of the deeds of your fathers ; for they killed them , and you build their tombs .

42011050	that the blood of all the prophets which was shed from the foundation of the world may be required of this generation ,
42011051	from the blood of Abel to the blood of Zechariah , who perished between the altar and the sanctuary . Yes , I tell you , it shall be required of this generation .
42011052	Woe to you lawyers ! For you have taken away the key of knowledge . You did not enter in yourselves , and you hindered those who were entering . «
42011053	As he went away from there , the scribes and the Pharisees began to press him hard , and to provoke him to speak of many things ,
42011054	lying in wait for him , to catch at something he might say .
42012001	In the meantime , when so many thousands of the multitude had gathered together that they trampled one another , he began to say to his disciples first of all , » Beware of the leaven of the Pharisees , which is hypocrisy .
42012002	There is nothing covered up that will not be revealed , or hidden that will not be known .
42012003	Therefore whatever you have said in the dark will be heard in the light , and what you have whispered in the ear in the inner rooms will be proclaimed from the housetops .
42012004	» I tell you , my friends , do not be afraid of those who kill the body , and after that have no more that they can do .
42012005	But I will show you whom you should fear : fear him who , after he has killed , has power to cast into hell ; yes , I tell you , fear him !
42012006	Are not five sparrows sold for two pennies ? And not one of them is forgotten before God .
42012007	Indeed , the very hairs of your head are all numbered . Fear not ; you are of more value than many sparrows .
42012008	» I tell you , whoever acknowledges me before men , the Son of Man will also acknowledge him before the angels of God .
42012009	But he who denies me before men will be denied before the angels of God .
42012010	And everyone who speaks a word against the Son of Man will be forgiven ; but he who blasphemes against the Holy Spirit will not be forgiven .
42012011	Now when they bring you before the synagogues and rulers and authorities , do not worry about how or what you should answer , or what you are to say ;
42012012	for the Holy Spirit will teach you in that very hour what you ought to say . «
42012013	Someone in the crowd said to him , » Teacher , tell my brother to divide the inheritance with me . «
42012014	But he said to him , » Man , who made me a judge or an arbitrator over you ? «
42012015	And he said to them , » Take heed , and beware of all covetousness ; for a man's life does not consist in the abundance of his possessions . «
42012016	And he told them a parable , saying : » The ground of a certain rich man yielded plentifully .
42012017	And he thought to himself , ‘ What shall I do , since I have no place to store my crops ? ’
42012018	And he said , ‘ I will do this : I will pull down my barns and build larger ones ; and there I will store all my grain and my goods .
42012019	And I will say to my soul , » Soul , you have many goods laid up for many years ; take your ease ; eat , drink , and be merry . « ’
42012020	But God said to him , ‘ Fool ! This night your soul will be required of you ; then whose will those things be which you have prepared ? ’
42012021	So is he who lays up treasure for himself , and is not rich toward God . «
42012022	Then he said to his disciples , » Therefore I tell you , do not worry about your life , what you will eat ; nor about your body , what you will put on .
42012023	For life is more than food , and the body more than clothing .
42012024	Consider the ravens : they neither sow nor reap , they have neither storehouse nor barn , and yet God feeds them . Of how much more value are you than the birds !
42012025	And which of you by worrying can add a single cubit to his span of life ?
42012026	If you then are not able to do this very little thing , why are you anxious about the rest ?
42012027	Consider the lilies , how they grow ; they neither toil nor spin ; yet I tell you , even Solomon in all his glory was not arrayed like one of these .
42012028	But if God so clothes the grass , which today is in the field and tomorrow is thrown into the oven , how much more will he clothe you , O you of little faith !
42012029	And do not seek what you will eat or what you will drink , nor have an anxious mind .
42012030	For all the nations of the world seek after these things , and your Father knows that you need them .
42012031	But seek his kingdom , and these things will be given to you as well .
42012032	Do not fear , little flock , for it is your Father's good pleasure to give you the kingdom .
42012033	Sell your possessions , and give alms ; provide yourselves purses that do not grow old , a treasure in the heavens that does not fail , where no thief approaches and no moth destroys .
42012034	For where your treasure is , there your heart will be also .
42012035	» Let your waist be girded and your lamps burning ,
42012036	and be like men who are waiting for their master to return from the wedding feast , so that they may open to him immediately when he comes and knocks .
42012037	Blessed are those servants whom the master finds watching when he comes . Truly , I say to you that he will gird himself and have them sit at table , and will come and serve them .
42012038	If he comes in the second watch , or in the third , and finds them so , blessed are those servants .
42012039	But know this , that if the owner of the house had known at what hour the thief was coming , he would not have allowed his house to be broken into .
42012040	Therefore you also must be ready , for the Son of Man is coming at an hour you do not expect . «
42012041	Peter said , » Lord , are you telling this parable to us , or to all ? «

42012044	Truly , I say to you , he will set him over all his possessions .

42012046	the master of that servant will come on a day when he does not expect him , and at an hour he is not aware of , and he will cut him to pieces and assign him a place with the unbelievers .
42012047	And that servant who knew his master's will , and did not ready himself or do according to his will , shall be beaten with many stripes .
42012048	But he who did not know , and committed things deserving of stripes , shall be beaten with few . From everyone who has been given much , much will be required ; and to whom they entrusted much , of him they will ask the more .

42012052	For from now on there will be five in one house divided : three against two , and two against three .

42013006	He told this parable : » A man had a fig tree planted in his vineyard , and he came seeking fruit on it and found none .

42013008	And he answered him , ‘ Sir , let it alone this year also , until I dig around it and fertilize it .
42013009	And if it bears fruit next year , fine ; but if not , you can cut it down . ’ «
42013010	Now he was teaching in one of the synagogues on the Sabbath .

42013015	Then the Lord answered him , » You hypocrites ! Does not each of you on the Sabbath untie his ox or his donkey from the stall , and lead it away to water it ?
42013016	Then ought not this woman , a daughter of Abraham , whom Satan has bound for eighteen years , be loosed on the Sabbath day from this bond ? «
42013017	When he said this , all his adversaries were put to shame ; and all the people rejoiced at all the glorious things that were done by him .
42013018	Then he said , » What is the kingdom of God like ? And to what shall I compare it ?

42013020	And again he said , » To what shall I compare the kingdom of God ?
42013021	It is like leaven , which a woman took and hid in three measures of flour till it was all leavened . «

42013023	Then one said to him , » Lord , will those who are saved be few ? « And he said to them ,
42013024	» Strive to enter through the narrow door , for many , I tell you , will seek to enter and will not be able .

42013026	Then you will begin to say , ‘ We ate and drank in your presence , and you taught in our streets . ’

42014001	One Sabbath , when he went to dine at the house of a ruler who belonged to the Pharisees , they watched him .
42014002	And behold , there was a man before him who had dropsy .
42014003	And Jesus spoke to the lawyers and Pharisees , saying , » Is it lawful to heal on the Sabbath , or not ? «
42014004	But they kept silent . And he took him and healed him , and let him go .
42014005	Then he said to them , » Which of you , having a son or an ox that has fallen into a well , will not immediately pull him out on the Sabbath day ? «
42014006	And they could not reply to this .
42014007	So he told a parable to those who were invited , when he noted how they chose the places of honor , saying to them :
42014008	» When you are invited by anyone to a wedding feast , do not sit down in a place of honor , lest one more distinguished than you be invited by him ;
42014009	and he who invited you both will come and say to you , ‘ Give place to this man , ’ and then you will begin with shame to take the lowest place .
42014010	But when you are invited , go and sit in the lowest place , so that when your host comes he may say to you , ‘ Friend , go up higher . ’ Then you will be honored in the presence of all who sit at table with you .
42014011	For everyone who exalts himself will be humbled , and he who humbles himself will be exalted . «
42014012	Then he also said to the one who invited him , » When you give a luncheon or a dinner , do not invite your friends or your brothers , your relatives or rich neighbors , lest they also invite you back , and you be repaid .
42014013	But when you give a feast , invite the poor , the maimed , the lame , the blind ,
42014014	and you will be blessed , because they cannot repay you . You will be repaid at the resurrection of the just . «
42014015	When one of those who sat at table with him heard this , he said to him , » Blessed is he who shall eat bread in the kingdom of God ! «
42014016	Then he said to him , » A certain man gave a great banquet and invited many .
42014017	And at the time of the banquet he sent his servant to say to those who had been invited , ‘ Come , for all is now ready . ’
42014018	But they all alike began to make excuses . The first said to him , ‘ I have bought a field , and I must go out and see it . I ask you to have me excused . ’
42014019	And another said , ‘ I have bought five yoke of oxen , and I am going to test them . I ask you to have me excused . ’
42014020	Still another said , ‘ I have married a wife , and therefore I cannot come . ’
42014021	So the servant came back and reported this to his master . Then the owner of the house became angry and said to his servant , ‘ Go out quickly into the streets and lanes of the city and bring in the poor and the maimed , the blind and the lame . ’
42014022	And the servant said , ‘ Sir , what you commanded has been done , and still there is room . ’
42014023	Then the master said to the servant , ‘ Go out into the highways and hedges , and compel them to come in , that my house may be filled .
42014024	For I tell you , none of those men who were invited shall taste my banquet . ’ «
42014025	Now great multitudes went with him ; and he turned and said to them ,
42014026	» If any one comes to me and does not hate his own father and mother , wife and children , brothers and sisters , yes , and even his own life , he cannot be my disciple .
42014027	And whoever does not bear his cross and come after me cannot be my disciple .
42014028	For which of you , intending to build a tower , does not sit down first and count the cost , whether he has enough to complete it ?
42014029	Otherwise , when he has laid the foundation , and is not able to finish , all who see it begin to mock him ,
42014030	saying , ‘ This man began to build , and was not able to finish . ’
42014031	Or what king , going to make war against another king , will not sit down first and consider whether he is able with ten thousand to meet him who comes against him with twenty thousand ?
42014032	And if not , while the other is still a great way off , he sends a delegation and asks terms of peace .
42014033	So likewise , whoever of you does not give up all that he has cannot be my disciple .
42014034	Salt is good ; but if the salt has lost its taste , how shall it be seasoned ?
42014035	It is neither fit for the land nor for the dunghill ; men throw it out . He who has ears to hear , let him hear ! «
42015001	Now the tax collectors and sinners were all drawing near to hear him .
42015002	And the Pharisees and the scribes murmured , saying , » This man receives sinners and eats with them . «
42015003	So he told them this parable :
42015004	» What man of you , having a hundred sheep , if he loses one of them , does not leave the ninety-nine in the wilderness , and go after the one which is lost until he finds it ?
42015005	And when he has found it , he lays it on his shoulders , rejoicing .
42015006	And when he comes home , he calls together his friends and neighbors , saying to them , ‘ Rejoice with me , for I have found my sheep which was lost . ’
42015007	I tell you that in the same way there will be more joy in heaven over one sinner who repents than over ninety-nine righteous persons who need no repentance .
42015008	» Or what woman , having ten silver coins , if she loses one coin , does not light a lamp and sweep the house and search carefully until she finds it ?
42015009	And when she has found it , she calls together her friends and neighbors , saying , ‘ Rejoice with me , for I have found the coin which I had lost . ’
42015010	In the same way , I tell you , there is joy in the presence of the angels of God over one sinner who repents . «
42015011	Then he said : » There was a man who had two sons .
42015012	And the younger of them said to his father , ‘ Father , give me the share of property that falls to me . ’ So he divided his living between them .
42015013	Not many days after , the younger son gathered together all he had and took his journey into a far country , and there he squandered his property in loose living .
42015014	And when he had spent everything , there arose a severe famine in that country , and he began to be in want .
42015015	So he went and joined himself to a citizen of that country , who sent him into his fields to feed swine .
42015016	And he would gladly have filled his stomach with the pods that the swine ate , and no one gave him anything .
42015017	But when he came to himself , he said , ‘ How many of my father's hired servants have bread enough and to spare , and here I perish with hunger !
42015018	I will arise and go to my father and will say to him , » Father , I have sinned against heaven and before you .
42015019	I am no longer worthy to be called your son ; make me like one of your hired servants . « ’
42015020	And he arose and came to his father . But while he was still a great way off , his father saw him and had compassion for him , and ran and fell on his neck and kissed him .
42015021	And the son said to him , ‘ Father , I have sinned against heaven and before you ; I am no longer worthy to be called your son . ’
42015022	But the father said to his servants , ‘ Bring out the best robe and put it on him , and put a ring on his hand and sandals on his feet .
42015023	And bring the fatted calf and kill it , and let us eat and be merry ;
42015024	for this my son was dead and is alive again ; he was lost and is found . ’ And they began to be merry .
42015025	» Now his older son was in the field . And as he came and drew near to the house , he heard music and dancing .
42015026	So he called one of the servants and asked what these things meant .
42015027	And he said to him , ‘ Your brother has come , and your father has killed the fatted calf , because he has received him safe and sound . ’
42015028	But he was angry and refused to go in . So his father came out and pleaded with him .
42015029	But he answered his father , ‘ Behold , these many years I have been serving you , and I never disobeyed your command ; yet you never gave me a young goat , that I might make merry with my friends .
42015030	But when this son of yours came , who has devoured your living with harlots , you killed for him the fatted calf ! ’
42015031	And he said to him , ‘ Son , you are always with me , and all that I have is yours .
42015032	It was right that we should make merry and be glad , for this your brother was dead , and is alive again ; he was lost , and is found . ’ «
42016001	He also said to his disciples : » There was a certain rich man who had a steward , and an accusation was brought to him that this man was wasting his goods .
42016002	So he called him and said to him , ‘ What is this I hear about you ? Give an account of your stewardship , for you can no longer be steward . ’
42016003	The steward said to himself , ‘ What shall I do , since my master is taking the stewardship away from me ? I am not strong enough to dig , and I am ashamed to beg .
42016004	I have decided what to do , so that people may receive me into their houses when I am put out of the stewardship . ’
42016005	So he called in each one of his master's debtors , and he said to the first , ‘ How much do you owe my master ? ’
42016006	And he said , ‘ A hundred measures of oil . ’ So he said to him , ‘ Take your bill , and sit down quickly and write fifty . ’
42016007	Then he said to another , ‘ And how much do you owe ? ’ And he said , ‘ A hundred measures of wheat . ’ He said to him , ‘ Take your bill , and write eighty . ’
42016008	So the master commended the dishonest steward because he had dealt shrewdly . For the sons of this world are more shrewd in dealing with their own generation than the sons of light .
42016009	And I tell you , make friends for yourselves by means of unrighteous mammon , so that when it fails , they may receive you into the eternal dwellings .
42016010	He who is faithful in a very little is faithful also in much ; and he who is dishonest in a very little is dishonest also in much .
42016011	If then you have not been faithful in the unrighteous mammon , who will trust you with the true riches ?
42016012	And if you have not been faithful in what is another's , who will give you what is your own ?
42016013	No servant can serve two masters ; for either he will hate the one and love the other , or else he will be devoted to the one and despise the other . You cannot serve God and mammon . «
42016014	The Pharisees , who were lovers of money , heard all this , and they scoffed at him .
42016015	He said to them , » You are those who justify yourselves before men , but God knows your hearts . For what is highly esteemed among men is an abomination in the sight of God .
42016016	The law and the prophets were until John . Since that time the good news of the kingdom of God is preached , and everyone is forcing his way into it .
42016017	But it is easier for heaven and earth to pass away , than for one dot of the law to fail .
42016018	Everyone who divorces his wife and marries another commits adultery , and he who marries a woman divorced from her husband commits adultery .
42016019	» There was a certain rich man who was clothed in purple and fine linen and feasted sumptuously every day .
42016020	And a certain beggar named Lazarus was laid at his gate , full of sores ,
42016021	longing to be fed with what fell from the rich man's table . Moreover the dogs came and licked his sores .
42016022	So the beggar died , and was carried by the angels to Abraham's bosom . The rich man also died and was buried .
42016023	And in Hades , being in torment , he lifted up his eyes , and saw Abraham far off and Lazarus in his bosom .
42016024	And he called out , ‘ Father Abraham , have mercy upon me , and send Lazarus to dip the tip of his finger in water and cool my tongue ; for I am in agony in this flame . ’
42016025	But Abraham said , ‘ Son , remember that in your lifetime you received your good things , and Lazarus received evil things ; but now he is comforted here and you are in agony .
42016026	And besides all this , between us and you a great chasm has been fixed , so that those who want to pass from here to you cannot , nor can anyone cross over from there to us . ’
42016027	And he said , ‘ Then I beg you , father , to send him to my father's house ,
42016028	for I have five brothers , so that he may warn them , lest they also come to this place of torment . ’
42016029	Abraham said to him , ‘ They have Moses and the prophets ; let them hear them . ’
42016030	And he said , ‘ No , father Abraham ; but if someone goes to them from the dead , they will repent . ’
42016031	He said to him , ‘ If they do not hear Moses and the prophets , neither will they be convinced if some one should rise from the dead . ’ «
42017001	Then he said to his disciples , » Things that cause people to sin are bound to come , but woe to him through whom they do come !
42017002	It would be better for him if a millstone were hung round his neck and he were thrown into the sea , than that he should cause one of these little ones to sin .
42017003	Take heed to yourselves ; if your brother sins , rebuke him , and if he repents , forgive him .
42017004	And if he sins against you seven times in a day , and turns to you seven times , and says , ‘ I repent , ’ you must forgive him . «
42017005	The apostles said to the Lord , » Increase our faith ! «
42017006	So the Lord said , » If you have faith as a mustard seed , you can say to this mulberry tree , ‘ Be uprooted and be planted in the sea , ’ and it would obey you .
42017007	» Will any one of you , who has a servant plowing or keeping sheep , say to him when he has come in from the field , ‘ Come at once and sit down to eat ’ ?
42017008	Will he not rather say to him , ‘ Prepare my supper , and gird yourself and serve me , till I eat and drink ; and afterward you shall eat and drink' ?
42017009	Does he thank the servant because he did what he was commanded ?
42017010	So you also , when you have done all that is commanded you , say , ‘ We are unworthy servants ; we have only done what was our duty . ’ «
42017011	On the way to Jerusalem he was passing along between Samaria and Galilee .
42017012	As he entered a village , ten men who were lepers met him , who stood at a distance .
42017013	And they lifted up their voices and said , » Jesus , Master , have mercy on us ! «

42017021	nor will they say , ‘ Look , here it is ! ’ or ‘ There ! ’ for behold , the kingdom of God is within you . «

42017023	And they will say to you , ‘ Look here ! ’ or ‘ Look there ! ’ Do not go after them or follow them .
42017024	For as the lightning flashes and lights up the sky from one part to the other , so will the Son of Man be in his day .

42017026	Just as it was in the days of Noah , so also will it be in the days of the Son of Man .

42017028	Likewise as it was in the days of Lot : they ate , they drank , they bought , they sold , they planted , they built ;

42017031	On that day , let him who is on the housetop , with his goods in the house , not come down to take them away . And likewise let him who is in the field not turn back .

42018001	Then he told them a parable , to show that they ought always to pray and not lose heart .

42019016	Then came the first , saying , ‘ Master , your mina has earned ten minas more . ’

42019020	Then another came , saying , ‘ Master , here is your mina , which I have kept laid away in a handkerchief ;
42019021	for I was afraid of you , because you are a hard man . You take up what you did not lay down , and reap what you did not sow . ’

42020001	One day as he was teaching the people in the temple and preaching the gospel , the chief priests and the scribes , together with the elders , came up to him
42020002	and said to him , » Tell us by what authority are you doing these things ? Or who it is that gave you this authority . «
42020003	He answered them , » I also will ask you a question ; now tell me ,
42020004	the baptism of John — was it from heaven or from men ? «
42020005	And they reasoned among themselves , saying , » If we say , ‘ From heaven , ’ he will say , ‘ Why did you not believe him ? ’
42020006	But if we say , ‘ From men , ’ all the people will stone us , for they are persuaded that John was a prophet . «
42020007	So they answered that they did not know where it was from .
42020008	And Jesus said to them , » Neither will I tell you by what authority I do these things . «
42020009	Then he began to tell the people this parable : » A man planted a vineyard , leased it to vine-dressers , and went into another country for a long time .
42020010	At harvest time he sent a servant to the tenants , that they would give him some of the fruit of the vineyard . But the tenants beat him and sent him away empty-handed .
42020011	He sent another servant ; him also they beat and treated shamefully , and sent him away empty-handed .
42020012	He sent a third ; and they wounded him and cast him out .
42020013	Then the owner of the vineyard said , ‘ What shall I do ? I will send my beloved son ; perhaps they will respect him . ’
42020014	But when the tenants saw him , they reasoned among themselves and said , ‘ This is the heir . Let us kill him , that the inheritance may be ours . ’
42020015	So they cast him out of the vineyard and killed him . What then will the owner of the vineyard do to them ?
42020016	He will come and destroy those tenants , and give the vineyard to others . « When they heard this , they said , » May this never be ! «
42020017	But he looked at them and said , » What then is this that is written : ‘ The stone which the builders rejected has become the chief cornerstone ’ ?

42020026	And they were not able in the presence of the people to catch him by what he said . But marveling at his answer they were silent .

42020030	And the second
42020031	and then the third took her , and in the same way the seven died , and they left no children .

42021001	He looked up and saw the rich putting their gifts into the treasury ,
42021002	and he also saw a poor widow put in two copper coins .

42021031	So you also , when you see these things happening , know that the kingdom of God is near .
42021032	Truly , I say to you , this generation will not pass away till all things take place .
42021033	Heaven and earth will pass away , but my words will not pass away .
42021034	» But take heed to yourselves , lest your hearts be weighed down with dissipation and drunkenness and cares of this life , and that Day come on you unexpectedly like a trap .
42021035	For it will come upon all those who dwell on the face of the whole earth .
42021036	Watch at all times , and pray always that you may have strength to escape all these things that will take place , and to stand before the Son of Man . «
42021037	And every day he was teaching in the temple , but at night he went out to spend the night on the mount called Olivet .
42021038	And early in the morning all the people came to him in the temple to hear him .
42022001	Now the feast of Unleavened Bread drew near , which is called the Passover .
42022002	And the chief priests and the scribes were seeking how to kill him , for they feared the people .
42022003	Then Satan entered Judas , called Iscariot , who was numbered of the twelve .
42022004	So he went his way and conferred with the chief priests and officers , how he might betray him to them .

42022006	So he consented , and sought an opportunity to betray him to them in the absence of the multitude .
42022007	Then came the day of Unleavened Bread , on which the Passover lamb had to be sacrificed .

42022012	He will show you a large , furnished upper room ; there make ready . «
42022013	So they went , and found it just as he had told them ; and they prepared the Passover .

42022025	And he said to them , » The kings of the Gentiles exercise lordship over them ; and those who exercise authority over them are called benefactors .
42022026	But not so among you ; on the contrary , he who is greatest among you , let him be as the youngest , and he who leads as one who serves .

42022028	You are those who have continued with me in my trials .

42022067	» If you are the Christ , tell us . « But he said to them , » If I tell you , you will not believe .

42023001	Then the whole body of them arose and led him to Pilate .
42023002	And they began to accuse him , saying , » We found this man perverting our nation and forbidding to pay taxes to Caesar , saying that he himself is Christ , a king . «
42023003	So Pilate asked him , » Are you the King of the Jews ? « He answered him , » It is as you say . «
42023004	Then Pilate said to the chief priests and the crowd , » I find no crime in this man . «

42023006	When Pilate heard this , he asked if the man was a Galilean .
42023007	And when he learned that he belonged to Herod’s jurisdiction , he sent him to Herod , who also was in Jerusalem at that time .
42023008	Now when Herod saw Jesus , he was very glad , for he had desired to see him for a long time , because he had heard about him , and he hoped to see some miracle done by him .
42023009	Then he questioned him with many words , but he gave him no answer .
42023010	The chief priests and the scribes stood by , vehemently accusing him .
42023011	And Herod with his soldiers treated him with contempt and mocked him ; then , dressing him in a gorgeous robe , he sent him back to Pilate .
42023012	That very day Pilate and Herod became friends with each other , for before this they had been at enmity with each other .
42023013	Pilate then called together the chief priests , the rulers , and the people ,
42023014	and said to them , » You have brought this man to me as one who was inciting the people to rebellion . And behold , having examined him in your presence , I have found no guilt in this man concerning those charges which you make against him ;
42023015	neither did Herod , for he sent him back to us . Behold , nothing deserving death has been done by him ;
42023016	I will therefore chastise him and release him . «
42023018	But they all cried out together , » Away with this man , and release to us Barabbas « —
42023019	a man who had been thrown into prison for an insurrection in the city , and for murder .
42023020	Wanting to release Jesus , Pilate addressed to them again .
42023021	But they shouted , » Crucify him , crucify him ! «
42023022	Then he said to them the third time , » Why , what evil has he done ? I have found in him no crime deserving death . I will therefore chastise him and release him . «
42023023	But they were insistent , demanding with loud voices that he be crucified . And their voices prevailed .
42023024	So Pilate gave sentence that their demand should be granted .
42023025	And he released the man who had been thrown into prison for insurrection and murder , the one they asked for ; but Jesus he delivered up to their will .
42023026	And as they led him away , they seized one Simon of Cyrene , who was coming in from the country , and laid on him the cross , to carry it behind Jesus .

42023030	
42023031	For if they do these things when the wood is green , what will happen when it is dry ? «
42023032	Two others , criminals , were also led with him to be put to death .

42023034	Then Jesus said , » Father , forgive them , for they know not what they do . « And they divided his garments and cast lots .
42023035	And the people stood watching ; but even the rulers sneered at him , saying , » He saved others ; let him save himself if he is the Christ of God , the Chosen One . «
42023036	The soldiers also mocked him , coming up and offering him wine vinegar ,
42023037	and saying , » If you are the King of the Jews , save yourself . «

42023040	But the other rebuked him , saying , » Do you not fear God , since you are under the same sentence of condemnation ?
42023041	And we indeed justly , for we are receiving the due reward of our deeds ; but this man has done nothing wrong . «
42023042	Then he said , » Jesus , remember me when you come into your kingdom . «

42023050	Now there was a man named Joseph , a member of the Council , a good and righteous man ,
42023051	who had not consented to their decision and deed . He came from of Arimathea , a city of the Jews , and he was waiting for the kingdom of God .
42023052	This man went to Pilate and asked for the body of Jesus .
42023053	Then he took it down and wrapped it in linen cloth , and laid it in a tomb that was hewn out of the rock , where no one had ever yet been laid .

42024001	But on the first day of the week , at early dawn , they came to the tomb , bringing the spices which they had prepared .
42024002	And they found the stone rolled away from the tomb ,

42024011	But their words seemed to them like idle tales , and they did not believe them .

42024013	Now behold , that same day two of them were going to a village called Emmaus , about seven miles from Jerusalem .
42024014	And they were talking with each other about all these things that had happened .
42024015	While they talked and discussed , Jesus himself drew near and went with them .
42024016	But their eyes were kept from recognizing him .

42024040	When he had said this , he showed them his hands and his feet .

42024042	They gave him a piece of broiled fish ,
42024043	and he took it and ate in their presence .

43001001	In the beginning was the Word , and the Word was with God , and the Word was God .
43001002	He was with God in the beginning .
43001003	All things were made through him , and without him nothing was made that was made .
43001004	In him was life , and the life was the light of men .
43001005	The light shines in the darkness , and the darkness did not comprehend it .
43001006	There was a man sent from God , whose name was John .
43001007	He came for a witness , to bear witness of the light , that all might believe through him .
43001008	He was not the light , but came to bear witness of the light .
43001009	The true light that gives light to every man was coming into the world .
43001010	He was in the world , and the world was made through him , and the world did not know him .
43001011	He came to his own , and his own did not receive him .
43001012	But to all who received him , to those who believed in his name , he gave the right to become children of God —
43001013	who were born , not of blood nor of the will of the flesh nor of the will of man , but of God .
43001014	And the Word became flesh and dwelt among us , and we have seen his glory , the glory as of the only begotten from the Father , full of grace and truth .
43001015	John bore witness of him and cried out , saying , » This was he of whom I said , ‘ He who comes after me ranks before me , for he was before me . ’ «
43001016	And from his fullness have we all received , grace upon grace .
43001017	For the law was given through Moses ; grace and truth came through Jesus Christ .
43001018	No one has ever seen God ; God the only Son , who is in the bosom of the Father , he has made him known .
43001019	Now this is the testimony of John , when the Jews sent priests and Levites from Jerusalem to ask him , » Who are you ? «
43001020	He confessed , he did not deny , but confessed , » I am not the Christ . «
43001021	And they asked him , » What then ? Are you Elijah ? « He said , » I am not . « » Are you the prophet ? « And he answered , » No . «
43001022	Then they said to him , » Who are you ? Give us an answer for those who sent us . What do you say about yourself ? «
43001023	He said , » I am the voice of one crying in the wilderness , ‘ Make straight the way of the Lord , ’ as the prophet Isaiah said . «
43001024	Now they had been sent from the Pharisees .
43001025	They asked him , » Then why do you baptize , if you are not the Christ , nor Elijah , nor the prophet ? «
43001026	John answered them , » I baptize with water , but there stands One among you whom you do not know .
43001027	It is he who comes after me , the thong of whose sandal I am not worthy to untie . «
43001028	This took place in Bethany beyond the Jordan , where John was baptizing .
43001029	The next day John saw Jesus coming toward him , and said , » Behold , the Lamb of God , who takes away the sin of the world !
43001030	This is he of whom I said , ‘ After me comes a man who ranks before me , for he was before me . ’
43001031	I myself did not know him ; but for this I came baptizing with water , that he might be revealed to Israel . «
43001032	And John bore witness , » I saw the Spirit descend as a dove from heaven , and it remained on him .
43001033	I did not know him , but he who sent me to baptize with water said to me , ‘ He on whom you see the Spirit descend and remain , this is he who baptizes with the Holy Spirit . ’
43001034	And I have seen and testified that this is the Son of God . «
43001035	Again the next day John was standing with two of his disciples .
43001036	And he looked at Jesus as he walked , and said , » Behold , the Lamb of God ! «
43001037	The two disciples heard him say this , and they followed Jesus .
43001038	Jesus turned , and saw them following , and said to them , » What do you seek ? « They said to him , » Rabbi « ( which means Teacher ) , » where are you staying ? «
43001039	He said to them , » Come and see . « They came and saw where he was staying ; and they stayed with him that day , for it was about the tenth hour .
43001040	One of the two who heard John speak , and followed him , was Andrew , Simon Peter's brother .
43001041	He first found his own brother Simon , and said to him , » We have found the Messiah « ( which means the Christ ) .
43001042	He brought him to Jesus . Jesus looked at him and said , » You are Simon son of John . You shall be called Cephas « ( which means Peter ) .
43001043	The next day Jesus wanted to go to Galilee . And he found Philip and said to him , » Follow me . «
43001044	Now Philip was from Bethsaida , the city of Andrew and Peter .
43001045	Philip found Nathanael and said to him , » We have found him of whom Moses in the law , and also the prophets , wrote – Jesus of Nazareth , the son of Joseph . «
43001046	And Nathanael said to him , » Can anything good come out of Nazareth ? « Philip said to him , » Come and see . «
43001047	Jesus saw Nathanael coming toward him , and said of him , » Behold , an Israelite indeed , in whom is no deceit ! «
43001048	Nathanael said to him , » How do you know me ? « Jesus answered him , » Before Philip called you , when you were under the fig tree , I saw you . «
43001049	Nathanael answered him , » Rabbi , you are the Son of God ! You are the King of Israel ! «

43001051	And he said to him , » Truly , truly , I say to you , you shall see heaven open , and the angels of God ascending and descending upon the Son of Man . «
43002001	On the third day there was a wedding at Cana in Galilee , and the mother of Jesus was there .
43002002	And Jesus and his disciples had also been invited to the wedding .
43002003	When the wine was gone , the mother of Jesus said to him , » They have no wine . «
43002004	Jesus said to her , » Woman , what have you to do with me ? My hour has not yet come . «
43002005	His mother said to the servants , » Do whatever he tells you . «
43002006	Now six stone jars were standing there , according to the manner for purification of the Jews , each holding twenty or thirty gallons .
43002007	Jesus said to them , » Fill the jars with water . « And they filled them up to the brim .
43002008	He said to them , » Now draw some out , and take it to the master of the feast . « So they took it .
43002009	When the master of the feast had tasted the water that was made wine , and did not know where it had come from ( though the servants who had drawn the water knew ) , the master of the feast called the bridegroom .
43002010	And he said to him , » Every man sets out the good wine first ; and when the guests have drunk freely , then the poor wine ; but you have kept the good wine until now . «
43002011	This , the first of his signs , Jesus did at Cana in Galilee , and manifested his glory ; and his disciples believed in him .
43002012	After this he went down to Capernaum , with his mother and his brothers and his disciples ; and there they stayed for a few days .
43002013	The Passover of the Jews was at hand , and Jesus went up to Jerusalem .
43002014	In the temple he found those who were selling oxen and sheep and doves , and the money-changers at their business .
43002015	And he made a whip of cords , and drove them all , with the sheep and oxen , out of the temple ; and he poured out the coins of the money-changers and overturned their tables .
43002016	And he said to those who sold doves , » Take these things away ! You shall not make my Father's house a house of merchandise ! «
43002017	His disciples remembered that it was written , » Zeal for your house will consume me . «
43002018	Then the Jews said to him , » What sign do you show to us , since you do this ? «
43002019	Jesus answered them , » Destroy this temple , and in three days I will raise it up . «
43002020	The Jews then said , » It has taken forty-six years to build this temple , and will you raise it up in three days ? «
43002021	But he was speaking of the temple of his body .
43002022	When therefore he was raised from the dead , his disciples remembered that he had said this ; and they believed the scripture and the word which Jesus had spoken .
43002023	Now when he was in Jerusalem at the Passover feast , many believed in his name when they saw the signs which he did .
43002024	But Jesus did not trust himself to them , because he knew all men ,
43002025	and he had no need for anyone to bear witness of man , for he knew what was in man .
43003001	Now there was a man of the Pharisees , named Nicodemus , a ruler of the Jews .
43003002	This man came to Jesus by night and said to him , » Rabbi , we know that you are a teacher come from God ; for no one can do these signs that you do unless God is with him . «
43003003	Jesus answered him , » Truly , truly , I say to you , unless one is born again , he cannot see the kingdom of God . «
43003004	Nicodemus said to him , » How can a man be born when he is old ? Can he enter a second time into his mother's womb and be born ? «
43003005	Jesus answered , » Truly , truly , I say to you , unless one is born of water and the Spirit , he cannot enter the kingdom of God .
43003006	That which is born of the flesh is flesh , and that which is born of the Spirit is spirit .
43003007	Do not marvel that I said to you , ‘ You must be born again . ’
43003008	The wind blows where it wishes , and you hear the sound of it , but you cannot tell where it comes from or where it goes . So it is with everyone who is born of the Spirit . «
43003009	Nicodemus said to him , » How can this be ? «
43003010	Jesus answered him , » Are you the teacher of Israel , and yet you do not understand these things ?
43003011	Truly , truly , I say to you , we speak of what we know , and testify to what we have seen ; but you do not receive our testimony .
43003012	If I have told you earthly things and you do not believe , how will you believe if I tell you heavenly things ?
43003013	No one has ascended into heaven , but he who came from heaven – the Son of Man .
43003014	And as Moses lifted up the serpent in the wilderness , so must the Son of Man be lifted up ,
43003015	that whoever believes in him may have eternal life .
43003016	For God so loved the world that he gave his only Son , that whoever believes in him should not perish but have eternal life .
43003017	For God did not send his Son into the world to condemn the world , but that the world through him might be saved .
43003018	He who believes in him is not condemned ; but he who does not believe is condemned already , because he has not believed in the name of the only Son of God .
43003019	And this is the judgment , that the light has come into the world , and men loved darkness rather than light , because their deeds were evil .
43003020	For every one who does evil hates the light , and does not come to the light , lest his deeds should be exposed .
43003021	But he who does the truth comes to the light , that it may be clearly seen that his deeds have been done in God . «
43003022	After this Jesus and his disciples went into the land of Judea , and there he remained with them and baptized .
43003023	Now John also was baptizing at Aenon near Salim , because there was much water there ; and people came and were baptized .
43003024	For John had not yet been put in prison .
43003025	Now a discussion arose between some of John's disciples and a Jew over purifying .
43003026	And they came to John and said to him , » Rabbi , he who was with you beyond the Jordan , to whom you have testified — behold , he is baptizing , and all are going to him . «
43003027	John answered , » A man can receive only what is given to him from heaven .
43003028	You yourselves bear me witness , that I said , ‘ I am not the Christ , ’ but I have been sent before him .
43003029	He who has the bride is the bridegroom ; but the friend of the bridegroom , who stands and hears him , rejoices greatly because of the bridegroom's voice . Therefore this joy of mine is now full .
43003030	He must increase , but I must decrease .
43003031	» He who comes from above is above all ; he who is of the earth belongs to the earth , and of the earth he speaks . He who comes from heaven is above all .
43003032	He testifies to what he has seen and heard ; yet no one receives his testimony .
43003033	He who has received his testimony has certified that God is true .
43003034	For he whom God has sent speaks the words of God , for God gives the Spirit without measure .
43003035	The Father loves the Son , and has given all things into his hand .
43003036	He who believes in the Son has eternal life ; he who does not obey the Son shall not see life , but the wrath of God remains on him . «
43004001	Now when the Lord knew that the Pharisees had heard that Jesus was making and baptizing more disciples than John
43004002	( although Jesus himself did not baptize , but only his disciples ) ,
43004003	he left Judea and departed again to Galilee .
43004004	Now he had to go through Samaria .
43004005	So he came to a city of Samaria which is called Sychar , near the plot of ground that Jacob gave to his son Joseph .
43004006	Jacob's well was there , and Jesus , wearied as he was from his journey , sat down by the well . It was about the sixth hour .
43004007	There came a woman of Samaria to draw water . Jesus said to her , » Give me a drink . «
43004008	For his disciples had gone away into the city to buy food .
43004009	Then the woman of Samaria said to him , » How is it that you , being a Jew , ask a drink from me , a Samaritan woman ? « For Jews have no dealings with Samaritans .
43004010	Jesus answered her , » If you knew the gift of God , and who it is that is saying to you , ‘ Give me a drink , ’ you would have asked him , and he would have given you living water . «
43004011	The woman said to him , » Sir , you have nothing to draw with , and the well is deep . Where do you get that living water ?
43004012	Are you greater than our father Jacob , who gave us the well , and drank from it himself , as well as his sons and his cattle ? «
43004013	Jesus answered her , » Everyone who drinks of this water will thirst again ,
43004014	but whoever drinks of the water that I shall give him will never thirst . The water that I shall give him will become in him a spring of water welling up to eternal life . «
43004015	The woman said to him , » Sir , give me this water , that I may not thirst , nor come here to draw . «
43004016	Jesus said to her , » Go , call your husband , and come here . «
43004017	The woman answered , » I have no husband . « Jesus said to her , » You are right in saying , ‘ I have no husband ’ ;
43004018	for you have had five husbands , and the one whom you now have is not your husband ; this you have said truly . «
43004019	The woman said to him , » Sir , I perceive that you are a prophet .
43004020	Our fathers worshiped on this mountain , and you Jews say that in Jerusalem is the place where men ought to worship . «
43004021	Jesus said to her , » Woman , believe me , the hour is coming when neither on this mountain nor in Jerusalem will you worship the Father .
43004022	You worship what you do not know ; we worship what we know , for salvation is from the Jews .
43004023	But the hour is coming , and now is , when the true worshipers will worship the Father in spirit and truth , for such the Father seeks to worship him .
43004024	God is spirit , and those who worship him must worship in spirit and truth . «
43004025	The woman said to him , » I know that Messiah is coming « ( who is called Christ ) . » When he comes , he will tell us all things . «
43004026	Jesus said to her , » I who speak to you am he . «
43004027	Just then his disciples came . And they marveled that he was talking with a woman , but no one said , » What do you wish ? « or , » Why are you talking with her ? «
43004028	Then the woman left her water jar , and went away into the city , and said to the people ,
43004029	» Come , see a man who told me all that I ever did . Could this be the Christ ? «
43004030	They went out of the city and came to him .
43004031	Meanwhile his disciples urged him , saying , » Rabbi , eat . «
43004032	But he said to them , » I have food to eat of which you do not know . «
43004033	So the disciples said to one another , » Has any one brought him food ? «
43004034	Jesus said to them , » My food is to do the will of him who sent me , and to finish his work .
43004035	Do you not say , ‘ There are yet four months and then comes the harvest ’ ? Behold , I tell you , lift up your eyes , and look at the fields ! They are already white for harvest .
43004036	And he who reaps receives wages , and gathers fruit for eternal life , so that sower and reaper may rejoice together .
43004037	For here the saying is true , ‘ One sows and another reaps . ’
43004038	I sent you to reap that for which you have not labored ; others have labored , and you have entered into their labor . «
43004039	Many of the Samaritans from that city believed in him because of the woman's testimony , » He told me all that I ever did . «
43004040	So when the Samaritans came to him , they urged him to stay with them ; and he stayed there two days .
43004041	And many more believed because of his word .
43004042	They said to the woman , » We no longer believe just because of what you said ; now we have heard for ourselves , and we know that this man is indeed the Savior of the world . «
43004043	After the two days he departed to Galilee .
43004044	For Jesus himself testified that a prophet has no honor in his own country .
43004045	So when he came to Galilee , the Galileans welcomed him , having seen all that he had done in Jerusalem at the feast , for they too had gone to the feast .
43004046	So he came again to Cana in Galilee , where he had made the water wine . And at Capernaum there was an official whose son was sick .
43004047	When he heard that Jesus had come from Judea to Galilee , he went to him and begged him to come down and heal his son , for he was at the point of death .
43004048	Jesus said to him , » Unless you people see signs and wonders , you will never believe . «
43004049	The official said to him , » Sir , come down before my child dies . «
43004050	Jesus said to him , » Go ; your son will live . « The man believed the word that Jesus spoke to him and went his way .
43004051	As he was going down , his servants met him and told him that his son was living .
43004052	So he inquired of them the hour when his son got better , and they said to him , » Yesterday at the seventh hour the fever left him . «
43004053	So the father knew that it was at the same hour in which Jesus had said to him , » Your son will live . « And he himself believed , and all his household .
43004054	This was now the second sign that Jesus did when he had come from Judea to Galilee .
43005001	After this there was a feast of the Jews , and Jesus went up to Jerusalem .
43005002	Now there is in Jerusalem by the Sheep Gate a pool , which is called in Hebrew , Bethesda , having five porches .
43005003	In these lay a multitude of disabled people , blind , lame , paralyzed .
43005005	One man who was there had been an invalid for thirty-eight years .
43005006	When Jesus saw him lying there and knew that he had been in this condition for a long time , he said to him , » Do you want to be made well ? «
43005007	The sick man answered him , » Sir , I have no man to put me into the pool when the water is stirred up ; but while I am coming , another steps down before me . «
43005008	Jesus said to him , » Rise , take up your bed , and walk . «
43005009	And at once the man was healed , and he took up his bed and walked . Now that day was the Sabbath .
43005010	So the Jews said to the man who was cured , » It is the Sabbath ; it is not lawful for you to carry your bed . «
43005011	But he answered them , » The man who made me well said to me , ‘ Take up your bed , and walk . ’ «
43005012	They asked him , » Who is the man who said to you , ‘ Take up your bed , and walk ’ ? «
43005013	Now the man who had been healed did not know who it was , for Jesus had withdrawn , as there was a crowd in that place .
43005014	Afterward , Jesus found him in the temple , and said to him , » See , you are well . Sin no more , so that nothing worse may happen to you . «
43005015	The man went away and told the Jews that it was Jesus who had made him well .
43005016	For this reason the Jews persecuted Jesus , because he was doing these things on the Sabbath .
43005017	But Jesus answered them , » My Father is working still , and I am working . «
43005018	Therefore the Jews sought all the more to kill him , because he not only broke the Sabbath , but also said that God was his Father , making himself equal with God .
43005019	Jesus said to them , » Truly , truly , I say to you , the Son can do nothing of himself , but only what he sees the Father doing ; for whatever he does , the Son also does .
43005020	For the Father loves the Son , and shows him all things that he himself does ; and he will show him greater works than these , that you may marvel .
43005021	For as the Father raises the dead and gives life to them , even so the Son gives life to whom he will .
43005022	For the Father judges no one , but has given all judgment to the Son ,
43005023	that all may honor the Son just as they honor the Father . He who does not honor the Son does not honor the Father who sent him .
43005024	Truly , truly , I say to you , he who hears my word and believes him who sent me , has eternal life ; and shall not come into judgment , but has passed from death to life .
43005025	Truly , truly , I say to you , the hour is coming , and now is , when the dead will hear the voice of the Son of God ; and those who hear will live .
43005026	For as the Father has life in himself , so he has granted the Son also to have life in himself ,
43005027	and has given him authority to execute judgment , because he is the Son of Man .
43005028	Do not marvel at this ; for the hour is coming when all who are in the graves will hear his voice
43005029	and come forth – those who have done good , to the resurrection of life , and those who have done evil , to the resurrection of judgment .
43005030	» I can do nothing of myself ; as I hear , I judge ; and my judgment is just , because I seek not my own will but the will of him who sent me .
43005031	» If I bear witness of myself , my testimony is not true .
43005032	There is another who bears witness of me , and I know that the testimony which he bears of me is true .
43005033	You have sent to John , and he has borne witness to the truth .
43005034	Not that the testimony which I receive is from man ; but I say this that you may be saved .
43005035	He was a burning and shining lamp , and you were willing to rejoice for a time in his light .
43005036	But the testimony which I have is greater than that of John ; for the works which the Father has given me to finish , these very works which I am doing , bear witness of me , that the Father has sent me .
43005037	And the Father who sent me has himself testified of me . You have never heard his voice , nor seen his form .
43005038	And you do not have his word abiding in you , for you do not believe him whom he has sent .
43005039	You search the Scriptures , because in them you think that you have eternal life ; and these are they that testify of me .
43005040	Yet you refuse to come to me that you may have life .
43005041	» I do not receive glory from men .
43005042	But I know you , that you do not have the love of God in you .
43005043	I have come in my Father's name , and you do not receive me ; if another comes in his own name , him you will receive .
43005044	How can you believe , who receive glory from one another , and do not seek the glory that comes from the only God ?
43005045	Do not think that I shall accuse you to the Father ; it is Moses who accuses you , on whom you set your hope .
43005046	If you believed Moses , you would believe me , for he wrote about me .
43005047	But if you do not believe his writings , how will you believe my words ? «
43006001	After this Jesus went to the other side of the Sea of Galilee , which is the Sea of Tiberias .
43006002	And a great multitude followed him , because they saw his signs which he performed on those who were diseased .
43006003	Jesus went up on the mountain , and there sat down with his disciples .
43006004	Now the Passover , the feast of the Jews , was near .
43006005	Then Jesus lifted up his eyes , and seeing a great multitude coming toward him , he said to Philip , » Where shall we buy bread , that these people may eat ? «
43006006	But this he said to test him , for he himself knew what he would do .
43006007	Philip answered him , » Two hundred denarii would not buy enough bread for each one of them to have a little . «
43006008	One of his disciples , Andrew , Simon Peter's brother , said to him ,
43006009	» There is a lad here who has five barley loaves and two small fish , but what are they among so many ? «
43006010	Jesus said , » Make the people sit down . « Now there was much grass in the place ; so the men sat down , in number about five thousand .
43006011	Jesus then took the loaves , and when he had given thanks , he distributed them to those who were seated ; so also the fish , as much as they wanted .
43006012	And when they had eaten their fill , he said to his disciples , » Gather up the fragments left over , that nothing may be lost . «
43006013	So they gathered them up and filled twelve baskets with the fragments of the five barley loaves , left over by those who had eaten .
43006014	When the people saw the sign that Jesus did , they said , » Surely this is the Prophet who is to come into the world . «
43006015	Perceiving then that they were about to come and take him by force to make him king , Jesus withdrew again to the mountain by himself .
43006016	When evening came , his disciples went down to the sea ,
43006017	got into a boat , and started across the sea to Capernaum . It was now dark , and Jesus had not yet come to them .
43006018	The sea rose because a strong wind was blowing .
43006019	So when they had rowed about three or four miles , they saw Jesus walking on the sea and drawing near the boat ; and they were afraid .
43006020	But he said to them , » It is I ; do not be afraid . «
43006021	Then they were glad to take him into the boat , and immediately the boat was at the land where they were going .
43006022	On the next day the people who remained on the other side of the sea saw that there had been only one boat there , and that Jesus had not entered the boat with his disciples , but that his disciples had gone away alone .
43006023	However , boats from Tiberias came near the place where they ate the bread after the Lord had given thanks .
43006024	So when the people saw that Jesus was not there , nor his disciples , they also got into the boats and went to Capernaum , seeking Jesus .
43006025	When they found him on the other side of the sea , they said to him , » Rabbi , when did you come here ? «
43006026	Jesus answered them , » Truly , truly , I say to you , you seek me , not because you saw the signs , but because you ate your fill of the loaves .
43006027	Do not labor for the food which perishes , but for the food which endures to eternal life , which the Son of Man will give to you ; for on him has God the Father set his seal . «
43006028	Then they said to him , » What must we do , to be doing the works of God ? «
43006029	Jesus answered them , » This is the work of God , that you believe in him whom he has sent . «
43006030	So they said to him , » What sign will you perform then , that we may see it and believe you ? What work will you do ?
43006031	Our fathers ate the manna in the desert ; as it is written , ‘ He gave them bread from heaven to eat . ’ «
43006032	Jesus then said to them , » Truly , truly , I say to you , it was not Moses who gave you the bread from heaven ; but my Father gives you the true bread from heaven .
43006033	For the bread of God is he who comes down from heaven and gives life to the world . «
43006034	Then they said to him , » Lord , give us this bread always . «
43006035	And Jesus said to them , » I am the bread of life . He who comes to me shall never hunger , and he who believes in me shall never thirst .
43006036	But I said to you that you have seen me and yet do not believe .
43006037	All that the Father gives me will come to me , and the one who comes to me I will by no means cast out .
43006038	For I have come down from heaven , not to do my own will , but the will of him who sent me .
43006039	And this is the will of him who sent me , that I should lose nothing of all that he has given me , but raise it up at the last day .
43006040	For this is the will of my Father , that every one who sees the Son and believes in him should have eternal life ; and I will raise him up at the last day . «
43006041	The Jews then began to murmur about him , because he said , » I am the bread which came down from heaven . «
43006042	They said , » Is not this Jesus , the son of Joseph , whose father and mother we know ? How does he now say , ‘ I have come down from heaven ’ ? «
43006043	Jesus answered them , » Do not murmur among yourselves .
43006044	No one can come to me unless the Father who sent me draws him ; and I will raise him up at the last day .
43006045	It is written in the prophets , ‘ And they shall all be taught by God . ’ Everyone who has heard and learned from the Father comes to me .
43006046	Not that any one has seen the Father except the one who is from God ; he has seen the Father .
43006047	Truly , truly , I say to you , he who believes has everlasting life .
43006048	I am the bread of life .
43006049	Your fathers ate the manna in the wilderness , and they died .
43006050	This is the bread which comes down from heaven , that a man may eat of it and not die .
43006051	I am the living bread which came down from heaven . If anyone eats of this bread , he will live for ever ; and the bread which I shall give for the life of the world is my flesh . «
43006052	Then the Jews began to argue among themselves , saying , » How can this man give us his flesh to eat ? «
43006053	So Jesus said to them , » Truly , truly , I say to you , unless you eat the flesh of the Son of Man and drink his blood , you have no life in you .
43006054	Whoever eats my flesh and drinks my blood has eternal life , and I will raise him up at the last day .
43006055	For my flesh is food indeed , and my blood is drink indeed .
43006056	He who eats my flesh and drinks my blood abides in me , and I in him .
43006057	As the living Father sent me , and I live because of the Father , so he who feeds on me will live because of me .
43006058	This is the bread which came down from heaven , not as your fathers ate the manna and died . He who eats this bread will live for ever . «
43006059	This he said in the synagogue as he taught in Capernaum .
43006060	Many of his disciples , when they heard it , said , » This is a hard saying ; who can listen to it ? «
43006061	When Jesus knew in himself that his disciples complained about this , he said to them , » Does this offend you ?
43006062	What then if you should see the Son of Man ascend to where he was before ?
43006063	It is the Spirit who gives life ; the flesh profits nothing . The words that I have spoken to you are spirit , and they are life .
43006064	But there are some of you who do not believe . « For Jesus knew from the beginning who they were who did not believe , and who would betray him .
43006065	And he said , » This is why I told you that no one can come to me unless it has been granted to him by the Father . «
