43006066	From this time many of his disciples went back and no longer walked with him .
43006067	Then Jesus said to the twelve , » Do you also want to go away ? «
43006068	Simon Peter answered him , » Lord , to whom shall we go ? You have the words of eternal life .
43006069	And we believe , and have come to know , that you are the Holy One of God . «
43006070	Jesus answered them , » Did I not choose you , the twelve , and one of you is a devil ? «
43006071	He spoke of Judas Iscariot , the son of Simon , for it was he who was to betray him , though one of the twelve .
43007001	After this Jesus went about in Galilee ; he would not go about in Judea , because the Jews sought to kill him .
43007002	Now the Jews' feast of Tabernacles was at hand .
43007003	So his brothers said to him , » Leave here and go to Judea , that your disciples may see the works you are doing .
43007004	For no one works in secret if he seeks to be known openly . If you do these things , show yourself to the world . «
43007005	For even his brothers did not believe in him .
43007006	Jesus said to them , » My time has not yet come , but your time is always ready .
43007007	The world cannot hate you , but it hates me because I testify of it that its works are evil .
43007008	You go up to the feast . I am not yet going up to this feast , for my time has not yet fully come . «
43007009	Having said this , he remained in Galilee .
43007010	But after his brothers had gone up to the feast , then he also went up , not publicly , but in secret .
43007011	The Jews were looking for him at the feast , and saying , » Where is he ? «
43007012	And there was much complaining among the people about him . Some said , » He is a good man « ; others said , » No , on the contrary , he deceives the people . «
43007013	However , no one spoke openly of him for fear of the Jews .
43007014	Now about the middle of the feast Jesus went up into the temple and taught .
43007015	And the Jews marveled , saying , » How did this man get such learning , having never studied ? «
43007016	Jesus answered them , » My teaching is not mine , but his who sent me .
43007017	If anyone is willing to do his will , he shall know whether the teaching is from God or whether I speak on my own authority .
43007018	He who speaks from himself seeks his own glory ; but he who seeks the glory of the One who sent him is true , and in him there is no falsehood .
43007019	Did not Moses give you the law ? Yet none of you keeps the law . Why do you seek to kill me ? «
43007020	The people answered , » You have a demon . Who is seeking to kill you ? «
43007021	Jesus answered them , » I did one deed , and you all marvel .
43007022	Moses therefore gave you circumcision ( not that it is from Moses , but from the fathers ) , and you circumcise a man on the Sabbath .
43007023	If on the Sabbath a man receives circumcision , so that the law of Moses may not be broken , are you angry with me because on the Sabbath I made a man's whole body well ?
43007024	Do not judge by appearances , but judge with right judgment . «
43007025	Then some of the people of Jerusalem said , » Is not this the man whom they seek to kill ?
43007026	Here he is , speaking publicly , and they say nothing to him ! Can it be that the authorities really know that he is the Christ ?
43007027	But we know where this man is from ; when the Christ comes , no one will know where he is from . «
43007028	Then Jesus cried out , as he taught in the temple , » You know me , and you know where I am from ; and I have not come on my own , but he who sent me is true , and him you do not know .
43007029	But I know him , for I am from him , and he sent me . «
43007030	Then they sought to take him ; but no one laid a hand on him , because his hour had not yet come .
43007031	And many of the people believed in him , and they said , » When the Christ comes , will he do more signs than this man has done ? «
43007032	The Pharisees heard the crowd muttering these things about him , and the Pharisees and the chief priests sent officers to arrest him .
43007033	Then Jesus said to them , » I shall be with you a little while longer , and then I go to him who sent me .
43007034	You will seek me , and you will not find me ; where I am you cannot come . «
43007035	The Jews said to one another , » Where does this man intend to go that we shall not find him ? Does he intend to go to the Dispersion among the Greeks and teach the Greeks ?
43007036	What does he mean when he said , ‘ You will seek me and you will not find me , ’ and , ‘ Where I am you cannot come ’ ? «
43007037	On the last day , that great day of the feast , Jesus stood and cried out , » If anyone thirsts , let him come to me and drink .
43007038	He who believes in me , as the Scripture has said , out of his heart will flow rivers of living water . «
43007039	Now this he said about the Spirit , whom those who believed in him were to receive ; for as yet the Spirit had not been given , because Jesus was not yet glorified .
43007040	When they heard these words , some of the people said , » Surely this is the prophet . «
43007041	Others said , » This is the Christ . « But some said , » Will the Christ come from Galilee ?
43007042	Has not the scripture said that the Christ comes from David , and from Bethlehem , the town where David was ? «
43007043	So there was a division among the people because of him .
43007044	Some of them wanted to seize him , but no one laid hands on him .
43007045	The officers then went back to the chief priests and Pharisees , who said to them , » Why did you not bring him ? «
43007046	The officers answered , » No man ever spoke like this man ! «
43007047	The Pharisees answered them , » Are you deceived , you also ?
43007048	Have any of the rulers or of the Pharisees believed in him ?
43007049	But this crowd that does not know the law is accursed . «
43007050	Nicodemus , who had gone to Jesus before , and who was one of them , said to them ,
43007051	» Does our law judge a man without first giving him a hearing and learning what he is doing ? «
43007052	They replied , » Are you from Galilee , too ? Search and look , and you will find that no prophet is to rise out of Galilee . «
43007053	Then each went to his own house .
43008001	But Jesus went to the Mount of Olives .
43008002	Early in the morning he came again to the temple ; all the people came to him , and he sat down and taught them .
43008003	Then the scribes and the Pharisees brought to him a woman caught in adultery . And when they had set her in the midst ,
43008004	they said to him , » Teacher , this woman was caught in the act of adultery .
43008005	Now in the law Moses commanded us to stone such . What do you say ? «
43008006	They said this to test him , that they might have something of which to accuse him . But Jesus bent down and wrote on the ground with his finger .
43008007	And when they continued to ask him , he stood up and said to them , » Let him who is without sin among you be the first to throw a stone at her . «
43008008	And again he stooped down and wrote on the ground .
43008009	Then those who heard it went away one by one , beginning with the oldest even to the last , and Jesus was left alone , with the woman standing before him .
43008010	Jesus straightened up and said to her , » Woman , where are they ? Has no one condemned you ? «
43008011	She said , » No one , Lord . « And Jesus said , » Neither do I condemn you ; go , and sin no more . «
43008012	Again Jesus spoke to them , saying , » I am the light of the world . He who follows me will not walk in darkness , but will have the light of life . «
43008013	The Pharisees then said to him , » You are bearing witness of yourself ; your testimony is not true . «
43008014	Jesus answered , » Even if I bear witness of myself , my testimony is true , for I know where I came from and where I am going ; but you do not know where I come from and where I am going .
43008015	You judge according to the flesh ; I judge no one .
43008016	And yet if I do judge , my judgment is true , for I am not alone , but I am with the Father who sent me .
43008017	In your own law it is written that the testimony of two men is true .
43008018	I am One who bears witness of myself , and the Father who sent me bears witness of me . «
43008019	Then they said to him , » Where is your Father ? « Jesus answered , » You know neither me nor my Father ; if you knew me , you would know my Father also . «
43008020	These words he spoke in the treasury , as he taught in the temple ; but no one arrested him , because his hour had not yet come .
43008021	Then Jesus said to them again , » I am going away , and you will seek me , and will die in your sin . Where I go you cannot come . «
43008022	Then the Jews said , » Will he kill himself , since he says , ‘ Where I go you cannot come ’ ? «
43008023	He said to them , » You are from below ; I am from above . You are of this world ; I am not of this world .
43008024	Therefore I told to you that you would die in your sins ; for if you do not believe that I am he , you will die in your sins . «
43008025	They said to him , » Who are you ? « Jesus said to them , » Just what I have been saying to you from the beginning .
43008026	I have much to say about you and much to judge ; but he who sent me is true , and I declare to the world what I have heard from him . «
43008027	They did not understand that he spoke to them of the Father .
43008028	So Jesus said , » When you have lifted up the Son of man , then you will know that I am he , and that I do nothing on my own authority but speak just what the Father taught me .
43008029	And he who sent me is with me ; he has not left me alone , for I always do what is pleasing to him . «
43008030	As he spoke these words , many believed in him .
43008031	Jesus then said to the Jews who had believed in him , » If you continue in my word , you are truly my disciples .
43008032	And you will know the truth , and the truth will make you free . «
43008033	They answered him , » We are Abraham's descendants , and have never been in bondage to anyone . How can you say , ‘ You will be made free ’ ? «
43008034	Jesus answered them , » Truly , truly , I say to you , everyone who commits sin is a slave of sin .
43008035	And a slave does not continue in the house forever , but a son continues forever .
43008036	So if the Son makes you free , you will be free indeed .
43008037	I know that you are Abraham's descendants , yet you seek to kill me , because my word has no place in you .
43008038	I speak of what I have seen with my Father , and you do what you have heard from your Father . «
43008039	They answered him , » Abraham is our father . « Jesus said to them , » If you were Abraham's children , you would do the things Abraham did ,
43008040	but now you seek to kill me , a man who has told you the truth which I heard from God . This is not what Abraham did .
43008041	You do the deeds of your father . « They said to him , » We were not born of fornication ; we have one Father – God . «
43008042	Jesus said to them , » If God were your Father , you would love me , for I proceeded and came forth from God ; I have not come of my own accord , but he sent me .
43008043	Why do you not understand what I say ? It is because you are not able to hear my word .
43008044	You are of your father the devil , and you want to do your father's desires . He was a murderer from the beginning , and does not stand in the truth , because there is no truth in him . When he lies , he speaks according to his own nature , for he is a liar and the father of lies .
43008045	But because I tell the truth , you do not believe me .
43008046	Which of you convicts me of sin ? If I tell the truth , why do you not believe me ?
43008047	He who is of God hears the words of God ; the reason you do not hear them is that you are not of God . «
43008048	The Jews answered him , » Are we not right in saying that you are a Samaritan and have a demon ? «
43008049	Jesus answered , » I do not have a demon ; but I honor my Father , and you dishonor me .
43008050	Yet I do not seek my own glory ; there is One who seeks it and he will be the judge .
43008051	Truly , truly , I say to you , if anyone keeps my word he will never see death . «
43008052	The Jews said to him , » Now we know that you have a demon ! Abraham died , as did the prophets ; and you say , ‘ If anyone keeps my word , he will never taste death . ’
43008053	Are you greater than our father Abraham ? He died , and so did the prophets . Who do you claim to be ? «
43008054	Jesus answered , » If I glorify myself , my glory is nothing . It is my Father who glorifies me , of whom you say that he is your God .
43008055	But you have not known him ; I know him . If I said , I do not know him , I would be a liar like you ; but I do know him and keep his word .
43008056	Your father Abraham rejoiced to see my day ; he saw it and was glad . «
43008057	The Jews then said to him , » You are not yet fifty years old , and have you seen Abraham ? «
43008058	Jesus said to them , » Truly , truly , I say to you , before Abraham was , I am . «
43008059	So they took up stones to throw at him ; but Jesus hid himself , and went out of the temple .
43009001	As he passed by , he saw a man blind from birth .
43009002	And his disciples asked him , » Rabbi , who sinned , this man or his parents , that he was born blind ? «
43009003	Jesus answered , » Neither this man sinned nor his parents sinned . But that the works of God might be revealed in him ,
43009004	we must work the works of him who sent me , while it is day . Night is coming , when no one can work .
43009005	As long as I am in the world , I am the light of the world . «
43009006	As he said this , he spat on the ground and made clay of the saliva , and anointed the man's eyes with the clay .
43009007	And he said to him , » Go , wash in the pool of Siloam « ( which means , Sent ) . So he went and washed , and came back seeing .
43009008	The neighbors and those who had seen him before as a beggar , said , » Is not this the man who used to sit and beg ? «
43009009	Some said , » It is he . « Others said , » No , but he is like him . « He said , » I am the man . «
43009010	They said to him , » Then how were your eyes opened ? «
43009011	He answered and said , » A man called Jesus made clay and anointed my eyes and said to me , ‘ Go to the pool of Siloam and wash . ’ So I went and washed , and I received sight . «
43009012	They said to him , » Where is he ? « He said , » I do not know . «
43009013	They brought to the Pharisees the man who had formerly been blind .
43009014	Now it was a Sabbath day when Jesus made the clay and opened his eyes .
43009015	Then the Pharisees also asked him again how he had received his sight . He said to them , » He put clay on my eyes , and I washed , and I see . «
43009016	Some of the Pharisees said , » This man is not from God , for he does not keep the Sabbath . « But others said , » How can a man who is a sinner do such signs ? « And there was a division among them .
43009017	So they again said to the blind man , » What do you say about him , since he has opened your eyes ? « He said , » He is a prophet . «
43009018	The Jews did not believe that he had been blind , and had received his sight , until they called the parents of the man who had received his sight .
43009019	And they asked them , » Is this your son , who you say was born blind ? How then does he now see ? «
43009020	His parents answered , » We know that this is our son , and that he was born blind ;
43009021	but how he now sees we do not know , nor do we know who opened his eyes . Ask him . He is of age ; he will speak for himself . «
43009022	His parents said this because they feared the Jews , for the Jews had agreed already that if anyone confessed that he was Christ , he would be put out of the synagogue .
43009023	Therefore his parents said , » He is of age ; ask him . «
43009024	So for the second time they called the man who had been blind , and said to him , » Give God the glory ; we know that this man is a sinner . «
43009025	He answered , » Whether he is a sinner or not , I do not know . One thing I know , that though I was blind , now I see . «
43009026	Then they said to him , » What did he do to you ? How did he open your eyes ? «
43009027	He answered them , » I have told you already and you did not listen . Why do you want to hear it again ? Do you want to become his disciples , too ? «
43009028	Then they reviled him and said , » You are his disciple , but we are disciples of Moses .
43009029	We know that God spoke to Moses , but as for this fellow , we do not know where he comes from . «
43009030	The man answered , » Why , this is a marvel ! You do not know where he comes from , and yet he opened my eyes .
43009031	We know that God does not listen to sinners , but if any one is a worshiper of God and does his will , he listens to him .
43009032	Never since the world began has it been heard that anyone opened the eyes of a man born blind .
43009033	If this man were not from God , he could do nothing . «
43009034	They answered him , » You were born in utter sin , and are you teaching us ? « And they cast him out .
43009035	Jesus heard that they had cast him out , and when he found him , he said , » Do you believe in the Son of Man ? «
43009036	He answered , » Who is he , sir , that I may believe in him ? «
43009037	Jesus said to him , » You have seen him , and it is he who speaks with you . «
43009038	Then he said , » Lord , I believe ! « And he worshiped him .
43009039	Jesus said , » For judgment I have come into this world , that those who do not see may see , and that those who see may become blind . «
43009040	Then some of the Pharisees who were with him heard this , and said to him , » Are we blind also ? «
43009041	Jesus said to them , » If you were blind , you would have no guilt ; but now that you say , ‘ We see , ’ your sin remains .
43010001	» Truly , truly , I say to you , the man who does not enter the sheepfold by the door , but climbs in by some other way , he is a thief and a robber .
43010002	But he who enters by the door is the shepherd of the sheep .
43010003	To him the doorkeeper opens , and the sheep hear his voice ; and he calls his own sheep by name and leads them out .
43010004	When he has brought out all his own , he goes on before them , and the sheep follow him , for they know his voice .
43010005	A stranger they will not follow , but they will flee from him , for they do not know the voice of strangers . «
43010006	This figure Jesus used with them , but they did not understand what he was saying to them .
43010007	Then Jesus said to them again , » Truly , truly , I say to you , I am the door of the sheep .
43010008	All who ever came before me are thieves and robbers , but the sheep did not hear them .
43010009	I am the door . If anyone enters by me , he will be saved , and will go in and out and find pasture .
43010010	The thief comes only to steal and kill and destroy ; I have come that they may have life , and have it abundantly .
43010011	I am the good shepherd . The good shepherd lays down his life for the sheep .
43010012	But he who is a hireling and not the shepherd , who does not own the sheep , sees the wolf coming and leaves the sheep and flees ; and the wolf snatches the sheep and scatters them .
43010013	He flees because he is a hireling and cares nothing for the sheep .
43010014	I am the good shepherd ; I know my sheep , and my sheep know me —
43010015	just as the Father knows me and I know the Father ; and I lay down my life for the sheep .
43010016	And I have other sheep that are not of this fold ; I must bring them also , and they will heed my voice . So there shall be one flock and one shepherd .
43010017	For this reason my Father loves me , because I lay down my life , that I may take it again .
43010018	No one takes it from me , but I lay it down of my own accord . I have power to lay it down , and I have power to take it again . This command I have received from my Father . «
43010019	There was again a division among the Jews because of these words .
43010020	Many of them said , » He has a demon , and is mad . Why listen to him ? «
43010021	Others said , » These are not the sayings of one who has a demon . Can a demon open the eyes of the blind ? «
43010022	Then came the Feast of Dedication at Jerusalem . It was winter ,
43010023	and Jesus was in the temple , walking in Solomon's Porch .
43010024	So the Jews gathered round him and said to him , » How long will you keep us in suspense ? If you are the Christ , tell us plainly . «
43010025	Jesus answered them , » I told you , and you do not believe . The works that I do in my Father's name , they bear witness of me ;
43010026	but you do not believe , because you are not of my sheep .
43010027	My sheep hear my voice , and I know them , and they follow me .
43010028	I give them eternal life , and they shall never perish ; no one shall snatch them out of my hand .
43010029	My Father , who has given them to me , is greater than all ; and no one is able to snatch them out of my Father's hand .
43010030	I and the Father are one . «
43010031	The Jews took up stones again to stone him .
43010032	Jesus answered them , » I have shown you many good works from the Father . For which of these do you stone me ? «
43010033	The Jews answered him , » For a good work we do not stone you , but for blasphemy , and because you , being a man , make yourself God . «
43010034	Jesus answered them , » Is it not written in your law , ‘ I said , you are gods ’ ?
43010035	If he called them gods , to whom the word of God came ( and the Scripture cannot be broken ) ,
43010036	do you say of him whom the Father sanctified and sent into the world , ‘ You are blaspheming , ’ because I said , ‘ I am the Son of God ’ ?
43010037	If I do not do the works of my father , do not believe me ;
43010038	but if I do them , even though you do not believe me , believe the works , that you may know and understand that the Father is in me , and I am in the Father . «
43010039	Again they tried to seize him , but he escaped from their hands .
43010040	He went away again across the Jordan to the place where John was baptizing at first , and there he stayed .
43010041	And many came to him and they said , » John performed no sign , but all that John said about this man was true . «
43010042	And many believed in him there .
43011001	Now a certain man was sick , Lazarus of Bethany , the village of Mary and her sister Martha .
43011002	It was this Mary who anointed the Lord with fragrant oil and wiped his feet with her hair , whose brother Lazarus was sick .
43011003	So the sisters sent to him , saying , » Lord , he whom you love is sick . «
43011004	When Jesus heard it , he said , » This sickness is not unto death , but for the glory of God , so that the Son of God may be glorified through it . «
43011005	Now Jesus loved Martha and her sister and Lazarus .
43011006	So , when he heard that he was sick , he stayed two more days in the place where he was .
43011007	Then after this he said to the disciples , » Let us go to Judea again . «
43011008	The disciples said to him , » Rabbi , the Jews were just now seeking to stone you , and are you going there again ? «
43011009	Jesus answered , » Are there not twelve hours in the day ? If anyone walks in the day , he does not stumble , because he sees the light of this world .
43011010	But if one walks in the night , he stumbles , because the light is not in him . «
43011011	These things he said , and after that he said to them , » Our friend Lazarus has fallen asleep , but I go to wake him up . «
43011012	His disciples said , » Lord , if he sleeps , he will recover . «
43011013	Now Jesus had spoken of his death , but they thought that he meant taking rest in sleep .
43011014	So then Jesus told them plainly , » Lazarus is dead ;
43011015	and for your sake I am glad that I was not there , so that you may believe . But let us go to him . «
43011016	Then Thomas , who is called the Twin , said to his fellow disciples , » Let us also go , that we may die with him . «
43011017	So when Jesus came , he found that he had already been in the tomb four days .
43011018	Bethany was near Jerusalem , about two miles off ,
43011019	and many of the Jews had come to Martha and Mary to comfort them concerning their brother .
43011020	When Martha heard that Jesus was coming , she went and met him , but Mary sat in the house .
43011021	Martha said to Jesus , » Lord , if you had been here , my brother would not have died .
43011022	But even now I know that whatever you ask of God , God will give you . «
43011023	Jesus said to her , » Your brother will rise again . «
43011024	Martha said to him , » I know that he will rise again in the resurrection at the last day . «
43011025	Jesus said to her , » I am the resurrection and the life . He who believes in me , though he die , yet shall he live ;
43011026	and whoever lives and believes in me shall never die . Do you believe this ? «
43011027	She said to him , » Yes , Lord , I believe that you are the Christ , the Son of God , who is to come into the world . «
43011028	And when she had said this , she went her way and called Mary her sister , saying , » The Teacher is here and is calling for you . «
43011029	When she heard it , she rose quickly and went to him .
43011030	Now Jesus had not yet come to the village , but was still in the place where Martha had met him .
43011031	The Jews who were with her in the house , and comforting her , when they saw that Mary rose up quickly and went out , followed her , supposing that she was going to the tomb to weep there .
43011032	Then Mary , when she came where Jesus was and saw him , fell at his feet , saying to him , » Lord , if you had been here , my brother would not have died . «
43011033	When Jesus saw her weeping , and the Jews who came with her also weeping , he was deeply moved in spirit and troubled .
43011034	And he said , » Where have you laid him ? « They said to him , » Lord , come and see . «
43011035	Jesus wept .
43011036	Then the Jews said , » See how he loved him ! «
43011037	But some of them said , » Could not he who opened the eyes of the blind man have kept this man from dying ? «
43011038	Then Jesus , deeply moved again , came to the tomb . It was a cave , and a stone lay against it .
43011039	Jesus said , » Take away the stone . « Martha , the sister of the dead man , said to him , » Lord , by this time there is a bad odor , for he has been dead four days . «
43011040	Jesus said to her , » Did I not tell you that if you would believe you would see the glory of God ? «
43011041	So they took away the stone . And Jesus lifted up his eyes and said , » Father , I thank you that you have heard me .
43011042	I knew that you always hear me , but I said this for the benefit of the people standing by , that they may believe that you sent me . «
43011043	When he had said this , he cried with a loud voice , » Lazarus , come out ! «
43011044	The dead man came out , his hands and feet bound with grave clothes , and his face wrapped with a cloth . Jesus said to them , » Unbind him , and let him go . «
43011045	Many of the Jews therefore , who had come to Mary and had seen what Jesus did , believed in him .
43011046	But some of them went to the Pharisees and told them what Jesus had done .
43011047	Then the chief priests and the Pharisees gathered a council , and said , » What are we to do ? For this man performs many signs .
43011048	If we let him go on like this , everyone will believe in him , and the Romans will come and take away both our place and our nation . «
43011049	But one of them , Caiaphas , who was high priest that year , said to them , » You know nothing at all !
43011050	You do not understand that it is expedient for you that one man should die for the people , and that the whole nation not perish . «
43011051	He did not say this on his own , but being high priest that year he prophesied that Jesus would die for the nation ,
43011052	and not for that nation only , but also that he would gather together into one the children of God who were scattered abroad .
43011053	So from that day on they plotted to put him to death .
43011054	Jesus therefore no longer went about openly among the Jews , but went from there to the country near the wilderness , to a town called Ephraim ; and there he stayed with his disciples .
43011055	Now the Passover of the Jews was at hand , and many went from the country up to Jerusalem before the Passover , to purify themselves .
43011056	They were looking for Jesus and saying to one another as they stood in the temple , » What do you think ? That he will not come to the feast ? «
43011057	Now the chief priests and the Pharisees had given orders that if anyone knew where he was , he should report it , so that they might arrest him .
43012001	Then , six days before the Passover , Jesus came to Bethany where Lazarus was , whom Jesus had raised from the dead .
43012002	There they made him a supper ; and Martha served , while Lazarus was one of those who sat at the table with him .
43012003	Then Mary took a pound of very costly perfume of pure nard , anointed the feet of Jesus , and wiped his feet with her hair . And the house was filled with the fragrance of the perfume .
43012004	But one of his disciples , Judas Iscariot , who was later to betray him , said ,
43012005	» Why was this perfume not sold for three hundred denarii and given to the poor ? «
43012006	This he said , not that he cared for the poor , but because he was a thief ; and as he had the money box , he used to take what was put into it .
43012007	Jesus said , » Let her alone , she has kept this for the day of my burial .
43012008	The poor you always have with you , but you do not always have me . «
43012009	Now a great crowd of the Jews learned that he was there , and they came , not only on account of Jesus but also to see Lazarus , whom he had raised from the dead .
43012010	So the chief priests planned to put Lazarus also to death ,
43012011	because on account of him many of the Jews were going away and believing in Jesus .
43012012	The next day a great crowd that had come to the feast heard that Jesus was coming to Jerusalem .
43012013	They took branches of palm trees and went out to meet him , crying , » Hosanna ! Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord ! The King of Israel ! «
43012014	Jesus found a young donkey and sat upon it , as it is written ,
43012015	
43012016	His disciples did not understand this at first ; but when Jesus was glorified , then they remembered that these things had been written about him and that they had done these things to him .
43012017	The crowd that had been with him when he called Lazarus out of the tomb and raised him from the dead bore witness .
43012018	For this reason the people went to meet him , because they heard that he had done this sign .
43012019	The Pharisees then said to one another , » You see that you are accomplishing nothing . Look , The world has gone after him ! «
43012020	Now there were some Greeks among those who went up to worship at the Feast .
43012021	Then they came to Philip , who was from Bethsaida in Galilee , and said to him , » Sir , we wish to see Jesus . «
43012022	Philip went and told Andrew ; and in turn Andrew and Philip told Jesus .
43012023	Jesus answered them , » The hour has come for the Son of Man to be glorified .
43012024	Truly , truly , I say to you , unless a grain of wheat falls into the ground and dies , it remains alone ; but if it dies , it produces much fruit .
43012025	He who loves his life will lose it , and he who hates his life in this world will keep it for eternal life .
43012026	If anyone serves me , he must follow me ; and where I am , there my servant will be also . If anyone serves me , him my Father will honor .
43012027	» Now is my soul troubled , and what shall I say ? ‘ Father , save me from this hour ’ ? No , for this purpose I came to this hour .
43012028	Father , glorify your name . « Then a voice came from heaven , » I have glorified it , and I will glorify it again . «
43012029	The crowd standing by heard it and said that it had thundered . Others said , » An angel has spoken to him . «
43012030	Jesus answered , » This voice has come for your sake , not for mine .
43012031	Now is the judgment of this world ; now the ruler of this world will be cast out .
43012032	And I , when I am lifted up from the earth , will draw all men to myself . «
43012033	He said this to show by what death he was to die .
43012034	The crowd answered him , » We have heard from the Law that the Christ remains forever ; and how can you say , ‘ The Son of Man must be lifted up ’ ? Who is this Son of Man ? «
43012035	Then Jesus said to them , » A little while longer the light is with you . Walk while you have the light , lest the darkness overtake you ; he who walks in the darkness does not know where he is going .
43012036	While you have the light , believe in the light , that you may become sons of light . « When Jesus had said this , he departed and hid himself from them .
43012037	Though he had done so many signs before them , yet they did not believe in him ;
43012038	that the word of Isaiah the prophet might be fulfilled , which he spoke : » Lord , who has believed our report ? And to whom has the arm of the Lord been revealed ? «
43012039	Therefore they could not believe , because Isaiah said again :
43012040	
43012041	Isaiah said this because he saw his glory and spoke of him .
43012042	Nevertheless even among the rulers many believed in him , but because of the Pharisees they did not confess him , lest they should be put out of the synagogue ;
43012043	for they loved the praise of men more than the praise of God .
43012044	Then Jesus cried out and said , » He who believes in me , believes not in me but in him who sent me .
43012045	And he who sees me sees him who sent me .
43012046	I have come as a light into the world , that whoever believes in me should not remain in darkness .
43012047	If anyone hears my words and does not keep them , I do not judge him ; for I did not come to judge the world but to save the world .
43012048	He who rejects me and does not receive my words has a judge ; the word that I have spoken will condemn him on the last day .
43012049	For I have not spoken on my own authority ; but the Father who sent me gave me a command , what to say and what to speak .
43012050	And I know that his command is eternal life . Whatever I say , therefore , I say just as the Father has told me . «
43013001	Now before the feast of the Passover , when Jesus knew that his hour had come to depart from this world to the Father , having loved his own who were in the world , he loved them to the end .
43013002	And during supper , when the devil had already put it into the heart of Judas Iscariot , Simon's son , to betray him ,
43013003	Jesus , knowing that the Father had given all things into his hands , and that he had come from God and was going to God ,
43013004	rose from supper , laid aside his garments , took a towel and girded himself .
43013005	After that , he poured water into a basin and began to wash the disciples' feet , and to wipe them with the towel with which he was girded .
43013006	Then he came to Simon Peter . And Peter said to him , » Lord , are you going to wash my feet ? «
43013007	Jesus answered him , » You do not realize now what I am doing , but later you will understand . «
43013008	Peter said to him , » You shall never wash my feet . « Jesus answered him , » If I do not wash you , you have no part with me . «
43013009	Simon Peter said to him , » Lord , not my feet only , but also my hands and my head ! «
43013010	Jesus said to him , » He who has bathed needs only to wash his feet , but is completely clean ; and you are clean , but not every one of you . «
43013011	For he knew who was to betray him ; that was why he said , » You are not all clean . «
43013012	When he had washed their feet , and taken his garments , and returned to his place , he said to them , » Do you know what I have done to you ?
43013013	You call me Teacher and Lord , and you are right , for so I am .
43013014	If I then , your Lord and Teacher , have washed your feet , you also ought to wash one another's feet .
43013015	For I have given you an example , that you should do as I have done to you .
43013016	Truly , truly , I say to you , a servant is not greater than his master ; nor is he who is sent greater than he who sent him .
43013017	If you know these things , blessed are you if you do them .
43013018	I am not speaking of you all . I know whom I have chosen ; but that the Scripture may be fulfilled , ‘ he who ate my bread has lifted up his heel against me . ’
43013019	Now I tell you before it comes , that when it does take place , you may believe that I am he .
43013020	Truly , truly , I say to you , he who receives anyone I send receives me ; and he who receives me receives him who sent me . «
43013021	When Jesus had said this , he was troubled in spirit , and testified , » Truly , truly , I say to you , one of you will betray me . «
43013022	The disciples looked at one another , uncertain of whom he spoke .
43013023	One of his disciples , whom Jesus loved , was leaning close to the breast of Jesus .
43013024	Simon Peter motioned to him and said , » Ask who it is of whom he speaks . «
43013025	Then , leaning back on the breast of Jesus , he said to him , » Lord , who is it ? «
43013026	Jesus answered , » It is he to whom I shall give this piece of bread when I have dipped it . « And having dipped the bread , he gave it to Judas Iscariot , the son of Simon .
43013027	Then after the bread , Satan entered into him . Jesus said to him , » What you are going to do , do quickly . «
43013028	But no one at the table knew why he said this to him .
43013029	Some thought that , because Judas had the money box , Jesus was telling him , » Buy what we need for the feast « ; or , that he should give something to the poor .
43013030	Having received the piece of bread , he went out immediately . And it was night .
43013031	When he had gone out , Jesus said , » Now is the Son of Man glorified , and in him God is glorified .
43013032	If God is glorified in him , God will also glorify him in himself , and glorify him at once .
43013033	Little children , I shall be with you a little while longer . You will seek me ; and as I said to the Jews , ‘ Where I am going , you cannot come , ’ so now I say to you .
43013034	A new commandment I give to you , that you love one another ; as I have loved you , that you also love one another .
43013035	By this all men will know that you are my disciples , if you have love for one another . «
43013036	Simon Peter said to him , » Lord , where are you going ? « Jesus answered , » Where I am going you cannot follow me now ; but you shall follow afterward . «
43013037	Peter said to him , » Lord , why can I not follow you now ? I will lay down my life for you . «
43013038	Jesus answered , » Will you lay down your life for me ? Truly , truly , I say to you , the rooster will not crow , till you have denied me three times .
43014001	» Let not your hearts be troubled ; believe in God , believe also in me .
43014002	In my Father's house are many rooms ; if it were not so , I would have told you . I go to prepare a place for you .
43014003	And if I go and prepare a place for you , I will come again and take you to myself , that where I am you may be also .
43014004	And you know the way where I am going . «
43014005	Thomas said to him , » Lord , we do not know where you are going , and how can we know the way ? «
43014006	Jesus said to him , » I am the way , and the truth , and the life . No one comes to the Father except through me .
43014007	If you had known me , you would have known my Father also ; and from now on you know him and have seen him . «
43014008	Philip said to him , » Lord , show us the Father , and that will be enough for us . «
43014009	Jesus said to him , » Have I been with you so long , and yet you do not know me , Philip ? He who has seen me has seen the Father ; how can you say , ‘ Show us the Father ’ ?
43014010	Do you not believe that I am in the Father , and the Father in me ? The words that I say to you I do not speak on my own authority ; but the Father who dwells in me does his works .
43014011	Believe me that I am in the Father and the Father in me ; or else believe me for the sake of the works themselves .
43014012	Truly , truly , I say to you , he who believes in me will also do the works that I do ; and greater works than these will he do , because I go to the Father .
43014013	And whatever you ask in my name , I will do , that the Father may be glorified in the Son .
43014014	If you ask anything in my name , I will do it .
43014015	» If you love me , you will keep my commandments .
43014016	And I will ask the Father , and he will give you another Counselor , to be with you forever –
43014017	the Spirit of truth , whom the world cannot receive , because it neither sees him nor knows him ; but you know him , for he dwells with you and will be in you .
43014018	I will not leave you orphans ; I will come to you .
43014019	A little while longer , and the world will see me no more , but you will see me . Because I live , you will live also .
43014020	In that day you will know that I am in my Father , and you in me , and I in you .
43014021	He who has my commandments and keeps them , it is he who loves me . And he who loves me will be loved by my Father , and I will love him and manifest myself to him . «
43014022	Judas ( not Iscariot ) said to him , » Lord , how is it that you will manifest yourself to us , and not to the world ? «
43014023	Jesus answered him , » If anyone loves me , he will keep my word , and my Father will love him , and we will come to him and make our home with him .
43014024	He who does not love me does not keep my words ; and the word which you hear is not mine but the Father's who sent me .
43014025	» These things I have spoken to you , while I am still with you .
43014026	But the Counselor , the Holy Spirit , whom the Father will send in my name , he will teach you all things , and bring to your remembrance all that I have said to you .
43014027	Peace I leave with you ; my peace I give to you ; not as the world gives do I give to you . Let not your hearts be troubled , neither let them be afraid .
43014028	You have heard me say to you , ‘ I am going away and coming back to you . ’ If you loved me , you would rejoice because I said , ‘ I am going to the Father , ’ for the Father is greater than I .
43014029	And now I have told you before it takes place , so that when it does take place , you may believe .
43014030	I will no longer talk much with you , for the ruler of this world is coming , and he has nothing in me .
43014031	But I do as the Father commanded me , so that the world may know that I love the Father . Rise , let us go from here .
43015001	» I am the true vine , and my Father is the vinedresser .
43015002	Every branch in me that bears no fruit he takes away ; and every branch that does bear fruit he prunes , so that it may bear more fruit .
43015003	You are already clean because of the word which I have spoken to you .
43015004	Abide in me , and I in you . As the branch cannot bear fruit by itself , unless it abides in the vine , neither can you , unless you abide in me .
43015005	I am the vine , you are the branches . He who abides in me , and I in him , he bears much fruit ; for apart from me you can do nothing .
43015006	If anyone does not abide in me , he is like a branch that is cast away and withers ; and the branches are gathered , thrown into the fire and burned .
43015007	If you abide in me , and my words abide in you , ask whatever you will , and it shall be done for you .
43015008	By this my Father is glorified , that you bear much fruit , and so prove to be my disciples .
43015009	As the Father has loved me , I also have loved you ; abide in my love .
43015010	If you keep my commandments , you will abide in my love , just as I have kept my Father's commandments and abide in his love .
43015011	» These things I have spoken to you , that my joy may be in you , and that your joy may be full .
43015012	This is my commandment , that you love one another as I have loved you .
43015013	Greater love has no one than this , that he lay down his life for his friends .
43015014	You are my friends if you do what I command you .
43015015	No longer do I call you servants , for a servant does not know what his master is doing ; but I have called you friends , for all that I have heard from my Father I have made known to you .
43015016	You did not choose me , but I chose you and appointed you that you should go and bear fruit , and that your fruit should remain , that whatever you ask the Father in my name he may give you .
43015017	This I command you , that you love one another .
43015018	» If the world hates you , know that it hated me before it hated you .
43015019	If you were of the world , the world would love its own . But because you are not of the world , but I chose you out of the world , therefore the world hates you .
43015020	Remember the word that I said to you , ‘ A servant is not greater than his master . ’ If they persecuted me , they will also persecute you . If they kept my word , they will keep yours also .
43015021	But all this they will do to you for my name's sake , because they do not know him who sent me .
43015022	If I had not come and spoken to them , they would not have sin , but now they have no excuse for their sin .
43015023	He who hates me hates my Father also .
43015024	If I had not done among them the works which no one else did , they would not have sin ; but now they have seen and hated both me and my Father .
43015025	But this is to fulfill the word that is written in their law , ‘ They hated me without a cause . ’
43015026	» But when the Counselor comes , whom I shall send to you from the Father , the Spirit of truth who proceeds from the Father , he will testify of me .
43015027	And you also will bear witness , because you have been with me from the beginning .
43016001	» I have said all this to you so that you will not go astray .
43016002	They will put you out of the synagogues ; yes , the time is coming when whoever kills you will think he is offering service to God .
43016003	And they will do these things because they have not known the Father , nor me .
43016004	But I have told you these things , that when the time comes , you may remember that I told you of them . » I did not say these things to you at the beginning , because I was with you .
43016005	But now I am going to him who sent me , yet none of you asks me , ‘ Where are you going ? ’
43016006	But because I have said these things to you , sorrow has filled your heart .
43016007	Nevertheless I tell you the truth : it is to your advantage that I go away . For if I do not go away , the Counselor will not come to you ; but if I go , I will send him to you .
43016008	And when he comes , he will convict the world of sin , and of righteousness , and of judgment :
43016009	of sin , because they do not believe in me ;
43016010	of righteousness , because I go to the Father , and you see me no more ;
43016011	of judgment , because the ruler of this world is judged .
43016012	» I have many more things to say to you , but you cannot bear them now .
43016013	But when he , the Spirit of truth , comes , he will guide you into all truth ; for he will not speak on his own authority , but whatever he hears he will speak ; and he will tell you things to come .
43016014	He will glorify me , for he will take of what is mine and declare it to you .
43016015	All that the Father has is mine . Therefore I said that he will take of what is mine and declare it to you .
43016016	» A little while , and you will see me no more ; again a little while , and you will see me . «
43016017	Then some of his disciples said to one another , » What is this that he says to us , ‘ A little while , and you will not see me , and again a little while , and you will see me ’ ; and , ‘ because I go to the Father ’ ? «
43016018	They said , » What does he mean by ‘ a little while ’ ? We do not know what he is saying . «
43016019	Now Jesus knew that they wanted to ask him , so he said to them , » Are you asking yourselves about what I meant when I said , ‘ A little while , and you will not see me ; and again a little while , and you will see me ’ ?
43016020	Truly , truly , I say to you , you will weep and lament , but the world will rejoice ; you will be sorrowful , but your sorrow will turn into joy .
43016021	When a woman is in labor she has sorrow , because her hour has come ; but as soon as she gives birth to the child , she no longer remembers the anguish , for joy that a child has been born into the world .
43016022	So you have sorrow now , but I will see you again and your heart will rejoice , and no one will take your joy from you .
43016023	In that day you will ask me nothing . Truly , truly , I say to you , whatever you ask the Father in my name he will give you .
43016024	Until now you have asked nothing in my name . Ask , and you will receive , that your joy may be full .
43016025	» I have said this to you in figurative language ; but the time is coming when I will no longer speak to you in figures , but I will tell you plainly about the Father .
43016026	In that day you will ask in my name . And I do not say to you that I shall pray the Father for you ;
43016027	for the Father himself loves you , because you have loved me and have believed that I came from God .
43016028	I came from the Father and have come into the world ; again , I am leaving the world and going to the Father . «
43016029	His disciples said , » See , now you are speaking plainly , and not using a figure of speech !
43016030	Now we are sure that you know all things , and have no need for anyone to question you . By this we believe that you came from God . «
43016031	Jesus answered them , » Do you now believe ?
43016032	Indeed the hour is coming , yes , has now come , when you will be scattered , each to his own , and will leave me alone . And yet I am not alone , for the Father is with me .
43016033	I have said these things to you , that in me you may have peace . In the world you will have tribulation . But take courage ! I have overcome the world . «
43017001	When Jesus had spoken these words , he lifted up his eyes to heaven , and said : » Father , the hour has come . Glorify your Son , that your Son also may glorify you ,
43017002	as you have given him authority over all flesh , that he should give eternal life to all those you have given him .
43017003	And this is eternal life , that they may know you , the only true God , and Jesus Christ whom you have sent .
43017004	I have glorified you on the earth , having finished the work which you have given me to do .
43017005	And now , Father , glorify me in your own presence with the glory which I had with you before the world was made .
43017006	» I have manifested your name to the men whom you have given me out of the world . They were yours ; you gave them to me , and they have kept your word .
43017007	Now they know that everything you have given me comes from you .
43017008	For I have given them the words which you have given me , and they have received them and know in truth that I came from you ; and they have believed that you sent me .
43017009	I pray for them . I am not praying for the world , but for those whom you have given me , for they are yours .
43017010	And all mine are yours , and yours are mine , and I am glorified in them .
43017011	And now I am no longer in the world , but they are in the world , and I am coming to you . Holy Father , keep them in your name – the name you gave me – that they may be one , even as we are one .
43017012	While I was with them , I kept them in your name – the name you gave me . I have guarded them , and none of them is lost except the son of perdition , that the Scripture might be fulfilled .
43017013	But now I am coming to you , and these things I speak in the world , that they may have my joy fulfilled in themselves .
43017014	I have given them your word ; and the world has hated them because they are not of the world , even as I am not of the world .
43017015	I do not pray that you should take them out of the world , but that you should keep them from the evil one .
43017016	They are not of the world , even as I am not of the world .
43017017	Sanctify them by the truth ; your word is truth .
43017018	As you sent me into the world , I also have sent them into the world .
43017019	And for their sakes I sanctify myself , that they also may be sanctified in truth .
43017020	» I do not pray for these alone , but also for those who will believe in me through their word ;
43017021	that they all may be one , as you , Father , are in me , and I in you ; that they also may be in us , that the world may believe that you sent me .
43017022	And the glory which you gave me I have given them , that they may be one just as we are one :
43017023	I in them , and you in me ; that they may become perfectly one , and that the world may know that you have sent me , and have loved them even as you have loved me .
43017024	Father , I desire that they also whom you have given me may be with me where I am , that they may behold my glory which you have given me , for you loved me before the foundation of the world .
43017025	O righteous Father , the world has not known you , but I have known you ; and these know that you sent me .
43017026	I have made known to them your name , and will make it known , that the love with which you loved me may be in them , and I in them . «
43018001	When Jesus had spoken these words , he went out with his disciples over the Kidron valley , where there was a garden , which he and his disciples entered .
43018002	Now Judas , who betrayed him , also knew the place ; for Jesus often met there with his disciples .
43018003	So Judas , having received a detachment of soldiers and some officers from the chief priests and the Pharisees , came there with lanterns , torches , and weapons .
43018004	Then Jesus , knowing all that was to come upon him , went forward and said to them , » Whom do you seek ? «
43018005	They answered him , » Jesus of Nazareth . « Jesus said to them , » I am he . « And Judas , who betrayed him , was standing with them .
43018006	When he said to them , » I am he , « they drew back and fell to the ground .
43018007	Again he asked them , » Whom do you seek ? « And they said , » Jesus of Nazareth . «
43018008	Jesus answered , » I told you that I am he . So , if you seek me , let these men go . «
43018009	This happened so that the words which he had spoken would be fulfilled , » Of those whom you gave me I have lost none . «
43018010	Then Simon Peter , having a sword , drew it and struck the high priest’s servant , and cut off his right ear . The servant’s name was Malchus .
43018011	Jesus said to Peter , » Put your sword into its sheath ; shall I not drink the cup which the Father has given me ? «
43018012	Then the detachment of soldiers and their captain and the officers of the Jews arrested Jesus and bound him .
43018013	And they led him to Annas first ; for he was the father-in-law of Caiaphas , who was high priest that year .
43018014	Now it was Caiaphas who had advised the Jews that it was expedient that one man should die for the people .
43018015	Simon Peter followed Jesus , and so did another disciple . As this disciple was known to the high priest , he went with Jesus into the courtyard of the high priest .
43018016	But Peter stood at the door outside . Then the other disciple , who was known to the high priest , went out and spoke to the girl who kept the door , and brought Peter in .
43018017	Then the girl who kept the door said to Peter , » You are not also one of this man’s disciples , are you ? « He said , » I am not . «
43018018	Now the servants and officers had made a charcoal fire , because it was cold , and they were standing and warming themselves . Peter also was with them , standing and warming himself .
43018019	The high priest then questioned Jesus about his disciples and his teaching .
43018020	Jesus answered him , » I have spoken openly to the world . I always taught in synagogues and in the temple , where all the Jews come together , and I have said nothing in secret .
43018021	Why do you ask me ? Ask those who have heard me what I said to them . They know what I said . «
43018022	And when he had said this , one of the officers standing by struck Jesus with his hand , saying , » Is that the way you answer the high priest ? «
43018023	Jesus answered him , » If I have spoken wrongly , bear witness to the wrong ; but if I have spoken rightly , why do you strike me ? «
43018024	Then Annas sent him bound to Caiaphas the high priest .
43018025	Now Simon Peter stood warming himself . Therefore they said to him , » You are not also one of his disciples , are you ? « He denied it and said , » I am not . «
43018026	One of the servants of the high priest , a relative of him whose ear Peter had cut off , said , » Did I not see you in the garden with him ? «
43018027	Peter again denied it ; and at once a rooster crowed .
43018028	Then they led Jesus from Caiaphas to the Praetorium , and it was early morning . But they did not enter the Praetorium themselves , so that they might not be defiled , but might eat the Passover .
43018029	So Pilate went out to them and said , » What accusation do you bring against this man ? «
43018030	They answered him , » If he were not an evildoer , we would not have handed him over to you . «
43018031	Pilate said to them , » Take him yourselves and judge him by your own law . « The Jews said to him , » It is not lawful for us to put anyone to death . «
43018032	This happened so that the words Jesus had spoken would be fulfilled , showing by what death he was going to die .
43018033	Then Pilate entered the Praetorium again , called Jesus , and said to him , » Are you the King of the Jews ? «
43018034	Jesus answered , » Do you say this on your own , or did others say it to you about me ? «
43018035	Pilate answered , » Am I a Jew ? Your own nation and the chief priests have handed you over to me ; what have you done ? «
43018036	Jesus answered , » My kingdom is not of this world . If my kingdom were of this world , my servants would fight , so that I should not be delivered to the Jews ; but now my kingship is not from here . «
43018037	Pilate said to him , » You are a king then ? « Jesus answered , » You say what I am — a king . For this I was born , and for this I have come into the world , to bear witness to the truth . Everyone who is of the truth hears my voice . «
43018038	Pilate said to him , » What is truth ? « After he had said this , he went out to the Jews again , and told them , » I find no crime in him .
43018039	But you have a custom that I should release one man for you at the Passover . So do you want me to release to you the King of the Jews ? «
43018040	Then they all cried again , » Not this man , but Barabbas ! « Now Barabbas was a robber .
43019001	So then Pilate took Jesus and scourged him .
43019002	And the soldiers twisted a crown of thorns and put it on his head , and they clothed him in a purple robe .
43019003	They came up to him , saying , » Hail , King of the Jews ! « and struck him with their hands .
43019004	Pilate went out again , and said to them , » See , I am bringing him out to you , that you may know that I find no crime in him . «
43019005	So Jesus came out , wearing the crown of thorns and the purple robe . Pilate said to them , » Behold the man ! «
43019006	When the chief priests and officers saw him , they cried out , » Crucify him , crucify him ! « Pilate said to them , » You take him and crucify him , for I find no fault in him . «
43019007	The Jews answered him , » We have a law , and according to that law he ought to die , because he made himself the Son of God . «
43019008	When Pilate heard these words , he was the more afraid ,
43019009	and he went again into the Praetorium and said to Jesus , » Where are you from ? « But Jesus gave him no answer .
43019010	Pilate said to him , » You will not speak to me ? Do you not know that I have power to release you , and power to crucify you ? «
43019011	Jesus answered , » You would have no power over me unless it had been given you from above . Therefore the one who delivered me to you has the greater sin . «
43019012	From then on Pilate sought to release him , but the Jews cried out , » If you let this man go , you are not Caesar’s friend . Anyone who makes himself a king sets himself against Caesar . «
43019013	When Pilate heard these words , he brought Jesus out , and sat down on the judgment seat at a place that is called The Pavement , but in Hebrew , Gabbatha .
43019014	Now it was the day of Preparation of the Passover , about the sixth hour . And he said to the Jews , » Behold your King ! «
43019015	But they cried out , » Away with him ! Away with him ! Crucify him ! « Pilate said to them , » Shall I crucify your King ? « The chief priests answered , » We have no King but Caesar . «
43019016	Then he handed him over to them to be crucified . So they took Jesus .
43019017	And he , bearing his cross , went out to a place called the Place of the Skull , which is called in Hebrew , Golgotha .
43019018	There they crucified him , and two others with him , one on either side , and Jesus in the center .
43019019	Pilate wrote a title and put it on the cross . It read : JESUS OF NAZARETH , THE KING OF THE JEWS .
43019020	Many of the Jews read this title , for the place where Jesus was crucified was near the city ; and it was written in Hebrew , Greek , and Latin .
43019021	The chief priests of the Jews then said to Pilate , » Do not write , ‘ The King of the Jews , ’ but , ‘ This man said , I am King of the Jews . ’ «
43019022	Pilate answered , » What I have written , I have written . «
43019023	When the soldiers had crucified Jesus , they took his garments , and made four parts , one for each soldier , and also his tunic . Now the tunic was without seam , woven in one piece from top to bottom .
43019024	So they said to one another , » Let us not tear it , but cast lots for it , whose it shall be . « This happened that the Scripture might be fulfilled which says : » They divided my garments among them , and for my clothing they cast lots . « This is what the soldiers did .
43019025	By the cross of Jesus stood his mother , and his mother's sister , Mary the wife of Clopas , and Mary Magdalene .
43019026	When Jesus saw his mother , and the disciple whom he loved standing by , he said to his mother , » Woman , behold your son ! «
43019027	Then he said to the disciple , » Behold , your mother ! « And from that hour the disciple took her to his own home .
43019028	After this , Jesus , knowing that all was now accomplished , that the Scripture might be fulfilled , said , » I thirst . «
43019029	Now a vessel full of wine vinegar was sitting there ; so they filled a sponge with the vinegar , put it on hyssop , and put it to his mouth .
43019030	So when Jesus had received the vinegar , he said , » It is finished ! « And he bowed his head and gave up his spirit .
43019031	Therefore , because it was the day of Preparation , that the bodies should not remain on the cross on the Sabbath ( for that Sabbath was a high day ) , the Jews asked Pilate that their legs might be broken , and that they might be taken away .
43019032	Then the soldiers came and broke the legs of the first , and of the other who had been crucified with him .
43019033	But when they came to Jesus and saw that he was already dead , they did not break his legs .
43019034	But one of the soldiers pierced his side with a spear , and immediately blood and water came out .
43019035	He who saw it has testified , and his testimony is true , and he knows that he tells the truth , that you also may believe .
43019036	For these things were done that the scripture should be fulfilled , » Not one of his bones shall be broken . «
43019037	And again another scripture says , » They shall look on him whom they have pierced . «
43019038	After this Joseph of Arimathea , who was a disciple of Jesus , but secretly , for fear of the Jews , asked Pilate that he might take away the body of Jesus , and Pilate gave him permission . So he came and took away his body .
43019039	And Nicodemus , who had at first come to Jesus by night , also came , bringing a mixture of myrrh and aloes , about a hundred pounds .
43019040	So they took the body of Jesus , and bound it in strips of linen with the spices , as is the burial custom of the Jews .
43019041	Now in the place where he was crucified there was a garden , and in the garden a new tomb in which no one had ever been laid .
43019042	So because of the Jewish day of Preparation , as the tomb was nearby , they laid Jesus there .
43020001	On the first day of the week Mary Magdalene went to the tomb early , while it was still dark , and saw that the stone had been taken away from the tomb .
43020002	So she ran , and came to Simon Peter and the other disciple , the one whom Jesus loved , and said to them , » They have taken the Lord out of the tomb , and we do not know where they have laid him . «
43020003	Peter therefore went out with the other disciple , and they were going toward the tomb .
43020004	They both ran , but the other disciple outran Peter and reached the tomb first .
43020005	And stooping to look in , he saw the linen cloths lying there , but he did not go in .
43020006	Then Simon Peter came , following him , and went into the tomb ; and he saw the linen cloths lying there ,
43020007	and the napkin that had been around his head , not lying with the linen cloths , but folded up in a place by itself .
43020008	Then the other disciple , who reached the tomb first , also went in ; and he saw and believed .
43020009	For as yet they did not know the Scripture , that he must rise from the dead .
43020010	Then the disciples went back to their homes .
43020011	But Mary stood weeping outside the tomb , and as she wept she stooped to look into the tomb .
43020012	And she saw two angels in white , sitting where the body of Jesus had lain , one at the head and the other at the feet .
43020013	They said to her , » Woman , why are you weeping ? « She said to them , » Because they have taken away my Lord , and I do not know where they have laid him . «
43020014	Saying this , she turned around and saw Jesus standing there , but she did not know that it was Jesus .
43020015	Jesus said to her , » Woman , why are you weeping ? Whom are you seeking ? « Supposing him to be the gardener , she said to him , » Sir , if you have carried him away , tell me where you have laid him , and I will take him away . «
43020016	Jesus said to her , » Mary ! « She turned and said to him in Hebrew , » Rabboni ! « ( which means , Teacher ) .
43020017	Jesus said to her , » Do not hold me , for I have not yet ascended to the Father ; but go to my brethren and say to them , » I am ascending to my Father and your Father , to my God and your God . ’ «
43020018	Mary Magdalene went and said to the disciples , » I have seen the Lord ! « And she told them that he had said these things to her .
43020019	On the evening of that day , the first day of the week , the doors being shut where the disciples were , for fear of the Jews , Jesus came and stood among them and said to them , » Peace be with you . «
43020020	When he had said this , he showed them his hands and his side . Then the disciples were glad when they saw the Lord .
43020021	Jesus said to them again , » Peace be with you ! As the Father has sent me , I also send you . «
43020022	And when he had said this , he breathed on them , and said to them , » Receive the Holy Spirit .
43020023	If you forgive the sins of any , they are forgiven them ; if you retain the sins of any , they are retained . «
43020024	Now Thomas , one of the twelve , called the Twin , was not with them when Jesus came .
43020025	So the other disciples told him , » We have seen the Lord . « But he said to them , » Unless I see in his hands the print of the nails , and put my finger in the mark of the nails , and put my hand in his side , I will not believe . «
43020026	Eight days later , his disciples were again in the house , and Thomas was with them . The doors were shut , but Jesus came and stood among them , and said , » Peace be with you ! «
43020027	Then he said to Thomas , » Put your finger here , and see my hands . Reach out your hand , and put it into my side ; do not be unbelieving , but believing . «
43020028	Thomas answered him , » My Lord and my God ! «
43020029	Jesus said to him , » Have you believed because you have seen me ? Blessed are those who have not seen and yet have believed . «
43020030	Jesus did many other signs in the presence of his disciples , which are not written in this book ;
43020031	but these are written that you may believe that Jesus is the Christ , the Son of God , and that believing you may have life in his name .
43021001	After this Jesus showed himself again to the disciples by the Sea of Tiberias , and in this way he showed himself :
43021002	Simon Peter , Thomas called the Twin , Nathanael of Cana in Galilee , the sons of Zebedee , and two others of his disciples were together .
43021003	Simon Peter said to them , » I am going fishing . « They said to him , » We will go with you . « They went out and got into the boat ; but that night they caught nothing .
43021004	But early in the morning , Jesus stood on the shore ; yet the disciples did not know that it was Jesus .
43021005	Jesus said to them , » Children , have you any fish ? « They answered him , » No . «
43021006	He said to them , » Cast the net on the right side of the boat , and you will find some . « So they cast , and now they were not able to haul it in because of the great number of fish .
43021007	Then that disciple whom Jesus loved said to Peter , » It is the Lord ! « Now when Simon Peter heard that it was the Lord , he put on his outer garment ( for he had removed it ) , and threw himself into the sea .
43021008	But the other disciples came in the boat , dragging the net full of fish , for they were not far from land , but about a hundred yards off .
43021009	When they had come to land , they saw a fire of coals there , with fish lying on it , and bread .
43021010	Jesus said to them , » Bring some of the fish you have just caught . «
43021011	Simon Peter went aboard and dragged the net ashore , full of large fish , one hundred and fifty-three ; and although there were so many , the net was not torn .
43021012	Jesus said to them , » Come and have breakfast . « Now none of the disciples dared ask him , » Who are you ? « They knew it was the Lord .
43021013	Jesus came and took the bread and gave it to them , and did the same with the fish .
43021014	This was now the third time Jesus appeared to his disciples after he was raised from the dead .
43021015	When they had finished breakfast , Jesus said to Simon Peter , » Simon , son of John , do you love me more than these ? « He said to him , » Yes , Lord ; you know that I love you . « He said to him , » Feed my lambs . «
43021016	He said to him again a second time , » Simon , son of John , do you love me ? « He said to him , » Yes , Lord ; you know that I love you . « He said to him , » Tend my sheep . «
43021017	He said to him the third time , » Simon , son of John , do you love me ? « Peter was grieved because he said to him the third time , » Do you love me ? « And he said to him , » Lord , you know all things ; you know that I love you . « Jesus said to him , » Feed my sheep .
43021018	Truly , truly , I say to you , when you were younger , you girded yourself and walked where you wished ; but when you are old , you will stretch out your hands , and another will gird you and carry you where you do not wish to go . «
43021019	This he said to show by what death he would glorify God . And after this he said to him , » Follow me . «
43021020	Peter turned and saw following them the disciple whom Jesus loved , who had leaned on his breast at the supper and had said , » Lord , who is the one who is going to betray you ? «
43021021	When Peter saw him , he said to Jesus , » Lord , what about this man ? «
43021022	Jesus said to him , » If I want him to remain until I come , what is that to you ? You follow me . «
43021023	Then the saying spread among the brethren that this disciple would not die . Yet Jesus did not say to him that he would not die , but , » If I want him to remain until I come , what is that to you ? «
43021024	This is the disciple who testifies to these things , and who wrote these things ; and we know that his testimony is true .
43021025	But there are also many other things which Jesus did . If every one of them were to be written , I suppose that even the world itself could not contain the books that would be written .
44001001	In the first book , O Theophilus , I wrote about all that Jesus began to do and to teach ,
44001002	until the day when he was taken up to heaven , after he had given orders through the Holy Spirit to the apostles whom he had chosen .
44001003	To these he also presented himself alive after his suffering , by many convincing proofs , appearing to them over a period of forty days and speaking of the things concerning the kingdom of God .
44001004	And while staying with them , he commanded them not to leave Jerusalem , but to wait for what the Father had promised , » Which , « he said , » you heard of from me ;
44001005	for John baptized with water , but before many days you will be baptized with the Holy Spirit . «
44001006	So when they had come together , they asked him , » Lord , are you at this time going to restore the kingdom to Israel ? «
44001007	He said to them , » It is not for you to know times or seasons which the Father has fixed by his own authority .
44001008	But you will receive power when the Holy Spirit has come upon you ; and you shall be my witnesses both in Jerusalem , and in all Judea and Samaria , and even to the ends of the earth . «
44001009	And after he had said this , as they were looking on , he was lifted up , and a cloud took him out of their sight .
44001010	And as they were gazing intently into the sky while he was going , behold , two men in white clothing stood beside them .
44001011	They also said , » Men of Galilee , why do you stand looking into the sky ? This Jesus , who has been taken up from you into heaven , will come in just the same way as you have watched him go into heaven . «
44001012	Then they returned to Jerusalem from the mount called Olivet , which is near Jerusalem , a Sabbath day's journey away .
44001013	And when they had entered , they went up to the upper room , where they were staying ; Peter and John and James and Andrew , Philip and Thomas , Bartholomew and Matthew , James the son of Alphaeus and Simon the Zealot and Judas the son of James .
44001014	All these with one mind devoted themselves to prayer , along with the women and Mary the mother of Jesus , and with his brothers .
44001015	In those days Peter stood up among the brethren ( the company of persons was in all about a hundred and twenty ) , and said ,
44001016	» Brethren , the scripture had to be fulfilled , which the Holy Spirit spoke beforehand by the mouth of David , concerning Judas who was guide to those who arrested Jesus .
44001017	For he was counted among us and received his share in this ministry . «
44001018	( Now this man bought a field with the reward of his wickedness ; and falling headlong , he burst open in the middle and all his intestines gushed out .
44001019	And it became known to all the inhabitants of Jerusalem , so that the field was called in their language Akeldama , that is , Field of Blood . )
44001020	For it is written in the book of Psalms , ‘ Let his homestead be made desolate , and let there be no one to dwell in it ’ ; and , ‘ let another man take his office . ’
44001021	Therefore it is necessary that of the men who have accompanied us all the time that the Lord Jesus went in and out among us ,
44001022	beginning from the baptism of John until the day when he was taken up from us — one of these men must become with us a witness to his resurrection . «
44001023	So they put forward two men , Joseph called Barsabbas ( who was also called Justus ) , and Matthias .
44001024	And they prayed and said , » You , Lord , who know the hearts of all men , show which one of these two you have chosen
44001025	to take the place in this ministry and apostleship from which Judas turned aside , to go to his own place . «
44001026	And they cast lots for them , and the lot fell to Matthias ; and he was added to the eleven apostles .
44002001	When the day of Pentecost had come , they were all together in one place .
44002002	And suddenly there came from heaven a sound like the rush of a violent wind , and it filled the whole house where they were sitting .
44002003	And there appeared to them tongues as of fire distributing themselves , and they rested on each one of them .
44002004	And they were all filled with the Holy Spirit and began to speak in other tongues , as the Spirit gave them utterance .
44002005	Now there were Jews living in Jerusalem , devout men from every nation under heaven .
44002006	And at this sound the crowd came together , and they were bewildered , because each one heard them speaking in his own language .
44002007	They were amazed and wondered , saying , » Are not all these who are speaking Galileans ?
44002008	And how is it that we hear them , each of us in his own native language ?
44002009	Parthians and Medes and Elamites , and residents of Mesopotamia , Judea and Cappadocia , Pontus and Asia ,
44002010	Phrygia and Pamphylia , Egypt and the parts of Libya around Cyrene , and visitors from Rome , both Jews and proselytes ,
44002011	Cretans and Arabs — we hear them in our own tongues speaking of the mighty deeds of God . «
44002012	And they were all amazed and perplexed , saying to one another , » What does this mean ? «
44002013	But others were mocking and said , » They are full of sweet wine . «
44002014	But Peter , taking his stand with the eleven , raised his voice and addressed them : » Men of Judea and all you who live in Jerusalem , let this be known to you and give heed to my words .
44002015	For these men are not drunk , as you suppose , since it is only the third hour of the day ;
44002016	but this is what was spoken by the prophet Joel :
44002017
