44002019	
44002020	
44002021	
44002022	» Men of Israel , listen to these words : Jesus of Nazareth , a man attested to you by God with miracles and wonders and signs which God did through him in your midst , as you yourselves know —
44002023	this man , delivered over by the predetermined plan and foreknowledge of God , you nailed to a cross by the hands of godless men and put him to death .
44002024	But God raised him up , having loosed the agony of death , because it was impossible for him to be held in its power .
44002025	For David says concerning him , ‘ I saw the Lord always before me ; for he is at my right hand , so that I will not be shaken .
44002026	
44002027	
44002028	
44002029	» Brethren , I may say to you confidently of the patriarch David that he both died and was buried , and his tomb is with us to this day .
44002030	And so , because he was a prophet , and knew that God had sworn with an oath to him that he would set one of his descendants on his throne ,
44002031	he looked ahead and spoke of the resurrection of the Christ , that he was not abandoned to hades , nor did his flesh see decay .
44002032	This Jesus God raised up again , and of that we are all witnesses .
44002033	Being therefore exalted at the right hand of God , and having received from the Father the promise of the Holy Spirit , he has poured out this which you see and hear .

44002035

44002037	Now when they heard this they were cut to the heart , and said to Peter and the rest of the apostles , » Brethren , what shall we do ? «
44002038	And Peter said to them , » Repent , and be baptized every one of you in the name of Jesus Christ for the forgiveness of your sins ; and you will receive the gift of the Holy Spirit .
44002039	For the promise is for you and your children and for all who are far off , for all whom the Lord our God will call to himself . «
44002040	And he testified with many other words and exhorted them , saying , » Save yourselves from this perverse generation . «
44002041	So those who received his word were baptized , and there were added that day about three thousand souls .
44002042	They devoted themselves to the apostles' teaching and to the fellowship , to the breaking of bread and to prayer .
44002043	Everyone was filled with awe ; and many wonders and signs were done through the apostles .
44002044	And all who believed were together and had all things in common ;
44002045	and they sold their possessions and goods and distributed them to all , as anyone had need .
44002046	And day by day , attending the temple together and breaking bread in their homes , they ate together with glad and sincere hearts ,
44002047	praising God and having favor with all the people . And the Lord added to their number day by day those who were being saved .
44003001	Now Peter and John were going up to the temple at the hour of prayer , the ninth hour .
44003002	And a man lame from birth was being carried , whom they set down every day at the gate of the temple which is called Beautiful to beg alms of those who entered the temple .
44003003	When he saw Peter and John about to go into the temple , he asked for alms .
44003004	And Peter , along with John , directed his gaze at him , and said , » Look at us . «
44003005	And he gave them his attention , expecting to receive something from them .
44003006	But Peter said , » I do not have silver and gold , but I give you what I have ; in the name of Jesus Christ of Nazareth , walk . «
44003007	And taking him by the right hand , he raised him up ; and immediately his feet and ankles were made strong .
44003008	With a leap he stood upright and began to walk ; and he entered the temple with them , walking and leaping and praising God .
44003009	And all the people saw him walking and praising God ,
44003010	and they recognized him as the one who used to sit at the Beautiful Gate of the temple to beg alms , and they were filled with wonder and amazement at what had happened to him .
44003011	While he clung to Peter and John , all the people ran together to them in the porch called Solomon's , astounded .
44003012	And when Peter saw this he addressed the people , » Men of Israel , why do you wonder at this , or why do you stare at us , as if by our own power or piety we had made him walk ?
44003013	The God of Abraham , Isaac and Jacob , the God of our fathers , has glorified his servant Jesus , the one whom you delivered and disowned in the presence of Pilate , when he had decided to release him .
44003014	But you disowned the Holy and Righteous One and asked for a murderer to be granted to you ,
44003015	but killed the Author of life , whom God raised from the dead . To this we are witnesses .
44003016	And his name , by faith in his name , has made this man strong whom you see and know ; and the faith which comes through Jesus has given him perfect health in the presence of you all .
44003017	And now , brethren , I know that you acted in ignorance , as did also your rulers .
44003018	But what God foretold by the mouth of all the prophets , that his Christ would suffer , he thus fulfilled .
44003019	Repent therefore , and turn again , so that your sins may be wiped out , that times of refreshing may come from the presence of the Lord ,
44003020	and that he may send the Christ appointed for you , Jesus ,
44003021	whom heaven must receive until the time for establishing all that God spoke by the mouth of his holy prophets from long ago .
44003022	Moses said , ‘ The Lord God will raise up for you a prophet like me from your brethren ; you shall listen to everything he tells you .
44003023	And it shall be that every soul that does not listen to that prophet will be destroyed from among the people . ’
44003024	And likewise , all the prophets who have spoken , from Samuel and those who came afterwards , also announced these days .
44003025	You are the sons of the prophets and of the covenant which God made with your fathers , saying to Abraham , ‘ And in your seed all the families of the earth shall be blessed . ’
44003026	For you first , God raised up his servant and sent him to bless you by turning every one of you from your wicked ways . «
44004001	And as they were speaking to the people , the priests and the captain of the temple guard and the Sadducees came up to them ,
44004002	being greatly disturbed because they were teaching the people and proclaiming in Jesus the resurrection from the dead .
44004003	And they seized them and put them in jail until the next day , for it was already evening .
44004004	But many of those who heard the message believed ; and the number of the men came to about five thousand .
44004005	On the next day , their rulers and elders and scribes were gathered together in Jerusalem ;
44004006	and Annas the high priest was there , and Caiaphas and John and Alexander , and all who were of the high-priestly family .
44004007	And when they had set them in the midst , they began to inquire , » By what power or by what name did you do this ? «
44004008	Then Peter , filled with the Holy Spirit , said to them , » Rulers of the people and elders ,
44004009	if we are being examined today for a good deed done to a cripple , as to how this man has been healed ,
44004010	be it known to you all , and to all the people of Israel , that by the name of Jesus Christ of Nazareth , whom you crucified , whom God raised from the dead , by him this man stands before you healed .
44004011	He is the stone which was rejected by you , the builders , but which has become the chief cornerstone .
44004012	And there is salvation in no one else , for there is no other name under heaven given among men by which we must be saved . «
44004013	Now when they saw the boldness of Peter and John , and perceived that they were uneducated , common men , they were astonished ; and they recognized that they had been with Jesus .
44004014	And seeing the man who had been healed standing with them , they had nothing to say in reply .
44004015	But when they had ordered them to leave the Council , they conferred with one another ,
44004016	saying , » What shall we do with these men ? For that a noteworthy miracle has been performed through them is apparent to all the inhabitants of Jerusalem , and we cannot deny it .
44004017	But in order that it may spread no further among the people , let us warn them to speak no longer to any one in this name . «
44004018	Then they called them in again and commanded them not to speak or teach at all in the name of Jesus .
44004019	But Peter and John answered them , » Whether it is right in the sight of God to listen to you rather than to God , you must judge ;
44004020	for we cannot stop speaking about what we have seen and heard . «
44004021	And when they had further threatened them , they let them go , finding no way to punish them , because of the people ; for all the people were praising God for what had happened .
44004022	For the man on whom this sign of healing was performed was more than forty years old .
44004023	When they had been released , they went to their own companions and reported all that the chief priests and the elders had said to them .
44004024	And when they heard this , they lifted their voices to God together and said , » Sovereign Lord , it is you who made the heaven and the earth and the sea , and everything in them ,
44004025	who by the Holy Spirit , through the mouth of our father David your servant , said , ‘ Why did the gentiles rage , and the peoples plot futile things ?
44004026	
44004027	For truly in this city there were gathered together against your holy servant Jesus , whom you anointed , both Herod and Pontius Pilate , along with the Gentiles and the peoples of Israel ,
44004028	to do whatever your hand and your plan had predestined to take place .
44004029	And now , Lord , look upon their threats , and grant to your servants to speak your word with all boldness ,
44004030	while you stretch out your hand to heal , and signs and wonders take place through the name of your holy servant Jesus . «
44004031	And when they had prayed , the place where they were gathered together was shaken ; and they were all filled with the Holy Spirit and spoke the word of God with boldness .
44004032	Now the company of those who believed were of one heart and soul , and no one claimed that any of the things which he possessed was his own , but they had everything in common .
44004033	And with great power the apostles gave their testimony to the resurrection of the Lord Jesus , and great grace was upon them all .
44004034	For there was not a needy person among them , For all who were owners of land or houses sold them and brought the proceeds of the sales
44004035	and laid it at the apostles' feet , and it was distributed to each as any had need .
44004036	Thus Joseph who was called by the apostles Barnabas ( which means , Son of Encouragement ) , a Levite , a native of Cyprus ,
44004037	sold a field which he owned , and brought the money and laid it at the apostles' feet .
44005001	But a man named Ananias , with his wife Sapphira , sold a piece of property ,
44005002	and with his wife's full knowledge he kept back some of the money for himself , and brought only a part and laid it at the apostles' feet .
44005003	But Peter said , » Ananias , why has Satan filled your heart to lie to the Holy Spirit and to keep back some of the price of the land ?
44005004	While it remained unsold , did it not remain your own ? And after it was sold , was it not at your disposal ? How is it that you have conceived this deed in your heart ? You have not lied to men but to God . «
44005005	When Ananias heard these words , he fell down and died . And great fear came upon all who heard of it .
44005006	The young men arose and wrapped him up , carried him out , and buried him .
44005007	After an interval of about three hours his wife came in , not knowing what had happened .
44005008	Peter said to her , » Tell me whether you sold the land for such and such a price . « And she said , » Yes , that was the price . «
44005009	Then Peter said to her , » How is it that you have agreed together to test the Spirit of the Lord ? Look , the feet of those who have buried your husband are at the door , and they will carry you out . «
44005010	Immediately she fell down at his feet and died . When the young men came in they found her dead , and they carried her out and buried her beside her husband .
44005011	And great fear came upon the whole church , and upon all who heard of these things .
44005012	Now many signs and wonders were done among the people by the hands of the apostles . And they were all together in Solomon's Porch .
44005013	None of the rest dared join them , but the people held them in high honor .
44005014	And all the more believers in the Lord , multitudes of men and women , were constantly added to their number ,
44005015	so that they even carried out the sick into the streets , and laid them on beds and pallets , so that as Peter came by at least his shadow might fall on some of them .
44005016	The people also gathered from the towns around Jerusalem , bringing the sick and those afflicted with unclean spirits , and they were all healed .
44005017	But the high priest rose up and all who were with him , that is , the party of the Sadducees , and they were filled with jealousy .
44005018	They arrested the apostles and put them in the public jail .
44005019	But during the night an angel of the Lord opened the doors of the prison , and brought them out , and said ,
44005020	» Go , stand and speak to the people in the temple the whole message of this Life . «
44005021	And when they heard this , they entered into the temple about daybreak and began to teach . Now when the high priest and his associates came , they called the Council together , even all the Senate of the sons of Israel , and sent orders to the prison house for them to be brought .
44005022	But when the officers came , they did not find them in the prison , and they returned and reported back ,
44005023	» We found the prison securely locked , and the guards standing at the doors ; but when we opened them , we found no one inside . «
44005024	Now when the captain of the temple guard and the chief priests heard these words , they were much perplexed about them , wondering what would come of this .
44005025	And someone came and told them , » Look ! The men whom you put in prison are standing in the temple and teaching the people . «
44005026	Then the captain went along with the officers and brought them back without violence , for they were afraid of the people , that they might be stoned .
44005027	When they had brought them , they set them before the council . The high priest questioned them ,
44005028	saying , » We gave you strict orders not to teach in this name , and yet , you have filled Jerusalem with your teaching and intend to bring this man's blood upon us . «
44005029	But Peter and the apostles answered , » We must obey God rather than men .
44005030	The God of our fathers raised Jesus — whom you had killed by hanging him on a tree .
44005031	God exalted him to his own right hand as Prince and Savior , to give repentance and forgiveness of sins to Israel .
44005032	We are witnesses of these things , and so is the Holy Spirit , whom God has given to those who obey him . «
44005033	When they heard this , they were furious and wanted to kill them .
44005034	But a Pharisee in the council named Gamaliel , a teacher of the law , held in honor by all the people , stood up and ordered the men to be put outside for a while .
44005035	And he said to them , » Men of Israel , take care what you propose to do with these men .
44005036	For some time ago Theudas rose up , claiming to be somebody , and a group of about four hundred men joined him . But he was killed , and all who followed him were dispersed and came to nothing .
44005037	After this man , Judas the Galilean rose up in the days of the census and drew away some people after him ; he too perished , and all those who followed him were scattered .
44005038	So in the present case I tell you , keep away from these men and let them alone , for if this plan or action is of men , it will fail ;
44005039	but if it is of God , you will not be able to overthrow them ; or else you may even be found fighting against God . «
44005040	So they took his advice , and they called the apostles in and had them flogged . Then they ordered them not to speak in the name of Jesus , and let them go .
44005041	Then they left the presence of the council , rejoicing that they had been counted worthy to suffer dishonor for the name .
44005042	And every day , in the temple and from house to house , they never stopped teaching and preaching Jesus as the Christ .
44006001	Now in those days when the number of disciples was increasing , the Hellenistic Jews among them complained against the native Hebrews because their widows were being overlooked in the daily distribution of food .
44006002	So the twelve summoned the congregation of the disciples and said , » It is not right for us to neglect the word of God in order to serve tables .
44006003	Therefore , brethren , pick out from among you seven men of good reputation , full of the Spirit and of wisdom , whom we may appoint to this duty .
44006004	But we will devote ourselves to prayer and to the ministry of the word . «
44006005	And the statement pleased the whole congregation ; and they chose Stephen , a man full of faith and of the Holy Spirit , and Philip , Prochorus , Nicanor , Timon , Parmenas and Nicolas , a proselyte from Antioch .
44006006	These they set before the apostles , and they prayed and laid their hands on them .
44006007	The word of God increased ; and the number of the disciples multiplied greatly in Jerusalem , and a great many of the priests were obedient to the faith .
44006008	And Stephen , full of grace and power , did great wonders and signs among the people .
44006009	Then some of those who belonged to the synagogue of the Freedmen ( as it was called ) , and of the Cyrenians , and of the Alexandrians , and of those from Cilicia and Asia , arose and disputed with Stephen .
44006010	But they could not stand against the wisdom and the Spirit with which he spoke .
44006011	Then they secretly induced men to say , » We have heard him speak blasphemous words against Moses and against God . «
44006012	They stirred up the people and the elders and the scribes , and they came on him and seized him , and brought him before the council .
44006013	They put forward false witnesses who said , » This man never stops speaking against this holy place , and the law ;
44006014	for we have heard him say that this Jesus of Nazareth will destroy this place , and will change the customs which Moses handed down to us . «
44006015	And fixing their gaze on him , all who were sitting in the Council saw that his face was like the face of an angel .
44007001	The high priest said , » Are these things so ? «
44007002	And he said : » Hear me , brethren and fathers ! The God of glory appeared to our father Abraham when he was in Mesopotamia , before he lived in Haran ,
44007003	and said to him , ‘ Leave your country and your relatives , and go into the land that I will show you . ’
44007004	Then he left the land of the Chaldeans and settled in Haran . From there , after his father died , God had him move to this country in which you are now living .
44007005	But He gave him no inheritance in it , not even a foot of ground , and yet , even though he had no child , he promised that he would give it to him as a possession , and to his descendants after him .
44007006	But God spoke to this effect , that his descendants would be aliens in a foreign land , and that they would be enslaved and mistreated for four hundred years .
44007007	‘ But I will judge the nation which they serve , ’ said God , ‘ and after that they will come out and worship me in this place . ’
44007008	And he gave him the covenant of circumcision . And so Abraham became the father of Isaac , and circumcised him on the eighth day ; and Isaac became the father of Jacob , and Jacob of the twelve patriarchs .
44007009	» And the patriarchs , jealous of Joseph , sold him into Egypt . But God was with him ,
44007010	and rescued him from all his afflictions , and gave him favor and wisdom in the sight of Pharaoh , king of Egypt , and he made him governor over Egypt and all his household .
44007011	Now there came a famine throughout all Egypt and Canaan , and great affliction , and our fathers could find no food .
44007012	But when Jacob heard that there was grain in Egypt , he sent our fathers there the first time .
44007013	At the second visit Joseph made himself known to his brothers , and Joseph's family was made known to Pharaoh .
44007014	Then Joseph sent and called his father Jacob and all his relatives to him , seventy-five persons in all .
44007015	And Jacob went down to Egypt , and there he and our fathers died .
44007016	They were carried back to Shechem and laid in the tomb that Abraham had bought for a sum of money from the sons of Hamor in Shechem .
44007017	» But as the time of the promise drew near , which God had granted to Abraham , the people increased and multiplied in Egypt
44007018	until there arose another king over Egypt who knew nothing about Joseph .
44007019	He dealt craftily with our race and forced our fathers to expose their infants , so that they would not survive .
44007020	At this time Moses was born , and was beautiful before God . And he was brought up for three months in his father's house ;
44007021	and when he was placed outside , Pharaoh's daughter took him and brought him up as her own son .
44007022	Moses was educated in all the wisdom of the Egyptians , and he was mighty in his words and deeds .
44007023	» When he was forty years old , it came into his heart to visit his brethren , the sons of Israel .
44007024	And when he saw one of them being treated unjustly , he defended him and avenged the oppressed by striking down the Egyptian .
44007025	And he supposed that his brethren understood that God was granting them deliverance through him , but they did not understand .
44007026	On the following day he appeared to two of them as they were fighting , and tried to reconcile them , saying , ‘ Men , you are brethren ; why do you wrong each other ? ’
44007027	But the man who was wronging his neighbor pushed him aside , saying , ‘ Who made you a ruler and a judge over us ?
44007028	Do you want to kill me as you killed the Egyptian yesterday ? ’
44007029	At this remark Moses fled , and became an exile in the land of Midian , where he became the father of two sons .
44007030	» After forty years had passed , an angel appeared to him in the wilderness of Mount Sinai , in the flame of a burning bush .
44007031	When Moses saw it , he was amazed at the sight ; and as he approached to look more closely , there came the voice of the Lord :
44007032	‘ I am the God of your fathers , the God of Abraham and Isaac and Jacob . ’ Moses trembled with fear and did not dare to look .
44007033	And the Lord said to him , ‘ Take off the sandals from your feet , for the place where you are standing is holy ground .
44007034	I have certainly seen the oppression of my people in Egypt and have heard their groaning , and I have come down to rescue them . Come now , and I will send you to Egypt . ’
44007035	This Moses whom they rejected , saying , ‘ Who made you a ruler and a judge ? ’ is the one God sent to be both a ruler and a deliverer by the hand of the angel who appeared to him in the bush .
44007036	This man led them out , performing wonders and signs in the land of Egypt and in the Red Sea and in the wilderness for forty years .
44007037	This is the Moses who said to the Israelites , ‘ God will raise up for you a prophet like me from your brethren . ’
44007038	This is he who was in the congregation in the wilderness with the angel who spoke to him at Mount Sinai , and with our fathers ; and he received living oracles to pass on to us .
44007039	But our fathers refused to obey him . Instead , they rejected him and in their hearts turned back to Egypt ,
44007040	saying to Aaron , ‘ Make for us gods who will go before us ; as for this Moses who led us out from the land of Egypt — we do not know what has happened to him . ’
44007041	At that time they made a calf and brought a sacrifice to the idol , and were rejoicing in the works of their hands .
44007042	But God turned away and gave them over to worship the host of heaven , as it is written in the book of the prophets : ‘ Did you offer to me slain beasts and sacrifices , forty years in the wilderness , O house of Israel ?
44007043	
44007044	» Our fathers had the tabernacle of testimony in the wilderness , just as he who spoke to Moses directed him to make it according to the pattern which he had seen .
44007045	And having received it in their turn , our fathers brought it in with Joshua when they took the land from the nations whom God drove out before our fathers . So it was until the time of David ,
44007046	who found favor in God's sight , and asked that he might find a dwelling place for the God of Jacob .
44007047	But it was Solomon who built a house for him .
44007048	However , the Most High does not dwell in houses made by human hands ; as the prophet says :
44007049	
44007050	
44007051	» You stiff-necked people , uncircumcised in heart and ears , you always resist the Holy Spirit . You are doing just as your fathers did .
44007052	Which of the prophets did not your fathers persecute ? And they killed those who announced beforehand the coming of the Righteous One , whom you have now betrayed and murdered ,
44007053	you who received the law as delivered by angels , and yet did not keep it . «
44007054	Now when they heard this they were cut to the heart , and they gnashed their teeth at him .
44007055	But being full of the Holy Spirit , he gazed intently into heaven and saw the glory of God , and Jesus standing at the right hand of God ;
44007056	and he said , » Behold , I see the heavens opened , and the Son of Man standing at the right hand of God . «
44007057	But they cried out with a loud voice , and covered their ears and rushed together upon him with .
44007058	Then they cast him out of the city and began to stone him ; and the witnesses laid down their garments at the feet of a young man named Saul .
44007059	And as they were stoning Stephen , he prayed , » Lord Jesus , receive my spirit . «
44007060	Then he fell on his knees and cried out with a loud voice , » Lord , do not hold this sin against them . « And when he had said this , he fell asleep .
44008001	Saul was consenting to his death . And on that day a great persecution arose against the church in Jerusalem , and they were all scattered throughout the region of Judea and Samaria , except the apostles .
44008002	Devout men buried Stephen , and made great lamentation over him .
44008003	But Saul began ravaging the church , and , entering house after house , he dragged off men and women and put them in prison .
44008004	Now those who had been scattered went about preaching the word .
44008005	Philip went down to a city of Samaria and proclaimed Christ to them .
44008006	The crowds with one accord were giving attention to what was said by Philip , when they heard and saw the signs which he did .
44008007	For unclean spirits , crying with a loud voice , came out of many who were possessed ; and many who were paralyzed and lame were healed .
44008008	So there was much joy in that city .
44008009	Now there was a man named Simon , who had formerly practiced magic in the city and amazed all the people of Samaria . He boasted that he was someone great ,
44008010	and they all , from the least to the greatest , gave attention to him , saying , » This man is what is called the Great Power of God . «
44008011	And they gave heed to him , because for a long time he had amazed them with his magic .
44008012	But when they believed Philip as he preached good news about the kingdom of God and the name of Jesus Christ , they were baptized , both men and women .
44008013	Even Simon himself believed , and after being baptized he continued with Philip . And seeing signs and great miracles performed , he was amazed .
44008014	Now when the apostles in Jerusalem heard that Samaria had received the word of God , they sent them Peter and John ,
44008015	who came down and prayed for them that they might receive the Holy Spirit .
44008016	For he had not yet fallen upon any of them ; they had simply been baptized in the name of the Lord Jesus .
44008017	Then they laid their hands on them , and they received the Holy Spirit .
44008018	Now when Simon saw that the Spirit was given through the laying on of the apostles' hands , he offered them money ,
44008019	saying , » Give me also this power , so that everyone on whom I lay my hands may receive the Holy Spirit . «
44008020	But Peter said to him , » May your silver perish with you , because you thought you could obtain the gift of God with money !
44008021	You have no part or share in this matter , for your heart is not right before God .
44008022	Repent therefore of this wickedness of yours , and pray to the Lord that , if possible , the intent of your heart may be forgiven you .
44008023	For I see that you are in the gall of bitterness and in the bond of iniquity . «
44008024	And Simon answered , » Pray for me to the Lord , so that nothing of what you have said may come upon me . «
44008025	Now when they had testified and spoken the word of the Lord , they returned to Jerusalem , preaching the gospel to many villages of the Samaritans .
44008026	But an angel of the Lord said to Philip , » Get up and go toward the south to the road that goes down from Jerusalem to Gaza . « This is a desert road .
44008027	So he got up and went . And there was an Ethiopian eunuch , a court official of Candace , queen of the Ethiopians , who was in charge of all her treasure ; and he had come to Jerusalem to worship ,
44008028	and he was returning and sitting in his chariot , and was reading the prophet Isaiah .
44008029	And the Spirit said to Philip , » Go up and join this chariot . «
44008030	So Philip ran up to him , and heard him reading Isaiah the prophet , and asked , » Do you understand what you are reading ? «
44008031	And he said , » How can I , unless someone guides me ? « And he invited Philip to come up and sit with him .
44008032	Now the passage of Scripture which he was reading was this : » He was led as a sheep to slaughter ; and as a lamb before its shearer is silent , so he does not open his mouth .
44008033	
44008034	And the eunuch said to Philip , » Please tell me , of whom does the prophet say this , about himself or about someone else ? «
44008035	Then Philip opened his mouth , and beginning with this scripture he told him the good news of Jesus .
44008036	And as they went along the road they came to some water ; and the eunuch said , » Look , here is water ! What prevents me from being baptized ? «
44008038	And he commanded the chariot to stop , and they both went down into the water , Philip and the eunuch , and he baptized him .
44008039	And when they came up out of the water , the Spirit of the Lord snatched Philip away ; and the eunuch saw him no more , but went on his way rejoicing .
44008040	But Philip found himself at Azotus , and as he passed through he kept preaching the gospel to all the towns until he came to Caesarea .
44009001	Now Saul , still breathing threats and murder against the disciples of the Lord , went to the high priest ,
44009002	and asked for letters from him to the synagogues at Damascus , so that if he found any belonging to the Way , both men and women , he might bring them bound to Jerusalem .
44009003	Now as he journeyed he approached Damascus , and suddenly a light from heaven flashed around him .
44009004	And he fell to the ground and heard a voice saying to him , » Saul , Saul , why do you persecute me ? «
44009005	And he said , » Who are you , Lord ? « And he said , » I am Jesus whom you are persecuting ,
44009006	but get up and enter the city , and it will be told you what you must do . «
44009007	The men who were traveling with him stood speechless , hearing the voice but seeing no one .
44009008	Saul got up from the ground ; and when his eyes were opened , he could see nothing ; so they led him by the hand and brought him into Damascus .
44009009	And for three days he was without sight , and neither ate nor drank .
44009010	Now there was a disciple at Damascus named Ananias ; and the Lord said to him in a vision , » Ananias . « And he said , » Here I am , Lord . «
44009011	And the Lord said to him , » Get up and go to the street called Straight , and inquire at the house of Judas for a man from Tarsus named Saul , for he is praying ,
44009012	and in a vision he has seen a man named Ananias come in and lay his hands on him so that he might regain his sight . «
44009013	But Ananias answered , » Lord , I have heard from many about this man , how much harm he has done to your saints at Jerusalem ;
44009014	and here he has authority from the chief priests to bind all who call on your name . «
44009015	But the Lord said to him , » Go , for he is a chosen instrument of mine to carry my name before the Gentiles and kings and the sons of Israel ;
44009016	for I will show him how much he must suffer for the sake of my name . «
44009017	So Ananias departed and entered the house . And after laying his hands on him said , » Brother Saul , the Lord Jesus , who appeared to you on the road by which you were coming , has sent me so that you may regain your sight and be filled with the Holy Spirit . «
44009018	And immediately there fell from his eyes something like scales , and he regained his sight . And he got up and was baptized ,
44009019	and he took food and was strengthened . Now for several days he was with the disciples who were at Damascus .
44009020	And immediately he began to proclaim Jesus in the synagogues , saying , » He is the Son of God . «
44009021	All those who heard him were amazed , and said , » Is this not he who made havoc in Jerusalem of those who called on this name , and who had come here for the purpose of bringing them bound before the chief priests ? «
44009022	But Saul increased all the more in strength , and confounded the Jews who lived at Damascus by proving that this Jesus is the Christ .
44009023	When many days had passed , the Jews plotted to kill him ,
44009024	but their plot became known to Saul . They were watching the gates day and night , to kill him ;
44009025	but his disciples took him by night and let him down through an opening in the wall , lowering him in a basket .
44009026	When he came to Jerusalem , he tried to join the disciples ; but they were all afraid of him , not believing that he was a disciple .
44009027	But Barnabas took him and brought him to the apostles . And he declared to them how he had seen the Lord on the road , and that he had spoken to him , and how he had preached boldly at Damascus in the name of Jesus .
44009028	And he was with them moving about freely in Jerusalem , speaking out boldly in the name of the Lord .
44009029	And he was talking and arguing with the Hellenistic Jews ; but they were seeking to kill him .
44009030	But when the brethren learned of it , they brought him down to Caesarea and sent him off to Tarsus .
44009031	So the church throughout all Judea and Galilee and Samaria enjoyed peace and was built up ; and going on in the fear of the Lord and in the comfort of the Holy Spirit , it continued to increase .
44009032	Now as Peter went through all those regions , he came down also to the saints who lived at Lydda .
44009033	There he found a man named Aeneas , who had been bedridden for eight years and was paralyzed .
44009034	Peter said to him , » Aeneas , Jesus Christ heals you ; get up and make your bed . « Immediately he got up .
44009035	And all who lived at Lydda and Sharon saw him , and they turned to the Lord .
44009036	Now there was at Joppa a certain disciple named Tabitha ( which is translated Dorcas ) . She was full of good works and acts of charity .
44009037	And at that time she fell sick and died ; and when they had washed her , they laid her body in an upper room .
44009038	Since Lydda was near Joppa , the disciples , having heard that Peter was there , sent two men to him , imploring him , » Please come to us without delay . «
44009039	So Peter rose and went with them . And when he arrived , they took him to the upper room . All the widows stood beside him , weeping and showing the tunics and other garments that Dorcas made while she was with them .
44009040	But Peter sent them all out and knelt down and prayed ; then turning to the body , he said , » Tabitha , arise . « And she opened her eyes , and when she saw Peter , she sat up .
44009041	And he gave her his hand and raised her up . Then calling the saints and widows he presented her alive .
44009042	It became known all over Joppa , and many believed in the Lord .
44009043	And Peter stayed for many days in Joppa with a tanner named Simon .
44010001	At Caesarea there was a man named Cornelius , a centurion of what was known as the Italian Cohort ,
44010002	a devout man and one who feared God with all his household , and gave alms generously to the people and prayed to God continually .
44010003	About the ninth hour of the day he clearly saw in a vision an angel of God who had just come in and said to him , » Cornelius ! «
44010004	And he stared at him in terror , and said , » What is it , Lord ? « And he said to him , » Your prayers and alms have ascended as a memorial before God .
44010005	Now send men to Joppa , and bring a man named Simon who is called Peter ;
44010006	he is staying with a tanner named Simon , whose house is by the sea . «
44010007	When the angel who spoke to him had left , he called two of his servants and a devout soldier of those who were his personal attendants ,
44010008	and after he had explained everything to them , he sent them to Joppa .
44010009	The next day , as they were on their journey and approaching the city , Peter went up on the housetop about the sixth hour to pray .
44010010	And he became hungry and was desiring something to eat ; but while they were preparing it , he fell into a trance
44010011	and he saw heaven opened , and something descending , like a great sheet , let down by four corners to the earth .
44010012	In it were all kinds of four-footed animals and reptiles of the earth and birds of the air .
44010013	A voice came to him , » Get up , Peter . Kill and eat ! «
44010014	But Peter said , » No , Lord ; for I have never eaten anything that is common or unclean . «
44010015	And the voice came to him again a second time , » What God has cleansed , you must not call common . «
44010016	This happened three times , and immediately the thing was taken up to heaven .
44010017	Now while Peter was inwardly perplexed as to what the vision which he had seen might mean , behold , the men that were sent by Cornelius , having made inquiry for Simon's house , appeared at the gate .
44010018	They called out , asking whether Simon who was known as Peter was staying there .
44010019	While Peter was reflecting on the vision , the Spirit said to him , » Behold , three men are looking for you .
44010020	But get up , go downstairs and accompany them without hesitation , for I have sent them myself . «
44010021	Peter went down to the men and said , » Behold , I am the one you are looking for ; what is the reason you have come ? «
44010022	They said , » Cornelius , a centurion , a righteous and God-fearing man , who is well spoken of by the whole Jewish nation , was directed by a holy angel to send for you to come to his house , and to hear what you have to say . «
44010023	So he invited them in to be his guests . The next day he rose and went off with them , and some of the brethren from Joppa accompanied him .
44010024	On the following day he entered Caesarea . Now Cornelius was expecting them and had called together his relatives and close friends .
44010025	When Peter entered , Cornelius met him and fell down at his feet and worshipped him .
44010026	But Peter raised him up , saying , » Stand up ; I too am just a man . «
44010027	As he talked with him , he went in and found many people assembled .
44010028	And he said to them , » You yourselves know how unlawful it is for a Jew to associate with a foreigner or to visit him ; but God has shown me that I should not call any man common or unclean .
44010029	So when I was sent for , I came without raising any objection . I ask then why you sent for me . «
44010030	Cornelius said , » Four days ago to this hour , I was praying in my house during the ninth hour ; and behold , a man stood before me in shining garments ,
44010031	and he said , ‘ Cornelius , your prayer has been heard and your alms have been remembered before God .
44010032	Send therefore to Joppa and ask for Simon who is called Peter ; he is lodging in the house of Simon , a tanner , by the sea . ’
44010033	So I sent for you immediately , and you have been kind enough to come . Now therefore we are all here present in the sight of God , to hear all that you have been commanded by the Lord . «
44010034	And opening his mouth , Peter said : » I most certainly understand now that God is not one to show partiality ,
44010035	but in every nation the man who fears him and does what is right is welcome to him .
44010036	You know the word which he sent to Israel , preaching good news of peace through Jesus Christ ( he is Lord of all ) .
44010037	You know what has happened throughout all Judea , beginning from Galilee after the baptism which John preached :
44010038	how God anointed Jesus of Nazareth with the Holy Spirit and with power , and how he went about doing good and healing all who were oppressed by the devil , for God was with him .
44010039	We are witnesses of all that he did both in the country of the Jews and in Jerusalem . They put him to death by hanging him on a tree ;
44010040	but God raised him up on the third day and caused him to be seen ,
44010041	not to all the people but to us who were chosen by God as witnesses , who ate and drank with him after he rose from the dead .
44010042	And he commanded us to preach to the people , and to testify that he is the one appointed by God to be judge of the living and the dead .
44010043	Of him all the prophets bear witness that everyone who believes in him receives forgiveness of sins through his name . «
44010044	While Peter was still speaking these words , the Holy Spirit fell on all who heard the message .
44010045	All the circumcised believers who came with Peter were amazed , because the gift of the Holy Spirit had been poured out even on the Gentiles .
44010046	For they heard them speaking in tongues and praising God . Then Peter said ,
44010047	» Can anyone refuse the water for these people to be baptized who have received the Holy Spirit just as we have ? «
44010048	And he ordered them to be baptized in the name of Jesus Christ . Then they asked him to stay on for a few days .
44011001	Now the apostles and the brethren who were throughout Judea heard that the Gentiles also had received the word of God .
44011002	So when Peter went up to Jerusalem , the circumcised believers criticized him ,
44011003	saying , » You went to uncircumcised men and ate with them . «
44011004	But Peter began and explained to them in order :
44011005	» I was in the city of Joppa praying ; and in a trance I saw a vision , something descending like a great sheet , let down from heaven by four corners ; and it came down to me .
44011006	And when I looked into it I saw four-footed animals of the earth , wild beasts , reptiles , and birds of the air .
44011007	Then I heard a voice saying to me , ‘ Get up , Peter . Kill and eat ! ’
44011008	But I said , ‘ No , Lord ; for nothing common or unclean has ever entered my mouth . ’
44011009	But the voice answered a second time from heaven , ‘ What God has cleansed you must not call common . ’
44011010	This happened three times , and all was drawn up again into heaven .
44011011	And behold , at that moment three men appeared at the house in which we were staying , having been sent to me from Caesarea .
44011012	The Spirit told me to go with them with no hesitation . These six brethren also went with me , and we entered the man's house .
44011013	And he told us how he had seen the angel standing in his house and saying , ‘ Send to Joppa and bring Simon , who is also called Peter ;
44011014	he will declare to you a message by which you will be saved , you and all your household . ’
44011015	As I began to speak , the Holy Spirit fell on them just as on us at the beginning .
44011016	And I remembered the word of the Lord , how he said , ‘ John baptized with water , but you will be baptized with the Holy Spirit . ’
44011017	So if God gave them the same gift as he gave us , who believed in the Lord Jesus Christ , who was I that I could oppose God ? «
44011018	When they heard this , they quieted down and glorified God , saying , » So then , God has granted to the Gentiles also the repentance unto life . «
44011019	Now those who were scattered because of the persecution that arose in connection with Stephen traveled as far as Phoenicia and Cyprus and Antioch , speaking the word to no one except Jews .
44011020	But there were some of them , men of Cyprus and Cyrene , who came to Antioch and began speaking to the Greeks also , preaching the Lord Jesus .
44011021	The hand of the Lord was with them , and a great number believed and turned to the Lord .
44011022	News of this reached the ears of the church at Jerusalem , and they sent Barnabas to Antioch .
44011023	When he arrived and saw the grace of God , he was glad and encouraged them all to remain true to the Lord with all their hearts ;
44011024	for he was a good man , full of the Holy Spirit and of faith . And a great number of people were brought to the Lord .
44011025	So Barnabas went to Tarsus to look for Saul ;
44011026	and when he had found him , he brought him to Antioch . So for a whole year they met with the church and taught great numbers of people ; and the disciples were called Christians first in Antioch .
44011027	Now at this time some prophets came down from Jerusalem to Antioch .
44011028	One of them named Agabus stood up and foretold by the Spirit that there would be a great famine all over the world . And this took place in the reign of Claudius .
44011029	And the disciples determined , each according to his ability , to send relief for the brethren living in Judea .
44011030	And this they did , sending it to the elders by Barnabas and Saul .
44012001	Now about that time Herod the king laid hands on some who belonged to the church in order to persecute them .
44012002	He had James the brother of John put to death with the sword .
44012003	When he saw that it pleased the Jews , he proceeded to arrest Peter also . This was during the days of Unleavened Bread .
44012004	When he had seized him , he put him in prison , and delivered him to four squads of soldiers to guard him , intending after the Passover to bring him out to the people .
44012005	So Peter was kept in prison , but earnest prayer for him was made to God by the church .
44012006	The very night when Herod was about to bring him out , Peter was sleeping between two soldiers , bound with two chains , and sentries before the door were guarding the prison .
44012007	And behold , an angel of the Lord suddenly appeared , and a light shone in the cell ; and he struck Peter's side and woke him up , saying , » Get up quickly . « And the chains fell off his hands .
44012008	And the angel said to him , » Dress yourself and put on your sandals . « And he did so . And he said to him , » Wrap your cloak around you and follow me . «
44012009	So he went out and followed him ; and he did not know that what was done by the angel was real , but thought he was seeing a vision .
44012010	When they had passed the first and the second guard , they came to the iron gate leading into the city . It opened for them by itself , and they went out and passed on through one street ; and immediately the angel left him .
44012011	When Peter came to himself , he said , » Now I know for sure that the Lord has sent his angel and rescued me from the hand of Herod and from all that the Jewish people were expecting . «
44012012	When he realized this , he went to the house of Mary , the mother of John who was also called Mark , where many were gathered together and were praying .
44012013	And when he knocked at the door of the gate , a servant-girl named Rhoda came to answer .
44012014	When she recognized Peter's voice , in her joy she did not open the gate , but ran in and announced that Peter was standing in front of the gate .
44012015	They said to her , » You are out of your mind ! « But she kept insisting that it was so . They said , » It is his angel . «
44012016	But Peter continued knocking ; and when they opened the door , they saw him and were amazed .
44012017	But motioning to them with his hand to be silent , he described to them how the Lord had brought him out of the prison . And he said , » Tell this to James and to the brethren . « Then he left and went to another place .
44012018	Now when day came , there was no small disturbance among the soldiers as to what had become of Peter .
44012019	When Herod had searched for him and could not find him , he examined the guards and ordered that they be put to death . Then he went down from Judea to Caesarea and stayed there a while .
44012020	Now he was angry with the people of Tyre and Sidon ; and they came to him in a body , and having persuaded Blastus , the king's chamberlain , they asked for peace , because their country depended on the king’s country for food .
44012021	On an appointed day Herod put on his royal robes , took his seat upon the throne , and made an address to them .
44012022	And the people shouted , » The voice of a god and not of a man ! «
44012023	Immediately an angel of the Lord struck him because he did not give God the glory , and he was eaten by worms and died .
44012024	But the word of God continued to grow and to be multiplied .
44012025	And Barnabas and Saul returned from Jerusalem when they had fulfilled their mission , taking along with them John , who was also called Mark .
44013001	Now in the church that was at Antioch there were prophets and teachers : Barnabas , Simeon who was called Niger , Lucius of Cyrene , Manaen who had been brought up with Herod the tetrarch , and Saul .
44013002	While they were worshipping the Lord and fasting , the Holy Spirit said , » Set apart for me Barnabas and Saul for the work to which I have called them . «
44013003	Then after they had fasted and prayed , they laid their hands on them and sent them off .
44013004	So , being sent out by the Holy Spirit , they went down to Seleucia and from there they sailed to Cyprus .
44013005	When they arrived at Salamis , they proclaimed the word of God in the synagogues of the Jews . And they had John as their helper .
44013006	When they had gone through the whole island as far as Paphos , they came upon a certain magician , a Jewish false prophet , named Bar-Jesus ,
44013007	who was with the proconsul , Sergius Paulus , a man of intelligence . This man summoned Barnabas and Saul and sought to hear the word of God .
44013008	But Elymas the magician ( for that is the meaning of his name ) was opposing them , seeking to turn the proconsul away from the faith .
44013009	But Saul , who was also called Paul , filled with the Holy Spirit , looked intently at him
44013010	and said , » You who are full of all deceit and fraud , you son of the devil , you enemy of all righteousness , will you not stop making crooked the straight ways of the Lord ?
44013011	Now , behold , the hand of the Lord is upon you , and you will be blind and unable to see the sun for a time . « And immediately a mist and a darkness fell upon him , and he went about seeking someone to lead him by the hand .
44013012	Then the proconsul believed , when he saw what had happened , for he was amazed at the teaching of the Lord .
44013013	Now Paul and his companions put out to sea from Paphos and came to Perga in Pamphylia ; but John left them and returned to Jerusalem .
44013014	But they passed on from Perga and came to Pisidian Antioch . And on the Sabbath day they went into the synagogue and sat down .
44013015	After the reading of the law and the prophets , the rulers of the synagogue sent to them , saying , » Brethren , if you have any word of exhortation for the people , say it . «
44013016	Paul stood up , and motioning with his hand said , » Men of Israel , and you who fear God , listen :
44013017	the God of this people Israel chose our fathers and made the people great during their stay in the land of Egypt , and with uplifted arm he led them out of it .
44013018	For about forty years he put up with them in the wilderness .
44013019	When he had destroyed seven nations in the land of Canaan , he gave them their land as an inheritance , for about four hundred and fifty years .
44013020	After these things he gave them judges until Samuel the prophet .
44013021	Then they asked for a king , and God gave them Saul the son of Kish , a man of the tribe of Benjamin , for forty years .
44013022	And after he had removed him , he raised up David to be their king ; concerning whom he testified and said , ‘ I have found in David the son of Jesse a man after my heart , who will do all my will . ’
44013023	From this man's descendants God has brought to Israel a Savior , Jesus , as he promised .
44013024	Before his coming John had preached a baptism of repentance to all the people of Israel .
44013025	And as John was completing his course , he said , ‘ What do you suppose that I am ? I am not he . No , but after me one is coming , the sandals of whose feet I am not worthy to untie . ’
44013026	» Brethren , sons of the family of Abraham , and those among you that fear God , to us has been sent the message of this salvation .
44013027	For those who live in Jerusalem and their rulers , because they did not recognize him nor the utterances of the prophets which are read every Sabbath , fulfilled these by condemning him .
44013028	Though they found no ground for a death sentence , they asked Pilate to have him executed .
44013029	When they had carried out all that was written about him , they took him down from the tree and laid him in a tomb .
44013030	But God raised him from the dead ;
44013031	and for many days he appeared to those who came up with him from Galilee to Jerusalem , who are now his witnesses to the people .
44013032	And we preach to you the good news that what God promised to the fathers ,
44013033	he has fulfilled for us , their children , by raising up Jesus . As it is also written in the second Psalm : ‘ You are my Son ; today I have begotten you . ’
44013034	As for the fact that he raised him from the dead , no more to return to decay , he spoke in this way : ‘ I will give you the holy and sure blessings of David . ’
44013035	Therefore he also says in another Psalm , ‘ You will not let your Holy One see decay . ’
44013036	For David , after he had served the purpose of God in his own generation , fell asleep , and was laid with his fathers and saw decay ;
44013037	but he whom God raised did not see decay .
44013038	Therefore let it be known to you , brethren , that through him forgiveness of sins is proclaimed to you ,
44013039	and through him everyone who believes is freed from everything from which you could not be freed by the law of Moses .
44013040	Therefore take care , so that what is said in the prophets may not come upon you :
44013041	
44013042	As Paul and Barnabas were going out , the people begged that these things might be spoken to them the next Sabbath .
44013043	When the meeting of the synagogue broke up , many Jews and devout converts to Judaism followed Paul and Barnabas , who spoke to them and urged them to continue in the grace of God .
44013044	The next Sabbath almost the whole city gathered to hear the word of the Lord .
44013045	But when the Jews saw the crowds , they were filled with jealousy , and contradicted what was spoken by Paul , and blasphemed .
44013046	Paul and Barnabas spoke out boldly and said , » It was necessary that the word of God be spoken to you first . Since you reject it and judge yourselves unworthy of eternal life , behold , we turn to the Gentiles .
44013047	For so the Lord has commanded us : ‘ I have made you a light for the Gentiles , that you may bring salvation to the ends of the earth . ’ «
44013048	When the Gentiles heard this , they were glad and glorified the word of the Lord ; and as many as were appointed to eternal life believed .
44013049	And the word of the Lord spread through the whole region .
44013050	But the Jews incited the devout women of high standing and the leading men of the city , and stirred up persecution against Paul and Barnabas , and drove them out of their district .
44013051	So they shook off the dust from their feet in protest against them and went to Iconium .
44013052	And the disciples were filled with joy and with the Holy Spirit .
44014001	Now at Iconium they entered together into the Jewish synagogue , and so spoke that a great number believed , both of Jews and of Greeks .
44014002	But the Jews who refused to believe stirred up the Gentiles and poisoned their minds against the brethren .
44014003	So they spent a long time there , speaking boldly for the Lord , who bore witness to the word of his grace , granting signs and wonders to be done by their hands .
44014004	But the people of the city were divided ; some sided with the Jews , and some with the apostles .
44014005	When an attempt was made by both the Gentiles and the Jews with their rulers , to mistreat them and to stone them ,
44014006	they became aware of it and fled to the cities of Lycaonia , Lystra and Derbe , and to the surrounding country ;
44014007	and there they continued to preach the gospel .
44014008	At Lystra there was a man sitting who had no strength in his feet , lame from birth , who had never walked .
44014009	He listened to Paul speaking ; and Paul , looking intently at him and seeing that he had faith to be made well ,
44014010	said with a loud voice , » Stand upright on your feet . « And he leaped up and began to walk .
44014011	And when the crowds saw what Paul had done , they lifted up their voices , saying in the Lycaonian language , » The gods have come down to us in the likeness of men ! «
44014012	Barnabas they called Zeus , and Paul , because he was the chief speaker , they called Hermes .
44014013	The priest of Zeus , whose temple was just outside the city , brought oxen and garlands to the gates , and wanted to offer sacrifice with the crowds .
44014014	But when the apostles Barnabas and Paul heard of it , they tore their robes and rushed out into the crowd , crying out
44014015	» Men , why are you doing this ? We also are men , of like nature with you , and bring you good news , that you should turn from these vain things to a living God who made the heaven and the earth and the sea and all that is in them .
44014016	In past generations he allowed all the nations to go their own ways ;
44014017	yet he did not leave himself without witness , in that he did good and gave you rains from heaven and fruitful seasons , satisfying your hearts with food and gladness . «
44014018	Even with these words , they had difficulty keeping the crowds from offering sacrifice to them .
44014019	But Jews came there from Antioch and Iconium ; and having won over the crowds , they stoned Paul and dragged him out of the city , supposing that he was dead .
44014020	But after the disciples had gathered around him , he got up and entered the city . And the next day he went with Barnabas to Derbe .
44014021	After they had preached the gospel to that city and had made many disciples , they returned to Lystra and to Iconium and to Antioch ,
44014022	strengthening the souls of the disciples , encouraging them to continue in the faith , and saying , » Through many tribulations we must enter the kingdom of God . «
44014023	And when they had appointed elders for them in every church , with prayer and fasting they committed them to the Lord in whom they believed .
44014024	They passed through Pisidia , and came into Pamphylia .
44014025	And when they had spoken the word in Perga , they went down to Attalia .
44014026	From there they sailed to Antioch , where they had been commended to the grace of God for the work which they had completed .
44014027	When they arrived , they gathered the church together and declared all that God had done with them , and how he had opened a door of faith to the Gentiles .
44014028	And they spent a long time with the disciples .
44015001	But some men came down from Judea and were teaching the brethren , » Unless you are circumcised according to the custom of Moses , you cannot be saved . «
44015002	And when Paul and Barnabas had no small dissension and debate with them , Paul and Barnabas and some of the others were appointed to go up to Jerusalem to the apostles and the elders about this question .
44015003	So , being sent on their way by the church , they passed through both Phoenicia and Samaria , reporting the conversion of the Gentiles , and they gave great joy to all the brethren .
44015004	When they came to Jerusalem , they were welcomed by the church and the apostles and the elders , and they reported all that God had done with them .
44015005	But some believers who belonged to the party of the Pharisees stood up , and said , » It is necessary to circumcise them , and to charge them to keep the Law of Moses . «
44015006	The apostles and the elders came together to consider this matter .
44015007	After there had been much debate , Peter stood up and said to them , » Brethren , you know that in the early days God made a choice among you , that by my mouth the Gentiles would hear the word of the gospel and believe .
44015008	And God , who knows the heart , bore witness to them giving them the Holy Spirit , just as he also did to us ;
44015009	and he made no distinction between us and them , but cleansed their hearts by faith .
44015010	Now therefore why do you test God by putting upon the neck of the disciples a yoke which neither our fathers nor we have been able to bear ?
44015011	But we believe that we are saved through the grace of the Lord Jesus , just as they are . «
44015012	All the assembly kept silent ; and they listened to Barnabas and Paul as they related what signs and wonders God had done through them among the Gentiles .
44015013	After they finished speaking , James replied , » Brethren , listen to me .
44015014	Simeon has related how God first showed his concern by taking from the Gentiles a people for his name .
44015015	With this the words of the Prophets agree , just as it is written ,
44015016	
44015017	
44015018	
44015019	Therefore it is my judgment that we should not trouble those who are turning to God from among the Gentiles ,
44015020	but that we should write to them to abstain from the pollutions of idols and from fornication and from what is strangled and from blood .
44015021	For Moses from ancient generations has in every city those who preach him , since he is read in the synagogues every Sabbath . «
44015022	Then it seemed good to the apostles and the elders , with the whole church , to choose men from among them and send them to Antioch with Paul and Barnabas . They sent Judas called Barsabbas , and Silas , leading men among the brethren ,
44015023	and they sent the following letter with them : » The apostles and the brethren who are elders , to the brethren in Antioch and Syria and Cilicia who are from the Gentiles , greetings .
44015024	Since we have heard that some persons from us have disturbed you with words , unsettling your minds , although we gave them no instructions ,
44015025	it has seemed good to us , having come to one accord , to choose men and send them to you with our beloved Barnabas and Paul ,
44015026	men who have risked their lives for the name of our Lord Jesus Christ .
44015027	We have therefore sent Judas and Silas , who themselves will tell you the same things by word of mouth .
44015028	For it seemed good to the Holy Spirit and to us to lay upon you no greater burden than these essentials :
44015029	that you abstain from things sacrificed to idols and from blood and from things strangled and from fornication . If you keep yourselves free from these , you will do well . Farewell . «
44015030	So when they were sent off , they went down to Antioch ; and having gathered the congregation together , they delivered the letter .
44015031	And when they read it , they rejoiced at its encouragement .
44015032	And Judas and Silas , who were themselves prophets , encouraged the brethren with many words and strengthened them .
44015033	And after they had spent some time there , they were sent off in peace by the brethren to those who had sent them .
44015035	But Paul and Barnabas remained in Antioch , teaching and preaching the word of the Lord , with many others also .
44015036	After some days Paul said to Barnabas , » Let us return and visit the brethren in every city where we proclaimed the word of the Lord , and see how they are . «
44015037	Barnabas wanted to take John , also called Mark , with them .
44015038	But Paul kept insisting that they should not take along one who had deserted them in Pamphylia , and had not gone with them to the work .
44015039	There arose such a sharp disagreement that they separated from one another , and Barnabas took Mark with him and sailed away to Cyprus .
44015040	But Paul chose Silas and left , being commended by the brethren to the grace of the Lord .
44015041	And he went through Syria and Cilicia , strengthening the churches .
44016001	And he came also to Derbe and to Lystra . A disciple was there , named Timothy , the son of a Jewish woman who was a believer ; but his father was a Greek ,
44016002	and he was well spoken of by the brethren who were in Lystra and Iconium .
44016003	Paul wanted this man to accompany him ; and he took him and circumcised him because of the Jews who were in those places , for they all knew that his father was a Greek .
44016004	As they went on their way through the cities , they delivered to them for observance the decisions which had been reached by the apostles and elders who were in Jerusalem .
44016005	So the churches were strengthened in the faith , and increased in numbers daily .
44016006	And they went through the region of Phrygia and Galatia , having been forbidden by the Holy Spirit to speak the word in Asia .
44016007	And when they came to Mysia , they tried to go into Bithynia , but the Spirit of Jesus did not allow them ;
44016008	so passing by Mysia , they went down to Troas .
44016009	A vision appeared to Paul in the night : a man of Macedonia was standing and begging him , and saying , » Come over to Macedonia and help us . «
44016010	When he had seen the vision , immediately we sought to go on into Macedonia , concluding that God had called us to preach the gospel to them .
44016011	So putting out to sea from Troas , we ran a straight course to Samothrace , and on the day following to Neapolis ;
44016012	and from there to Philippi , which is the leading city of the district of Macedonia , and a Roman colony . We stayed in this city some days ;
44016013	and on the Sabbath day we went outside the gate to the riverside , where we supposed there was a place of prayer ; and we sat down and began speaking to the women who had come together .
44016014	A woman named Lydia , from the city of Thyatira , a seller of purple fabrics , who was a worshiper of God , was listening . The Lord opened her heart to respond to the things spoken by Paul .
44016015	When she and her household had been baptized , she urged us , saying , » If you have judged me to be faithful to the Lord , come into my house and stay . « And she prevailed upon us .
44016016	It happened that as we were going to the place of prayer , we were met by a slave-girl who had a spirit of divination . She brought her owners much profit by fortune-telling .
44016017	She followed Paul and the rest of us , crying , » These men are servants of the Most High God , who are telling you the way of salvation . «
44016018	She continued doing this for many days . But Paul was greatly annoyed , and turned and said to the spirit , » I command you in the name of Jesus Christ to come out of her ! « And it came out at that very moment .
44016019	But when her owners saw that their hope of profit was gone , they seized Paul and Silas and dragged them into the marketplace before the authorities ,
44016020	and when they had brought them to the magistrates they said , » These men are Jews and they are throwing our city into an uproar .
44016021	They advocate customs which it is not lawful for us Romans to accept or practice . «
44016022	The crowd joined against them , and the magistrates tore the garments off them and ordered them to be beaten with rods .
44016023	And when they had inflicted many blows upon them , they threw them into prison , charging the jailer to guard them securely .
44016024	Having received such a charge , he put them into the inner prison and fastened their feet in the stocks .
44016025	But about midnight Paul and Silas were praying and singing hymns to God , and the prisoners were listening to them ,
44016026	and suddenly there came a great earthquake , so that the foundations of the prison were shaken ; and immediately all the doors were opened and everyone's chains were unfastened .
44016027	When the jailer woke and saw that the prison doors were open , he drew his sword and was about to kill himself , supposing that the prisoners had escaped .
44016028	But Paul cried with a loud voice , » Do not harm yourself , for we are all here ! «
44016029	And he called for lights and rushed in , and trembling with fear he fell down before Paul and Silas .
44016030	He brought them out and said , » Sirs , what must I do to be saved ? «
44016031	They said , » Believe in the Lord Jesus , and you will be saved , you and your household . «
44016032	They spoke the word of the Lord to him and to all who were in his house .
44016033	He took them that very hour of the night and washed their wounds , and immediately he was baptized , he and all his family .
44016034	Then he brought them up into his house , and set food before them ; and he rejoiced with his whole household that he had believed in God .
44016035	But when it was day , the magistrates sent their police , saying , » Release those men . «
44016036	And the jailer reported these words to Paul , saying , » The chief magistrates have sent to release you . Therefore come out now and go in peace . «
44016037	But Paul said to them , » They have beaten us publicly , without trial , men who are Roman citizens , and have thrown us into prison ; and do they now cast us out secretly ? No ! Let them come themselves and take us out . «
44016038	The police reported these words to the magistrates , and they were afraid when they heard that they were Roman citizens .
44016039	So they came and apologized to them , and they took them out and asked them to leave the city .
44016040	They went out of the prison and entered the house of Lydia , and when they saw the brethren , they encouraged them and departed .
44017001	Now when they had passed through Amphipolis and Apollonia , they came to Thessalonica , where there was a synagogue of the Jews .
44017002	And Paul went in , as was his custom , and for three weeks he reasoned with them from the scriptures ,
44017003	explaining and proving that the Christ had to suffer and rise again from the dead , and saying , » This Jesus whom I am proclaiming to you is the Christ . «
44017004	And some of them were persuaded , and joined Paul and Silas ; as did a large number of the God-fearing Greeks and not a few of the leading women .
44017005	But the Jews were jealous , and taking some wicked men from the market place , they formed a mob and set the city in an uproar ; they attacked the house of Jason , seeking to bring them out to the people .
44017006	When they did not find them , they dragged Jason and some of the brethren before the city authorities , shouting , » These men who have turned the world upside down have come here also ,
44017007	and Jason has welcomed them , and they are all acting against the decrees of Caesar , saying that there is another king , Jesus . «
44017008	The crowd and the city authorities were disturbed when they heard this .
44017009	And when they had taken a pledge from Jason and the others , they let them go .
44017010	The brethren immediately sent Paul and Silas away by night to Berea , and when they arrived , they went into the Jewish synagogue .
44017011	Now these were more noble-minded than those in Thessalonica , for they received the word with great eagerness , examining the Scriptures daily to see if these things were so .
44017012	Therefore many of them believed , along with a number of prominent Greek women and men .
44017013	But when the Jews of Thessalonica learned that the word of God was proclaimed by Paul in Berea also , they came there too , agitating and stirring up the crowds .
44017014	Then the brethren immediately sent Paul out to go as far as the sea , but Silas and Timothy remained there .
44017015	Now those who escorted Paul brought him as far as Athens ; and receiving a command for Silas and Timothy to come to him as soon as possible , they left .
44017016	Now while Paul was waiting for them at Athens , his spirit was provoked within him as he saw that the city was full of idols .
44017017	So he was reasoning in the synagogue with the Jews and the God-fearing Greeks , and in the market place every day with those who happened to be there .
44017018	And also some of the Epicurean and Stoic philosophers were conversing with him . Some said , » What would this idle babbler wish to say ? « Others , » He seems to be a proclaimer of foreign deities , « — because he was preaching Jesus and the resurrection .
44017019	And they took hold of him and brought him to the Areopagus , saying , » May we know what this new teaching is which you present ?
44017020	For you are bringing some strange things to our ears ; so we want to know what these things mean . «
44017021	( Now all the Athenians and the foreigners who lived there spent their time in nothing other than telling or hearing something new . )
44017022	So Paul stood up in the meeting of the Areopagus and said : » Men of Athens , I see that in every way you are very religious .
44017023	For as I passed along , and observed the objects of your worship , I found also an altar with this inscription , ‘ TO AN UNKNOWN GOD . ’ What therefore you worship as unknown , this I proclaim to you .
44017024	The God who made the world and everything in it , since he is Lord of heaven and earth , does not live in temples made by hands ;
44017025	nor is he served by human hands , as though he needed anything , since he himself gives to all men life and breath and everything .
44017026	And he made from one man every nation of men to live on all the face of the earth , having determined their appointed times and the boundaries of their habitation ,
44017027	that they would seek God , if perhaps they might grope for him and find him , though he is not far from each one of us .
44017028	
44017029	Being then God's offspring , we ought not to think that the Divine Nature is like gold or silver or stone , an image formed by the art and imagination of man .
44017030	The times of ignorance God overlooked , but now he commands all people everywhere to repent ,
44017031	because he has fixed a day on which he will judge the world in righteousness by a man whom he has appointed , and of this he has given proof to all men by raising him from the dead . «
44017032	Now when they heard about the resurrection of the dead , some of them sneered , but others said , » We want to hear you again on this subject . «
44017033	So Paul went out from among them .
44017034	But some men joined him and believed , among whom also were Dionysius the Areopagite and a woman named Damaris and others with them .
44018001	After this he left Athens and went to Corinth .
44018002	And he found a Jew named Aquila , a native of Pontus , having recently come from Italy with his wife Priscilla , because Claudius had commanded all the Jews to leave Rome . He went to see them ,
44018003	and because he was of the same trade he stayed with them , and they worked , for by trade they were tentmakers .
44018004	And every Sabbath he was reasoning in the synagogue , and trying to persuade Jews and Greeks .
44018005	When Silas and Timothy came from Macedonia , Paul devoted himself exclusively to preaching , testifying to the Jews that Jesus was the Christ .
44018006	But when they opposed him and blasphemed , he shook out his garments and said to them , » Your blood be on your own heads ! I am clean . From now on I will go to the Gentiles . «
44018007	Then he left there and went to the house of a man named Titius Justus , a worshiper of God , whose house was next door to the synagogue .
44018008	Crispus , the ruler of the synagogue , believed in the Lord , together with all his household ; and many of the Corinthians who heard him believed and were baptized .
44018009	And the Lord said to Paul one night in a vision , » Do not be afraid , but go on speaking and do not be silent ;
44018010	for I am with you , and no man will attack you to harm you , for I have many people in this city . «
44018011	And he stayed a year and six months , teaching the word of God among them .
44018012	But while Gallio was proconsul of Achaia , the Jews made a united attack upon Paul and brought him before the judgment seat ,
44018013	saying , » This man is persuading men to worship God contrary to the law . «
44018014	But when Paul was about to open his mouth , Gallio said to the Jews , » If it were a matter of wrong or of vicious crime , O Jews , it would be reasonable for me to put up with you ;
44018015	but since it is a matter of questions about words and names and your own law , see to it yourselves ; I refuse to be a judge of these things . «
44018016	And he drove them from the judgment seat .
44018017	And they all seized Sosthenes , the ruler of the synagogue , and beat him in front of the judgment seat . But Gallio paid no attention to this .
44018018	After this Paul stayed many days longer , and then took leave of the brethren and sailed for Syria , and with him were Priscilla and Aquila . In Cenchrea he had his hair cut , for he had taken a vow .
44018019	They came to Ephesus , and he left them there . Now he himself went into the synagogue and reasoned with the Jews .
44018020	When they asked him to stay for a longer time , he declined ;
44018021	but on taking leave of them he said , » I will return to you if God wills , « and he set sail from Ephesus .
44018022	When he had landed at Caesarea , he went up and greeted the church , and then went down to Antioch .
44018023	After spending some time there , he departed and went from place to place through the region of Galatia and Phrygia , strengthening all the disciples .
44018024	Now a Jew named Apollos , a native of Alexandria , came to Ephesus . He was an eloquent man , well versed in the scriptures .
