45009021	Does not the potter have right over the clay , to make out of the same lump one vessel for honor and another for dishonor ?
45009022	What if God , choosing to show his wrath and to make his power known , endured with much patience the vessels of wrath prepared for destruction ,
45009023	in order to make known the riches of his glory for the vessels of mercy , which he has prepared beforehand for glory ,
45009024	even us whom he has called , not from the Jews only , but also from the Gentiles ?
45009025	As indeed he says in Hosea : » I will call them who were not my people ‘ my people , ’ and her who was not beloved I will call ‘ my beloved . ’ «
45009026	
45009027	And Isaiah cries out concerning Israel : » Though the number of the sons of Israel be as the sand of the sea , only the remnant will be saved .
45009028	For the Lord will carry out his sentence on the earth with speed and finality . «
45009029	And as Isaiah said : » Unless the Lord of hosts had left us children , we would have become like Sodom , and we would have been made like Gomorrah . «
45009030	What shall we say , then ? That Gentiles who did not pursue righteousness have attained it , that is , righteousness through faith ;
45009031	but Israel , who pursued the law of righteousness , has not attained that law .
45009032	Why ? Because they did not pursue it by faith , but as if it were by works . They have stumbled over the stumbling stone ,
45009033	as it is written : » Behold , I lay in Zion a stone that will make men stumble , and a rock that will make them fall ; and he who believes in him will not be put to shame . «
45010001	Brethren , my heart's desire and prayer to God for them is that they may be saved .
45010002	For I bear them witness that they have a zeal for God , but it is not according to knowledge .
45010003	For , being ignorant of the righteousness that comes from God , and seeking to establish their own , they did not submit to God's righteousness .
45010004	For Christ is the end of the law , that there may be righteousness for everyone who believes .
45010005	For Moses writes about the righteousness which is of the law , » The man who does those things shall live by them . «
45010006	But the righteousness based on faith says , » Do not say in your heart , ‘ Who will ascend into heaven ? ’ « ( that is , to bring Christ down )
45010007	or » Who will descend into the abyss ? « ( that is , to bring Christ up from the dead ) .
45010008	But what does it say ? » The word is near you , in your mouth and in your heart « ( that is , the word of faith which we preach ) ;
45010009	because , if you confess with your mouth that Jesus is Lord and believe in your heart that God raised him from the dead , you will be saved .
45010010	For man believes with his heart and so is justified , and he confesses with his mouth and so is saved .
45010011	The scripture says , » No one who believes in him will be put to shame . «
45010012	For there is no distinction between Jew and Greek ; the same Lord is Lord of all and bestows his riches on all who call upon him .
45010013	For , » everyone who calls on the name of the Lord will be saved . «
45010014	How then can they call on him in whom they have not believed ? And how can they believe in him of whom they have not heard ? And how can they hear without a preacher ?
45010015	And how can they preach unless they are sent ? As it is written , » How beautiful are the feet of those who preach good news ! «
45010016	But they have not all obeyed the gospel . For Isaiah says , » Lord , who has believed our message ? «
45010017	So faith comes from hearing , and hearing by the word of Christ .
45010018	But I ask , have they not heard ? Indeed they have ; for » Their voice has gone out to all the earth , and their words to the ends of the world . «
45010019	Again I ask , did Israel not understand ? First Moses says , » I will make you jealous by those who are not a nation ; by a foolish nation I will make you angry . «
45010020	But Isaiah is very bold and says , » I was found by those who did not seek me ; I have shown myself to those who did not ask for me . «
45010021	But of Israel he says , » All day long I have held out my hands to a disobedient and contrary people . «
45011001	I ask , then , has God rejected his people ? Certainly not ! I myself am an Israelite , a descendant of Abraham , a member of the tribe of Benjamin .
45011002	God has not rejected his people whom he foreknew . Do you not know what the scripture says of Elijah , how he pleads with God against Israel ? —
45011003	» Lord , they have killed your prophets and torn down your altars , and I alone am left , and they seek my life . «
45011004	But what is God's reply to him ? » I have reserved for myself seven thousand men who have not bowed the knee to Baal . «
45011005	So too at the present time there is a remnant , chosen by grace .
45011006	And if it is by grace , then it is no longer on the basis of works ; otherwise , grace would no longer be grace .
45011007	What then ? Israel did not obtain what it sought . The elect obtained it , but the rest were hardened ,
45011008	as it is written : » God gave them a spirit of stupor , eyes that they should not see and ears that they should not hear , down to this very day . «
45011009	And David says : » Let their table become a snare and a trap , a stumbling block and a retribution for them .
45011010	
45011011	So I ask , have they stumbled so as to fall ? Certainly not ! But through their trespass salvation has come to the Gentiles , to make Israel jealous .
45011012	Now if their trespass means riches for the world , and if their failure means riches for the Gentiles , how much more will their fullness mean !
45011013	Now I am speaking to you Gentiles . Inasmuch then as I am an apostle to the Gentiles , I magnify my ministry
45011014	in the hope that I may somehow arouse to jealousy the kinsmen of my flesh and save some of them .
45011015	For if their rejection is the reconciliation of the world , what will their acceptance be but life from the dead ?
45011016	If the dough offered as firstfruits is holy , then the whole lump is holy ; and if the root is holy , so are the branches .
45011017	And if some of the branches were broken off , and you , a wild olive shoot , were grafted in among the rest to share the root of the olive tree ,
45011018	do not boast over the branches . If you do boast , remember that you do not support the root , but the root supports you .
45011019	You will say then , » Branches were broken off so that I might be grafted in . «
45011020	That is true . They were broken off because of their unbelief , but you stand fast only by faith . So do not be proud , but stand in awe .
45011021	For if God did not spare the natural branches , he will not spare you either .
45011022	Therefore consider the kindness and the severity of God : severity toward those who fell , but kindness to you , provided you continue in his kindness ; otherwise you also will be cut off .
45011023	And they also , if they do not persist in unbelief , will be grafted in , for God is able to graft them in again .
45011024	For if you were cut out of an olive tree that is wild by nature , and were grafted , contrary to nature , into a cultivated olive tree , how much more will these natural branches be grafted back into their own olive tree !
45011025	I do not want you to be ignorant of this mystery , brothers , so that you may not be conceited : Israel has experienced a hardening in part until the full number of the Gentiles has come in .
45011026	And so all Israel will be saved , as it is written : » The Deliverer will come from Zion , he will turn away ungodliness from Jacob ;
45011027	
45011028	As regards the gospel they are enemies of God , for your sake ; but as regards election they are beloved for the sake of their forefathers .
45011029	For the gifts and the call of God are irrevocable .
45011030	Just as you were once disobedient to God but now have received mercy because of their disobedience ,
45011031	so they have now been disobedient in order that by the mercy shown to you they also may receive mercy .
45011032	For God has bound all men over to disobedience , that he may have mercy upon all .
45011033	Oh , the depth of the riches and of the wisdom and knowledge of God ! How unsearchable are his judgments and his ways past finding out !
45011034	
45011035	
45011036	For from him and through him and to him are all things . To him be glory forever . Amen .
45012001	I appeal to you therefore , brethren , by the mercies of God , to present your bodies as a living sacrifice , holy and acceptable to God , which is your spiritual worship .
45012002	Do not be conformed to this world but be transformed by the renewing of your mind , that you may prove what is the will of God , what is good and acceptable and perfect .
45012003	For by the grace given to me I say to every one among you not to think of himself more highly than he ought to think , but to think with sober judgment , each according to the measure of faith which God has assigned him .
45012004	For as in one body we have many members , and all the members do not have the same function ,
45012005	so we , though many , are one body in Christ , and individually members one of another .
45012006	Having gifts that differ according to the grace given to us , let us use them : if prophecy , in proportion to our faith ;
45012007	if service , let us use it in our serving ; he who teaches , in his teaching ;
45012008	he who exhorts , in exhortation ; he who gives , with liberality ; he who leads , with diligence ; he who does acts of mercy , with cheerfulness .
45012009	Let love be genuine . Hate what is evil ; cling to what is good .
45012010	Be devoted to one another in brotherly love ; outdo one another in showing honor .
45012011	Never be lacking in zeal , be fervent in spirit , serving the Lord .
45012012	Rejoice in your hope , be patient in tribulation , be faithful in prayer .
45012013	Contribute to the needs of the saints , practice hospitality .
45012014	Bless those who persecute you ; bless and do not curse .
45012015	Rejoice with those who rejoice , weep with those who weep .
45012016	Live in harmony with one another . Do not be proud , but associate with the lowly . Do not be conceited .
45012017	Repay no one evil for evil , but have regard for what is noble in the sight of all .
45012018	If it is possible , as far as it depends on you , live peaceably with all .
45012019	Beloved , do not avenge yourselves , but leave it to the wrath of God ; for it is written , » Vengeance is mine , I will repay , « says the Lord .
45012020	No , » if your enemy is hungry , feed him ; if he is thirsty , give him drink ; for in so doing you will heap burning coals on his head . «
45012021	Do not be overcome by evil , but overcome evil with good .
45013001	Let every person be subject to the governing authorities . For there is no authority except from God , and the authorities that exist have been instituted by God .
45013002	Therefore he who resists the authority resists what God has appointed , and those who resist will bring judgment on themselves .
45013003	For rulers are not a terror to good works , but to evil . Do you want to have no fear of him who is in authority ? Then do what is good , and you will have praise from him .
45013004	For he is God's servant to you for good . But if you do wrong , be afraid , for he does not bear the sword in vain ; he is God’s servant , an avenger to execute wrath on the wrongdoer .
45013005	Therefore one must be subject , not only because of wrath but also for the sake of conscience .
45013006	For the same reason you also pay taxes , for the authorities are God's ministers , attending to this very thing .
45013007	Pay all of them their dues : taxes to whom taxes are due , revenue to whom revenue is due , respect to whom respect is due , honor to whom honor is due .
45013008	Owe no one anything , except to love one another ; for he who loves his neighbor has fulfilled the law .
45013009	The commandments , » You shall not commit adultery , « » You shall not murder , « » You shall not steal , « » You shall not covet , « and any other commandment there may be , are summed up in this sentence , » You shall love your neighbor as yourself . «
45013010	Love does no harm to a neighbor ; therefore love is the fulfillment of the law .
45013011	And do this , knowing the hour , that now it is full time for you to wake from sleep . For now our salvation is nearer than when we first believed .
45013012	The night is far gone , the day is at hand . Let us then cast off the works of darkness and put on the armor of light .
45013013	Let us walk properly , as in the day , not in reveling and drunkenness , not in lewdness and lust , not in quarreling and jealousy .
45013014	But put on the Lord Jesus Christ , and make no provision for the flesh , to gratify its desires .
45014001	As for the man who is weak in faith , accept him , but not for disputes over opinions .
45014002	One believes he may eat anything , but the man whose faith is weak eats only vegetables .
45014003	Let not him who eats despise him who does not , and let not him who does not eat pass judgment on him who eats ; for God has accepted him .
45014004	Who are you to judge the servant of another ? To his own master he stands or falls . And he will be made to stand , for the Master is able to make him stand .
45014005	One man esteems one day as better than another ; another man esteems every day alike . Let each one be fully convinced in his own mind .
45014006	He who observes the day , observes it to the Lord . He who eats , eats to the Lord , for he gives thanks to God ; and he who abstains , does so to the Lord and gives thanks to God .
45014007	For none of us lives to himself , and none of us dies to himself .
45014008	If we live , we live to the Lord ; and if we die , we die to the Lord . So then , whether we live or whether we die , we are the Lord's .
45014009	For to this end Christ died and lived again , that he might be Lord both of the dead and of the living .
45014010	Why do you judge your brother ? Or you , why do you despise your brother ? For we shall all stand before the judgment seat of God .
45014011	For it is written : » As I live , says the Lord , every knee shall bow to me , and every tongue shall confess to God . «
45014012	So then each of us shall give account of himself to God .
45014013	Therefore let us not pass judgment on one another anymore , but rather decide never to put a stumbling block or hindrance in our brother’s way .
45014014	I know and am convinced in the Lord Jesus that nothing is unclean in itself ; but if anyone regards something as unclean , then for him it is unclean .
45014015	If your brother is distressed because of what you eat , you are no longer walking in love . Do not by your eating destroy the one for whom Christ died .
45014016	So do not let your good be spoken of as evil .
45014017	For the kingdom of God is not eating and drinking , but righteousness and peace and joy in the Holy Spirit ;
45014018	he who serves Christ in this way is acceptable to God and approved by men .
45014019	Let us therefore pursue what makes for peace and for mutual edification .
45014020	Do not , for the sake of food , destroy the work of God . Everything is indeed clean , but it is wrong for a man to eat anything that causes someone else to stumble .
45014021	It is right not to eat meat or drink wine or do anything that makes your brother stumble .
45014022	The faith that you have , keep between yourself and God . Happy is he who does not condemn himself for what he approves .
45014023	But he who has doubts is condemned if he eats , because he does not act from faith ; for whatever is not from faith is sin .
45015001	We who are strong ought to bear with the failings of the weak , and not to please ourselves .
45015002	Let each of us please his neighbor for his good , to build him up .
45015003	For even Christ did not please himself ; but , as it is written , » The reproaches of those who reproached you fell on me . «
45015004	For whatever was written in former days was written for our instruction , that through perseverance and the encouragement of the scriptures we might have hope .
45015005	May the God of patience and encouragement grant you to live in harmony with one another , according to Christ Jesus ,
45015006	that you may with one mind and one mouth glorify the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ .
45015007	Therefore , welcome one another , just as Christ also welcomed you , to the glory of God .
45015008	For I tell you that Christ has become a servant of the circumcised to show God's truth , to confirm the promises made to the patriarchs ,
45015009	and in order that the Gentiles might glorify God for his mercy . As it is written : » Therefore I will praise you among the Gentiles , and sing to your name « ;
45015010	and again it says : » Rejoice , O Gentiles , with his people ! «
45015011	and again , » Praise the Lord , all you Gentiles , and praise him , all you peoples « ;
45015012	And again , Isaiah says : » There shall be a root of Jesse ; and he who shall rise to rule over the Gentiles , in him the Gentiles shall hope . «
45015013	May the God of hope fill you with all joy and peace in believing , so that by the power of the Holy Spirit you may abound in hope .
45015014	I myself am satisfied about you , my brethren , that you yourselves are full of goodness , filled with all knowledge , and able to instruct one another .
45015015	But I have written very boldly to you on some points , so as to remind you again , because of the grace that was given me from God ,
45015016	to be a minister of Christ Jesus to the Gentiles in the priestly service of the gospel of God , so that the offering of the Gentiles might be acceptable , sanctified by the Holy Spirit .
45015017	Therefore I have reason to glory in Christ Jesus in my service to God .
45015018	For I will not venture to speak of anything except what Christ has accomplished through me to win obedience from the Gentiles , by word and deed —
45015019	by the power of signs and wonders , by the power of the Spirit , so that from Jerusalem and as far round as Illyricum I have fully preached the gospel of Christ .
45015020	And so I have made it my ambition to preach the gospel , not where Christ has already been named , lest I build on another man's foundation ,
45015021	but as it is written : » They shall see who have not been told of him , and those who have not heard shall understand . «
45015022	This is the reason why I have often been hindered from coming to you .
45015023	But now , since I no longer have any place for work in these regions , and since I have longed for many years to come to you ,
45015024	I plan to do so when I go to Spain . I hope to see you while passing through , and to be helped by you on my journey there , after I have enjoyed your company for a while .
45015025	Now , however , I am going to Jerusalem with aid for the saints .
45015026	For Macedonia and Achaia have been pleased to make a contribution for the poor among the saints in Jerusalem .
45015027	They were pleased to do it , and indeed they are in debt to them . For if the Gentiles have come to share in their spiritual blessings , they ought also to be of service to them in material blessings .
45015028	When therefore I have completed this , and have delivered to them this fruit , I shall go on by way of you to Spain .
45015029	And I know that when I come to you , I shall come in the fullness of the blessing of Christ .
45015030	Now I urge you , brethren , by our Lord Jesus Christ and by the love of the Spirit , to strive together with me in your prayers to God for me ,
45015031	that I may be delivered from the unbelievers in Judea , and that my service for Jerusalem may be acceptable to the saints ,
45015032	so that by God's will I may come to you with joy , and together with you be refreshed .
45015033	The God of peace be with you all . Amen .
45016001	I commend to you Phoebe our sister , who is a servant of the church in Cenchrea ,
45016002	that you may receive her in the Lord in a manner worthy of the saints , and help her in whatever she has need from you , for she has been a helper of many and of myself also .
45016003	Greet Priscilla and Aquila , my fellow workers in Christ Jesus ,
45016004	who risked their necks for my life , to whom not only I but also all the churches of the Gentiles give thanks ;
45016005	greet also the church that meets in their house . Greet my beloved Epaenetus , who was the first convert of Asia for Christ .
45016006	Greet Mary , who has worked hard for you .
45016007	Greet Andronicus and Junias , my kinsmen and my fellow prisoners ; they are men of note among the apostles , and they were in Christ before me .
45016008	Greet Ampliatus , my beloved in the Lord .
45016009	Greet Urbanus , our fellow worker in Christ , and Stachys my beloved .
45016010	Greet Apelles , who is approved in Christ . Greet those who belong to the household of Aristobulus .
45016011	Greet Herodion , my kinsman . Greet those in the household of Narcissus who are in the Lord .
45016012	Greet Tryphena and Tryphosa , those workers in the Lord . Greet the beloved Persis , who has worked hard in the Lord .
45016013	Greet Rufus , chosen in the Lord , and his mother and mine .
45016014	Greet Asyncritus , Phlegon , Hermas , Patrobas , Hermes , and the brethren who are with them .
45016015	Greet Philologus and Julia , Nereus and his sister , and Olympas , and all the saints who are with them .
45016016	Greet one another with a holy kiss . All the churches of Christ greet you .
45016017	I urge you , brethren , to take note of those who cause divisions and difficulties , contrary to the doctrine which you have learned ; avoid them .
45016018	For such persons do not serve our Lord Christ , but their own appetites , and by smooth and flattering words they deceive the hearts of the simple .
45016019	For your obedience has become known to all , so I am full of joy over you ; but I want you to be wise about what is good , and innocent about what is evil .
45016020	And the God of peace will soon crush Satan under your feet . The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you .
45016021	Timothy , my fellow worker , greets you , as do Lucius , and Jason , and Sosipater , my kinsmen .
45016022	I , Tertius , who wrote this letter , greet you in the Lord .
45016023	Gaius , who is my host and the host of the whole church , greets you . Erastus , the treasurer of the city , greets you , and Quartus , our brother .
45016025	Now to him who is able to establish you according to my gospel and the preaching of Jesus Christ , according to the revelation of the mystery which was kept secret for long ages
45016026	but is now revealed and made known to all nations through the prophetic writings , according to the command of the eternal God , to bring about the obedience of faith —
45016027	to the only wise God be glory forever through Jesus Christ ! Amen .
46001001	Paul , called to be an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God , and our brother Sosthenes ,
46001002	to the church of God which is at Corinth , to those sanctified in Christ Jesus , called to be saints together with all those who in every place call on the name of our Lord Jesus Christ , both their Lord and ours :
46001003	grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
46001004	I thank my God always for you because of the grace of God which was given you in Christ Jesus ,
46001005	that in every way you were enriched in him in all speech and all knowledge —
46001006	even as the testimony of Christ was confirmed in you ,
46001007	so that you are not lacking in any spiritual gift , as you eagerly wait for the revealing of our Lord Jesus Christ ;
46001008	who will also confirm you to the end , blameless in the day of our Lord Jesus Christ .
46001009	God is faithful , by whom you were called into fellowship with his Son , Jesus Christ our Lord .
46001010	I appeal to you , brethren , by the name of our Lord Jesus Christ , that all of you agree and that there be no divisions among you , but that you be united in the same mind and in the same judgment .
46001011	For I have been informed by Chloe's people , that there are quarrels among you , my brethren .
46001012	What I mean is this , that each one of you says , » I am of Paul , « and » I of Apollos , « and » I of Cephas , « and » I of Christ . «
46001013	Is Christ divided ? Was Paul crucified for you ? Or were you baptized in the name of Paul ?
46001014	I am thankful that I baptized none of you except Crispus and Gaius ,
46001015	so that no one would say you were baptized in my name .
46001016	( Now I did baptize also the household of Stephanas ; beyond that , I do not know whether I baptized any one else . )
46001017	For Christ did not send me to baptize , but to preach the gospel — not with words of human wisdom , lest the cross of Christ be emptied of its power .
46001018	For the word of the cross is foolishness to those who are perishing , but to us who are being saved it is the power of God .
46001019	For it is written , » I will destroy the wisdom of the wise , and the cleverness of the clever I will frustrate . «
46001020	Where is the wise man ? Where is the scribe ? Where is the debater of this age ? Has not God made foolish the wisdom of the world ?
46001021	For since in the wisdom of God the world through its wisdom did not know God , God was pleased through the foolishness of what was preached to save those who believe .
46001022	Jews demand signs and Greeks look for wisdom ,
46001023	but we preach Christ crucified , to Jews a stumbling block and to Gentiles foolishness ,
46001024	but to those who are the called , both Jews and Greeks , Christ the power of God and the wisdom of God .
46001025	For the foolishness of God is wiser than men , and the weakness of God is stronger than men .
46001026	For consider your call , brethren ; not many of you were wise according to fleshly standards , not many were powerful , not many were of noble birth .
46001027	But God chose the foolish things of the world to shame the wise , God chose the weak things of the world to shame the strong ,
46001028	God chose the lowly things of this world and the despised things , and the things that are not , to nullify the things that are ,
46001029	so that no flesh may boast before God .
46001030	It is because of him that you are in Christ Jesus , who became to us wisdom from God , and righteousness and sanctification , and redemption ,
46001031	therefore , as it is written , » Let him who boasts , boast in the Lord . «
46002001	When I came to you , brethren , I did not come with superiority of speech or of wisdom , proclaiming to you the testimony of God .
46002002	For I resolved to know nothing among you except Jesus Christ , and him crucified .
46002003	I was with you in weakness and in fear and in much trembling ,
46002004	and my message and my preaching were not in persuasive words of wisdom , but in demonstration of the Spirit and of power ,
46002005	so that your faith might not rest on the wisdom of men , but on the power of God .
46002006	Yet we do speak a wisdom among the mature , a wisdom , however , not of this age nor of the rulers of this age , who are passing away .
46002007	But we speak of God's secret wisdom , a wisdom that has been hidden and which God destined for our glory before the ages .
46002008	None of the rulers of this age understood it ; for if they had , they would not have crucified the Lord of glory .
46002009	But , as it is written , » No eye has seen , nor ear heard , nor the heart of man conceived what God has prepared for those who love him , «
46002010	God has revealed them to us through the Spirit . For the Spirit searches all things , even the depths of God .
46002011	For who among men knows the thoughts of a man except the man's spirit which is in him ? Even so no one knows the thoughts of God except the Spirit of God .
46002012	Now we have received not the spirit of the world , but the Spirit who is from God , that we may understand the things freely given to us by God .
46002013	This is what we speak , not in words taught us by human wisdom but in words taught by the Spirit , expressing spiritual truths in spiritual words .
46002014	But the natural man does not accept the things of the Spirit of God , for they are foolishness to him ; and he cannot understand them , because they are spiritually discerned .
46002015	But the spiritual man judges all things , yet he himself is rightly judged by no one .
46002016	
46003001	But I , brethren , could not address you as spiritual men , but as carnal men , as infants in Christ .
46003002	I gave you milk , not solid food ; for you were not yet ready for it . Indeed , even now you are not ready ,
46003003	for you are still carnal . For since there is jealousy and strife among you , are you not carnal , and are you not walking like mere men ?
46003004	For when one says , » I am of Paul , « and another , » I am of Apollos , « are you not mere men ?
46003005	What then is Apollos ? And what is Paul ? Servants through whom you believed , even as the Lord assigned to each one .
46003006	I planted , Apollos watered , but God was causing the growth .
46003007	So neither he who plants nor he who waters is anything , but only God who gives the growth .
46003008	Now he who plants and he who waters are one , and each will receive his own reward according to his own labor .
46003009	For we are God's fellow workers ; you are God’s field , God’s building .
46003010	According to the grace of God which was given to me , like a wise master builder I laid a foundation , and another is building on it . But each man must be careful how he builds on it .
46003011	For no other foundation can any one lay than the one which is laid , which is Jesus Christ .
46003012	Now if any man builds on the foundation with gold , silver , precious stones , wood , hay , straw ,
46003013	each man's work will become evident ; for the day will show it , because it is to be revealed with fire , and the fire itself will test the quality of each man’s work .
46003014	If any man's work which he has built on it survives , he will receive a reward .
46003015	If any man's work is burned up , he will suffer loss ; but he himself will be saved , but only as through fire .
46003016	Do you not know that you are God's temple and that God’s Spirit dwells in you ?
46003017	If any one destroys God's temple , God will destroy him . For God’s temple is holy , and that temple you are .
46003018	Let no one deceive himself . If any one among you thinks that he is wise in this age , he must become a fool so that he may become wise .
46003019	For the wisdom of this world is foolishness with God . For it is written , » He catches the wise in their own craftiness « ;
46003020	and again , » The Lord knows the thoughts of the wise , that they are futile . «
46003021	So then let no one boast of men . For all things are yours ,
46003022	whether Paul or Apollos or Cephas or the world or life or death or the present or the future ; all belong to you ,
46003023	and you belong to Christ ; and Christ belongs to God .
46004001	This is how one should regard us , as servants of Christ and stewards of the mysteries of God .
46004002	Moreover it is required of stewards that they be found trustworthy .
46004003	But with me it is a very small thing that I should be judged by you , or by any human court ; I do not even judge myself .
46004004	I am not aware of anything against myself , but I am not acquitted by this . It is the Lord who judges me .
46004005	Therefore do not go on passing judgment before the time , but wait until the Lord comes who will both bring to light the things hidden in the darkness and disclose the motives of men's hearts . Then every man will receive his praise from God .
46004006	Now these things , brethren , I have figuratively applied to myself and Apollos for your benefit , so that in us you may learn not to go beyond what is written , so that no one of you will become arrogant in favor of one against the other .
46004007	For who regards you as different ? What do you have that you did not receive ? And if you did receive it , why do you boast as if you had not received it ?
46004008	You are already filled ! You have already become rich ! You have become kings without us ! And indeed , I wish that you had become kings so that we also might reign with you .
46004009	For , I think that God has exhibited us apostles last of all , like men condemned to death ; because we have become a spectacle to the world , both to angels and to men .
46004010	We are fools for Christ's sake , but you are wise in Christ ; we are weak , but you are strong ; you are distinguished , but we are without honor .
46004011	To this present hour we are both hungry and thirsty , and we are poorly clothed , and roughly treated , and homeless ;
46004012	and we toil , working with our own hands . When we are reviled , we bless ; when we are persecuted , we endure ;
46004013	when we are slandered , we try to conciliate ; we have become , and are now , as the scum of the world , the refuse of all things .
46004014	I do not write this to shame you , but to admonish you as my beloved children .
46004015	For though you have countless guides in Christ , you do not have many fathers , for in Christ Jesus I became your father through the gospel .
46004016	Therefore I urge you , be imitators of me .
46004017	For this reason I have sent to you Timothy , who is my beloved and faithful child in the Lord , and he will remind you of my ways which are in Christ , just as I teach everywhere in every church .
46004018	Now some have become arrogant , as though I were not coming to you .
46004019	But I will come to you soon , if the Lord wills , and I will find out , not the words of these arrogant people , but their power .
46004020	For the kingdom of God does not consist in talk but in power .
46004021	What do you desire ? Shall I come to you with a rod , or with love and a spirit of gentleness ?
46005001	It is actually reported that there is immorality among you , and of a kind that does not occur even among pagans : a man has his father's wife .
46005002	And you are arrogant ! Ought you not rather to have mourned ? Let the one who has done this be removed from your midst .
46005003	For though I am absent in body , I am present in spirit , and have already passed judgment on the one who has committed this , as if I were present .
46005004	In the name of our Lord Jesus , when you are assembled , and I with you in spirit , and the power of our Lord Jesus is present ,
46005005	you are to deliver this man to Satan for the destruction of the flesh , so that his spirit may be saved in the day of the Lord Jesus .
46005006	Your boasting is not good . Do you not know that a little leaven leavens the whole lump of dough ?
46005007	Cleanse out the old leaven that you may be a new lump , as you really are unleavened . For Christ , our Passover lamb , has been sacrificed .
46005008	Let us , therefore , celebrate the festival , not with the old leaven , the leaven of malice and wickedness , but with the unleavened bread of sincerity and truth .
46005009	I wrote you in my letter not to associate with immoral people ;
46005010	not at all meaning the immoral people of this world , or with the greedy and swindlers , or with idolaters , for then you would have to go out of the world .
46005011	But actually , I wrote to you not to associate with any one who bears the name of brother if he is an immoral person , or greedy , or an idolater , or a reviler , or a drunkard , or a swindler — not even to eat with such a one .
46005012	For what have I to do with judging outsiders ? Is it not those inside the church whom you are to judge ?
46005013	God judges those outside . » Expel the wicked man from among you . «
46006001	When any one of you has a grievance against a brother , does he dare go to law before the unrighteous instead of before the saints ?
46006002	Do you not know that the saints will judge the world ? And if the world is to be judged by you , are you not competent to try trivial cases ?
46006003	Do you not know that we will judge angels ? How much more matters of this life !
46006004	So if you have disputes about such matters , do you appoint them as judges who are of no account in the church ?
46006005	I say this to your shame . Can it be that there is no man among you wise enough to decide between his brethren ,
46006006	but brother goes to law against brother , and that before unbelievers ?
46006007	Actually , then , it is already a defeat for you , that you have lawsuits with one another . Why not rather be wronged ? Why not rather be defrauded ?
46006008	Instead , you yourselves defraud and do wrong , and you even do this to your brethren .
46006009	Or do you not know that the unrighteous will not inherit the kingdom of God ? Do not be deceived ; neither the immoral , nor idolaters , nor adulterers , nor sexual perverts ,
46006010	nor thieves , nor the greedy , nor drunkards , nor revilers , nor swindlers will inherit the kingdom of God .
46006011	And such were some of you . But you were washed , you were sanctified , you were justified in the name of the Lord Jesus Christ and in the Spirit of our God .
46006012	» All things are lawful for me , « but not all things are helpful . » All things are lawful for me , « but I will not be mastered by anything .
46006013	» Food is for the stomach and the stomach for food « — but God will destroy them both . The body is not meant for immorality , but for the Lord , and the Lord for the body .
46006014	By his power God raised the Lord , and he will also raise us up .
46006015	Do you not know that your bodies are members of Christ ? Shall I then take the members of Christ and make them members of a prostitute ? Never !
46006016	Or do you not know that he who joins himself to a prostitute becomes one body with her ? For , as it is written , » The two shall become one flesh . «
46006017	But he who unites himself with the Lord is one spirit with him .
46006018	Flee immorality . Every other sin that a man commits is outside the body , but the immoral man sins against his own body .
46006019	Do you not know that your body is a temple of the Holy Spirit , who is in you , whom you have received from God ? You are not your own ;
46006020	you were bought with a price . Therefore glorify God in your body .
46007001	Now concerning the matters about which you wrote , it is good for a man not to touch a woman .
46007002	But because of immorality , each man should have his own wife , and each woman her own husband .
46007003	The husband should fulfill his marital duty to his wife , and likewise the wife to her husband .
46007004	The wife does not have authority over her own body , but the husband does ; and likewise also the husband does not have authority over his own body , but the wife does .
46007005	Do not deprive one another , except by agreement for a time , so that you may devote yourselves to prayer , and then come together again so that Satan will not tempt you because of your lack of self-control .
46007006	I say this by way of concession , not of command .
46007007	I wish that all men were as I myself am . But each man has his own gift from God , one in this manner and another in that .
46007008	But I say to the unmarried and to the widows that it is good for them if they remain even as I .
46007009	But if they cannot exercise self-control , they should marry ; for it is better to marry than to burn with passion .
46007010	To the married I give charge , not I but the Lord , that the wife should not separate from her husband
46007011	( but if she does leave , she must remain unmarried , or else be reconciled to her husband ) , and that the husband should not divorce his wife .
46007012	But to the rest I say , not the Lord , that if any brother has a wife who is an unbeliever , and she consents to live with him , he must not divorce her .
46007013	If any woman has a husband who is an unbeliever , and he consents to live with her , she must not divorce him .
46007014	For the unbelieving husband is sanctified through his wife , and the unbelieving wife is sanctified through her husband . Otherwise , your children would be unclean , but as it is they are holy .
46007015	But if the unbelieving partner leaves , let him do so ; in such a case the brother or sister is not bound . For God has called us to peace .
46007016	For how do you know , O wife , whether you will save your husband ? Or how do you know , O husband , whether you will save your wife ?
46007017	Only , let each one lead the life which the Lord has assigned to him , and in which God has called him . This is the rule I lay down in all the churches .
46007018	Was any man called when he was already circumcised ? He is not to become uncircumcised . Has anyone been called in uncircumcision ? He is not to be circumcised .
46007019	Circumcision is nothing and uncircumcision is nothing , but keeping the commandments of God is what counts .
46007020	Each one should remain in the state in which he was called .
46007021	Were you a slave when you were called ? Do not let it trouble you — but if you can gain your freedom , do so .
46007022	For he who was called in the Lord as a slave is the Lord's freedman ; likewise he who was free when called is Christ's slave .
46007023	You were bought with a price ; do not become slaves of men .
46007024	Brethren , let each one remain with God in that condition in which he was called .
46007025	Now concerning virgins , I have no command of the Lord , but I give my opinion as one who by the Lord's mercy is trustworthy .
46007026	I think that in view of the present distress it is good for a person to remain as he is .
46007027	Are you bound to a wife ? Do not seek to be free . Are you free from a wife ? Do not seek marriage .
46007028	But if you marry , you have not sinned ; and if a virgin marries , she has not sinned . Yet those who marry will have troubles in this flesh , and I am trying to spare you .
46007029	I mean , brethren , the appointed time has grown very short ; so that from now on , those who have wives should live as though they had none ,
46007030	and those who mourn , as though they were not mourning ; and those who rejoice , as though they were not rejoicing ; and those who buy , as though they did not possess ;
46007031	and those who use the world , as though they did not make full use of it . For the form of this world is passing away .
46007032	But I want you to be free from concern . One who is unmarried is concerned about the affairs of the Lord , how he may please the Lord ;
46007033	but a married man is concerned about the affairs of the world , how he may please his wife ,
46007034	and his interests are divided . The unmarried woman , and the virgin , is concerned about the affairs of the Lord , that she may be holy both in body and spirit ; but the married woman is concerned about the affairs of the world , how she may please her husband .
46007035	This I say for your own benefit , not to put a restraint upon you , but to promote what is good and to secure undivided devotion to the Lord .
46007036	But if any man thinks that he is not acting properly toward his betrothed , if she is past her youth , and if it must be so , let him do what he wishes , he does not sin ; let them marry .
46007037	But he who stands firm in his heart , being under no constraint , but has control over his own will , and has decided this in his own heart , to keep her as his betrothed , he will do well .
46007038	So then he who marries his betrothed does well , and he who does not marry her will do better .
46007039	A wife is bound to her husband as long as he lives . But if her husband dies , she is free to be married to whom she wishes , only in the Lord .
46007040	But in my judgment she is happier if she remains as she is ; and I think that I also have the Spirit of God .
46008001	Now concerning food sacrificed to idols : we know that we all possess knowledge . Knowledge puffs up , but love builds up .
46008002	If anyone imagines that he knows something , he does not yet know as he ought to know .
46008003	But if anyone loves God , he is known by him .
46008004	Therefore concerning the eating of food sacrificed to idols , we know that an idol is nothing in the world , and that there is no God but one .
46008005	For even if there are so-called gods , whether in heaven or on earth ( as indeed there are many » gods « and many » lords « ) ,
46008006	yet for us there is but one God , the Father , from whom are all things and for whom we exist ; and one Lord , Jesus Christ , through whom are all things , and through whom we exist .
46008007	However , not all possess this knowledge . But some , being accustomed to idols , eat food as really sacrificed to an idol ; and their conscience , being weak , is defiled .
46008008	But food will not commend us to God ; we are no worse if we do not eat , and no better if we do .
46008009	But take care that this liberty of yours does not somehow become a stumbling block to the weak .
46008010	For if a man sees you , who have knowledge , at table in an idol's temple , will not his conscience , if he is weak , be encouraged to eat food sacrificed to idols ?
46008011	And so by your knowledge this weak man is destroyed , the brother for whom Christ died .
46008012	Thus , sinning against your brethren and wounding their conscience when it is weak , you sin against Christ .
46008013	Therefore , if food causes my brother to fall , I will never eat meat again , so that I will not cause my brother to fall .
46009001	Am I not free ? Am I not an apostle ? Have I not seen Jesus our Lord ? Are you not my work in the Lord ?
46009002	If to others I am not an apostle , at least I am to you ; for you are the seal of my apostleship in the Lord .
46009003	This is my defense to those who would examine me .
46009004	Do we not have the right to food and drink ?
46009005	Do we not have a right to take along a believing wife , even as the other apostles and the brothers of the Lord and Cephas ?
46009006	Or is it only Barnabas and I who have no right to refrain from working for a living ?
46009007	Who at any time serves as a soldier at his own expense ? Who plants a vineyard and does not eat of its fruit ? Who tends a flock and does not drink of the milk ?
46009008	Do I say this merely from a human point of view ? Does not the Law say the same thing ?
46009009	For it is written in the Law of Moses , » You shall not muzzle an ox while it is treading out the grain . « Is it for oxen that God is concerned ?
46009010	Or is he speaking altogether for our sake ? Yes , for our sake it was written , because the plowman ought to plow in hope , and the thresher to thresh in hope of sharing the crops .
46009011	If we have sown spiritual seed among you , is it too much if we reap a material harvest from you ?
46009012	If others share this right of support from you , do not we all the more ? Nevertheless , we did not make use of this right , but we endure anything rather than put an obstacle in the way of the gospel of Christ .
46009013	Do you not know that those who work in the temple get their food from the temple , and those who serve at the altar share in what is offered on the altar ?
46009014	In the same way , the Lord commanded that those who proclaim the gospel should get their living from the gospel .
46009015	But I have not used any of these rights . And I am not writing this in the hope that you will do such things for me . I would rather die than have anyone deprive me of my ground for boasting .
46009016	For if I preach the gospel , I have nothing to boast of , for I am under compulsion . For woe is me if I do not preach the gospel !
46009017	For if I do this voluntarily , I have a reward ; but if it is not of my will , I have a stewardship entrusted to me .
46009018	What then is my reward ? Just this : that in my preaching I may offer the gospel free of charge , and so not make full use of my right in the gospel .
46009019	For though I am free from all men , I have made myself a slave to all , that I might win the more .
46009020	To the Jews I became as a Jew , in order to win Jews ; to those under the law I became as one under the law — though not being myself under the law — so that I might win those under the law .
46009021	To those who are without law , I became as one without law , though not being without the law of God but under the law of Christ , so that I might win those who are without the law .
46009022	To the weak I became weak , that I might win the weak . I have become all things to all men , so that I might by all means save some .
46009023	I do it all for the sake of the gospel , that I may share in its blessings .
46009024	Do you not know that in a race all the runners run , but only one receives the prize ? Run in such a way that you may win .
46009025	Everyone who competes in the games exercises self-control in all things . They do it to receive a perishable wreath , but we an imperishable .
46009026	Therefore I do not run aimlessly . I do not box as a man beating the air .
46009027	But I discipline my body and make it my slave , so that , after I have preached to others , I myself will not be disqualified .
46010001	For I do not want you to be unaware , brethren , that our fathers were all under the cloud and all passed through the sea ;
46010002	and all were baptized into Moses in the cloud and in the sea ;
46010003	and all ate the same spiritual food ;
46010004	and all drank the same spiritual drink , for they drank from a spiritual rock which followed them ; and the rock was Christ .
46010005	Nevertheless , with most of them God was not pleased ; for they were overthrown in the wilderness .
46010006	Now these things are examples for us , not to desire evil things as they did .
46010007	Do not be idolaters , as some of them were ; as it is written , » The people sat down to eat and drink , and stood up to play . «
46010008	We must not indulge in immorality as some of them did , and twenty-three thousand fell in one day .
46010009	We must not put the Lord to the test , as some of them did and were destroyed by serpents .
46010010	Nor grumble , as some of them did , and were destroyed by the destroyer .
46010011	Now these things happened to them as an example , and they were written down for our instruction , upon whom the ends of the ages have come .
46010012	Therefore let any one who thinks that he stands take heed lest he fall .
46010013	No temptation has overtaken you but such as is common to man . And God is faithful , who will not let you be tempted beyond what you are able , but with the temptation will provide the way of escape also , so that you will be able to endure it .
46010014	Therefore , my beloved , flee from idolatry .
46010015	I speak as to sensible men ; judge for yourselves what I say .
46010016	The cup of blessing which we bless , is it not a participation in the blood of Christ ? The bread which we break , is it not a participation in the body of Christ ?
46010017	Because there is one bread , we who are many are one body , for we all partake of the one bread .
46010018	Consider Israel after the flesh ; are not those who eat the sacrifices partners in the altar ?
46010019	What do I mean then ? That a thing offered to idols is anything , or that an idol is anything ?
46010020	No , but I say that the things pagans sacrifice they offer to demons and not to God . I do not want you to be partners with demons .
46010021	You cannot drink the cup of the Lord and the cup of demons . You cannot partake of the table of the Lord and the table of demons .
46010022	Are we trying to provoke the Lord to jealousy ? Are we stronger than he ?
46010023	» All things are lawful , « but not all things are helpful . » All things are lawful , « but not all things build up .
46010024	Let no one seek his own good , but the good of his neighbor .
46010025	Eat anything that is sold in the meat market without raising questions of conscience ;
46010026	for , » The earth is the Lord's , and everything in it . «
46010027	If one of the unbelievers invites you to dinner and you want to go , eat whatever is set before you without raising questions of conscience .
46010028	But if anyone says to you , » This has been offered in sacrifice , « then do not eat it , both for the sake of the man who informed you and for conscience' sake —
46010029	the other man's conscience , I mean , not yours . For why should my freedom be judged by another's conscience ?
46010030	If I partake with thankfulness , why am I denounced because of that for which I give thanks ?
46010031	So , whether you eat or drink , or whatever you do , do all to the glory of God .
46010032	Give no offense either to Jews or to Greeks or to the church of God ,
46010033	just as I try to please all men in everything I do , not seeking my own advantage , but that of many , that they may be saved .
46011001	Be imitators of me , as I am of Christ .
46011002	I praise you because you remember me in everything and hold firmly to the traditions , just as I delivered them to you .
46011003	But I want you to understand that Christ is the head of every man , and the man is the head of a woman , and God is the head of Christ .
46011004	Every man who prays or prophesies with his head covered dishonors his head .
46011005	But every woman who prays or prophesies with her head uncovered dishonors her head — it is the same as if her head were shaved .
46011006	For if a woman does not cover her head , she should have her hair cut off ; but if it is disgraceful for a woman to have her hair cut or shaved off , let her cover her head .
46011007	For a man ought not to cover his head , since he is the image and glory of God ; but the woman is the glory of man .
46011008	For man does not originate from woman , but woman from man ;
46011009	neither was man created for woman , but woman for man .
46011010	Therefore the woman ought to have a symbol of authority on her head , because of the angels .
46011011	In the Lord , however , woman is not independent of man , nor is man independent of woman .
46011012	For as woman was made from man , so also man is born of woman . And all things are from God .
46011013	Judge for yourselves : is it proper for a woman to pray to God with her head uncovered ?
46011014	Does not even nature itself teach you that if a man has long hair , it is a dishonor to him ,
46011015	but if a woman has long hair , it is her glory ? For her hair is given to her for a covering .
46011016	If anyone wants to be contentious , we have no other practice , nor do the churches of God .
46011017	But in the following instructions , I do not praise you , because you come together not for the better but for the worse .
46011018	For , in the first place , when you come together as a church , I hear that there are divisions among you ; and I partly believe it .
46011019	For there must be factions among you in order that those who are genuine among you may be recognized .
46011020	Therefore when you meet together , it is not the Lord's supper that you eat ,
46011021	for in eating , each one goes ahead with his own meal , and one is hungry and another is drunk .
46011022	What ! Do you not have houses to eat and drink in ? Or do you despise the church of God and humiliate those who have nothing ? What shall I say to you ? Shall I praise you in this ? No , I will not .
46011023	For I received from the Lord what I also delivered to you , that the Lord Jesus on the night when he was betrayed took bread ,
46011024	and when he had given thanks , he broke it and said , » This is my body , which is for you ; do this in remembrance of me . «
46011025	In the same way he took the cup also after supper , saying , » This cup is the new covenant in my blood ; do this , as often as you drink it , in remembrance of me . «
46011026	For as often as you eat this bread and drink the cup , you proclaim the Lord's death until he comes .
46011027	Whoever , therefore , eats the bread or drinks the cup of the Lord in an unworthy manner will be guilty of profaning the body and blood of the Lord .
46011028	Let a man examine himself , and so eat of the bread and drink of the cup .
46011029	For anyone who eats and drinks without recognizing the body eats and drinks judgment on himself .
46011030	That is why many among you are weak and sick , and a number of you have fallen asleep .
46011031	But if we judged ourselves rightly , we would not be judged .
46011032	But when we are judged , we are disciplined by the Lord so that we will not be condemned along with the world .
46011033	So then , my brethren , when you come together to eat , wait for one another .
46011034	If anyone is hungry , let him eat at home , so that you will not come together for judgment . About the other things I will give directions when I come .
46012001	Now concerning spiritual gifts , brethren , I do not want you to be uninformed .
46012002	You know that when you were pagans , you were led astray to mute idols , however you may have been moved .
46012003	Therefore I tell you that no one who is speaking by the Spirit of God says , » Jesus be cursed , « and no one can say , » Jesus is Lord , « except by the Holy Spirit .
46012004	Now there are varieties of gifts , but the same Spirit .
46012005	And there are varieties of service , but the same Lord .
46012006	There are varieties of working , but the same God who works all of them in all men .
46012007	But to each one is given the manifestation of the Spirit for the common good .
46012008	To one is given through the Spirit the word of wisdom , and to another the word of knowledge according to the same Spirit ,
46012009	to another faith by the same Spirit , to another gifts of healing by the one Spirit ,
46012010	and to another the working of miracles , and to another prophecy , and to another distinguishing between spirits , to another various kinds of tongues , and to another the interpretation of tongues .
46012011	But one and the same Spirit works all these things , distributing to each one individually just as he wills .
46012012	For just as the body is one and has many members , and all the members of the body , though they are many , are one body , so it is with Christ .
46012013	For by one Spirit we were all baptized into one body — whether Jews or Greeks , slaves or free — and we were all made to drink of one Spirit .
46012014	For the body is not made up of one member but of many .
46012015	If the foot should say , » Because I am not a hand , I do not belong to the body , « it would not for that reason be any less a part of the body .
46012016	And if the ear should say , » Because I am not an eye , I do not belong to the body , « it would not for that reason be any less a part of the body .
46012017	If the whole body were an eye , where would be the hearing ? If the whole body were an ear , where would be the sense of smell ?
46012018	But now God has arranged the members in the body , each one of them , just as he desired .
46012019	If they were all one member , where would the body be ?
46012020	As it is , there are many parts , but one body .
46012021	And the eye cannot say to the hand , » I have no need of you , « nor again the head to the feet , » I have no need of you . «
46012022	On the contrary , the parts of the body that seem to be weaker are indispensable ,
46012023	and those parts of the body which we think less honorable we treat with the greater honor , and our unpresentable parts are treated with greater modesty ,
46012024	while our more presentable members have no need of it . But God has so composed the body , giving the greater honor to the parts that lacked it ,
46012025	so that there may be no division in the body , but that the members may have the same care for one another .
46012026	And if one member suffers , all the members suffer with it ; if one member is honored , all the members rejoice with it .
46012027	Now you are the body of Christ , and individually members of it .
46012028	And God has appointed in the church first apostles , second prophets , third teachers , then workers of miracles , then those having gifts of healings , helps , administrations , and those speaking in various kinds of tongues .
46012029	Are all apostles ? Are all prophets ? Are all teachers ? Do all work miracles ?
46012030	Do all have gifts of healing ? Do all speak with tongues ? Do all interpret ?
46012031	But earnestly desire the greater gifts . And I will show you a still more excellent way .
46013001	If I speak in the tongues of men and of angels , but have not love , I am a noisy gong or a clanging cymbal .
46013002	If I have the gift of prophecy , and understand all mysteries and all knowledge ; and if I have all faith , so as to remove mountains , but have not love , I am nothing .
46013003	If I give all I have to the poor , and if I surrender my body to be burned , but have not love , I gain nothing .
46013004	Love is patient , love is kind . It is not jealous or boastful , it is not arrogant
46013005	or rude , it does not seek its own , it is not provoked , it keeps no record of wrongs ,
46013006	it does not rejoice in evil , but rejoices with the truth .
46013007	Love bears all things , believes all things , hopes all things , endures all things .
46013008	Love never fails ; but where there are prophecies , they will cease ; where there are tongues , they will be stilled ; where there is knowledge , it will pass away .
46013009	For we know in part and we prophesy in part ;
46013010	but when the perfect comes , the partial will pass away .
46013011	When I was a child , I spoke like a child , I thought like a child , I reasoned like a child ; when I became a man , I put childish ways behind me .
46013012	For now we see in a mirror dimly , but then face to face . Now I know in part , but then I shall know fully — even as I have been fully known .
46013013	So now faith , hope , love abide , these three ; but the greatest of these is love .
46014001	Pursue love , and earnestly desire the spiritual gifts , especially that you may prophesy .
46014002	For one who speaks in a tongue does not speak to men but to God ; for no one understands him , but in his spirit he speaks mysteries .
46014003	But everyone who prophesies speaks to men for their edification and encouragement and comfort .
46014004	He who speaks in a tongue edifies himself , but he who prophesies edifies the church .
46014005	Now I want you all to speak in tongues , but even more that you would prophesy . He who prophesies is greater than he who speaks in tongues , unless some one interprets , so that the church may be edified .
46014006	But now , brethren , if I come to you speaking in tongues , what will I profit you unless I bring you some revelation or knowledge or prophecy or teaching ?
46014007	If even lifeless things , such as the flute or the harp , do not give a distinction in the notes , how will any one know what is played ?
46014008	And if the bugle gives an indistinct sound , who will get ready for battle ?
46014009	So it is with you , unless you utter by the tongue speech that is intelligible , how will anyone know what is spoken ? For you will be speaking into the air .
46014010	Undoubtedly there are many languages in the world , and none of them is without meaning .
46014011	If then I do not know the meaning of the language , I will be a foreigner to the one who is speaking , and the speaker will be a foreigner to me .
46014012	So it is with you ; since you are eager for spiritual gifts , strive to excel in building up the church .
46014013	Therefore , he who speaks in a tongue should pray that he may interpret .
46014014	For if I pray in a tongue , my spirit prays , but my mind is unfruitful .
46014015	What am I to do ? I will pray with the spirit and I will pray with the mind also ; I will sing with the spirit and I will sing with the mind also .
46014016	Otherwise , if you bless with the spirit , how can any one in the position of an outsider say the » Amen « to your thanksgiving , since he does not know what you are saying ?
46014017	For you may be giving thanks well enough , but the other man is not edified .
46014018	I thank God that I speak in tongues more than you all ;
46014019	but in the church I would rather speak five words with my mind , to instruct others , than ten thousand words in a tongue .
46014020	Brethren , do not be children in your thinking ; be infants in evil , but in thinking be mature .
46014021	In the law it is written , » By men of strange tongues and by the lips of foreigners will I speak to this people , and even then they will not listen to me , says the Lord . «
46014022	Tongues , then , are a sign , not for believers but for unbelievers ; but prophecy is for believers , not for unbelievers .
46014023	Therefore if the whole church assembles together and all speak in tongues , and outsiders or unbelievers enter , will they not say that you are mad ?
46014024	But if all prophesy , and an unbeliever or an outsider enters , he is convicted by all , he is called to account by all ;
46014025	the secrets of his heart are disclosed ; and so , he will fall on his face , and worship God , declaring that God is really among you .
46014026	What is the outcome then , brethren ? When you come together , each one has a hymn , or a teaching , or a revelation , or a tongue , or an interpretation . Let all things be done for edification .
46014027	If anyone speaks in a tongue , it should be by two or at the most three , and each in turn ; and one must interpret .
46014028	But if there is no interpreter , he must keep silent in the church ; and let him speak to himself and to God .
46014029	Let two or three prophets speak , and let the others weigh what is said .
46014030	But if a revelation is made to another who is sitting , the first one must keep silent .
46014031	For you can all prophesy one by one , so that all may learn and all be encouraged ;
46014032	and the spirits of prophets are subject to prophets .
46014033	For God is not a God of confusion but of peace . As in all the churches of the saints ,
46014034	the women should keep silent in the churches . For they are not permitted to speak , but should be submissive , as even the law says .
46014035	If they desire to learn anything , let them ask their own husbands at home ; for it is shameful for a woman to speak in church .
46014036	Did the word of God originate with you ? Or are you the only people it has reached ?
46014037	If anyone thinks he is a prophet or spiritual , let him acknowledge that what I am writing to you is the Lord's command .
46014038	But if anyone does not recognize this , he is not recognized .
46014039	Therefore , my brethren , desire earnestly to prophesy , and do not forbid speaking in tongues .
46014040	But all things should be done decently and in an orderly way .
46015001	Now I would remind you , brethren , of the gospel I preached to you , which you received , in which you stand ,
46015002	by which also you are saved , if you hold fast the word which I preached to you , unless you believed in vain .
46015003	For I delivered to you as of first importance what I also received , that Christ died for our sins according to the Scriptures ,
46015004	that he was buried , that he was raised on the third day according to the Scriptures ,
46015005	and that he appeared to Cephas , then to the twelve .
46015006	After that he appeared to more than five hundred brethren at one time , most of whom are still alive , though some have fallen asleep .
46015007	Then he appeared to James , then to all the apostles .
46015008	And last of all , as to one untimely born , he appeared to me also .
46015009	For I am the least of the apostles , and not fit to be called an apostle , because I persecuted the church of God .
46015010	But by the grace of God I am what I am , and his grace toward me was not in vain . No , I worked harder than all of them — yet not I , but the grace of God that was with me .
46015011	Whether then it was I or they , so we preach and so you believed .
46015012	Now if Christ is preached that he has been raised from the dead , how can some of you say that there is no resurrection of the dead ?
46015013	But if there is no resurrection of the dead , then not even Christ has been raised ;
46015014	if Christ has not been raised , then our preaching is in vain and so is your faith .
46015015	More than that , we are even found to be false witnesses of God , because we testified against God that he raised Christ , whom he did not raise , if in fact the dead are not raised .
46015016	For if the dead are not raised , then Christ has not been raised .
46015017	And if Christ has not been raised , your faith is futile ; you are still in your sins .
46015018	Then those also who have fallen asleep in Christ have perished .
46015019	If for this life only we have hoped in Christ , we are of all men most to be pitied .
46015020	But Christ has indeed been raised from the dead , the first fruits of those who have fallen asleep .
46015021	For since by a man came death , by a man came also the resurrection of the dead .
46015022	For as in Adam all die , so also in Christ all will be made alive .
46015023	But each in his own order : Christ the first fruits , then , at his coming , those who belong to him .
46015024	Then comes the end , when he hands over the kingdom to God the Father after he has destroyed all rule and all authority and power .
46015025	For he must reign until he has put all his enemies under his feet .
46015026	The last enemy to be destroyed is death .
46015027	» For God has put all things in subjection under his feet . « But when it says , » All things are put in subjection under him , « it is plain that he is excepted who put all things under him .
46015028	When all things are subjected to him , then the Son himself will also be subjected to the one who put all things under him , that God may be all in all .
46015029	Otherwise , what will those do who are baptized for the dead ? If the dead are not raised at all , why then are people baptized for them ?
46015030	Why are we also in danger every hour ?
46015031	I protest , brethren , by my pride in you which I have in Christ Jesus our Lord , I die every day .
46015032	If I fought wild beasts in Ephesus for merely human reasons , what have I gained ? If the dead are not raised , » Let us eat and drink , for tomorrow we die . «
46015033	Do not be deceived : » Bad company corrupts good morals . «
46015034	Come back to your senses as you ought , and stop sinning ; for some have no knowledge of God . I say this to your shame .
46015035	But someone will ask , » How are the dead raised ? With what kind of body do they come ? «
46015036	You foolish man ! What you sow does not come to life unless it dies .
46015037	And that which you sow , you do not sow the body which is to be , but a bare grain , perhaps of wheat or of something else .
46015038	But God gives it a body as he has determined , and to each kind of seed he gives its own body .
46015039	For not all flesh is the same flesh , but there is one kind of flesh of men , another flesh of animals , another of birds , and another of fish .
46015040	There are also heavenly bodies and there are earthly bodies ; but the glory of the heavenly is one , and the glory of the earthly is another .
46015041	There is one glory of the sun , and another glory of the moon , and another glory of the stars ; for star differs from star in glory .
46015042	So is it with the resurrection of the dead . It is sown a perishable body , it is raised imperishable ;
46015043	it is sown in dishonor , it is raised in glory ; it is sown in weakness , it is raised in power ;
46015044	it is sown a natural body , it is raised a spiritual body . If there is a natural body , there is also a spiritual body .
46015045	So it is written , » The first man Adam became a living being « ; the last Adam became a life-giving spirit .
46015046	However , the spiritual is not first , but the natural ; and then the spiritual .
46015047	The first man was from the earth , of dust ; the second man is from heaven .
46015048	As was the man of dust , so are those who are of the dust ; and as is the man of heaven , so also are those who are of heaven .
46015049	Just as we have borne the image of the man of dust , we shall also bear the image of the man of heaven .
46015050	Now I tell you this , brethren , that flesh and blood cannot inherit the kingdom of God ; nor does the perishable inherit the imperishable .
46015051	Behold , I tell you a mystery ; we will not all sleep , but we will all be changed ,
46015052	in a moment , in the twinkling of an eye , at the last trumpet . For the trumpet will sound , and the dead will be raised imperishable , and we will be changed .
46015053	For this perishable must put on the imperishable , and this mortal must put on immortality .
46015054	When the perishable puts on the imperishable , and the mortal puts on immortality , then will come to pass the saying that is written : » Death is swallowed up in victory . «
46015055	
46015056	The sting of death is sin , and the power of sin is the law .
46015057	But thanks be to God , who gives us the victory through our Lord Jesus Christ .
46015058	Therefore , my beloved brethren , be steadfast , immovable , always abounding in the work of the Lord , knowing that your labor is not in vain in the Lord .
46016001	Now concerning the collection for the saints : as I directed the churches of Galatia , so you must also do .
46016002	On the first day of every week , each one of you is to put something aside and store it up , as he may prosper , so that no collections be made when I come .
46016003	And when I arrive , I will send those whom you approve with letters to carry your gift to Jerusalem .
46016004	If it seems advisable for me to go also , they will accompany me .
46016005	But I will come to you after I go through Macedonia , for I am going through Macedonia ;
46016006	and perhaps I will stay with you or even spend the winter , so that you may help me on my journey , wherever I go .
46016007	For I do not want to see you now just in passing ; I hope to spend some time with you , if the Lord permits .
46016008	But I will stay in Ephesus until Pentecost ,
46016009	for a wide door for effective work has opened to me , and there are many adversaries .
46016010	Now if Timothy comes , see that he is with you with nothing to fear , for he is doing the work of the Lord , just as I am .
46016011	So let no one despise him . Send him on his way in peace , that he may return to me ; for I am expecting him with the brethren .
46016012	As for our brother Apollos , I strongly urged him to come to you with the other brethren , but it was not at all his will to come now . He will come when he has opportunity .
46016013	Be on the your guard , stand firm in the faith , act like men , be strong .
46016014	Let all that you do be done in love .
46016015	You know that the household of Stephanas were the first converts in Achaia , and they have devoted themselves to the service of the saints . Now I urge you , brethren ,
46016016	to be subject to such men and to everyone who helps in the work and labors .
46016017	I rejoice at the coming of Stephanas and Fortunatus and Achaicus , because they have supplied what was lacking on your part .
46016018	For they refreshed my spirit and yours also . Give recognition to such men .
46016019	The churches of Asia send you greetings . Aquila and Prisca greet you warmly in the lord , with the church that is in their house .
46016020	All the brethren send you greetings . Greet one another with a holy kiss .
46016021	I , Paul , write this greeting in my own hand .
46016022	If anyone does not love the Lord — let him be accursed . Come , O Lord !
46016023	The grace of The Lord Jesus be with you .
46016024	My love be with you all in Christ Jesus . Amen .
47001001	Paul , an apostle of Jesus Christ by the will of God , and Timothy our brother , to the church of God which is at Corinth , with all the saints who are throughout Achaia :
47001002	grace and peace to you from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
47001003	Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ , the Father of mercies and the God of all comfort ,
47001004	who comforts us in all our affliction , so that we may be able to comfort those who are in any affliction , with the comfort with which we ourselves are comforted by God .
47001005	For just as the sufferings of Christ flow over into our lives , so also through Christ our comfort overflows .
47001006	If we are afflicted , it is for your comfort and salvation ; and if we are comforted , it is for your comfort , which is effective in the patient enduring of the same sufferings that we suffer .
47001007	And our hope for you is firm , because we know that just as you share in our sufferings , so also you share in our comfort .
47001008	For we do not want you to be ignorant , brethren , of our affliction which came to us in Asia : that we were burdened beyond measure , above strength , so that we despaired even of life .
47001009	Indeed , we felt that we had received the sentence of death . But this happened that we might not rely on ourselves but on God , who raises the dead .
47001010	He delivered us from so deadly a peril , and he will deliver us ; on him we have set our hope that he will deliver us again .
47001011	You also must help us by your prayers , so that many will give thanks on our behalf for the blessing granted us in answer to the prayers of many .
47001012	For our boast is this : the testimony of our conscience , that with holiness and godly sincerity , not in worldly wisdom but in the grace of God , we have conducted ourselves in the world , and still more toward you .
47001013	For we write you nothing but what you can read and understand ; and I hope you will understand fully ,
47001014	as you have understood us in part , that you can be proud of us just as we can be of you , in the day of the Lord Jesus .
47001015	Because I was sure of this , I wanted to come to you first , so that you might have a double benefit .
47001016	I planned to visit you on my way to Macedonia and to come back to you from Macedonia , and then to have you send me on my way to Judea .
47001017	When I was planning this , did I do it lightly ? Or do I make my plans in a fleshly manner so that in the same breath I say , » Yes , Yes « and » No , No « ?
47001018	But as surely as God is faithful , our word to you has not been Yes and No .
47001019	For the Son of God , Christ Jesus , who was preached among you by us — by me and Silvanus and Timothy — was not Yes and No , but in him it has always been Yes .
47001020	For as many as are the promises of God , in him they are Yes . And so through him we speak our Amen to the glory of God .
47001021	Now it is God who establishes us with you in Christ , and has anointed us ;
47001022	he has put his seal on us and given us his Spirit in our hearts as a guarantee .
47001023	But I call God as my witness that it was in order to spare you that I did not return to Corinth .
47001024	Not that we lord it over your faith ; but we work with you for your joy , for you stand firm in your faith .
47002001	So I made up my mind that I would not make another painful visit to you .
47002002	For if I cause you pain , who is there to make me glad but the one whom I have pained ?
