47002003	And I wrote as I did , so that when I came I might not suffer pain from those who should have made me rejoice , for I had confidence in all of you , that my joy would be the joy of you all .
47002004	For I wrote you out of much affliction and anguish of heart and with many tears , not to cause you pain but to let you know the abundant love that I have for you .
47002005	But if any one has caused pain , he has caused it not to me , but in some measure — not to put it too severely — to all of you .
47002006	Sufficient for such a one is this punishment which was inflicted by the majority ,
47002007	so you should rather turn to forgive and comfort him , so that he will not be overwhelmed by excessive sorrow .
47002008	I urge you , therefore , to reaffirm your love for him .
47002009	For this is why I wrote , that I might test you and know whether you are obedient in everything .
47002010	Any one whom you forgive , I also forgive . What I have forgiven , if I have forgiven anything , has been for your sake in the presence of Christ ,
47002011	in order that Satan might gain no advantage over us ; for we are not ignorant of his schemes .
47002012	Now when I came to Troas to preach the gospel of Christ and when a door was opened for me in the Lord ,
47002013	I still had no rest in my mind , because I did not find my brother Titus there . So I took my leave of them and went on to Macedonia .
47002014	But thanks be to God , who in Christ always leads us in triumph , and through us spreads the fragrance of the knowledge of him everywhere .
47002015	For we are the aroma of Christ to God among those who are being saved and among those who are perishing ,
47002016	to the one a fragrance from death to death , to the other a fragrance from life to life . And who is sufficient for these things ?
47002017	For we are not , like so many , peddling the word of God ; but as men of sincerity , as from God , in the sight of God we speak in Christ .
47003001	Are we beginning to commend ourselves again ? Or do we need , as some do , letters of recommendation to you , or from you ?
47003002	You yourselves are our letter , written in our hearts , known and read by all men .
47003003	You show that you are a letter from Christ , delivered by us , written not with ink but with the Spirit of the living God , not on tablets of stone but on tablets of carnal hearts .
47003004	Such is the confidence that we have through Christ toward God .
47003005	Not that we are competent of ourselves to claim anything as coming from ourselves ; but our competence is from God ,
47003006	who has made us competent as ministers of a new covenant , not of the letter but of the Spirit ; for the letter kills , but the Spirit gives life .
47003007	Now if the ministry that brought death , which was engraved in letters on stone , came with glory , so that the Israelites could not look steadily at the face of Moses because of its glory , fading though it was ,
47003008	will not the ministry of the Spirit be even more glorious ?
47003009	For if the ministry of condemnation has glory , much more does the ministry of righteousness exceed it in glory .
47003010	For indeed what had glory , in this case has no glory because of the glory that surpasses it .
47003011	For if what was fading away came with glory , much more is the glory of that which lasts .
47003012	Therefore , since we have such a hope , we are very bold .
47003013	We are not like Moses , who would put a veil over his face to keep the Israelites from gazing at the end of the radiance that was fading away .
47003014	But their minds were hardened ; for to this day , when they read the old covenant , the same veil remains unlifted , because only in Christ is it removed .
47003015	Even to this day when Moses is read , a veil lies over their hearts .
47003016	But whenever a person turns to the Lord , the veil is taken away .
47003017	Now the Lord is the Spirit , and where the Spirit of the Lord is , there is freedom .
47003018	And we all , with unveiled face , beholding the glory of the Lord , are being transformed into his likeness from one degree of glory to another , for this comes from the Lord who is the Spirit .
47004001	Therefore , since we have this ministry , as we have received mercy , we do not lose heart .
47004002	But we have renounced secret and shameful ways ; we do not use deception , nor do we distort the word of God . On the contrary , by setting forth the truth plainly we commend ourselves to every man's conscience in the sight of God .
47004003	And even if our gospel is veiled , it is veiled to those who are perishing .
47004004	In their case the god of this world has blinded the minds of the unbelievers , so that they might not see the light of the gospel of the glory of Christ , who is the image of God .
47004005	For we do not preach ourselves , but Jesus Christ as Lord , and ourselves as your servants for Jesus' sake .
47004006	For it is the God who said , » Let light shine out of darkness , « who has shone in our hearts to give the light of the knowledge of the glory of God in the face of Christ .
47004007	But we have this treasure in earthen vessels , to show that this all-surpassing power is from God and not from us .
47004008	We are hard pressed on every side , but not crushed ; perplexed , but not in despair ;
47004009	persecuted , but not forsaken ; struck down , but not destroyed ;
47004010	always carrying about in the body the death of Jesus , so that the life of Jesus also may be manifested in our body .
47004011	For we who live are always being given up to death for Jesus' sake , so that the life of Jesus may be manifested in our mortal flesh .
47004012	So then death is at work in us , but life in you .
47004013	Since we have the same spirit of faith , according to what is written , » I believed and therefore I spoke , « we also believe and therefore speak ,
47004014	knowing that he who raised the Lord Jesus will raise us also with Jesus and bring us with you into his presence .
47004015	For all this is for your benefit , so that the grace that is reaching more and more people may cause thanksgiving to overflow to the glory of God .
47004016	Therefore we do not lose heart . Though our outer nature is wasting away , yet our inner nature is being renewed day by day .
47004017	For our light and momentary affliction is producing for us an eternal weight of glory far beyond all comparison ,
47004018	while we look not at the things which are seen , but at the things which are unseen ; for the things which are seen are temporary , but the things which are unseen are eternal .
47005001	For we know that if the earthly tent we live in is destroyed , we have a building from God , a house not made with hands , eternal in the heavens .
47005002	Here indeed we groan , longing to be clothed with our heavenly dwelling ,
47005003	so that when we are clothed , we will not be found naked .
47005004	For while we are in this tent , we groan and are burdened , because we do not wish to be unclothed , but to be further clothed , so that what is mortal may be swallowed up by life .
47005005	Now he who has prepared us for this very thing is God , who also has given us the Spirit as a guarantee .
47005006	Therefore we are always of good courage ; and we know that while we are at home in the body we are away from the Lord ,
47005007	for we walk by faith , not by sight .
47005008	We are confident , I say , and would rather be away from the body and at home with the Lord .
47005009	So whether we are at home or away , we make it our aim to please him .
47005010	For we must all appear before the judgment seat of Christ , that each one may receive the things done in the body , according to what he has done , whether good or bad .
47005011	Therefore , knowing the fear of the Lord , we persuade men ; but what we are is known to God , and I hope it is known also to your conscience .
47005012	We are not again commending ourselves to you , but are giving you an occasion to be proud of us , so that you may have an answer for those who take pride in appearance and not in heart .
47005013	For if we are beside ourselves , it is for God ; if we are in our right mind , it is for you .
47005014	For the love of Christ controls us , because we are convinced that one has died for all ; therefore all have died .
47005015	And he died for all , that those who live should no longer live for themselves but for him who died for them and was raised again .
47005016	From now on , therefore , we regard no one from a fleshly point of view ; even though we once regarded Christ from a fleshly point of view , we regard him thus no longer .
47005017	Therefore , if any one is in Christ , he is a new creation ; the old has passed away , behold , the new has come .
47005018	All this is from God , who through Christ reconciled us to himself and gave us the ministry of reconciliation ;
47005019	that is , God was in Christ reconciling the world to himself , not counting their trespasses against them , and he has committed to us the message of reconciliation .
47005020	We are therefore ambassadors for Christ , as though God were making his appeal through us . We beg you on behalf of Christ , be reconciled to God .
47005021	For our sake he made him to be sin who knew no sin , so that in him we might become the righteousness of God .
47006001	Working together with him , then , we urge you not to receive the grace of God in vain .
47006002	For he says , » At the acceptable time I have listened to you , and helped you on the day of salvation . « Behold , now is the acceptable time ; behold , now is the day of salvation .
47006003	We put no stumbling block in anyone's path , so that our ministry will not be discredited .
47006004	But as servants of God we commend ourselves in every way : through great endurance , in afflictions , hardships , distresses ,
47006005	in beatings , imprisonments , tumults , labors , sleeplessness , hunger ,
47006006	in purity , knowledge , patience , kindness , in the Holy Spirit , in genuine love ,
47006007	in truthful speech , and in the power of God ; with the weapons of righteousness for the right hand and for the left ;
47006008	through glory and dishonor , evil report and good report ; true , yet regarded as impostors ;
47006009	as unknown , and yet well known ; as dying , and behold we live ; as punished , and yet not killed ;
47006010	as sorrowful , yet always rejoicing ; as poor , yet making many rich ; as having nothing , and yet possessing everything .
47006011	Our mouth has spoken freely to you , O Corinthians . Our heart is opened wide .
47006012	You are not restricted by us , but you are restricted in your own affections .
47006013	Now in a fair exchange — I speak as to my children — open wide your hearts also .
47006014	Do not be yoked together with unbelievers . For what partnership have righteousness and lawlessness ? Or what fellowship has light with darkness ?
47006015	What harmony has Christ with Belial ? Or what has a believer in common with an unbeliever ?
47006016	What agreement has the temple of God with idols ? For we are the temple of the living God ; as God said , » I will live in them and walk among them , and I will be their God , and they shall be my people .
47006017	
47006018	
47007001	Since we have these promises , beloved , let us cleanse ourselves from every defilement of flesh and spirit , perfecting holiness in the fear of God .
47007002	Make room for us in your hearts ; we have wronged no one , we have corrupted no one , we have taken advantage of no one .
47007003	I do not say this to condemn you , for I have said before that you are in our hearts , to die together and to live together .
47007004	I have great confidence in you ; I have great pride in you ; I am filled with comfort . With all our affliction , I am overflowing with joy .
47007005	For even when we came into Macedonia , our flesh had no rest , but we were afflicted at every turn — conflicts on the outside and fears within .
47007006	But God , who comforts the downcast , comforted us by the coming of Titus ,
47007007	and not only by his coming but also by the comfort with which he was comforted in you , as he told us of your longing , your mourning , your zeal for me , so that I rejoiced still more .
47007008	For even if I made you sorry with my letter , I do not regret it . Though I did regret it — for I see that my letter hurt you , though only for a little while —
47007009	now I rejoice , not because you were made sorry , but because your sorrow led you to repentance ; for you became sorrowful as God intended , so that you suffered no loss through us .
47007010	For godly sorrow produces a repentance that leads to salvation and brings no regret , but worldly sorrow produces death .
47007011	For behold what this very thing , godly sorrow , has produced in you : what earnestness , what eagerness to clear yourselves , what indignation , what alarm , what longing , what zeal , what readiness to see justice done ! At every point you have proved yourselves to be innocent in this matter .
47007012	So although I wrote to you , it was not on account of the one who did the wrong , nor on account of the one who suffered the wrong , but in order that your zeal for us might be revealed to you in the sight of God .
47007013	Therefore we are comforted . And besides our own comfort , we rejoiced still more at the joy of Titus , because his spirit has been refreshed by you all .
47007014	For if I have boasted to him about you , I was not put to shame ; but just as everything we said to you was true , so our boasting before Titus has proved true .
47007015	And his affection goes out all the more to you , as he remembers the obedience of you all , how you received him with fear and trembling .
47007016	I rejoice , because I have perfect confidence in you .
47008001	Now , brethren , we want you to know about the grace of God which has been given in the churches of Macedonia ,
47008002	for in a severe test of affliction , their abundance of joy and their extreme poverty have overflowed in the wealth of their liberality .
47008003	For I testify that according to their ability , and even beyond their ability , they gave of their own free will ,
47008004	urgently pleading with us for the privilege of sharing in the relief of the saints .
47008005	And they did not do as we expected , but they first gave themselves to the Lord and to us by the will of God .
47008006	So we urged Titus that as he had previously made a beginning , he would also complete in you this work of grace .
47008007	But as you excel in everything — in faith , in utterance , in knowledge , in all earnestness , and in your love for us — see that you excel in this work of grace also .
47008008	I am not speaking this as a command , but I want to test the sincerity of your love by comparing it with the earnestness of others .
47008009	For you know the grace of our Lord Jesus Christ , that though he was rich , yet for your sakes he became poor , so that through his poverty you might become rich .
47008010	And in this matter I give my advice : it is best for you now to complete what a year ago you began not only to do but to desire .
47008011	Now finish the work , so that your readiness to do it may be matched by your completion of it , according to your means .
47008012	For if the readiness is there , it is acceptable according to what a man has , not according to what he does not have .
47008013	For I do not mean that others should be eased and you burdened ;
47008014	but at the present time your abundance should supply their need , so that their abundance may supply your need , that there may be equality .
47008015	As it is written , » He who gathered much had nothing left over , and he who gathered little had no lack . «
47008016	But thanks be to God who puts the same earnest care for you into the heart of Titus .
47008017	For he not only accepted our appeal , but being himself very earnest he is going to you of his own accord .
47008018	And we are sending along with him the brother who is praised by all the churches for his preaching of the gospel ;
47008019	and not only that , but he has been appointed by the churches to travel with us in this gracious work which we are carrying on , for the glory of the Lord himself and to show our good will .
47008020	We intend that no one should blame us about this liberal gift which we are administering ,
47008021	for we have regard for what is honorable , not only in the sight of the Lord , but also in the sight of men .
47008022	And with them we are sending our brother whom we have often proved diligent in many matters , but who is now more diligent than ever because of his great confidence in you .
47008023	As for Titus , he is my partner and fellow worker among you ; and as for our brethren , they are messengers of the churches , a glory to Christ .
47008024	Therefore openly before the churches , show these men the proof of your love and the reason for our boasting about you .
47009001	Now it is superfluous for me to write to you about the offering for the saints ,
47009002	for I know your readiness , of which I boast about you to the Macedonians , saying that Achaia has been ready since last year ; and your zeal has stirred up most of them .
47009003	But I am sending the brethren so that our boasting about you may not prove vain in this case , so that you may be ready , as I said you would be ;
47009004	lest if any Macedonians come with me and find you unprepared , we — not to say anything about you — would be ashamed of having been so confident .
47009005	So I thought it necessary to urge the brethren to go on to you before me , and arrange in advance for this gift you have promised , so that it may be ready not as an exaction but as a willing gift .
47009006	The point is this : he who sows sparingly will also reap sparingly , and he who sows bountifully will also reap bountifully .
47009007	Each one must give just as he has purposed in his heart , not reluctantly or under compulsion , for God loves a cheerful giver .
47009008	And God is able to make all grace abound toward you , so that you , always having all sufficiency in everything , may have an abundance for every good work .
47009009	As it is written , » He has scattered abroad , he gives to the poor ; his righteousness endures forever . «
47009010	Now he who supplies seed to the sower and bread for food will also supply and increase your store of seed and will multiply the harvest of your righteousness .
47009011	You will be enriched in every way for great generosity , which through us will produce thanksgiving to God .
47009012	For the ministry of this service is not only fully supplying the needs of the saints , but is also overflowing through many thanksgivings to God .
47009013	Because of the test of this service , you will glorify God by your obedience in your confession of the gospel of Christ , and by the generosity of your contribution for them and for all others ;
47009014	while they long for you and pray for you , because of the surpassing grace of God in you .
47009015	Thanks be to God for his indescribable gift !
47010001	I , Paul , myself urge you , by the meekness and gentleness of Christ — I who am humble when face to face with you , but bold to you when I am away ! —
47010002	I beg you that when I am present I may not have to be bold with that confidence by which I intend to be bold against some , who think of us as if we walked according to the flesh .
47010003	For though we live in the flesh , we do not wage war as the flesh does .
47010004	For the weapons of our warfare are not the weapons of the world , but they have divine power to destroy strongholds .
47010005	We demolish arguments and every pretension that sets itself up against the knowledge of God , and we take captive every thought to make it obedient to Christ ,
47010006	and we are ready to punish every disobedience , whenever your obedience is complete .
47010007	You look at things as they are outwardly . If anyone is confident in himself that he is Christ's , let him consider this again within himself , that just as he is Christ’s , so also are we .
47010008	For even if I boast somewhat further about our authority , which the Lord gave for building you up and not for destroying you , I shall not be put to shame .
47010009	I do not wish to seem as if I would terrify you by my letters .
47010010	For they say , » His letters are weighty and strong , but his personal presence is weak , and his speech of no account . «
47010011	Let such people realize that what we are in our letters when we are absent , we will be in our actions when we are present .
47010012	For we do not dare to class or compare ourselves with some of those who commend themselves . But when they measure themselves by themselves , and compare themselves with themselves , they are without understanding .
47010013	But we will not boast beyond proper limits , but will confine our boasting to the field God has apportioned to us , a field that reaches even to you .
47010014	For we are not overextending ourselves , as if we did not reach to you ; we were the first to come even as far as you with the gospel of Christ .
47010015	We do not go beyond limits by boasting in other men’s labors , but our hope is that as your faith grows , our sphere among you may be greatly enlarged ,
47010016	so that we can preach the gospel in the regions beyond you . For we do not want to boast of work already done in another man's territory .
47010017	But , » Let him who boasts boast in the Lord . «
47010018	For it is not he who commends himself that is approved , but he whom the Lord commends .
47011001	I wish that you would bear with me in a little foolishness ; but indeed you are bearing with me .
47011002	I am jealous for you with a godly jealousy ; for I betrothed you to one husband , so that to Christ I might present you as a pure virgin .
47011003	But I am afraid that just as the serpent deceived Eve by his cunning , your minds may somehow be led astray from your sincere and pure devotion to Christ .
47011004	For if someone comes to you and preaches a Jesus other than the one we preached , or if you receive a different spirit from the one you received , or a different gospel from the one you accepted , you put up with it easily enough .
47011005	I think that I am not in the least inferior to these super-apostles .
47011006	But even if I am unskilled in speech , I am not in knowledge ; in every way we have made this plain to you in all things .
47011007	Or did I commit a sin in humbling myself that you might be exalted , because I preached the gospel of God to you without charge ?
47011008	I robbed other churches by accepting support from them in order to serve you .
47011009	And when I was with you and needed something , I was not a burden to anyone , for the brethren who came from Macedonia supplied what I needed . I have kept myself from being a burden to you in any way , and will continue to do so .
47011010	As the truth of Christ is in me , this boasting of mine will not be stopped in the regions of Achaia .
47011011	Why ? Because I do not love you ? God knows I do !
47011012	And what I am doing , I will also continue to do , in order to cut the ground from under those who want an opportunity to be considered equal with us in the things of which they boast .
47011013	For such men are false apostles , deceitful workmen , disguising themselves as apostles of Christ .
47011014	And no wonder , for even Satan disguises himself as an angel of light .
47011015	Therefore it is not surprising if his servants also disguise themselves as servants of righteousness . Their end will be according to their deeds .
47011016	I repeat , let no one think me foolish ; but even if you do , receive me as a fool , so that I too may boast a little .
47011017	What I am saying I am not saying as the Lord would , but as a fool , in this confidence of boasting .
47011018	Since many boast according to the flesh , I too will boast .
47011019	For you put up with fools gladly , being so wise yourselves !
47011020	For you put up with anyone if he makes slaves of you , or preys upon you , or takes advantage of you , or exalts himself , or strikes you in the face .
47011021	To my shame , I must say that we were too weak for that ! But whatever anyone else dares to boast about — I am speaking as a fool — I also dare to boast about .
47011022	Are they Hebrews ? So am I . Are they Israelites ? So am I . Are they descendants of Abraham ? So am I .
47011023	Are they servants of Christ ? I am a better one — I am talking like a madman — in far more labors , in far more imprisonments , with more beatings , and often in danger of death .
47011024	Five times I received from the Jews the forty lashes minus one .
47011025	Three times I was beaten with rods , once I was stoned , three times I was shipwrecked , a night and a day I have spent in the open sea .
47011026	I have been on frequent journeys , in danger from rivers , in danger from robbers , in danger from my own countrymen , in danger from Gentiles , in danger in the city , in danger in the wilderness , in danger at sea , and in danger from false brethren ;
47011027	I have been in labor and hardship , through many sleepless nights , in hunger and thirst , often without food , in cold and exposure .
47011028	Besides such external things , there is the daily pressure on me of concern for all the churches .
47011029	Who is weak , and I am not weak ? Who is made to fall , and I do not inwardly burn ?
47011030	If I must boast , I will boast of the things that show my weakness .
47011031	The God and Father of the Lord Jesus , he who is blessed forever , knows that I am not lying .
47011032	In Damascus the governor under King Aretas had the city of the Damascenes guarded in order to arrest me ,
47011033	but I was let down in a basket through a window in the wall , and escaped his hands .
47012001	I must go on boasting , though there is nothing to be gained by it ; but I will go on to visions and revelations of the Lord .
47012002	I know a man in Christ who fourteen years ago was caught up to the third heaven . Whether it was in the body or out of the body I do not know — God knows .
47012003	And I know that this man — whether in the body or apart from the body I do not know , but God knows —
47012004	was caught up to paradise and heard inexpressible things , which a man is not permitted to tell .
47012005	On behalf of such a man I will boast , but on my own behalf I will not boast , except of my weaknesses .
47012006	Though if I should boast , I will not be a fool , for I will be speaking the truth . But I refrain from it , so that no one may think more of me than he sees in me or hears from me .
47012007	And to keep me from being too elated because of the abundance of revelations , there was given to me a thorn in the flesh , a messenger of Satan , to harass me , to keep me from being too elated .
47012008	Three times I pleaded with the Lord about this , that it should depart from me .
47012009	But he said to me , » My grace is sufficient for you , for my power is made perfect in weakness . « Therefore I will boast all the more gladly about my weaknesses , so that the power of Christ may rest on me .
47012010	That is why , for Christ's sake , I am content in weaknesses , in insults , in hardships , in persecutions , in difficulties ; for when I am weak , then I am strong .
47012011	I have been a fool ! You forced me to it , for I ought to have been commended by you . For I was not in the least inferior to these super-apostles , even though I am nothing .
47012012	The signs of a true apostle were performed among you in all perseverance , with signs and wonders and mighty works .
47012013	For in what respect were you inferior to the rest of the churches , except that I myself did not become a burden to you ? Forgive me this wrong !
47012014	Here for the third time I am ready to come to you . And I will not be a burden to you , for I seek not what is yours but you ; for children ought not to lay up for their parents , but parents for their children .
47012015	I will most gladly spend and be spent for your souls . If I love you the more , am I to be loved the less ?
47012016	But be that as it may , I did not burden you myself . Yet , crafty fellow that I am , I caught you by trickery !
47012017	Did I take advantage of you through any of those whom I sent to you ?
47012018	I urged Titus to go , and I sent the brother with him . Titus did not take advantage of you , did he ? Did we not act in the same spirit and walk in the same steps ?
47012019	Have you been thinking all along that we have been defending ourselves before you ? It is in the sight of God that we have been speaking in Christ , and all for your upbuilding , beloved .
47012020	For I am afraid that when I come I may not find you what I wish you to be , and you may not find me what you wish me to be ; I fear that there may be quarreling , jealousy , outbursts of anger , factions , slander , gossip , arrogance and disorder .
47012021	I am afraid that when I come again my God will humble me before you , and I will have to mourn over many of those who sinned before and have not repented of the impurity , immorality , and lewdness which they have practiced .
47013001	This is the third time I am coming to you . Every charge must be established by the evidence of two or three witnesses .
47013002	I warned those who sinned in the past and all the others , and I warn them now while absent , as I did when present the second time , that if I come again I will not spare them —
47013003	since you desire proof that Christ is speaking in me . He is not weak in dealing with you , but is powerful in you .
47013004	For he was crucified in weakness , yet he lives by the power of God . For we also are weak in him , but we shall live with him by the power of God for you .
47013005	Examine yourselves to see whether you are in the faith ; test yourselves . Do you not realize that Christ Jesus is in you — unless , indeed , you fail the test ?
47013006	I trust that you will realize that we have not failed the test .
47013007	Now we pray to God that you may not do wrong — not that we may appear to have met the test , but that you may do what is right , even though we may seem to have failed .
47013008	For we cannot do anything against the truth , but only for the truth .
47013009	For we are glad when we are weak and you are strong . What we pray for is your perfection .
47013010	I write these things while I am absent , in order that when I come I may not have to be severe in my use of the authority which the Lord gave me for building you up , and not for tearing you down .
47013011	Finally , brethren , farewell . Aim for perfection , listen to my appeal , be of one mind , live in peace . And the God of love and peace will be with you .
47013012	Greet one another with a holy kiss .
47013013	All the saints greet you .
47013014	The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ , and the love of God , and the fellowship of the Holy Spirit be with you all .
48001001	Paul , an apostle — sent not from men nor through man , but through Jesus Christ and God the Father , who raised him from the dead —
48001002	and all the brethren who are with me , to the churches of Galatia :
48001003	grace to you and peace from God the Father and our Lord Jesus Christ ,
48001004	who gave himself for our sins to rescue us from the present evil age , according to the will of our God and Father ,
48001005	to whom be the glory for ever and ever . Amen .
48001006	I am astonished that you are so quickly deserting him who called you by the grace of Christ and turning to a different gospel —
48001007	which is really not another gospel ; but there are some who are disturbing you , and want to pervert the gospel of Christ .
48001008	But even if we , or an angel from heaven , should preach to you a gospel contrary to what we preached to you , let him be accursed !
48001009	As we have said before , so I say again now , if any one is preaching to you a gospel contrary to what you received , let him be accursed !
48001010	Am I now seeking the favor of men , or of God ? Or am I trying to please men ? If I were still trying to please men , I would not be a servant of Christ .
48001011	For I would have you know , brethren , that the gospel which was preached by me is not according to man .
48001012	For I did not receive it from man , nor was I taught it , but I received it through a revelation of Jesus Christ .
48001013	For you have heard of my former way of life in Judaism , how intensely I persecuted the church of God and tried to destroy it ;
48001014	and I was advancing in Judaism beyond many of my own age among my people , so extremely zealous was I for the traditions of my fathers .
48001015	But when God , who had set me apart even from my mother's womb and called me through his grace , was pleased
48001016	to reveal his Son in me so that I might preach him among the Gentiles , I did not immediately consult with flesh and blood ,
48001017	nor did I go up to Jerusalem to those who were apostles before me , but I went away into Arabia ; and again I returned to Damascus .
48001018	Then after three years , I went up to Jerusalem to become acquainted with Cephas and stayed with him fifteen days .
48001019	But I saw none of the other apostles except James , the Lord's brother .
48001020	( Now in what I am writing to you , I assure you before God that I do not lie . )
48001021	Then I went into the regions of Syria and Cilicia .
48001022	I was still unknown by sight to the churches of Judea which were in Christ ;
48001023	they only heard it said , » He who once persecuted us is now preaching the faith he once tried to destroy . «
48001024	And they glorified God because of me .
48002001	Then after fourteen years I went up again to Jerusalem with Barnabas , taking Titus along also .
48002002	I went up because of a revelation ; and I set before them the gospel that I preach among the Gentiles . But I did this privately to those who were of reputation , for fear that I was running or had run my race in vain .
48002003	But even Titus , who was with me , was not compelled to be circumcised , though he was a Greek .
48002004	But it was because of the false brethren secretly brought in , who had slipped in to spy out our freedom which we have in Christ Jesus , in order to bring us into bondage .
48002005	We did not yield to them even for a moment , so that the truth of the gospel might remain with you .
48002006	And from those who were reputed to be something ( what they were makes no difference to me ; God shows no partiality ) — those , I say , who were of repute added nothing to me ;
48002007	but on the contrary , when they saw that I had been entrusted with the gospel to the uncircumcised , just as Peter had been entrusted with the gospel to the circumcised
48002008	( for he who effectually worked for Peter in his apostleship to the circumcised effectually worked for me also to the Gentiles ) ,
48002009	and when they perceived the grace that was given to me , James and Cephas and John , who were reputed to be pillars , gave to me and Barnabas the right hand of fellowship , that we should go to the Gentiles and they to the circumcised .
48002010	All they asked was that we should continue to remember the poor , the very thing I was eager to do .
48002011	But when Cephas came to Antioch , I opposed him to his face , because he stood condemned .
48002012	For before certain men came from James , he used to eat with the Gentiles ; but when they came , he began to draw back and separate himself , fearing the party of the circumcision .
48002013	The rest of the Jews joined him in hypocrisy , with the result that even Barnabas was carried away by their hypocrisy .
48002014	But when I saw that they were not straightforward about the truth of the gospel , I said to Cephas in the presence of them all , » If you , being a Jew , live like a Gentile and not like a Jew , how is it that you compel the Gentiles to live like Jews ?
48002015	» We ourselves , who are Jews by birth and not Gentile sinners ,
48002016	yet who know that a man is not justified by works of the law but through faith in Jesus Christ , even we have believed in Christ Jesus , so that we may be justified by faith in Christ , and not by works of the law , because by works of the law will no flesh be justified .
48002017	But if , while seeking to be justified in Christ , we ourselves have also been found sinners , is Christ then an agent of sin ? Certainly not !
48002018	For if I rebuild what I destroyed , I prove myself a transgressor .
48002019	For through the law I died to the law , so that I might live to God .
48002020	I have been crucified with Christ ; it is no longer I who live , but Christ who lives in me ; and the life I now live in the flesh I live by faith in the Son of God , who loved me and gave himself for me .
48002021	I do not nullify the grace of God , for if righteousness comes through the Law , then Christ died for nothing . «
48003001	You foolish Galatians ! Who has bewitched you , before whose eyes Jesus Christ was publicly portrayed as crucified ?
48003002	This is the only thing I want to find out from you : did you receive the Spirit by the works of the Law , or by hearing with faith ?
48003003	Are you so foolish ? Having begun with the Spirit , are you now being perfected by the flesh ?
48003004	Did you suffer so many things in vain — if it really was in vain ?
48003005	Does he who supplies the Spirit to you and works miracles among you do so by works of the law , or by hearing with faith ?
48003006	Even so Abraham » believed God , and it was reckoned to him as righteousness . «
48003007	Therefore , be sure that it is those who are of faith who are sons of Abraham .
48003008	And the Scripture , foreseeing that God would justify the Gentiles by faith , preached the gospel beforehand to Abraham , saying , » In you will all the nations be blessed . «
48003009	So then those who are of faith are blessed with Abraham , the man of faith .
48003010	For all who rely on works of the law are under a curse ; for it is written , » Cursed is everyone who does not abide by all things written in the book of the law , to do them . «
48003011	Now that no one is justified by the Law before God is evident ; for , » The righteous man shall live by faith . «
48003012	But the Law is not of faith ; on the contrary , » He who does them shall live by them . «
48003013	Christ redeemed us from the curse of the Law , having become a curse for us — for it is written , » Cursed is everyone who hangs on a tree « —
48003014	in order that in Christ Jesus the blessing of Abraham might come to the Gentiles , so that we might receive the promise of the Spirit through faith .
48003015	To give a human example , brethren : even though it is only a man's covenant , yet when it has been ratified , no one sets it aside or adds conditions to it .
48003016	Now the promises were spoken to Abraham and to his seed . He does not say , » And to seeds , « as referring to many , but rather to one , » And to your seed , « that is , Christ .
48003017	What I mean is this : the Law , which came four hundred and thirty years later , does not invalidate a covenant previously ratified by God , so as to nullify the promise .
48003018	For if the inheritance is based on the law , it is no longer based on a promise ; but God gave it to Abraham by a promise .
48003019	Why the Law then ? It was added because of transgressions , having been ordained through angels by the agency of a mediator , until the seed would come to whom the promise had been made .
48003020	Now a mediator does not represent just one party ; but God is one .
48003021	Is the law then opposed to the promises of God ? Certainly not ! For if a law had been given which could impart life , then righteousness would indeed have come by the law .
48003022	But the Scripture has bound everyone under sin , so that that what was promised by faith in Jesus Christ might be given to those who believe .
48003023	Now before faith came , we were bound under the law , kept under restraint until faith should be revealed .
48003024	So the law was our tutor to lead us to Christ , that we might be justified by faith .
48003025	But now that faith has come , we are no longer under a tutor .
48003026	For you are all sons of God , through faith in Christ Jesus .
48003027	For all of you who were baptized into Christ have clothed yourselves with Christ .
48003028	There is neither Jew nor Greek , there is neither slave nor free , there is neither male nor female ; for you are all one in Christ Jesus .
48003029	And if you belong to Christ , then you are Abraham's offspring , heirs according to promise .
48004001	I mean that the heir , as long as he is a child , is no different from a slave , although he is the owner of all the estate ;
48004002	but he is under guardians and trustees until the date set by the father .
48004003	So also , when we were children , we were in slavery under the elemental things of the world .
48004004	But when the time had fully come , God sent forth his Son , born of a woman , born under the law ,
48004005	to redeem those who were under the law , so that we might receive adoption as sons .
48004006	Because you are sons , God has sent the Spirit of his Son into our hearts , crying , » Abba ! Father ! «
48004007	So you are no longer a slave , but a son ; and if a son , then an heir through God .
48004008	Formerly , when you did not know God , you were slaves to those which by nature are no gods .
48004009	But now that you have come to know God , or rather to be known by God , how is it that you turn back again to the weak and worthless elemental things ? Do you desire to be enslaved all over again ?
48004010	You observe days and months and seasons and years !
48004011	I fear for you , that perhaps I have labored over you in vain .
48004012	Brethren , I beg you , become as I am , for I also have become as you are . You have done me no wrong ;
48004013	you know it was because of an illness in the flesh that I preached the gospel to you at first ;
48004014	and though my fleshly condition was a trial to you , you did not despise or scorn me , but you received me as an angel of God , as Christ Jesus himself .
48004015	What has become of the satisfaction you felt ? For I bear you witness that , if possible , you would have plucked out your eyes and given them to me .
48004016	Have I now become your enemy by telling you the truth ?
48004017	They seek you , but for no good purpose ; they want to shut you out , so that you may seek them .
48004018	But it is always good to seek a good purpose , and not only when I am present with you .
48004019	My children , with whom I am again in labor until Christ is formed in you —
48004020	I could wish to be present with you now and to change my tone , for I am perplexed about you .
48004021	Tell me , you who want to be under law , do you not listen to the law ?
48004022	For it is written that Abraham had two sons , one by the slave and one by the free woman .
48004023	But the son by the slave was born according to the flesh , and the son by the free woman through the promise .
48004024	This is allegorically speaking , for these women are two covenants . One is from Mount Sinai bearing children who are to be slaves ; she is Hagar .
48004025	Now this Hagar is Mount Sinai in Arabia and corresponds to the present Jerusalem , for she is in slavery with her children .
48004026	But the Jerusalem above is free , and she is our mother .
48004027	For it is written , » Rejoice , O barren woman who does not bear ; break forth and shout , you who are not in labor ; for the children of the desolate are more numerous than the children of her who has a husband . «
48004028	Now you , brethren , like Isaac , are children of promise .
48004029	But as at that time he who was born according to the flesh persecuted him who was born according to the Spirit , so it is now .
48004030	But what does the scripture say ? » Cast out the slave and her son , for the son of the slave shall not inherit with the son of the free woman . «
48004031	So then , brethren , we are not children of the slave , but of the free woman .
48005001	It was for freedom that Christ has set us free ; therefore keep standing firm and do not be subject again to a yoke of slavery .
48005002	Behold I , Paul , say to you that if you receive circumcision , Christ will be of no benefit to you .
48005003	I testify again to every man who receives circumcision , that he is under obligation to keep the whole Law .
48005004	You have been severed from Christ , you who are seeking to be justified by law ; you have fallen away from grace .
48005005	For through the Spirit , by faith , we wait for the hope of righteousness .
48005006	For in Christ Jesus neither circumcision nor uncircumcision is of any avail , but faith working through love .
48005007	You were running well ; who hindered you from obeying the truth ?
48005008	This persuasion did not come from him who calls you .
48005009	A little leaven leavens the whole lump of dough .
48005010	I have confidence in the Lord that you will take no other view than mine ; and the one who is troubling you will bear his judgment , whoever he is .
48005011	But if I , brethren , still preach circumcision , why am I still persecuted ? In that case the stumbling block of the cross has been abolished .
48005012	I wish that those who are troubling you would mutilate themselves !
48005013	For you were called to freedom , brethren ; only do not use your freedom as an opportunity for the flesh , but through love serve one another .
48005014	For the whole law is fulfilled in one word , » You shall love your neighbor as yourself . «
48005015	But if you bite and devour one another , take care that you are not consumed by one another .
48005016	But I say , walk by the Spirit , and you will not gratify the desires of the flesh .
48005017	For the desires of the flesh are against the Spirit , and the desires of the Spirit are against the flesh ; for these are opposed to each other , so that you may not do what you would .
48005018	But if you are led by the Spirit , you are not under the Law .
48005019	Now the deeds of the flesh are obvious : immorality , impurity , lewdness ,
48005020	idolatry , sorcery , hatred , strife , jealousy , outbursts of anger , disputes , dissensions , factions ,
48005021	envy , drunkenness , carousing , and the like . I warn you , as I warned you before , that those who do such things will not inherit the kingdom of God .
48005022	But the fruit of the Spirit is love , joy , peace , patience , kindness , goodness , faithfulness ,
48005023	gentleness , self-control ; against such things there is no law .
48005024	Those who belong to Christ Jesus have crucified the flesh with its passions and desires .
48005025	If we live by the Spirit , let us also walk by the Spirit .
48005026	Let us not become conceited , provoking one another , envying one another .
48006001	Brethren , even if anyone is caught in a trespass , you who are spiritual , restore such a one in a spirit of gentleness ; each one looking to yourself , so that you too will not be tempted .
48006002	Bear one another's burdens , and so fulfill the law of Christ .
48006003	For if anyone thinks he is something when he is nothing , he deceives himself .
48006004	But let each one test his own work , and then he will have reason to boast in himself alone , and not in his neighbor .
48006005	For each one will bear his own load .
48006006	Let the one who is taught the word share in all good things with him who teaches .
48006007	Do not be deceived ; God is not mocked , for whatever a man sows , that he will also reap .
48006008	For the one who sows to his own flesh will from the flesh reap corruption ; but the one who sows to the Spirit will from the Spirit reap eternal life .
48006009	Let us not lose heart in doing good , for in due time we will reap if we do not grow weary .
48006010	So then , as we have opportunity , let us do good to all people , and especially to those who are of the household of faith .
48006011	See with what large letters I am writing to you with my own hand .
48006012	Those who want to make a good showing in the flesh try to compel you to be circumcised , and only in order that they may not be persecuted for the cross of Christ .
48006013	For those who are circumcised do not even keep the Law themselves , but they desire to have you circumcised so that they may boast in your flesh .
48006014	But may it never be that I would boast , except in the cross of our Lord Jesus Christ , through which the world has been crucified to me , and I to the world .
48006015	For neither is circumcision anything , nor uncircumcision , but what counts is a new creation .
48006016	Peace and mercy be upon all who walk by this rule , upon the Israel of God .
48006017	From now on let no one cause me trouble , for I bear on my body the marks of Jesus .
48006018	The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirit , brethren . Amen .
49001001	Paul , an apostle of Jesus Christ by the will of God , to the saints who are in Ephesus and faithful in Christ Jesus :
49001002	grace and peace to you from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
49001003	Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ , who has blessed us with every spiritual blessing in the heavenly places in Christ ,
49001004	just as he chose us in him before the foundation of the world , that we would be holy and blameless before him . In love
49001005	he predestined us to be adopted as his sons through Jesus Christ , according to the good pleasure of his will ,
49001006	to the praise of his glorious grace , which he freely bestowed on us in the Beloved .
49001007	In him we have redemption through his blood , the forgiveness of our trespasses , according to the riches of his grace
49001008	which he lavished on us . In all wisdom and insight
49001009	he made known to us the mystery of his will according to his good pleasure , which he purposed in Christ ,
49001010	as a plan for the fullness of the times , to unite all things in Christ , things in heaven and things on earth . In him
49001011	also we have obtained an inheritance , having been predestined according to the purpose of him who works all things after the counsel of his will ,
49001012	in order that we , who were the first to hope in Christ , would be for the praise of his glory .
49001013	In him , you also have heard the word of truth , the gospel of your salvation . Having also believed , you were sealed in him with the promised Holy Spirit ,
49001014	who is a deposit guaranteeing our inheritance , until the redemption of those who are God's possession — to the praise of his glory .
49001015	For this reason , ever since I heard of your faith in the Lord Jesus and your love for all the saints ,
49001016	I do not cease giving thanks for you , remembering you in my prayers ,
49001017	that the God of our Lord Jesus Christ , the Father of glory , may give to you a spirit of wisdom and of revelation in the knowledge of him .
49001018	I pray also that the eyes of your heart may be enlightened , so that you may know what is the hope to which he has called you , what are the riches of his glorious inheritance in the saints ,
49001019	and what is the immeasurable greatness of his power in us who believe . These are in accordance with the working of the strength of his might
49001020	which he worked in Christ when he raised him from the dead and seated him at his right hand in the heavenly places ,
49001021	far above all rule and authority and power and dominion , and above every name that is named , not only in this age but also in the one to come .
49001022	And he put all things under his feet and gave him to be the head over all things for the church ,
49001023	which is his body , the fullness of him who fills all in all .
49002001	And you were dead in your trespasses and sins ,
49002002	in which you formerly walked according to the course of this world , according to the prince of the power of the air , the spirit that is now at work in the sons of disobedience .
49002003	Among them we all once lived in the lusts of our flesh , following the desires of flesh and mind , and so we were by nature children of wrath , like the rest of mankind .
49002004	But God , who is rich in mercy , because of his great love with which he loved us ,
49002005	even when we were dead in our transgressions , made us alive together with Christ ( by grace you have been saved ) ,
49002006	and raised us up with him , and seated us with him in the heavenly places in Christ Jesus ,
49002007	so that in the coming ages he might show the surpassing riches of his grace in kindness toward us in Christ Jesus .
49002008	For by grace you have been saved through faith ; and this is not of yourselves , it is the gift of God —
49002009	not as a result of works , so that no one may boast .
49002010	For we are his workmanship , created in Christ Jesus for good works , which God prepared beforehand , that we would walk in them .
49002011	Therefore remember that formerly you , the Gentiles in the flesh , who are called » Uncircumcision « by the so-called » Circumcision , « which is performed in the flesh by human hands —
49002012	remember that you were at that time separate from Christ , excluded from the commonwealth of Israel , and strangers to the covenants of promise , having no hope and without God in the world .
49002013	But now in Christ Jesus you who once were far off have been brought near in the blood of Christ .
49002014	For he himself is our peace , who has made us both one and has broken down the barrier , the dividing wall of hostility ,
49002015	by abolishing in his flesh the hostility , which is the Law of commandments and ordinances , so that he might create in himself one new man out of the two , thus making peace ,
49002016	and might reconcile them both to God in one body through the cross , by which he put to death the hostility .
49002017	And he came and preached peace to you who were far away , and peace to those who were near ;
49002018	for through him we both have our access in one Spirit to the Father .
49002019	So then you are no longer strangers and aliens , but you are fellow citizens with the saints , and are members of God's household ,
49002020	having been built on the foundation of the apostles and prophets , Christ Jesus himself being the cornerstone ,
49002021	in whom the whole building is joined together and rises to become a holy temple in the Lord ;
49002022	in whom you also are being built together into a dwelling of God in the Spirit .
49003001	For this reason I , Paul , am the prisoner of Christ Jesus for the sake of you Gentiles —
49003002	assuming that you have heard of the stewardship of God's grace that was given to me for you ,
49003003	that is , the mystery made known to me by revelation , as I have already written briefly .
49003004	When you read this , you can understand my insight into the mystery of Christ ,
49003005	which was not made known to the sons of men in other generations as it has now been revealed to his holy apostles and prophets by the Spirit ;
49003006	that is , how the Gentiles are fellow heirs and members of the same body , and partakers of the promise in Christ Jesus through the gospel .
49003007	Of this gospel I was made a minister according to the gift of God's grace which was given me by the working of his power .
49003008	To me , though I am the very least of all the saints , this grace was given , to preach to the Gentiles the unsearchable riches of Christ ,
49003009	and to make plain to everyone the administration of the mystery which for ages has been hidden in God who created all things ;
49003010	so that the manifold wisdom of God might now be made known through the church to the rulers and authorities in the heavenly places .
49003011	This was according to the eternal purpose which he carried out in Christ Jesus our Lord ,
49003012	in whom we have boldness and confidence of access through our faith in him .
49003013	Therefore I ask you not to lose heart at my tribulations for you , which are your glory .
49003014	For this reason I bow my knees before the Father ,
49003015	from whom every family in heaven and on earth derives its name ,
49003016	that according to the riches of his glory he may grant you to be strengthened with power through his Spirit in the inner man ,
49003017	so that Christ may dwell in your hearts through faith ; and that you , being rooted and grounded in love ,
49003018	may have power to comprehend with all the saints what is the breadth and length and height and depth ,
49003019	and to know the love of Christ which surpasses knowledge , that you may be filled with all the fullness of God .
49003020	Now to him who is able to do far more abundantly than all that we ask or think , according to the power that works within us ,
49003021	to him be glory in the church and in Christ Jesus to all generations , for ever and ever . Amen .
49004001	I therefore , a prisoner for the Lord , beg you to lead a life worthy of the calling to which you have been called ,
49004002	with all humility and gentleness , with patience , showing tolerance for one another in love ,
49004003	being diligent to preserve the unity of the Spirit in the bond of peace .
49004004	There is one body and one Spirit , just as you were called to the one hope that belongs to your call ,
49004005	one Lord , one faith , one baptism ,
49004006	one God and Father of all , who is over all and through all and in all .
49004007	But to each one of us grace was given according to the measure of Christ's gift .
49004008	Therefore it says , » When he ascended on high , he led a host of captives , and he gave gifts to men . «
49004009	( In saying , » He ascended , « what does it mean except that he had also descended into the lower parts of the earth ?
49004010	He who descended is also he who ascended far above all the heavens , so that he might fill all things . )
49004011	And he gave some to be apostles , some prophets , some evangelists , some pastors and teachers ,
49004012	to equip the saints for the work of service , for the building up of the body of Christ ;
49004013	until we all attain to the unity of the faith and of the knowledge of the Son of God , to become mature , to the measure of the stature of the fullness of Christ .
49004014	As a result , we are no longer to be children , tossed here and there by waves and carried about by every wind of doctrine , by the cunning of men , by their craftiness in deceitful scheming .
49004015	But speaking the truth in love , we are to grow up in all aspects into him , who is the head , into Christ ,
49004016	from whom the whole body , being joined and held together by what every joint supplies , according to the proper working of each part , causes the growth of the body and builds itself up in love .
49004017	Now this I affirm and testify in the Lord , that you must no longer live as the Gentiles do , in the futility of their minds ,
49004018	they are darkened in their understanding , alienated from the life of God because of the ignorance that is in them , due to the hardness of their heart ;
49004019	and they , having become callous , have given themselves over to sensuality , greedy for the practice of every kind of impurity .
49004020	But you did not learn Christ in this way ,
49004021	assuming that you have heard about him and were taught in him , as the truth is in Jesus .
49004022	You were taught , with regard to your former manner of life , to put off your old self , which is being corrupted by its deceitful lusts ;
49004023	and be renewed in the spirit of your minds ,
49004024	and put on the new nature , created after the likeness of God in true righteousness and holiness .
49004025	Therefore , laying aside falsehood , each one of you must speak truth with his neighbor , for we are members of one another .
49004026	Be angry , and yet do not sin ; do not let the sun go down on your anger ,
49004027	and do not give the devil an opportunity .
49004028	He who has been stealing must steal no longer , but rather must labor , doing useful work with his own hands , so that he may have something to share with those in need .
49004029	Let no unwholesome talk come out of your mouths , but only such as is good for building others up according to the need of the moment , that it may impart grace to those who hear .
49004030	And do not grieve the Holy Spirit of God , in whom you were sealed for the day of redemption .
49004031	Let all bitterness and wrath and anger and clamor and slander be put away from you , along with all malice .
49004032	Be kind and tenderhearted to one another , forgiving each other , just as in Christ God forgave you .
49005001	Therefore be imitators of God , as beloved children ;
49005002	and walk in love , just as Christ loved us and gave himself up for us as a fragrant offering and sacrifice to God .
49005003	But immorality or any impurity or greed must not even be named among you , as is proper among saints .
49005004	And there must be no filthiness and silly talk , or coarse jesting , which are not fitting , but rather let there be thanksgiving .
49005005	For of this you can be sure , that no immoral , impure , or covetous person — such a man is an idolater — has any inheritance in the kingdom of Christ and of God .
49005006	Let no one deceive you with empty words , for because of these things the wrath of God comes upon the sons of disobedience .
49005007	Therefore do not be partners with them ;
49005008	for once you were darkness , but now you are light in the Lord ; walk as children of light
49005009	( for the fruit of the light consists in all goodness and righteousness and truth ) ,
49005010	and try to learn what is pleasing to the Lord .
49005011	Do not participate in the unfruitful deeds of darkness , but instead expose them .
49005012	For it is a shame even to speak of the things that they do in secret .
49005013	But all things become visible when they are exposed by the light , for everything that becomes visible is light .
49005014	For this reason it is said , » Awake , O sleeper , and arise from the dead , and Christ will shine on you . «
49005015	Be careful , then , how you walk , not as unwise men , but as wise ,
49005016	making the most of your time , because the days are evil .
49005017	Therefore do not be foolish , but understand what the will of the Lord is .
49005018	And do not get drunk with wine , for that is debauchery ; but be filled with the Spirit ,
49005019	speaking to one another in psalms and hymns and spiritual songs , singing and making melody with your heart to the Lord ,
49005020	always giving thanks to God the Father for everything , in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ .
49005021	Be subject to one another out of reverence for Christ .
49005022	Wives , be subject to your husbands , as to the Lord .
49005023	For the husband is the head of the wife as Christ is the head of the church , his body , of which he is himself the Savior .
49005024	As the church is subject to Christ , so let wives also be subject to their husbands in everything .
49005025	Husbands , love your wives , just as Christ loved the church and gave himself up for her ,
49005026	that he might sanctify her , having cleansed her by the washing of water with the word ,
49005027	that he might present the church to himself in all her glory , without spot or wrinkle or any such thing , that she might be holy and blameless .
49005028	So husbands ought also to love their wives as their own bodies . He who loves his wife loves himself .
49005029	For no one ever hated his own flesh , but nourishes and cherishes it , just as Christ also does the church ,
49005030	because we are members of his body .
49005031	» For this reason a man shall leave his father and mother and be joined to his wife , and the two shall become one flesh . «
49005032	This is a profound mystery ; but I am saying that it refers to Christ and the church .
49005033	However , each one of you must also love his wife as himself , and the wife must see that she respects her husband .
49006001	Children , obey your parents in the Lord , for this is right .
49006002	» Honor your father and mother « ( which is the first commandment with a promise ) ,
49006003	» that it may be well with you and that you may live long on the earth . «
49006004	Fathers , do not provoke your children to anger , but bring them up in the discipline and instruction of the Lord .
49006005	Slaves , be obedient to those who are your masters according to the flesh , with fear and trembling , in sincerity of heart , as to Christ ;
49006006	not in the way of eye-service , as men-pleasers , but as slaves of Christ , doing the will of God from the heart .
49006007	Render service with good will , as to the Lord , and not to men ,
49006008	knowing that whatever good thing each one does , this he will receive back from the Lord , whether he is a slave or free .
49006009	Masters , do the same to them , and give up threatening , knowing that he who is both their Master and yours is in heaven , and that there is no partiality with him .
49006010	Finally , be strong in the Lord and in the strength of his might .
49006011	Put on the full armor of God , so that you may be able to stand against the schemes of the devil .
49006012	For our struggle is not against flesh and blood , but against the rulers , against the powers , against the world forces of this darkness , against the spiritual forces of wickedness in the heavenly places .
49006013	Therefore , take up the full armor of God , so that you may be able to resist in the evil day , and having done everything , to stand firm .
49006014	Stand firm therefore , having girded your loins with truth , and having put on the breastplate of righteousness ,
49006015	and having shod your feet with the preparation of the gospel of peace ;
49006016	in addition to all this , taking up the shield of faith , with which you can extinguish all the flaming arrows of the evil one .
49006017	And take the helmet of salvation , and the sword of the spirit , which is the word of God .
49006018	Pray at all times in the Spirit , with all prayer and petition . And with this in view , keep alert with all perseverance and petition for all the saints ,
49006019	and also pray for me , that in the opening of my mouth , utterance may be given me so that I will fearlessly make known the mystery of the gospel ,
49006020	for which I am an ambassador in chains ; that I may declare it boldly , as I ought to speak .
49006021	Tychicus , the beloved brother and faithful minister in the Lord , will tell you everything , so that you also may know how I am and what I am doing .
49006022	I have sent him to you for this very purpose , that you may know how we are , and that he may encourage your hearts .
49006023	Peace be to the brethren , and love with faith , from God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
49006024	Grace be with all who love our Lord Jesus Christ with an undying love .
50001001	Paul and Timothy , servants of Christ Jesus , to all the saints in Christ Jesus who are at Philippi , with the overseers and deacons :
50001002	grace and peace to you from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
50001003	I thank my God in all my remembrance of you ,
50001004	always making my prayer with joy in every prayer of mine for you all ,
50001005	because of your partnership in the gospel from the first day until now .
50001006	For I am confident of this , that he who began a good work in you will carry it on to completion until the day of Christ Jesus .
50001007	For it is only right for me to feel this way about you all , because I have you in my heart , since both in my imprisonment and in the defense and confirmation of the gospel , you all are partakers of grace with me .
50001008	For God is my witness , how I long for you all with the affection of Christ Jesus .
50001009	And this is my prayer , that your love may abound still more and more in real knowledge and all discernment ,
50001010	so that you may approve what is excellent , and may be pure and blameless until the day of Christ ;
50001011	having been filled with the fruit of righteousness which comes through Jesus Christ , to the glory and praise of God .
50001012	Now I want you to know , brethren , that what has happened to me has really served to advance the gospel ,
50001013	so that my imprisonment for Christ has become well known throughout the whole praetorian guard and to everyone else ,
50001014	and that most of the brethren , trusting in the Lord because of my imprisonment , have been encouraged to speak the word of God without fear .
50001015	Some indeed preach Christ from envy and rivalry , but others from good will .
50001016	The latter do it out of love , knowing that I am put here for the defense of the gospel ;
50001017	the former proclaim Christ out of selfish ambition , not sincerely , but thinking to cause me distress in my imprisonment .
50001018	What then ? Only that in every way , whether in pretense or in truth , Christ is proclaimed ; and in this I rejoice . Yes , and I will rejoice ,
50001019	for I know that through your prayers and the help of the Spirit of Jesus Christ this will turn out for my deliverance ,
50001020	as it is my eager expectation and hope that I will not be ashamed in anything , but that with full courage now as always Christ will be exalted in my body , whether by life or by death .
50001021	For to me , to live is Christ and to die is gain .
50001022	But if I am to live on in the flesh , this will mean fruitful labor for me . Yet which I shall choose I do not know .
50001023	I am hard pressed between the two . My desire is to depart and be with Christ , for that is far better ;
50001024	but to remain on in the flesh is more necessary for your sake .
50001025	Convinced of this , I know that I will remain and continue with you all , for your progress and joy in the faith ,
50001026	so that your proud confidence in me may abound in Christ Jesus through my coming to you again .
50001027	Only conduct yourselves in a manner worthy of the gospel of Christ , so that whether I come and see you or remain absent , I will hear of you that you stand firm in one spirit , with one mind striving together for the faith of the gospel ,
50001028	in no way frightened by your opponents . This is a sign of destruction to them , but of salvation for you – and that too , from God .
50001029	For to you it has been granted for the sake of Christ , not only to believe in him , but also to suffer for his sake ,
50001030	having the same conflict which you saw in me , and now hear to be in me .
50002001	Therefore if there is any encouragement in Christ , if there is any consolation of love , if there is any fellowship of the Spirit , if any affection and compassion ,
50002002	make my joy complete by being of the same mind , having the same love , being one in spirit and purpose .
50002003	Do nothing from selfishness or empty conceit , but in humility consider others better than yourselves .
50002004	Each of you should look not only to your own interests , but also to the interests of others .
50002005	Have this attitude in yourselves which was also in Christ Jesus ,
50002006	who , though he was in the form of God , did not consider equality with God a thing to be grasped ,
50002007	but emptied himself , taking the form of a servant , being made in the likeness of men .
50002008	And being found in appearance as a man , he humbled himself and became obedient to deatheven death on a cross .
50002009	Therefore God also highly exalted him , and bestowed on him the name which is above every name ,
50002010	that at the name of Jesus every knee should bow , in heaven and on earth and under the earth ,
50002011	and every tongue confess that Jesus Christ is Lord , to the glory of God the Father .
50002012	Therefore , my beloved , as you have always obeyed , so now , not only as in my presence but much more in my absence , work out your salvation with fear and trembling ;
50002013	for it is God who is at work in you , both to will and to work for his good pleasure .
50002014	Do all things without grumbling or arguing ,
50002015	so that you may be blameless and innocent , children of God without blemish in the midst of a crooked and perverse generation , among whom you shine as lights in the world ,
50002016	holding fast the word of life , so that in the day of Christ I may be proud that I did not run in vain or labor in vain .
50002017	But even if I am being poured out as a drink offering upon the sacrifice and service of your faith , I am glad and rejoice with you all .
50002018	So you too should be glad and rejoice with me .
50002019	I hope in the Lord Jesus to send Timothy to you soon , that I also may be cheered when I receive news of you .
50002020	I have no one else like him , who will be genuinely concerned for your welfare .
50002021	For they all seek after their own interests , not those of Christ Jesus .
50002022	But you know that he has proved his worth , because as a son with his father he has served with me in the work of the gospel .
50002023	Therefore I hope to send him immediately , as soon as I see how things go with me ;
50002024	and I trust in the Lord that shortly I myself will come also .
50002025	But I thought it necessary to send to you Epaphroditus , my brother and fellow worker and fellow soldier , who is also your messenger and minister to my need ;
50002026	for he was longing for you all and was distressed because you had heard that he was ill .
50002027	Indeed he was ill , near to death . But God had mercy on him , and not only on him but on me also , lest I should have sorrow upon sorrow .
50002028	Therefore I am all the more eager to send him , so that when you see him again you may rejoice and I may have less anxiety .
50002029	So receive him in the Lord with all joy ; and honor men like him ,
50002030	because he almost died for the work of Christ , risking his life to complete what was deficient in your service to me .
50003001	Finally , my brethren , rejoice in the Lord . To write the same things to you again is no trouble to me , and it is a safeguard for you .
50003002	Watch out for the dogs , watch out for the evil workers , watch out for those mutilators of the body .
50003003	For we are the true circumcision , who worship in the Spirit of God , and glory in Christ Jesus , and put no confidence in the flesh ,
50003004	though I myself have reasons for confidence in the flesh . If anyone else thinks he has reasons to put confidence in the flesh , I have more :
50003005	circumcised on the eighth day , of the people of Israel , of the tribe of Benjamin , a Hebrew of Hebrews ; as to the law , a Pharisee ;
50003006	as to zeal , a persecutor of the church ; as to righteousness under the law , blameless .
50003007	But whatever was gain to me , I counted as loss for the sake of Christ .
50003008	More than that , I count everything to be loss because of the surpassing worth of knowing Christ Jesus my Lord . For his sake I have suffered the loss of all things , and count them as rubbish , in order that I may gain Christ
50003009	and be found in him , not having a righteousness of my own that comes from the law , but that which is through faith in Christthe righteousness that comes from God and is by faith ,
50003010	that I may know him , and the power of his resurrection , and the fellowship of his sufferings , becoming like him in his death ;
50003011	in order that I may attain to the resurrection from the dead .
50003012	Not that I have already obtained this , or have already been made perfect , but I press on to take hold of that for which Christ Jesus took hold of me .
50003013	Brethren , I do not consider myself yet to have taken hold of it ; but one thing I do : forgetting what lies behind and straining forward to what lies ahead ,
50003014	I press on toward the goal for the prize of the upward call of God in Christ Jesus .
50003015	Let those of us who are mature have this attitude ; and if in anything you have a different attitude , God will reveal that also to you .
50003016	Only let us live up to what we have already attained .
50003017	Brethren , join in following my example , and observe those who live according to the pattern you have in us .
50003018	For many , of whom I have often told you and now tell you even with tears , live as enemies of the cross of Christ .
50003019	Their end is destruction , their god is the belly , and they glory in their shame , with minds set on earthly things .
50003020	But our citizenship is in heaven , from which also we eagerly wait for a Savior , the Lord Jesus Christ ;
50003021	who will transform our lowly body to be like his glorious body , by the power that enables him even to subject all things to himself .
50004001	Therefore , my brethren , whom I love and long for , my joy and crown , stand firm thus in the Lord , my beloved .
50004002	I plead with Euodia and I plead with Syntyche to agree with each other in the Lord .
50004003	Yes , and I ask you also , true yoke-fellow , to help these women who have struggled at my side in the cause of the gospel , together with Clement also and the rest of my fellow workers , whose names are in the book of life .
50004004	Rejoice in the Lord always ; again I will say , Rejoice !
50004005	Let your gentle spirit be known to all men . The Lord is near .
50004006	Do not be anxious about anything , but in everything by prayer and supplication with thanksgiving let your requests be made known to God .
50004007	And the peace of God , which passes all understanding , will guard your hearts and your minds in Christ Jesus .
50004008	Finally , brethren , whatever is true , whatever is honorable , whatever is right , whatever is pure , whatever is lovely , whatever is gracious , if there is any excellence , if there is anything worthy of praise , think about these things .
50004009	Practice what you have learned and received and heard and seen in me , and the God of peace will be with you .
50004010	I rejoice in the Lord greatly , that now at last you have revived your concern for me ; indeed , you were concerned before , but you had no opportunity .
50004011	Not that I speak from want , for I have learned to be content in whatever circumstances I am .
50004012	I know how to be in need , and I also know how to have plenty ; in any and every circumstance I have learned the secret of being filled and going hungry , both of having abundance and want .
50004013	I can do all things through him who strengthens me .
50004014	Yet it was good of you to share in my troubles .
50004015	You yourselves also know , Philippians , that in the first preaching of the gospel , when I left Macedonia , no church shared with me in the matter of giving and receiving except you only ;
50004016	for even in Thessalonica you sent me a gift once and again for my needs .
50004017	Not that I seek the gift itself , but I seek for the profit which increases to your account .
50004018	I have received full payment and even more ; I am amply supplied , having received from Epaphroditus the gifts you sent , a fragrant offering , an acceptable sacrifice , pleasing to God .
50004019	And my God will supply all your needs according to his riches in glory in Christ Jesus .
50004020	To our God and Father be glory for ever and ever . Amen .
