50004021	Greet every saint in Christ Jesus . The brethren who are with me greet you .
50004022	All the saints greet you , especially those of Caesar's household .
50004023	The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirit .
51001001	Paul , an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God , and Timothy our brother ,
51001002	to the saints and faithful brethren in Christ who are at Colossae : grace to you and peace from God our Father .
51001003	We always thank God , the Father of our Lord Jesus Christ , when we pray for you ,
51001004	because we have heard of your faith in Christ Jesus and of the love which you have for all the saints ,
51001005	because of the hope laid up for you in heaven . Of this you have heard before in the word of the truth , the gospel
51001006	which has come to you , just as in all the world it is bearing fruit and growing , even as it has been doing among you since the day you heard it and understood the grace of God in truth ;
51001007	as you learned it from Epaphras , our beloved fellow servant , who is a faithful minister of Christ on our behalf ,
51001008	and who also told us of your love in the Spirit .
51001009	For this reason also , since the day we heard it , we have not ceased to pray for you , asking that you may be filled with the knowledge of his will in all spiritual wisdom and understanding ,
51001010	so that you will live a life worthy of the Lord , to please him in all respects , bearing fruit in every good work and increasing in the knowledge of God .
51001011	May you be strengthened with all power , according to his glorious might , for all endurance and patience with joy ,
51001012	giving thanks to the Father , who has qualified us to share in the inheritance of the saints in light .
51001013	For he has rescued us from the dominion of darkness and transferred us into the kingdom of his beloved Son ,
51001014	in whom we have redemption , the forgiveness of sins .
51001015	He is the image of the invisible God , the firstborn over all creation .
51001016	For by him all things were created , in heaven and on earth , visible and invisible , whether thrones or dominions or rulers or authorities — all things were created through him and for him .
51001017	He is before all things , and in him all things hold together .
51001018	And he is the head of the body , the church ; he is the beginning , the firstborn from the dead , so that he might have the first place in everything .
51001019	For all the fullness of God was pleased to dwell in him
51001020	and through him , to reconcile to himself all things , whether things on earth or things in heaven , by making peace through the blood of his cross .
51001021	And although you were once alienated and hostile in mind , doing evil deeds ,
51001022	yet he has now reconciled you in his fleshly body through death , in order to present you before him holy and blameless and beyond reproach —
51001023	if indeed you continue in the faith firmly established and steadfast , and are not moved away from the hope of the gospel that you have heard , which has been proclaimed to every creature under heaven , and of which I , Paul , have become a minister .
51001024	Now I rejoice in my sufferings for your sake , and in my flesh I do my share for the sake of his body , which is the church , in filling up what is lacking in Christ's afflictions .
51001025	Of this church I became a minister according to the stewardship from God which was given to me for you , to make the word of God fully known ,
51001026	the mystery that has been kept hidden for ages and generations , but is now disclosed to the saints .
51001027	To them God willed to make known what is the riches of the glory of this mystery among the Gentiles , which is Christ in you , the hope of glory .
51001028	We proclaim him , admonishing every man and teaching every man with all wisdom , so that we may present every man complete in Christ .
51001029	For this end I labor , striving with all his energy , which so mightily works within me .
51002001	For I want you to know how greatly I strive for you , and for those at Laodicea , and for all who have not seen my face in the flesh ,
51002002	that their hearts may be encouraged as they are knit together in love , to have all the riches of assured understanding and the knowledge of God's mystery , that is , Christ himself ,
51002003	in whom are hidden all the treasures of wisdom and knowledge .
51002004	I say this so that no one may delude you with fine-sounding arguments .
51002005	For even though I am absent in flesh , nevertheless I am with you in spirit , rejoicing to see your good order and the firmness of your faith in Christ .
51002006	Therefore as you have received Christ Jesus the Lord , so live in him ,
51002007	rooted and built up in him and established in the faith , just as you were taught , overflowing with thanksgiving .
51002008	See to it that no one takes you captive through philosophy and empty deception , according to human tradition , according to the elementary principles of the world , rather than according to Christ .
51002009	For in him all the fullness of Deity dwells in bodily form ,
51002010	and you have been made complete in him , who is the head over all rule and authority .
51002011	In him you were also circumcised with a circumcision made without hands , by putting off the body of the flesh by the circumcision of Christ ;
51002012	having been buried with him in baptism , in which you were also raised up with him through faith in the working of God , who raised him from the dead .
51002013	When you were dead in your sins and the uncircumcision of your flesh , God made you alive together with him , having forgiven us all our sins ,
51002014	having canceled the certificate of debt , which stood against us with its decrees . He took what was hostile away from us , nailing it to the cross .
51002015	And having disarmed the powers and authorities , he made a public spectacle of them , triumphing over them through him .
51002016	Therefore let no one judge you in questions of food or drink or with regard to a festival or a new moon or a Sabbath day .
51002017	These things are only a shadow of what is to come ; but the substance belongs to Christ .
51002018	Let no one disqualify you for the prize by delighting in self-abasement and the worship of the angels , taking his stand on visions he has seen , puffed up without cause by his fleshly mind ,
51002019	and not holding fast to the head , from whom the whole body , nourished and held together by its joints and ligaments , grows with a growth that is from God .
51002020	If with Christ you died to the elementary principles of the world , why , as if you still belonged to it , do you submit to regulations such as ,
51002021	» Do not handle , do not taste , do not touch ! «
51002022	( referring to things which are all destined perish with use ) , according to human commandments and teachings ?
51002023	These indeed have an appearance of wisdom in promoting self-made religion and self-abasement and severe treatment of the body , but they are of no value against fleshly indulgence .
51003001	If then you have been raised with Christ , seek the things that are above , where Christ is , seated at the right hand of God .
51003002	Set your minds on the things above , not on things that are on earth .
51003003	For you have died , and your life is hidden with Christ in God .
51003004	When Christ , who is our life , appears , then you also will appear with him in glory .
51003005	Put to death , therefore , whatever belongs to your earthly nature : sexual immorality , impurity , passion , evil desire and greed , which is idolatry .
51003006	Because of these , the wrath of God is coming .
51003007	In these you once walked , when you lived in them .
51003008	But now you must put them all away : anger , wrath , malice , slander , and filthy language from your mouth .
51003009	Do not lie to one another , since you have put off the old self with its practices
51003010	and have put on the new self , which is being renewed in knowledge in the image of its Creator .
51003011	Here there is no Greek and Jew , circumcised and uncircumcised , barbarian , Scythian , slave and free , but Christ is all , and in all .
51003012	So , as God's chosen ones , holy and beloved , put on a heart of compassion , kindness , humility , gentleness and patience ;
51003013	bearing with one another and , if one has a complaint against another , forgiving each other ; as the Lord forgave you , so you also must forgive .
51003014	And over all these virtues put on love , which binds them all together in perfect unity .
51003015	Let the peace of Christ rule in your hearts , to which indeed you were called in the one body . And be thankful .
51003016	Let the word of Christ dwell in you richly , teach and admonish one another with all wisdom , and sing psalms and hymns and spiritual songs with thankfulness in your hearts to God .
51003017	And whatever you do , in word or deed , do all in the name of the Lord Jesus , giving thanks to God the Father through him .
51003018	Wives , be subject to your husbands , as is fitting in the Lord .
51003019	Husbands , love your wives and do not be harsh with them .
51003020	Children , obey your parents in everything , for this pleases the Lord .
51003021	Fathers , do not provoke your children , or they will become discouraged .
51003022	Slaves , in everything obey those who are your masters according to the flesh , not with eye-service , as men-pleasers , but in sincerity of heart , fearing the Lord .
51003023	Whatever you do , do your work heartily , as for the Lord and not for men ,
51003024	knowing that you will receive an inheritance from the Lord as a reward . It is the Lord Christ you are serving .
51003025	For he who does wrong will be paid back for the wrong he has done , and there is no partiality .
51004001	Masters , provide your slaves with what is right and fair , knowing that you also have a Master in heaven .
51004002	Devote yourselves to prayer , being watchful in it with thanksgiving .
51004003	And pray for us as well , that God may open a door to us for the word , so that we may proclaim the mystery of Christ , for which I am in chains ,
51004004	so that I may make it clear , as I ought to speak .
51004005	Conduct yourselves with wisdom toward outsiders , making the most of the opportunity .
51004006	Let your speech always be full of grace , seasoned with salt , so that you may know how you ought to answer everyone .
51004007	Tychicus will tell you all about my affairs . He is a beloved brother , a faithful minister and fellow servant in the Lord .
51004008	I have sent him to you for this very purpose , that you may know about our circumstances and that he may encourage your hearts ;
51004009	and with him Onesimus , the faithful and beloved brother , who is one of yourselves . They will tell you everything that has taken place here .
51004010	My fellow prisoner Aristarchus sends you his greetings , and also Mark , the cousin of Barnabas ( about whom you have received instructions ; if he comes to you , welcome him . )
51004011	and also Jesus who is called Justus . These are the only men of the circumcision among my fellow workers for the kingdom of God , and they have proved to be a comfort to me .
51004012	Epaphras , who is one of your number , a servant of Jesus Christ , sends you his greetings , always laboring earnestly for you in his prayers , that you may stand mature and fully assured in all the will of God .
51004013	I testify for him that he has worked hard for you and for those who are in Laodicea and Hierapolis .
51004014	Luke , the beloved physician , and Demas send you greetings .
51004015	Give my greetings to the brethren at Laodicea , and to Nympha and the church in her house .
51004016	When this letter has been read among you , have it also read in the church of the Laodiceans ; and see that you read the letter from Laodicea .
51004017	Say to Archippus , » See to the ministry which you have received in the Lord , that you may fulfill it . «
51004018	I , Paul , write this greeting with my own hand . Remember my chains . Grace be with you .
52001001	Paul , Silvanus and Timothy , to the church of the Thessalonians in God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ : grace and peace to you .
52001002	We give thanks to God always for all of you , mentioning you in our prayers ;
52001003	remembering before our God and Father your work of faith and labor of love and steadfastness of hope in our Lord Jesus Christ .
52001004	For we know , brethren beloved by God , that he has chosen you ;
52001005	for our gospel came to you not only in word , but also in power and in the Holy Spirit and with full conviction . You know what kind of men we proved to be among you for your sake .
52001006	You became imitators of us and of the Lord , for you received the word in much affliction , with the joy of the Holy Spirit ;
52001007	so that you became an example to all the believers in Macedonia and in Achaia .
52001008	For not only has the word of the Lord sounded forth from you in Macedonia and Achaia , but your faith in God has gone forth everywhere , so that we have no need to say anything .
52001009	For they themselves report about us what kind of a reception we had with you , and how you turned to God from idols to serve a living and true God ,
52001010	and to wait for his Son from heaven , whom he raised from the dead — Jesus , who rescues us from the wrath to come .
52002001	For you yourselves know , brethren , that our visit to you was not in vain ;
52002002	but after we had already suffered and been shamefully treated in Philippi , as you know , we had the boldness in our God to speak to you the gospel of God in the face of great opposition .
52002003	For our appeal does not spring from error or impurity , nor is it made with deceit ;
52002004	but just as we have been approved by God to be entrusted with the gospel , so we speak , not to please men , but to please God who tests our hearts .
52002005	For , as you know , we never used flattery nor a pretext for greed — God is witness —
52002006	nor did we seek glory from men , either from you or from others , though we might have made demands as apostles of Christ .
52002007	But we were gentle among you , like a mother nursing her little children .
52002008	Having so fond an affection for you , we were ready to share with you not only the gospel of God but also our own lives , because you had become very dear to us .
52002009	For you remember our labor and toil , brethren ; we worked night and day , that we might not be a burden to any of you , while we preached to you the gospel of God .
52002010	You are witnesses , and God also , how holy and righteous and blameless we behaved toward you believers ;
52002011	for you know how , as a father with his own children , we exhorted each one of you and encouraged you and charged you
52002012	to live a life worthy of God , who calls you into his own kingdom and glory .
52002013	And we also thank God constantly for this , that when you received the word of God which you heard from us , you accepted it not as the word of men but as what it really is , the word of God , which is at work in you who believe .
52002014	For you , brethren , became imitators of the churches of God in Christ Jesus which are in Judea , for you suffered the same things from your own countrymen as they did from the Jews ,
52002015	who both killed the Lord Jesus and the prophets , and also drove us out . They displease God and are hostile to all men ,
52002016	hindering us from speaking to the Gentiles so that they may be saved ; with the result that they always fill up the measure of their sins . But wrath has come upon them at last .
52002017	But since we were taken away from you , brethren , for a short time , in person not in heart , we endeavored the more eagerly and with great desire to see you face to face .
52002018	For we wanted to come to you — I , Paul , again and again — but Satan hindered us .
52002019	For who is our hope or joy or crown of exultation ? Is it not even you , in the presence of our Lord Jesus at his coming ?
52002020	For you are our glory and joy .
52003001	Therefore when we could endure it no longer , we thought it best to be left behind at Athens alone ,
52003002	and we sent Timothy , our brother and God's fellow worker in the gospel of Christ , to strengthen and encourage you in your faith ,
52003003	so that no one would be unsettled by these afflictions . You yourselves know that we have been destined for this .
52003004	For indeed when we were with you , we kept telling you in advance that we were going to suffer affliction ; and so it came to pass , as you know .
52003005	For this reason , when I could endure it no longer , I also sent to find out about your faith , for fear that the tempter might have tempted you , and our labor would be in vain .
52003006	But now that Timothy has come to us from you , and has brought us the good news of your faith and love and reported that you always remember us kindly and long to see us , just as we long to see you —
52003007	for this reason , brethren , in all our distress and affliction we were comforted about you through your faith ;
52003008	for now we really live , if you stand firm in the Lord .
52003009	For what thanksgiving can we render to God for you in return for all the joy which we feel for your sake before our God ,
52003010	as we night and day keep praying most earnestly that we may see you face to face and supply what is lacking in your faith ?
52003011	Now may our God and Father himself , and our Lord Jesus , direct our way to you ;
52003012	and may the Lord make you increase and abound in love for one another and for all , just as we do for you ,
52003013	so that he may establish your hearts without blame in holiness before our God and Father , at the coming of our Lord Jesus with all his saints .
52004001	Finally , brethren , we request and exhort you in the Lord Jesus , that as you learned from us how you ought to live and to please God , just as you are doing , you do so more and more .
52004002	For you know what instructions we gave you by the authority of the Lord Jesus .
52004003	For this is the will of God , your sanctification : that is , that you should abstain from sexual immorality ;
52004004	that each one of you know how to take his own spouse for himself in holiness and honor ,
52004005	not in the passion of lust like the heathen , who do not know God ;
52004006	and that no man transgress and wrong his brother in this matter because the Lord is the avenger in all these things , just as we also told you before and solemnly warned you .
52004007	For God has not called us to impurity , but to holiness .
52004008	Therefore , he who rejects this instruction does not reject man but God , who gives you his Holy Spirit .
52004009	Now concerning love of the brethren you have no need to have any one write to you , for you yourselves have been taught by God to love one another ;
52004010	and indeed you do love all the brethren throughout Macedonia . But we urge you , brethren , to do so more and more .
52004011	Make it your ambition to lead a quiet life , to mind your own business and to work with your hands , just as we told you ,
52004012	so that your daily life may win the respect of outsiders and so that you will not be dependent on anyone .
52004013	But we do not want you to be ignorant , brethren , about those who are asleep , so that you will not grieve as do the rest who have no hope .
52004014	For if we believe that Jesus died and rose again , even so God will bring with him those who have fallen asleep in Jesus .
52004015	For this we declare to you by the word of the Lord , that we who are alive , who are left until the coming of the Lord , will not precede those who have fallen asleep .
52004016	For the Lord himself will descend from heaven , with a loud command , with the voice of the archangel and with the trumpet call of God , and the dead in Christ will rise first .
52004017	Then we who are alive and are left will be caught up together with them in the clouds to meet the Lord in the air , and so we shall always be with the Lord .
52004018	Therefore comfort one another with these words .
52005001	Now as to the times and the seasons , brethren , you have no need to have anything written to you .
52005002	For you yourselves know well that the day of the Lord will come like a thief in the night .
52005003	While people are saying , » Peace and safety , « then destruction will come upon them suddenly as labor pains upon a woman with child , and they will not escape .
52005004	But you , brethren , are not in darkness so that this day should surprise you like a thief .
52005005	For you are all sons of light and sons of the day ; we are not of the night or of darkness .
52005006	So then let us not sleep , as others do , but let us be alert and sober .
52005007	For those who sleep , sleep at night ; and those who get drunk , get drunk at night .
52005008	But , since we belong to the day , let us be sober , and put on the breastplate of faith and love , and as a helmet the hope of salvation .
52005009	For God has not destined us to wrath , but to obtain salvation through our Lord Jesus Christ ,
52005010	who died for us , so that whether we are awake or asleep , we will live together with him .
52005011	Therefore encourage one another and build up one another , just as you also are doing .
52005012	But we ask you , brethren , to respect those who labor among you and are over you in the Lord and admonish you ,
52005013	and that you esteem them very highly in love because of their work . Live in peace with one another .
52005014	And we urge you , brethren , admonish the idlers , encourage the fainthearted , help the weak , be patient with everyone .
52005015	See that none of you repays evil for evil , but always seek to do good to one another and to all .
52005016	Rejoice always ,
52005017	pray without ceasing ,
52005018	give thanks in all circumstances ; for this is God's will for you in Christ Jesus .
52005019	Do not quench the Spirit ;
52005020	do not despise prophecies .
52005021	But test everything ; hold fast to what is good .
52005022	Abstain from every form of evil .
52005023	Now may the God of peace himself sanctify you entirely ; and may your whole spirit and soul and body be kept blameless at the coming of our Lord Jesus Christ .
52005024	He who calls you is faithful , and he will do it .
52005025	Brethren , pray for us .
52005026	Greet all the brethren with a holy kiss .
52005027	I charge you by the Lord to have this letter read to all the brethren .
52005028	The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you .
53001001	Paul , Silvanus and Timothy , to the church of the Thessalonians in God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ :
53001002	grace and peace to you from God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
53001003	We ought to give thanks to God always for you , brethren , as is fitting , because your faith is growing abundantly , and the love of every one of you for one another is increasing .
53001004	Therefore we ourselves boast of you among the churches of God for your perseverance and faith in all your persecutions and in the afflictions which you are enduring .
53001005	This is evidence of God's righteous judgment , so that you will be considered worthy of the kingdom of God , for which indeed you are suffering .
53001006	For after all it is only just for God to repay with affliction those who afflict you ,
53001007	and to give relief to you who are afflicted and to us as well when the Lord Jesus will be revealed from heaven with his mighty angels in flaming fire ,
53001008	inflicting vengeance on those who do not know God and on those who do not obey the gospel of our Lord Jesus .
53001009	They will suffer the punishment of eternal destruction and exclusion from the presence of the Lord and from the glory of his power ,
53001010	when he comes to be glorified in his saints on that day , and to be marveled at among all who have believed — because our testimony to you was believed .
53001011	To this end we always pray for you , that our God may count you worthy of his calling , and may fulfill every good resolve and work of faith by his power ,
53001012	so that the name of our Lord Jesus may be glorified in you , and you in him , according to the grace of our God and the Lord Jesus Christ .
53002001	Now concerning the coming of our Lord Jesus Christ and our gathering together to him , we beg you , brethren ,
53002002	not to be quickly shaken in mind or excited , either by spirit or by word , or by letter as if from us , to the effect that the day of the Lord has come .
53002003	Let no one deceive you in any way ; for that day will not come , unless the rebellion comes first , and the man of lawlessness is revealed , the son of destruction ,
53002004	who opposes and exalts himself above every so-called god or object of worship , so that he takes his seat in the temple of God , proclaiming himself to be God .
53002005	Do you not remember that when I was still with you I told you these things ?
53002006	And you know what restrains him now , so that in his time he may be revealed .
53002007	For the mystery of lawlessness is already at work ; only he who now restrains will do so until he is taken out of the way .
53002008	And then the lawless one will be revealed , whom the Lord Jesus will slay with the breath of his mouth and destroy by the splendor of his coming .
53002009	The coming of the lawless one by the activity of Satan will be with all power and with pretended signs and wonders ,
53002010	and with all the deception of wickedness for those who are to perish , because they refused to love the truth and so be saved .
53002011	For this reason God sends upon them a strong delusion so that they will believe what is false ,
53002012	so that all may be condemned who did not believe the truth but had pleasure in wickedness .
53002013	But we are bound to give thanks to God always for you , brethren beloved by the Lord , because God chose you from the beginning to be saved , through sanctification by the Spirit and belief in the truth .
53002014	He called you to this through our gospel , that you may share in the glory of our Lord Jesus Christ .
53002015	So then , brethren , stand firm and hold to the traditions which you were taught , whether by word of mouth or by letter from us .
53002016	Now may our Lord Jesus Christ himself and God our Father , who loved us and gave us eternal comfort and good hope by grace ,
53002017	comfort and strengthen your hearts in every good work and word .
53003001	Finally , brethren , pray for us that the word of the Lord may spread rapidly and be honored , just as it did also with you ,
53003002	and that we may be delivered from wicked and evil men ; for not all have faith .
53003003	But the Lord is faithful , and he will strengthen and protect you from the evil one .
53003004	And we have confidence in the Lord about you , that you are doing and will continue to do the things which we command .
53003005	May the Lord direct your hearts into the love of God and into the steadfastness of Christ .
53003006	Now we command you , brethren , in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ , that you keep away from every brother who is living in idleness and not according to the tradition which you received from us .
53003007	For you yourselves know how you ought to follow our example . We were not idle when we were with you ,
53003008	nor did we eat anyone's bread without paying for it , but with labor and hardship we worked night and day so that we would not be a burden to any of you .
53003009	We did this , not because we do not have the right to such help , but in order to make ourselves an example for you to follow .
53003010	For even when we were with you , we gave you this rule : » If anyone will not work , he shall not eat . «
53003011	For we hear that some among you are leading an undisciplined life , not doing any work at all , but acting like busybodies .
53003012	Now such persons we command and exhort in the Lord Jesus Christ to work in quiet fashion and earn their own bread to eat .
53003013	But as for you , brethren , do not grow weary of doing good .
53003014	If anyone does not obey our instruction in this letter , take special note of that person and do not associate with him , so that he may be ashamed .
53003015	Yet do not regard him as an enemy , but warn him as a brother .
53003016	Now may the Lord of peace himself give you peace at all times in every way . The Lord be with you all .
53003017	I , Paul , write this greeting with my own hand . This is a distinguishing mark in every letter ; this is the way I write .
53003018	The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you all .
54001001	Paul , an apostle of Christ Jesus by the command of God our Savior and of Christ Jesus our hope ,
54001002	to Timothy , my true child in the faith : grace , mercy and peace from God the Father and Christ Jesus our Lord .
54001003	As I urged you when I went into Macedonia , remain on at Ephesus so that you may instruct certain men not to teach strange doctrines ,
54001004	nor to devote themselves to myths and endless genealogies . These promote controversies rather than the divine training — which is by faith .
54001005	But the goal of our instruction is love from a pure heart and a good conscience and a sincere faith .
54001006	For some men have wandered away from these things and turned aside to fruitless discussion ,
54001007	wanting to be teachers of the Law , even though they do not understand either what they are saying or the matters about which they make confident assertions .
54001008	But we know that the Law is good , if one uses it lawfully ,
54001009	realizing the fact that law is not made for a righteous person , but for those who are lawless and rebellious , for the ungodly and sinners , for the unholy and profane , for those who kill their fathers or mothers , for murderers
54001010	and immoral men and homosexuals and kidnappers and liars and perjurers , and whatever else is contrary to sound doctrine ,
54001011	according to the glorious gospel of the blessed God , with which I have been entrusted .
54001012	I thank Christ Jesus our Lord , who has given me strength , because he considered me faithful , appointing me to his service .
54001013	Even though I was formerly a blasphemer and a persecutor and a violent aggressor , I was shown mercy because I acted ignorantly in unbelief ;
54001014	and the grace of our Lord was overflowing for me , with the faith and love that are found in Christ Jesus .
54001015	It is a trustworthy saying that deserves full acceptance , that Christ Jesus came into the world to save sinners — of whom I am the foremost .
54001016	But I received mercy for this reason , so that in me , as the foremost , Jesus Christ might display his perfect patience for an example to those who would believe in him for eternal life .
54001017	Now to the King eternal , immortal , invisible , the only God , be honor and glory for ever and ever . Amen .
54001018	I give you this command , Timothy , my son , in accordance with the prophecies once made about you , that by them you may fight the good fight ,
54001019	holding faith and a good conscience , which some have rejected and made shipwreck of their faith .
54001020	Among them are Hymenaeus and Alexander , whom I have handed over to Satan so that they will be taught not to blaspheme .
54002001	First of all , then , I urge that requests , prayers , intercessions , and thanksgivings be made for all men ,
54002002	for kings and all who are in authority , so that we may lead a quiet and peaceable life in all godliness and dignity .
54002003	This is good and acceptable in the sight of God our Savior ,
54002004	who desires all men to be saved and to come to the knowledge of the truth .
54002005	For there is one God , and one mediator also between God and men , the man Christ Jesus ,
54002006	who gave himself as a ransom for all — the testimony given at the proper time .
54002007	For this I was appointed a preacher and an apostle ( I am telling the truth , I am not lying ) as a teacher of the Gentiles in faith and truth .
54002008	Therefore I want the men in every place to pray , lifting up holy hands , without anger or quarreling .
54002009	I also want women to adorn themselves with proper clothing , modestly and sensibly , not with braided hair or gold or pearls or costly garments ,
54002010	but with good deeds , as is proper for women who profess godliness .
54002011	Let a woman learn in silence with all submissiveness .
54002012	I do not permit a woman to teach or to have authority over a man ; she must be silent .
54002013	For Adam was formed first , then Eve .
54002014	And it was not Adam who was deceived , but the woman was deceived and became a transgressor .
54002015	But women will be saved through the bearing of children , if they continue in faith and love and holiness with self-restraint .
54003001	It is a trustworthy saying : if any one aspires to the office of overseer , he desires a noble task .
54003002	Now the overseer must be above reproach , the husband of one wife , temperate , self-controlled , respectable , hospitable , able to teach ,
54003003	not given to drunkenness , not violent but gentle , not quarrelsome , not a lover of money .
54003004	He must manage his own household well , keeping his children under control with all dignity
54003005	( If a man does not know how to manage his own household , how can he take care of God's church ? ) .
54003006	He must not be a recent convert , or he may become conceited and fall into the same condemnation as the devil .
54003007	He must also have a good reputation with outsiders , so that he will not fall into reproach and the snare of the devil .
54003008	Deacons likewise must be men of dignity , not double-tongued , not addicted to much wine , and not fond of sordid gain ;
54003009	they must hold the mystery of the faith with a clear conscience .
54003010	They must also first be tested ; and then if they are beyond reproach , let them serve as deacons .
54003011	The women must likewise be dignified , not malicious gossips , but temperate , faithful in all things .
54003012	Deacons must be the husband of one wife , and must manage their children and their households well .
54003013	For those who have served well as deacons gain for themselves a high standing and great confidence in the faith that is in Christ Jesus .
54003014	Although I hope to come to you soon , I am writing you these instructions so that ,
54003015	if I am delayed , you will know how one ought to conduct himself in the household of God , which is the church of the living God , the pillar and support of the truth .
54003016	By common confession , great is the mystery of godliness : he was revealed in the flesh , was vindicated in the Spirit , seen by angels , preached among the nations , believed on in the world , taken up in glory .
54004001	Now the Spirit expressly says that in later times some will fall away from the faith by giving heed to deceitful spirits and doctrines of demons ,
54004002	through the pretensions of liars , whose consciences have been seared as with a hot iron ,
54004003	who forbid marriage and advocate abstaining from foods which God created to be received with thanksgiving by those who believe and know the truth .
54004004	For everything created by God is good , and nothing is to be rejected if it is received with thanksgiving ;
54004005	for it is consecrated by the word of God and prayer .
54004006	If you point out these things to the brethren , you will be a good minister of Christ Jesus , constantly nourished on the words of the faith and of the good doctrine which you have followed .
54004007	Have nothing to do with godless myths and old wives' tales ; rather , train yourself in godliness .
54004008	For bodily training is of some value , but godliness is of value in all things , as it holds promise for the present life and also for the life to come .
54004009	It is a trustworthy saying worthy of full acceptance .
54004010	For to this end we labor and strive , because we have our hope set on the living God , who is the Savior of all men , especially of those who believe .
54004011	Command and teach these things .
54004012	Let no one look down on your youth , but set the believers an example in speech and conduct , in love , in faith , in purity .
54004013	Until I come , devote yourself to the public reading of Scripture , to preaching and to teaching .
54004014	Do not neglect the gift you have , which was given you through prophetic utterance when the council of elders laid their hands on you .
54004015	Be diligent in these matters ; give yourself wholly to them , so that all may see your progress .
54004016	Take heed to yourself and to your teaching ; persevere in them , for if you do , you will save both yourself and your hearers .
54005001	Do not rebuke an older man , but exhort him as a father , younger men as brothers ,
54005002	older women as mothers , and younger women as sisters , in all purity .
54005003	Honor widows who are real widows .
54005004	But if a widow has children or grandchildren , they must first learn to practice their religion in regard to their own family and to make some return to their parents ; for this is acceptable in the sight of God .
54005005	Now she who is a real widow , and who has been left all alone , has set her hope on God and continues in supplications and prayers night and day .
54005006	But she who lives for pleasure is dead even while she lives .
54005007	Command these things as well , so that they may be above reproach .
54005008	If any one does not provide for his relatives , and especially for his own family , he has denied the faith and is worse than an unbeliever .
54005009	A widow is to be put on the list only if she is not less than sixty years old , having been the wife of one husband ,
54005010	and she must be well known for her good deeds , as one who has brought up children , shown hospitality , washed the feet of the saints , relieved those in distress , and devoted herself to doing good in every way .
54005011	But refuse to put younger widows on the list , for when they feel sensual desires in disregard of Christ , they want to marry ,
54005012	thus bringing condemnation , because they have set aside their first pledge .
54005013	Besides , they learn to be idle , going about from house to house . And not only do they become idlers , but also gossips and busybodies , saying things they ought not to .
54005014	So I would have younger widows marry , bear children , manage their homes , and give the enemy no occasion for reproach .
54005015	For some have already turned aside to follow Satan .
54005016	If any woman who is a believer has dependent widows , she must assist them , and let not the church be burdened , so that it may assist those who are real widows .
54005017	The elders who rule well are to be considered worthy of double honor , especially those who work hard at preaching and teaching .
54005018	For the scripture says , » You shall not muzzle an ox while it is treading out the grain , « and , » The laborer deserves his wages . «
54005019	Do not receive an accusation against an elder except on the basis of two or three witnesses .
54005020	Those who continue in sin , rebuke in the presence of all , so that the rest also may be fearful of sinning .
54005021	I charge you , in the presence of God and of Christ Jesus and of the elect angels , to keep these instructions without partiality , doing nothing out of favoritism .
54005022	Do not be hasty in the laying on of hands , and do not share in the sins of others ; keep yourself pure .
54005023	No longer drink only water , but use a little wine for the sake of your stomach and your frequent ailments .
54005024	The sins of some men are obvious , going before them to judgment ; for others , their sins appear later .
54005025	In the same way , good deeds are obvious , and even those that are not cannot be hidden .
54006001	Let all who are under the yoke of slavery regard their masters as worthy of all honor , so that the name of God and the teaching may not be spoken against .
54006002	Those who have believing masters must not be disrespectful to them because they are brethren , but they must serve them all the better , because those who benefit by their service are believers and beloved . Teach and urge these duties .
54006003	If anyone teaches otherwise and does not agree with the sound words of our Lord Jesus Christ and the teaching which accords with godliness ,
54006004	he is conceited and understands nothing ; but he has a morbid interest in controversial questions and disputes about words , which produce envy , strife , malicious talk , evil suspicions ,
54006005	and constant friction between men of depraved mind and deprived of the truth , who imagine that godliness is a means of gain .
54006006	But godliness with contentment is itself great gain .
54006007	For we brought nothing into the world , and we cannot take anything out of it .
54006008	But if we have food and clothing , with these we shall be content .
54006009	But those who want to get rich fall into temptation and a snare and into many foolish and harmful desires that plunge men into ruin and destruction .
54006010	For the love of money is a root of all sorts of evil , and some by longing for it have wandered away from the faith and pierced themselves with many griefs .
54006011	But you , man of God , flee from all this , and pursue righteousness , godliness , faith , love , endurance and gentleness .
54006012	Fight the good fight of the faith ; take hold of the eternal life to which you were called when you made the good confession in the presence of many witnesses .
54006013	I charge you in the presence of God , who gives life to all things , and of Christ Jesus , who made the good confession before Pontius Pilate ,
54006014	to keep the commandment without stain or reproach until the appearing of our Lord Jesus Christ ,
54006015	which he will bring about at the proper time — he who is the blessed and only Sovereign , the King of kings and Lord of lords ,
54006016	who alone has immortality and dwells in unapproachable light , whom no man has ever seen or can see . To him be honor and eternal dominion . Amen .
54006017	Instruct those who are rich in this present world not to be conceited or to fix their hope on the uncertainty of riches , but on God , who richly supplies us with everything to enjoy .
54006018	Instruct them to do good , to be rich in good deeds , to be generous and ready to share ,
54006019	storing up for themselves the treasure of a good foundation for the future , so that they may take hold of that life which is life indeed .
54006020	O Timothy , guard what has been entrusted to you . Avoid godless chatter and the opposing ideas of what is falsely called knowledge ,
54006021	which some have professed and in so doing have wandered from the faith . Grace be with you .
55001001	Paul , an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God , according to the promise of life that is in Christ Jesus ,
55001002	to Timothy , my beloved son : grace , mercy and peace from God the Father and Christ Jesus our Lord .
55001003	I thank God , whom I serve with a clear conscience the way my forefathers did , as I constantly remember you in my prayers night and day .
55001004	As I recall your tears , I long to see you , so that I may be filled with joy .
55001005	For I am reminded of your sincere faith , which first dwelt in your grandmother Lois , and your mother Eunice , and I am sure is in you as well .
55001006	For this reason I remind you to fan into flame the gift of God which is in you through the laying on of my hands .
55001007	For God did not give us a spirit of timidity , but a spirit of power and love and self-discipline .
55001008	So do not be ashamed to testify of our Lord or of me his prisoner , but join with me in suffering for the gospel according to the power of God ,
55001009	who has saved us and called us with a holy calling , not according to our works , but according to his own purpose and the grace which was granted us in Christ Jesus from all eternity ,
55001010	but has now been revealed through the appearing of our Savior Jesus Christ , who has abolished death and brought life and immortality to light through the gospel .
55001011	For this gospel I was appointed a preacher and an apostle and a teacher .
55001012	For this reason I also suffer as I do . But I am not ashamed , for I know whom I have believed and I am convinced that he is able to guard what I have entrusted to him until that day .
55001013	Follow the pattern of sound words which you have heard from me , in the faith and love which are in Christ Jesus .
55001014	Guard , through the Holy Spirit who dwells in us , the treasure that has been entrusted to you .
55001015	You are aware of the fact that all who are in Asia turned away from me , among whom are Phygelus and Hermogenes .
55001016	May the Lord grant mercy to the household of Onesiphorus , for he often refreshed me and was not ashamed of my chains ;
55001017	but when he was in Rome , he eagerly searched for me and found me —
55001018	may the Lord grant him to find mercy from the Lord on that Day — and you know very well all the service he rendered at Ephesus .
55002001	You then , my son , be strong in the grace that is in Christ Jesus .
55002002	And the things you have heard from me in the presence of many witnesses , entrust to faithful men who will be able to teach others also .
55002003	Share in hardship as a good soldier of Christ Jesus .
55002004	No soldier in active service gets entangled in civilian affairs , since his aim is to please the one who enlisted him as a soldier .
55002005	Also if anyone competes as an athlete , he does not win the prize unless he competes according to the rules .
55002006	The hard-working farmer ought to be the first to receive his share of the crops .
55002007	Consider what I say , for the Lord will give you understanding in everything .
55002008	Remember Jesus Christ , risen from the dead , descended from David according to my gospel ,
55002009	for which I am suffering even to the point of wearing chains like a criminal . But the word of God is not chained .
55002010	Therefore I endure everything for the sake of the elect , that they too may obtain the salvation that is in Christ Jesus , with eternal glory .
55002011	Here is a trustworthy saying : if we died with him , we will also live with him ;
55002012	
55002013	
55002014	Remind them of these things , and charge them in the presence of God to avoid disputing about words , which does no good , but only ruins the hearers .
55002015	Do your best to present yourself to God as one approved , a workman who does not need to be ashamed , rightly handling the word of truth .
55002016	Avoid godless chatter , for it will lead people into more and more ungodliness ,
55002017	and their talk will spread like gangrene . Among them are Hymenaeus and Philetus ,
55002018	who have gone astray from the truth . They say that the resurrection has already taken place , and upset the faith of some .
55002019	Nevertheless , God's firm foundation stands , having this seal : » The Lord knows those who are his , « and , » Everyone who names the name of the Lord must turn away from wickedness . «
55002020	In a large house there are not only vessels of gold and silver but also of wood and earthenware , and some for noble use , some for ignoble .
55002021	If anyone cleanses himself from what is ignoble , he will be a vessel for noble purposes , made holy , useful to the Master and prepared to do any good work .
55002022	Now flee from youthful lusts , and pursue righteousness , faith , love and peace , along with those who call on the Lord from a pure heart .
55002023	Don't have anything to do with foolish and stupid arguments , because you know that they produce quarrels .
55002024	And the Lord's servant must not be quarrelsome , but he must be kind to everyone , able to teach , patient when wronged ,
55002025	with gentleness correcting those who are in opposition , if perhaps God will grant them repentance leading to the knowledge of the truth ,
55002026	and they may come to their senses and escape from the snare of the devil , having been held captive by him to do his will .
55003001	But understand this , that in the last days there will come times of stress .
55003002	For men will be lovers of self , lovers of money , boastful , arrogant , abusive , disobedient to their parents , ungrateful , unholy ,
55003003	unloving , unforgiving , slanderous , without self-control , brutal , haters of good ,
55003004	treacherous , reckless , conceited , lovers of pleasure rather than lovers of God ,
55003005	holding a form of godliness but denying its power . Avoid such people .
55003006	For among them are those who make their way into households and capture weak women , weighed down with sins and swayed by various impulses ,
55003007	always learning and never able to come to the knowledge of the truth .
55003008	Just as Jannes and Jambres opposed Moses , so these men also oppose the truth , men of depraved mind , rejected in regard to the faith .
55003009	But they will not get very far , for their folly will be plain to all , as was that of those two men .
55003010	You , however , know all about my teaching , my conduct , my purpose , faith , patience , love , endurance ,
55003011	persecutions , and sufferings , such as happened to me at Antioch , at Iconium and at Lystra ; what persecutions I endured , yet the Lord rescued me from them all .
55003012	Indeed all who desire to live a godly life in Christ Jesus will be persecuted ,
55003013	while evil men and impostors will go from bad to worse , deceiving and being deceived .
55003014	But as for you , continue in what you have learned and have become convinced of , knowing from whom you learned it ,
55003015	and how from childhood you have known the sacred writings which are able to make you wise for salvation through faith in Christ Jesus .
55003016	All scripture is inspired by God and profitable for teaching , for reproof , for correction , and for training in righteousness ;
55003017	so that the man of God may be complete , equipped for every good work .
55004001	I solemnly charge you in the presence of God and of Christ Jesus , who is to judge the living and the dead , and by his appearing and his kingdom :
55004002	preach the word ; be ready in season and out of season ; correct , rebuke , and exhort , with great patience and instruction .
55004003	For the time will come when they will not endure sound doctrine ; but having itching ears , they will accumulate for themselves teachers to suit their own desires ,
55004004	and will turn their ears away from the truth and turn aside to myths .
55004005	But you , be sober in all things , endure hardship , do the work of an evangelist , fulfill your ministry .
55004006	For I am already being poured out as a drink offering , and the time of my departure has come .
55004007	I have fought the good fight , I have finished the race , I have kept the faith .
55004008	In the future there is laid up for me the crown of righteousness , which the Lord , the righteous Judge , will award to me on that day ; and not only to me , but also to all who have loved his appearing .
55004009	Do your best to come to me soon ;
55004010	for Demas , having loved this present world , has deserted me and gone to Thessalonica . Crescens has gone to Galatia , and Titus to Dalmatia .
55004011	Only Luke is with me . Get Mark and bring him with you , for he is useful to me in my ministry .
55004012	But Tychicus I have sent to Ephesus .
55004013	When you come , bring the cloak that I left with Carpus at Troas , and the books , especially the parchments .
55004014	Alexander the coppersmith did me great harm ; the Lord will repay him for his deeds .
55004015	Be on guard against him yourself , for he strongly opposed our message .
55004016	At my first defense no one came to my support , but all deserted me ; may it not be counted against them .
55004017	But the Lord stood at my side and gave me strength , so that through me the message might be fully proclaimed and all the Gentiles might hear it . And I was rescued from the lion's mouth .
55004018	The Lord will rescue me from every evil attack and will bring me safely to his heavenly kingdom . To him be the glory for ever and ever . Amen .
55004019	Greet Prisca and Aquila , and the household of Onesiphorus .
55004020	Erastus remained at Corinth , but Trophimus I left sick at Miletus .
55004021	Do your best to come before winter . Eubulus greets you , and so do Pudens and Linus and Claudia and all the brethren .
55004022	The Lord be with your spirit . Grace be with you .
56001001	Paul , a servant of God and an apostle of Jesus Christ , for the faith of God's elect and the knowledge of the truth which leads to godliness ,
56001002	in the hope of eternal life , which God , who cannot lie , promised long ages ago ,
56001003	and at the proper time manifested in his word through the preaching with which I have been entrusted by the command of God our Savior ,
56001004	to Titus , my true child in a common faith : grace and peace from God the Father and Christ Jesus our Savior .
56001005	For this reason I left you in Crete , that you might straighten out what was left unfinished , and appoint elders in every town as I directed you ,
56001006	namely , if any man is blameless , the husband of one wife , and his children believe and are not open to the charge of being wild or rebellious .
56001007	For the overseer must be blameless as God's steward , not self-willed , not quick-tempered , not addicted to wine , not violent , not fond of sordid gain ,
56001008	but hospitable , a lover of what is good , master of himself , upright , holy , and self-controlled ;
56001009	he must hold firm to the sure word as taught , so that he may be able to give instruction in sound doctrine and also to refute those who contradict it .
56001010	For there are many rebellious men , empty talkers and deceivers , especially those of the circumcision .
56001011	They must be silenced , because they are upsetting whole families by teaching things they ought not to teach for the sake of sordid gain .
56001012	One of themselves , a prophet of their own , said , » Cretans are always liars , evil beasts , lazy gluttons . «
56001013	This testimony is true . Therefore , rebuke them sharply , so that they may be sound in the faith
56001014	and will pay no attention to Jewish myths or to the commands of men who reject the truth .
56001015	To the pure , all things are pure ; but to those who are corrupted and unbelieving , nothing is pure , but both their minds and consciences are corrupted .
56001016	They profess to know God , but they deny him by their deeds ; they are detestable and disobedient , unfit for any good deed .
56002001	But as for you , teach what befits sound doctrine .
56002002	The older men are to be temperate , serious , sensible , sound in faith , in love , and in endurance .
56002003	The older women likewise are to be reverent in behavior , not to be slanderers or slaves to much wine , but they are to teach what is good ,
56002004	so they can train the young women to love their husbands and children ,
56002005	to be sensible , pure , workers at home , kind , being subject to their own husbands , so that the word of God will not be dishonored .
56002006	Likewise urge the young men to be sensible .
56002007	Show yourself in all respects an example of good deeds , and in your teaching show integrity , seriousness ,
56002008	and sound speech that cannot be condemned , so that an opponent may be put to shame , having nothing bad to say about us .
56002009	Teach slaves to be subject to their masters in everything , to be well-pleasing , not to talk back to them ,
56002010	and not to steal , but to show that they can be fully trusted , so that in everything they will adorn the doctrine of God our Savior .
56002011	For the grace of God that brings salvation has appeared to all men ,
56002012	training us to renounce ungodliness and worldly passions , and to live sober , upright , and godly lives in this present age ,
56002013	looking for the blessed hope and the appearing of the glory of our great God and Savior , Christ Jesus ,
56002014	who gave himself for us to redeem us from all wickedness and to purify for himself a people that are his very own , zealous for good deeds .
56002015	Speak these things ; exhort and reprove with all authority . Let no one disregard you .
56003001	Remind them to be subject to rulers and authorities , to be obedient , to be ready for every good deed ,
56003002	to speak evil of no one , to be peaceable and gentle , and to show true humility toward all men .
56003003	For we ourselves were once foolish , disobedient , deceived , enslaved to various passions and pleasures , passing our days in malice and envy , hated by men and hating one another .
56003004	But when the kindness and love of God our Savior appeared ,
56003005	he saved us , not on the basis of deeds which we have done in righteousness , but because of his own mercy , by the washing of regeneration and renewal in the Holy Spirit ,
56003006	whom he poured out upon us richly through Jesus Christ our Savior ,
56003007	so that we might be justified by his grace and become heirs according to the hope of eternal life .
56003008	This is a trustworthy saying ; and concerning these things I want you to speak confidently , so that those who have believed God may be careful to devote themselves to good deeds . These things are excellent and profitable for men .
56003009	But avoid foolish controversies and genealogies and strife and quarrels about the Law , for they are unprofitable and useless .
56003010	Warn a man who is factious once , and then warn him a second time . After that , have nothing to do with him ,
56003011	knowing that such a man is perverted and sinful ; he is self-condemned .
56003012	When I send Artemas or Tychicus to you , do your best to come to me at Nicopolis , for I have decided to spend the winter there .
56003013	Do your best to help Zenas the lawyer and Apollos on their way ; see that they lack nothing .
56003014	Our people must also learn to devote themselves to good deeds , so that they may help cases of urgent need , and not be unfruitful .
56003015	All who are with me send you greetings . Greet those who love us in the faith . Grace be with you all .
57001001	Paul , a prisoner of Christ Jesus , and Timothy our brother , to Philemon our beloved brother and fellow worker ,
57001002	and to Apphia our sister , and to Archippus our fellow soldier , and to the church in your house :
57001003	grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
57001004	I thank my God always when I remember you in my prayers ,
57001005	because I hear of your love and of the faith which you have toward the Lord Jesus and all the saints ,
57001006	and I pray that the sharing of your faith may become effective through the knowledge of every good thing that is ours in Christ .
57001007	For I have derived much joy and comfort from your love , my brother , because the hearts of the saints have been refreshed through you .
57001008	Therefore , though I am bold enough in Christ to order you to do what is proper ,
57001009	yet for love's sake I rather appeal to yousince I am such a person as Paul , the aged , and now also a prisoner of Christ Jesus
57001010	I appeal to you for my child , Onesimus , whose father I have become in my imprisonment .
57001011	Formerly he was useless to you , but now he is useful both to you and to me .
57001012	I am sending him back to you , sending my very heart .
57001013	I would have been glad to keep him with me , so that he might serve me on your behalf during my imprisonment for the gospel ;
57001014	but without your consent I did not want to do anything , so that your goodness would not be , in effect , by compulsion but of your own free will .
57001015	Perhaps this is the reason he was separated from you for a while , that you might have him back for ever ,
57001016	no longer as a slave , but more than a slave , as a beloved brother , especially to me , but how much more to you , both in the flesh and in the Lord .
57001017	So if you consider me a partner , welcome him as you would welcome me .
57001018	If he has wronged you in any way , or owes you anything , charge that to my account .
57001019	I , Paul , am writing this with my own hand , I will pay it backnot to mention that you owe me even your own self .
57001020	Yes , brother , let me have some benefit from you in the Lord ; refresh my heart in Christ .
57001021	Confident of your obedience , I write to you , knowing that you will do even more than I say .
57001022	At the same time , prepare a guest room for me , for I hope through your prayers to be granted to you .
57001023	Epaphras , my fellow prisoner in Christ Jesus , sends you greetings ,
57001024	and so do Mark , Aristarchus , Demas , and Luke , my fellow workers .
57001025	The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirit .
58001001	In the past God spoke to our fathers by the prophets at many times and in various ways ,
58001002	but in these last days he has spoken to us by his Son , whom he appointed heir of all things , and through whom also he made the world .
58001003	He is the radiance of his glory and the exact representation of his being , and upholds all things by the word of his power . When he had made purification for sins , he sat down at the right hand of the Majesty on high ,
58001004	having become as much superior to angels as the name he has inherited is more excellent than theirs .
58001005	For to which of the angels did God ever say , » You are my son , today I have begotten you « ? And again , » I will be a father to him and he shall be a son to me « ?
58001006	And again , when God brings the first-born into the world , he says , » Let all God's angels worship him . «
58001007	Of the angels he says , » Who makes his angels winds , and his servants flames of fire . «
58001008	But of the Son he says , » Your throne , O God , is for ever and ever , and the righteous scepter is the scepter of your kingdom .
58001009	
58001010	And , » You , Lord , in the beginning laid the foundation of the earth , and the heavens are the work of your hands ;
58001011	
58001012	
58001013	But to which of the angels has he ever said , » Sit at my right hand , until I make your enemies a stool for your feet « ?
58001014	Are they not all ministering spirits , sent forth to serve for the sake of those who will inherit salvation ?
58002001	Therefore we must pay more careful attention to what we have heard , lest we drift away from it .
58002002	For if the message spoken by angels was valid , and every transgression and disobedience received a just punishment ,
58002003	how shall we escape if we neglect such a great salvation ? It was declared at first by the Lord , and it was confirmed to us by those who heard him ,
58002004	while God also bore witness , by signs and wonders and various miracles , and by gifts of the Holy Spirit distributed according to his own will .
58002005	For it is not to angels that he subjected the world to come , about which we are speaking .
58002006	But there is a place where someone has testified , » What is man that you are mindful of him , or the son of man that you care for him ?
58002007	
58002008	
58002009	But we see Jesus , who for a little while was made lower than the angels , crowned with glory and honor because of the suffering of death , so that by the grace of God he might taste death for everyone .
58002010	For it was fitting that he , for whom and through whom all things exist , in bringing many sons to glory , should make the author of their salvation perfect through suffering .
58002011	For both he who sanctifies and those who are being sanctified are all of one . That is why he is not ashamed to call them brethren ,
58002012	saying , » I will declare your name to my brethren , in the midst of the congregation I will sing your praise . «
58002013	And again , » I will put my trust in him . « And again , » Here am I , and the children God has given me . «
58002014	Since therefore the children share in flesh and blood , he himself likewise partook of the same nature , that through death he might destroy him who has the power of death , that is , the devil ,
58002015	and might free those who through fear of death were subject to slavery all their lives .
58002016	For surely it is not with angels that he is concerned , but with the descendants of Abraham .
58002017	Therefore he had to be made like his brethren in every respect , so that he might become a merciful and faithful high priest in the service of God , to make atonement for the sins of the people .
58002018	For because he himself has suffered , being tempted , he is able to help those who are tempted .
58003001	Therefore , holy brethren , who share in a heavenly calling , consider Jesus , the apostle and high priest of our confession .
58003002	He was faithful to him who appointed him , just as Moses also was faithful in all God's house .
58003003	Yet Jesus has been counted worthy of as much more glory than Moses as the builder of a house has more honor than the house .
58003004	For every house is built by someone , but the builder of all things is God .
58003005	Now Moses was faithful in all God's house as a servant , to testify to the things that were to be spoken later ,
58003006	but Christ is faithful as a son over God's house . And we are his house , if we hold fast to our confidence and the hope of which we boast .
58003007	Therefore , as the Holy Spirit says : » Today , if you will hear his voice ,
58003008	
58003009	
58003010	
58003011	
58003012	Take care , brethren , lest there be in any one of you an evil , unbelieving heart , leading you to fall away from the living God .
58003013	But exhort one another every day , as long as it is called » Today , « so that none of you may be hardened by the deceitfulness of sin .
58003014	For we have come to share in Christ if we hold our first confidence firm to the end ,
58003015	while it is said , » Today , if you will hear his voice , do not harden your hearts as in the rebellion . «
58003016	Who were they who heard and rebelled ? Were they not all those Moses led out of Egypt ?
58003017	And with whom was he angry for forty years ? Was it not with those who sinned , whose bodies fell in the wilderness ?
58003018	And to whom did he swear that they would never enter his rest , but to those who were disobedient ?
58003019	So we see that they were not able to enter because of unbelief .
58004001	Therefore , while the promise of entering his rest remains , let us fear lest any one of you be judged to have come short of it .
58004002	For we also have had the good news preached to us , just as they did ; but the message they heard was of no value to them , because those who heard did not combine it with faith .
58004003	For we who have believed enter that rest , as he has said , » As I swore in my wrath , ‘ They shall never enter my rest , ’ « although his works were finished from the foundation of the world .
58004004	For he has somewhere spoken of the seventh day in this way : » And God rested on the seventh day from all his works . «
58004005	And again in this place he said , » They shall never enter my rest . «
58004006	Since therefore it remains for some to enter it , and those who formerly had the good news preached to them failed to enter because of disobedience ,
58004007	God again set a certain day , » Today , « saying through David after so long a time just as has been said before , » Today , if you hear his voice , do not harden your hearts . «
58004008	For if Joshua had given them rest , God would not have spoken later of another day .
58004009	So then , there remains a Sabbath rest for the people of God ;
58004010	for anyone who enters God's rest also rests from his own work , just as God did from his .
58004011	Therefore let us be diligent to enter that rest , so that no one will fall by following the same example of disobedience .
58004012	For the word of God is living and active , sharper than any two-edged sword , piercing even to the division of soul and spirit , of joints and marrow , and discerning the thoughts and intentions of the heart .
58004013	And there is no creature hidden from his sight , but all things are open and laid bare to the eyes of him with whom we have to do .
58004014	Since then we have a great high priest who has passed through the heavens , Jesus , the Son of God , let us hold fast our confession .
58004015	For we do not have a high priest who is unable to sympathize with our weaknesses , but one who in every respect has been tempted as we are , yet without sin .
58004016	Let us then with confidence draw near to the throne of grace , that we may receive mercy and find grace to help in time of need .
58005001	For every high priest chosen from among men is appointed to act on behalf of men in relation to God , to offer gifts and sacrifices for sins .
58005002	He can deal gently with those who are ignorant and going astray , since he himself is beset with weakness .
58005003	Because of this he has to offer sacrifices for his own sins , as well as for the sins of the people .
58005004	And no one takes the honor upon himself , but he is called by God , just as Aaron was .
58005005	So also Christ did not exalt himself to become a high priest , but it was he who said to him , » You are my son , today I have begotten you « ;
58005006	as he says also in another place , » You are a priest forever , after the order of Melchizedek . «
58005007	In the days of his flesh , Jesus offered up prayers and supplications , with loud cries and tears , to the one who was able to save him from death , and he was heard because of his godly fear .
58005008	Although he was a Son , he learned obedience from what he suffered ;
58005009	and , once made perfect , he became the source of eternal salvation for all who obey him ,
58005010	being designated by God as a high priest according to the order of Melchizedek .
58005011	About this we have much to say which is hard to explain , since you have become dull of hearing .
58005012	For though by this time you ought to be teachers , you need someone to teach you again the first principles of God's word . You need milk , not solid food ;
58005013	for every one who lives on milk is unskilled in the word of righteousness , for he is a babe .
58005014	But solid food is for the mature , for those who have their sense trained by practice to distinguish good from evil .
58006001	Therefore let us leave the elementary teachings about Christ and go on to maturity , not laying again a foundation of repentance from dead works , and of faith toward God ,
58006002	with instruction about baptisms , the laying on of hands , the resurrection of the dead , and eternal judgment .
58006003	And this we will do , if God permits .
58006004	For it is impossible for those who have once been enlightened , who have tasted the heavenly gift , and have become partakers of the Holy Spirit ,
58006005	and have tasted the goodness of the word of God and the powers of the age to come ,
58006006	and then have fallen away , to renew them again to repentance , since they crucify again for themselves the Son of God , and put him to an open shame .
58006007	For land which drinks the rain that often falls upon it , and brings forth vegetation useful to those for whose sake it is cultivated , receives a blessing from God .
58006008	But if it bears thorns and thistles , it is worthless and near to being cursed ; its end is to be burned .
58006009	Even though we speak like this , beloved , we are confident of better things in your case , things that accompany salvation .
58006010	For God is not so unjust as to forget your work and the love which you have shown for his sake in serving the saints , as you still do .
58006011	And we desire each one of you to show the same diligence in realizing the full assurance of hope until the end ,
58006012	so that you may not be sluggish , but imitators of those who through faith and patience inherit the promises .
58006013	For when God made a promise to Abraham , since he had no one greater by whom to swear , he swore by himself ,
58006014	saying , » I will surely bless you and multiply you . «
58006015	And so Abraham , having patiently endured , obtained the promise .
58006016	Men swear by one greater than themselves , and in all their disputes the oath is final for confirmation .
58006017	So when God desired to show more convincingly to the heirs of the promise the unchangeable character of his purpose , he interposed with an oath ,
58006018	so that , by two unchangeable things in which it is impossible for God to lie , we who have taken refuge would have strong encouragement to take hold of the hope set before us .
58006019	We have this as a sure and steadfast anchor of the soul , a hope that enters into the inner sanctuary behind the curtain ,
58006020	where Jesus has entered as a forerunner on our behalf , having become a high priest forever according to the order of Melchizedek .
58007001	For this Melchizedek , king of Salem , priest of the Most High God , met Abraham returning from the slaughter of the kings and blessed him .
58007002	And to him Abraham gave a tenth part of everything . He is first , by translation of his name , king of righteousness , and then he is also king of Salem , that is , king of peace .
58007003	Without father , without mother , without genealogy , having neither beginning of days nor end of life , but made like the Son of God , he remains a priest continually .
58007004	See how great he was ! Even the patriarch Abraham gave him a tenth of the spoils .
58007005	And those descendants of Levi who receive the priestly office have a commandment in the law to take a tenth from the people , that is , from their brethren , though these also are descended from Abraham .
58007006	But this man whose genealogy is not derived from them received a tenth from Abraham and blessed him who had the promises .
58007007	And without dispute the lesser person is blessed by the greater .
58007008	In this case tithes are received by mortal men , but in that case by one of whom it is witnessed that he lives on .
58007009	One might even say that Levi himself , who receives tithes , paid tithes through Abraham ,
58007010	for he was still in the loins of his ancestor when Melchizedek met him .
58007011	Now if perfection could have been through the Levitical priesthood ( for on the basis of it the people received the Law ) , what further need was there for another priest to arise according to the order of Melchizedek , and not one designated according to the order of Aaron ?
58007012	For when there is a change of the priesthood , there must also be a change of the law .
58007013	For the one of whom these things are spoken belonged to another tribe , from which no one has ever served at the altar .
58007014	For it is evident that our Lord was descended from Judah , and in regard to that tribe Moses said nothing about priests .
58007015	This becomes even more evident if another priest arises in the likeness of Melchizedek ,
58007016	who has become a priest not on the basis of a law of carnal requirement , but according to the power of an indestructible life .
58007017	For it is declared of him , » You are a priest forever , after the order of Melchizedek . «
58007018	On the one hand , a former commandment is set aside because of its weakness and uselessness
58007019	( for the law made nothing perfect ) ; and on the other hand , a better hope is introduced , through which we draw near to God .
58007020	And it was not without an oath .
58007021	Those who formerly became priests took their office without an oath , but he became a priest with an oath through the One who said to him , » The Lord has sworn and will not change his mind , ‘ You are a priest forever . ’ «
58007022	Because of this oath , Jesus has become the guarantee of a better covenant .
58007023	The former priests were many in number , because they were prevented by death from continuing in office ;
58007024	but he holds his priesthood forever , because he continues for ever .
58007025	Therefore he is able also to save forever those who draw near to God through him , since he always lives to make intercession for them .
58007026	For it was fitting that we should have such a high priest , holy , blameless , unstained , separated from sinners , exalted above the heavens .
58007027	He does not need , like those high priests , to offer up daily sacrifices , first for his own sins and then for the sins of the people , because he did this once for all when he offered up himself .
58007028	For the Law appoints men as high priests who are weak , but the word of the oath , which came after the Law , appoints a Son who has been made perfect forever .
58008001	Now the point in what we are saying is this : we have such a high priest , one who is seated at the right hand of the throne of the Majesty in heaven ,
58008002	a minister in the sanctuary , the true tabernacle which is set up by the Lord , not by man .
58008003	For every high priest is appointed to offer both gifts and sacrifices ; and so it is necessary for this priest also to have something to offer .
58008004	Now if he were on earth , he would not be a priest at all , since there are priests who offer the gifts according to the law .
58008005	They serve a copy and shadow of the heavenly sanctuary ; for when Moses was about to erect the tabernacle , he was instructed by God , saying , » See that you make everything according to the pattern which was shown you on the mountain . «
58008006	But as it is , he has obtained a ministry which is as much more excellent than the old as the covenant he mediates is better , since it is enacted on better promises .
58008007	For if that first covenant had been faultless , there would have been no place sought for a second .
58008008	For he finds fault with them when he says : » The days are coming , says the Lord , when I will make a new covenant with the house of Israel and with the house of Judah ;
58008009	
58008010	
58008011	
58008012	
58008013	When he said , » A new covenant , « he has made the first obsolete . And what is becoming obsolete and growing old is ready to vanish away .
58009001	Now even the first covenant had regulations for worship and an earthly sanctuary .
58009002	For there was a tabernacle prepared , the first one , in which were the lampstand and the table and the sacred bread ; this is called the holy place .
58009003	Behind the second curtain was a tabernacle called the Holy of Holies ,
58009004	having the golden altar of incense and the ark of the covenant covered on all sides with gold , which contained a golden jar holding the manna , and Aaron's rod that budded , and the tables of the covenant ;
58009005	and above it were the cherubim of glory overshadowing the mercy seat . But of these things we cannot now speak in detail .
58009006	These preparations having thus been made , the priests go continually into the outer tabernacle , performing their ritual duties .
