58009007	But into the second only the high priest goes , and he but once a year , and not without taking blood , which he offers for himself and for the sins of the people committed in ignorance .
58009008	The Holy Spirit was showing by this that the way into the holy place had not yet been disclosed as long as the outer tabernacle was still standing .
58009009	This is symbolic for the present time . According to this arrangement , gifts and sacrifices are offered which cannot perfect the conscience of the worshiper ,
58009010	since they relate only to food and drink and various washings – regulations for the flesh imposed until the time of reformation .
58009011	But when Christ appeared as a high priest of the good things that have come , he entered through the greater and more perfect tabernacle , not made with hands , that is to say , not of this creation .
58009012	He did not enter by means of the blood of goats and calves , but he entered the holy place once for all by his own blood , having obtained eternal redemption .
58009013	For if the blood of goats and bulls and the ashes of a heifer sprinkling those who have been defiled sanctify for the cleansing of the flesh ,
58009014	how much more will the blood of Christ , who through the eternal Spirit offered himself without blemish to God , cleanse your conscience from dead works to serve the living God ?
58009015	For this reason he is the mediator of a new covenant , that those who are called may receive the promised eternal inheritance , now that he has died as a ransom to set them free from the transgressions committed under the first covenant .
58009016	For where a will is , there must of necessity be the death of the one who made it .
58009017	For a will is in force only when somebody has died , since it never takes effect while the one who made it is living .
58009018	This is why even the first covenant was not ratified without blood .
58009019	For when every commandment of the law had been declared by Moses to all the people , he took the blood of calves and goats , with water and scarlet wool and hyssop , and sprinkled both the book itself and all the people ,
58009020	saying , » This is the blood of the covenant which God has commanded you . «
58009021	And in the same way he sprinkled with the blood both the tabernacle and all the vessels used in worship .
58009022	Indeed , under the law almost everything is cleansed with blood , and without the shedding of blood there is no forgiveness of sins .
58009023	It was necessary , then , for the copies of the heavenly things to be purified with these sacrifices , but the heavenly things themselves with better sacrifices than these .
58009024	For Christ did not enter a holy place made with hands , a copy of the true one , but into heaven itself , now to appear in the presence of God for us .
58009025	Nor was it that he should offer himself again and again , as the high priest enters the holy place year by year with blood not his own .
58009026	For then he would have had to suffer repeatedly since the foundation of the world . But now , he has appeared once for all at the end of the ages to put away sin by the sacrifice of himself .
58009027	And just as it is appointed for men to die once , and after that comes judgment ,
58009028	so Christ , having been offered once to bear the sins of many , will appear a second time , not to bear sin but to bring salvation to those who are eagerly waiting for him .
58010001	For since the law has only a shadow of the good things to come and not the true form of these realities , it can never , by the same sacrifices which are continually offered year after year , make perfect those who draw near .
58010002	Otherwise , would they not have ceased to be offered ? If the worshipers had once been cleansed , they would no longer have any consciousness of sins .
58010003	But in these sacrifices there is a reminder of sins year after year .
58010004	For it is impossible for the blood of bulls and goats to take away sins .
58010005	Therefore , when Christ came into the world , he said : » Sacrifice and offering you did not desire , but a body you prepared for me ;
58010006	
58010007	
58010008	When he said above , » You did not desire , nor did you take pleasure in sacrifices and offerings and burnt offerings and sin offerings « ( these are offered according to the law ) ,
58010009	then he said , » Behold , I have come to do your will . « He takes away the first in order to establish the second .
58010010	And by that will we have been sanctified through the offering of the body of Jesus Christ once for all .
58010011	And every priest stands daily at his service , offering time after time the same sacrifices , which can never take away sins .
58010012	But when he had offered for all time one sacrifice for sins , he sat down at the right hand of God ,
58010013	waiting from that time until his enemies be made a stool for his feet .
58010014	For by one offering he has perfected for all time those who are sanctified .
58010015	And the Holy Spirit also bears witness to us ; for after saying ,
58010016	
58010017	then he adds , » Their sins and their lawless deeds I will remember no more . «
58010018	Where there is forgiveness of these , there is no longer any offering for sin .
58010019	Therefore , brethren , since we have confidence to enter the holy place by the blood of Jesus ,
58010020	by a new and living way which he opened for us through the curtain , that is , his flesh ,
58010021	and since we have a great priest over the house of God ,
58010022	let us draw near with a true heart in full assurance of faith , having our hearts sprinkled clean from an evil conscience and our bodies washed with pure water .
58010023	Let us hold fast the confession of our hope without wavering , for he who promised is faithful ;
58010024	and let us consider how to stir up one another to love and good works ,
58010025	not forsaking our own assembling together , as is the habit of some , but encouraging one another ; and all the more , as you see the Day drawing near .
58010026	For if we sin deliberately after we have received the knowledge of the truth , there no longer remains a sacrifice for sins ,
58010027	but a fearful expectation of judgment , and a fury of fire which will consume the adversaries .
58010028	Anyone who has rejected the law of Moses dies without mercy on the testimony of two or three witnesses .
58010029	How much severer punishment do you think a man will deserve who has trampled under foot the Son of God , and has regarded as an unclean thing the blood of the covenant by which he was sanctified , and has insulted the Spirit of grace ?
58010030	For we know him who said , » Vengeance is mine , I will repay . « And again , » The Lord will judge his people . «
58010031	It is a fearful thing to fall into the hands of the living God .
58010032	But remember the former days when , after you were enlightened , you endured a great struggle with sufferings ,
58010033	sometimes being publicly exposed to insult and persecution ; and at other times standing side by side with those who were so treated .
58010034	For you had compassion on the prisoners , and you joyfully accepted the plundering of your property , since you knew that you yourselves had a better possession and an abiding one .
58010035	Therefore do not throw away your confidence , which has a great reward .
58010036	For you have need of endurance , so that when you have done the will of God , you may receive what was promised .
58010037	
58010038	
58010039	But we are not of those who shrink back and are destroyed , but of those who have faith and keep their souls .
58011001	Now faith is the assurance of things hoped for , the conviction of things not seen .
58011002	For by it the men of old received divine approval .
58011003	By faith we understand that the world was created by the word of God , so that what is seen was not made out of things which are visible .
58011004	By faith Abel offered God a more acceptable sacrifice than Cain , through which he was commended as a righteous man , when God spoke well of his gifts . And through faith he still speaks , even though he is dead .
58011005	By faith Enoch was taken up so that he should not see death ; and he was not found , because God had taken him . For before he was taken he was attested as having pleased God .
58011006	And without faith it is impossible to please God , for anyone who comes to him must believe that he exists and that he rewards those who earnestly seek him .
58011007	By faith Noah , being warned by God about things not yet seen , in godly fear prepared an ark for the salvation of his household , by which he condemned the world , and became an heir of the righteousness which comes by faith .
58011008	By faith Abraham obeyed when he was called to go out to a place which he was to receive as an inheritance ; and he went out , not knowing where he was going .
58011009	By faith he lived in the land of promise , as in a foreign land , dwelling in tents with Isaac and Jacob , heirs with him of the same promise ;
58011010	for he was looking forward to the city which has foundations , whose architect and builder is God .
58011011	By faith Sarah herself received power to conceive , even when she was past the age , because she considered him faithful who had promised .
58011012	Therefore from one man , and him as good as dead , were born descendants as many as the stars of heaven and as the innumerable grains of sand by the seashore .
58011013	These all died in faith , not having received the promises , but having seen them and greeted them from a distance , and having acknowledged that they were strangers and exiles on the earth .
58011014	For people who say such things make it clear that they are seeking a country of their own .
58011015	And if they had been thinking of that country from which they had gone out , they would have had opportunity to return .
58011016	But as it is , they desire a better country , that is , a heavenly one . Therefore God is not ashamed to be called their God , for he has prepared for them a city .
58011017	By faith Abraham , when he was tested , offered up Isaac , and he who had received the promises was ready to offer up his only son ,
58011018	of whom it was said , » Through Isaac shall your descendants be called . «
58011019	He considered that God was able to raise men even from the dead ; from which , figuratively speaking , he did receive him back .
58011020	By faith Isaac blessed Jacob and Esau in regard to their future .
58011021	By faith Jacob , when he was dying , blessed each of the sons of Joseph , and worshipped as he leaned on the top of his staff .
58011022	By faith Joseph , when he was at the end of his life , made mention of the exodus of the Israelites , and gave orders concerning his bones .
58011023	By faith Moses , when he was born , was hidden for three months by his parents , because they saw he was a beautiful child ; and they were not afraid of the king's edict .
58011024	By faith Moses , when he was grown up , refused to be called the son of Pharaoh's daughter ,
58011025	choosing rather to share ill-treatment with the people of God than to enjoy the fleeting pleasures of sin .
58011026	He considered abuse suffered for the Christ greater wealth than the treasures of Egypt , for he was looking ahead to his reward .
58011027	By faith he left Egypt , not fearing the anger of the king ; for he endured as seeing him who is invisible .
58011028	By faith he kept the Passover and the sprinkling of the blood , so the destroyer of the firstborn would not touch them .
58011029	By faith the people passed through the Red Sea as on dry land ; but when the Egyptians tried to do so , they were drowned .
58011030	By faith the walls of Jericho fell down after they had been encircled for seven days .
58011031	By faith Rahab the harlot did not perish with those who were disobedient , because she had welcomed the spies .
58011032	And what more shall I say ? For time will fail me if I tell of Gideon , Barak , Samson , Jephthah , of David and Samuel and the prophets ,
58011033	who through faith conquered kingdoms , performed acts of justice , received promises , shut the mouths of lions ,
58011034	quenched the power of fire , escaped the edge of the sword , whose weakness was turned to strength , who became mighty in war , and put foreign armies to flight .
58011035	Women received back their dead , raised to life again . Others were tortured and refused to be released , so that they might gain a better resurrection .
58011036	And others experienced mockings and scourgings , yes , also chains and imprisonment .
58011037	They were stoned , they were sawn in two , they were killed with the sword ; they went about in skins of sheep and goats , destitute , afflicted , ill-treated –
58011038	of whom the world was not worthy – wandering in deserts and mountains , and in caves and holes in the ground .
58011039	And all these , though well attested by their faith , did not receive what was promised ,
58011040	because God had provided something better for us , that apart from us they should not be made perfect .
58012001	Therefore , since we are surrounded by so great a cloud of witnesses , let us also lay aside every weight , and the sin which so easily entangles us , and let us run with perseverance the race that is set before us ,
58012002	fixing our eyes on Jesus , the author and perfecter of our faith , who for the joy that was set before him endured the cross , despising the shame , and sat down at the right hand of the throne of God .
58012003	Consider him who endured from sinners such hostility against himself , so that you may not grow weary and lose heart .
58012004	In your struggle against sin , you have not yet resisted to the point of shedding your blood .
58012005	And have you forgotten the exhortation which addresses you as sons ? – » My son , do not regard lightly the discipline of the Lord , nor lose courage when you are rebuked by him .
58012006	
58012007	It is for discipline that you endure . God is treating you as sons ; for what son is there whom his father does not discipline ?
58012008	If you are left without discipline , in which all have become partakers , then you are illegitimate children and not sons .
58012009	Besides this , we have had fathers of our flesh to discipline us and we respected them . Shall we not much more be subject to the Father of spirits and live ?
58012010	For they disciplined us for a short time as seemed best to them , but he disciplines us for our good , that we may share his holiness .
58012011	For the moment all discipline seems painful rather than pleasant ; but later it yields the peaceful fruit of righteousness to those who have been trained by it .
58012012	Therefore lift your feeble hands and strengthen your weak knees ,
58012013	and make straight paths for your feet , so that what is lame may not be put out of joint , but rather be healed .
58012014	Strive for peace with all men , and for the holiness without which no one will see the Lord .
58012015	See to it that no one comes short of the grace of God ; that no root of bitterness spring up and cause trouble , and by it many become defiled ;
58012016	that no one be immoral or godless like Esau , who sold his own birthright for a single meal .
58012017	For you know that afterward , when he desired to inherit the blessing , he was rejected , for he found no place for repentance , though he sought it diligently with tears .
58012018	For you have not come to a mountain that can be touched and to a blazing fire , and to darkness and gloom and whirlwind ,
58012019	and the blast of a trumpet , and the sound of a voice whose words made the hearers beg that no further word be spoken to them .
58012020	For they could not endure the order that was given , » If even a beast touches the mountain , it shall be stoned . «
58012021	The sight was so terrifying that Moses said , » I am trembling with fear . «
58012022	But you have come to Mount Zion and to the city of the living God , the heavenly Jerusalem , and to myriads of angels , to the joyful assembly
58012023	and church of the firstborn who are enrolled in heaven , and to God , the Judge of all , and to the spirits of righteous men made perfect ,
58012024	and to Jesus , the mediator of a new covenant , and to the sprinkled blood that speaks better than the blood of Abel .
58012025	See to it that you do not refuse him who is speaking . For if they did not escape when they refused him who warned them on earth , how much less shall we escape , if we turn away from him who warns us from heaven ?
58012026	Then his voice shook the earth , but now he has promised , » Yet once more I will shake not only the earth , but also heaven . «
58012027	This phrase , » Yet once more , « indicates the removing of those things which can be shaken , as of created things , in order that what cannot be shaken may remain .
58012028	Therefore , since we are receiving a kingdom that cannot be shaken , let us be thankful , and offer to God acceptable worship with reverence and awe ,
58012029	for our God is a consuming fire .
58013001	Let brotherly love continue .
58013002	Do not forget to show hospitality to strangers , for by so doing some people have entertained angels without knowing it .
58013003	Remember the prisoners , as though in prison with them , and those who are ill-treated , since you yourselves are also in the body .
58013004	Let marriage be held in honor among all , and let the marriage bed be undefiled ; for God will judge the immoral and adulterous .
58013005	Keep your lives free from the love of money and be content with what you have , for God has said , » I will never leave you , nor will I forsake you . «
58013006	So we say with confidence , » The Lord is my helper ; I will not be afraid . What can man do to me ? «
58013007	Remember your leaders , those who spoke to you the word of God ; consider the outcome of their life , and imitate their faith .
58013008	Jesus Christ is the same yesterday and today and forever .
58013009	Do not be carried away by varied and strange teachings ; for it is good for the heart to be strengthened by grace , not by foods , through which those who were so occupied were not benefited .
58013010	We have an altar from which those who serve the tabernacle have no right to eat .
58013011	For the bodies of those animals whose blood is brought into the holy place by the high priest as an offering for sin , are burned outside the camp .
58013012	And so Jesus also suffered outside the city gate to sanctify the people through his own blood .
58013013	Let us , then , go to him outside the camp , bearing the disgrace he bore .
58013014	For here we do not have an enduring city , but we are looking for the city which is to come .
58013015	Through him then let us continually offer up a sacrifice of praise to God , that is , the fruit of lips that acknowledge his name .
58013016	Do not forget to do good and to share with others , for with such sacrifices God is pleased .
58013017	Obey your leaders and submit to them ; for they are keeping watch over your souls , as men who will have to give account . Let them do this with joy , and not with grief , for that would be of no advantage to you .
58013018	Pray for us , for we are sure that we have a clear conscience , desiring to live honorably in all things .
58013019	I urge you all the more to do this so that I may be restored to you the sooner .
58013020	Now may the God of peace who brought again from the dead our Lord Jesus , that great shepherd of the sheep , through the blood of the eternal covenant ,
58013021	equip you with every good thing to do his will , working in us that which is pleasing in his sight , through Jesus Christ , to whom be glory for ever and ever . Amen .
58013022	I urge you , brethren , bear with my word of exhortation , for I have written to you briefly .
58013023	You should know that our brother Timothy has been released , with whom I will see you if he comes soon .
58013024	Greet all your leaders and all the saints . Those who come from Italy send you greetings .
58013025	Grace be with you all .
59001001	James , a servant of God and of the Lord Jesus Christ , to the twelve tribes in the Dispersion : greetings .
59001002	Consider it all joy , my brethren , when you encounter various trials ,
59001003	for you know that the testing of your faith produces endurance .
59001004	And let endurance have its perfect result , so that you may be perfect and complete , lacking in nothing .
59001005	If any of you lacks wisdom , let him ask of God , who gives to all generously and without reproach , and it will be given to him .
59001006	But he must ask in faith , with no doubting , for he who doubts is like a wave of the sea that is driven and tossed by the wind .
59001007	For that man ought not to expect that he will receive anything from the Lord ,
59001008	being a double-minded man , unstable in all his ways .
59001009	But the brother of humble circumstances is to glory in his high position ;
59001010	and the rich man is to glory in his humiliation , because like the flower of the grass he will pass away .
59001011	For the sun rises with its scorching heat and withers the grass ; its flower falls and its beauty is destroyed . So will the rich man fade away in the midst of his pursuits .
59001012	Blessed is the man who perseveres under trial , for when he has stood the test , he will receive the crown of life that God has promised to those who love him .
59001013	Let no one say when he is tempted , » I am being tempted by God « ; for God cannot be tempted by evil , and he himself does not tempt anyone .
59001014	But each one is tempted when he is carried away and enticed by his own desire .
59001015	Then when desire has conceived , it gives birth to sin ; and when sin is full-grown , it brings forth death .
59001016	Do not be deceived , my beloved brethren .
59001017	Every good thing given and every perfect gift is from above , coming down from the Father of lights , with whom there is no variation or shifting shadow .
59001018	Of his own will he brought us forth by the word of truth , that we should be a kind of first fruits of his creatures .
59001019	This you know , my beloved brethren . But everyone must be quick to hear , slow to speak and slow to anger ,
59001020	for the anger of man does not produce the righteousness of God .
59001021	Therefore , putting aside all filthiness and rank growth of wickedness , in humility receive the implanted word , which is able to save your souls .
59001022	But prove yourselves doers of the word , and not merely hearers who deceive themselves .
59001023	For if anyone is a hearer of the word and not a doer , he is like a man who looks at his natural face in a mirror ;
59001024	for he looks at himself and goes away , and immediately forgets what he was like .
59001025	But one who looks intently into the perfect law , the law of liberty , and abides by it , not having become a forgetful hearer but a doer that acts , this man will be blessed in what he does .
59001026	If anyone thinks himself to be religious , and yet does not bridle his tongue but deceives his own heart , this man's religion is worthless .
59001027	Religion that is pure and undefiled in the sight of our God and Father is this : to visit orphans and widows in their distress , and to keep oneself unstained by the world .
59002001	My brethren , show no favoritism as you hold your faith in our glorious Lord Jesus Christ .
59002002	For if a man comes into your assembly with a gold ring and dressed in fine clothes , and there also comes in a poor man in shabby clothes ,
59002003	and you pay special attention to the one who is wearing the fine clothes and say , » Have a seat here in a good place , « and you say to the poor man , » You stand there , « or , » Sit by my feet , «
59002004	have you not made distinctions among yourselves , and become judges with evil thoughts ?
59002005	Listen , my beloved brethren : has not God chosen those who are poor in the world to be rich in faith and heirs of the kingdom which he has promised to those who love him ?
59002006	But you have dishonored the poor man . Is it not the rich who oppress you ? Is it not they who drag you into court ?
59002007	Is it not they who blaspheme the honorable name by which you have been called ?
59002008	If you really fulfill the royal law , according to the scripture , » You shall love your neighbor as yourself , « you are doing well .
59002009	But if you show partiality , you commit sin , and are convicted by the law as transgressors .
59002010	For whoever keeps the whole law and yet stumbles in one point has become guilty of all of it .
59002011	For he who said , » Do not commit adultery , « said also , » Do not murder . « If you do not commit adultery but do commit murder , you have become a transgressor of the law .
59002012	So speak and so act as those who are to be judged by the law of liberty .
59002013	For judgment will be without mercy to one who has shown no mercy ; mercy triumphs over judgment .
59002014	What good is it , my brethren , if a man says he has faith but has no works ? Can such faith save him ?
59002015	If a brother or sister is without clothing and in need of daily food ,
59002016	and one of you says to them , » Go in peace , be warmed and filled , « and yet you do not give them what is necessary for their body , what use is that ?
59002017	So faith by itself , if it has no works , is dead .
59002018	But someone will say , » You have faith and I have works . « Show me your faith without the works , and I will show you my faith by my works .
59002019	You believe that God is one ; you do well . Even the demons believe — and shudder .
59002020	But are you willing to know , O foolish man , that faith without works is useless ?
59002021	Was not Abraham our father justified by works when he offered up Isaac his son on the altar ?
59002022	You see that faith was working with his works , and faith was completed by works ,
59002023	and the scripture was fulfilled which says , » Abraham believed God , and it was reckoned to him as righteousness « , and he was called the friend of God .
59002024	You see that a man is justified by works and not by faith alone .
59002025	In the same way was not Rahab the harlot also justified by works , when she received the messengers and sent them out by another way ?
59002026	For as the body without the spirit is dead , so faith without works is dead also .
59003001	Let not many of you become teachers , my brethren , for you know that we who teach will be judged with greater strictness .
59003002	For we all stumble in many ways . If anyone does not stumble in what he says , he is a perfect man , able to bridle the whole body as well .
59003003	If we put bits into the mouths of horses that they may obey us , we guide their whole bodies .
59003004	Look at the ships also ; though they are so great and are driven by strong winds , they are guided by a very small rudder wherever the will of the pilot directs .
59003005	So also the tongue is a small part of the body , and yet it boasts of great things . See how great a forest is set aflame by such a small fire !
59003006	And the tongue is a fire , a world of evil among the members of the body . The tongue corrupts our whole person , sets the whole course of our life on fire , and is itself set on fire by hell .
59003007	For every species of beasts and birds , of reptiles and creatures of the sea , is tamed and has been tamed by the human race .
59003008	But no man can tame the tongue . It is a restless evil , full of deadly poison .
59003009	With it we bless our Lord and Father , and with it we curse men , who have been made in the likeness of God .
59003010	From the same mouth come blessing and cursing . My brethren , this ought not to be so .
59003011	Does a spring pour forth from the same opening both fresh and bitter water ?
59003012	Can a fig tree , my brethren , produce olives , or a grapevine produce figs ? Nor can salt water produce fresh .
59003013	Who is wise and understanding among you ? By his good life let him show his deeds in the humility of wisdom .
59003014	But if you have bitter jealousy and selfish ambition in your hearts , do not boast and be false to the truth .
59003015	This wisdom is not such as comes down from above , but is earthly , unspiritual , demonic .
59003016	For where jealousy and selfish ambition exist , there will be disorder and every evil practice .
59003017	But the wisdom from above is first pure , then peaceable , gentle , open to reason , full of mercy and good fruits , without uncertainty or hypocrisy .
59003018	And the harvest of righteousness is sown in peace by those who make peace .
59004001	What causes quarrels and fights among you ? Is it not your passions that are at war in your members ?
59004002	You desire and do not have ; so you kill . And you covet and cannot obtain ; so you fight and quarrel . You do not have , because you do not ask .
59004003	You ask and do not receive , because you ask with wrong motives , so that you may spend it on your pleasures .
59004004	You adulteresses , do you not know that friendship with the world is hostility toward God ? Therefore whoever wishes to be a friend of the world makes himself an enemy of God .
59004005	Or do you think that the Scripture says without reason : » He jealously desires the Spirit which he has made to dwell in us « ?
59004006	But he gives more grace . Therefore it says , » God opposes the proud , but gives grace to the humble . «
59004007	Submit yourselves therefore to God . Resist the devil and he will flee from you .
59004008	Draw near to God and he will draw near to you . Cleanse your hands , you sinners , and purify your hearts , you double-minded .
59004009	Be miserable and mourn and weep . Let your laughter be turned to mourning and your joy to gloom .
59004010	Humble yourselves before the Lord , and he will exalt you .
59004011	Do not speak against one another , brethren . He who speaks against a brother or judges his brother , speaks against the law and judges the law . But if you judge the law , you are not a doer of the law but a judge of it .
59004012	There is only one Lawgiver and Judge , the one who is able to save and destroy . But you — who are you to judge your neighbor ?
59004013	Come now , you who say , » Today or tomorrow we will go to such and such a city , and spend a year there and engage in business and make a profit . «
59004014	Yet you do not know what will happen tomorrow . What is your life ? You are a mist that appears for a little while and then vanishes .
59004015	Instead , you ought to say , » If the Lord wills , we will live and do this or that . «
59004016	As it is , you boast in your arrogance . All such boasting is evil .
59004017	Therefore , to one who knows the right thing to do and does not do it , to him it is sin .
59005001	Come now , you rich , weep and howl for the miseries that are coming upon you .
59005002	Your riches have rotted and your garments are moth-eaten .
59005003	Your gold and silver have rusted , and their rust will be evidence against you and will eat your flesh like fire . You have laid up treasure in the last days .
59005004	Behold , the wages of the laborers who mowed your fields , which you kept back by fraud , cry out against you ; and the cries of the harvesters have reached the ears of the Lord of hosts .
59005005	You have lived on the earth in luxury and in pleasure ; you have fattened your hearts in a day of slaughter .
59005006	You have condemned and put to death the righteous man ; he does not resist you .
59005007	Therefore be patient , brethren , until the coming of the Lord . See how the farmer waits for the precious fruit of the earth , being patient over it , until it receives the early and late rains .
59005008	You too be patient ; strengthen your hearts , for the coming of the Lord is near .
59005009	Do not grumble , brethren , against one another , that you may not be judged ; behold , the Judge is standing at the door .
59005010	As an example , brethren , of suffering and patience , take the prophets who spoke in the name of the Lord .
59005011	Behold , we call those blessed who endured . You have heard of the endurance of Job , and you have seen the purpose of the Lord , how the Lord is full of compassion and mercy .
59005012	But above all , my brethren , do not swear , either by heaven or by earth or with any other oath , but let your yes be yes and your no be no , that you may not fall under condemnation .
59005013	Is anyone among you suffering ? He should pray . Is anyone cheerful ? Let him sing praise .
59005014	Is any among you sick ? Let him call for the elders of the church , and let them pray over him , anointing him with oil in the name of the Lord ;
59005015	and the prayer offered in faith will save the sick man , and the Lord will raise him up ; and if he has committed sins , he will be forgiven .
59005016	Therefore , confess your sins to one another , and pray for one another so that you may be healed . The prayer of a righteous man is powerful and effective .
59005017	Elijah was a man with a nature like ours , and he prayed earnestly that it would not rain , and it did not rain on the earth for three years and six months .
59005018	Then he prayed again , and the heavens gave rain and the earth produced its fruit .
59005019	My brethren , if anyone among you wanders from the truth and someone brings him back ,
59005020	let him know that whoever turns a sinner from the error of his way will save his soul from death and will cover a multitude of sins .
60001001	Peter , an apostle of Jesus Christ , to the chosen exiles in the Dispersion , scattered throughout Pontus , Galatia , Cappadocia , Asia and Bithynia ,
60001002	who have been chosen according to the foreknowledge of God the Father , by the sanctifying work of the Spirit , for obedience to Jesus Christ and sprinkling with his blood : may grace and peace be yours in abundance .
60001003	Blessed be to the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ ! In his great mercy he has caused us to be born again into a living hope through the resurrection of Jesus Christ from the dead ,
60001004	to obtain an inheritance which is imperishable and undefiled and will not fade away , kept in heaven for you ,
60001005	who are protected by God's power through faith for a salvation ready to be revealed in the last time .
60001006	In this you greatly rejoice , though now for a little while you may have to suffer various trials ,
60001007	so that the proof of your faith , being more precious than gold which is perishable , even though tested by fire , may be found to result in praise and glory and honor at the revelation of Jesus Christ .
60001008	Though you have not seen him , you love him ; and even though you do not see him now , you believe in him and rejoice with an inexpressible and glorious joy ,
60001009	as you obtain the outcome of your faith , the salvation of your souls .
60001010	As to this salvation , the prophets who prophesied of the grace that would come to you inquired and searched carefully ,
60001011	seeking to know what person or time the Spirit of Christ within them was indicating when he predicted the sufferings of Christ and the glories to follow .
60001012	It was revealed to them that they were not serving themselves , but you , in these things which now have been announced to you through those who preached the gospel to you by the Holy Spirit sent from heaven — things into which angels long to look .
60001013	Therefore , prepare your minds for action , be sober in spirit , set your hope fully on the grace to be given you at the revelation of Jesus Christ .
60001014	As obedient children , do not be conformed to the former lusts which were yours in your ignorance ,
60001015	but as he who called you is holy , be holy yourselves in all your conduct ;
60001016	because it is written , » You shall be holy , for I am holy . «
60001017	If you address as Father the One who impartially judges according to each one's work , conduct yourselves in fear during the time of your exile on earth .
60001018	You know that you were redeemed from the futile way of life inherited from your forefathers , not with perishable things such as silver or gold ,
60001019	but with the precious blood of Christ , like that of a lamb without blemish or spot .
60001020	He was destined before the foundation of the world , but was revealed in these last times for your sake .
60001021	Through him you have confidence in God , who raised him from the dead and gave him glory , so that your faith and hope are in God .
60001022	Since you have purified your souls by obedience to the truth for a sincere love of the brethren , love one another earnestly from the heart .
60001023	For you have been born again , not of perishable seed , but of imperishable , through the living and enduring word of God .
60001024	For , » All flesh is like grass , and all its glory like the flower of grass . The grass withers , and the flower falls ,
60001025	
60002001	Therefore , put away all malice and all deceit and hypocrisy and envy and all slander .
60002002	Like newborn babes , long for the pure spiritual milk , so that by it you may grow up in your salvation ,
60002003	for you have tasted the kindness of the Lord .
60002004	As you come to him , the living Stone — rejected by men but chosen and precious in the sight of God —
60002005	you also , like living stones , are being built into a spiritual house to be a holy priesthood , to offer spiritual sacrifices acceptable to God through Jesus Christ .
60002006	For it stands in scripture : » Behold , I lay in Zion a stone , a cornerstone chosen and precious , and he who believes in him will not be put to shame . «
60002007	To you therefore who believe , this is precious , but for those who do not believe , » The very stone which the builders rejected has become the chief cornerstone , «
60002008	and , » A stone that causes men to stumble and a rock that makes them fall ; « they stumble because they disobey the word — as they were desstined to do .
60002009	But you are a chosen race , a royal priesthood , a holy nation , a people for God's own possession , that you may declare the praises of him who called you out of darkness into his marvelous light .
60002010	
60002011	Beloved , I urge you as aliens and strangers to abstain from fleshly lusts which wage war against your soul .
60002012	Maintain good conduct among the Gentiles , so that in case they speak against you as wrongdoers , they may see your good deeds and glorify God on the day of visitation .
60002013	Submit yourselves for the Lord's sake to every human institution , whether to a king as the supreme authority ,
60002014	or to governors as sent by him to punish those who do wrong and to praise those who do right .
60002015	For it is God's will that by doing right you should silence the ignorance of foolish men .
60002016	Live as free men , but do not use your freedom as a covering for evil ; live as servants of God .
60002017	Honor all people , love the brotherhood , fear God , honor the king .
60002018	Servants , be submissive to your masters with all respect , not only to those who are good and gentle , but also to those who are overbearing .
60002019	For a man is approved if , mindful of God , he bears up under pain while suffering unjustly .
60002020	For what credit is it , if when you do wrong and are beaten for it you patiently endure ? But if when you do right and suffer for it you patiently endure , you have favor with God .
60002021	For to this you have been called , because Christ also suffered for you , leaving you an example , that you should follow in his steps .
60002022	
60002023	when he was reviled , he did not revile in return ; when he suffered , he uttered no threats , but he trusted himself to him who judges justly .
60002024	He himself bore our sins in his body on the tree , so that we might die to sin and live for righteousness ; by his wounds you have been healed .
60002025	For you were straying like sheep , but now you have returned to the Shepherd and Guardian of your souls .
60003001	You wives , in the same way be submissive to your husbands so that , if any of them do not believe the word , they may be won over without a word by the behavior of their wives ,
60003002	when they see your chaste and respectful behavior .
60003003	Your adornment must not be merely outward — braiding the hair , and wearing gold jewelry , or putting on fine clothing ;
60003004	but let it be the hidden person of the heart , with the imperishable beauty of a gentle and quiet spirit , which is precious in God's sight .
60003005	For in this way in former times the holy women also , who hoped in God , used to adorn themselves , and were submissive to their own husbands ;
60003006	just as Sarah obeyed Abraham , calling him lord . And you are her children if you do what is right and are not frightened by any fear .
60003007	Husbands , in the same way be considerate as you live with your wives , and treat them with honor as the weaker partner , since you are joint heirs of the grace of life , so that your prayers will not be hindered .
60003008	Finally , all of you , live in harmony with one another ; be sympathetic , love as brothers , be compassionate and humble in spirit .
60003009	Do not return evil for evil or insult for insult , but give a blessing instead ; for to this you were called , that you may inherit a blessing .
60003010	For , » He who would love life and see good days must keep his tongue from evil and his lips from speaking deceit .
60003011	
60003012	
60003013	Who is there to harm you if you are zealous for what is good ?
60003014	But even if you should suffer for the sake of righteousness , you are blessed . Do not fear their intimidation , and do not be troubled ,
60003015	but in your hearts reverence Christ as Lord . Always be prepared to make a defense to everyone who asks you to give an account for the hope that is in you , yet do it with gentleness and respect ;
60003016	and keep a clear conscience , so that , when you are abused , those who revile your good behavior in Christ may be put to shame .
60003017	For it is better to suffer for doing right , if that should be God's will , than for doing wrong .
60003018	For Christ also died for sins once for all , the righteous for the unrighteous , that he might bring us to God , being put to death in the flesh but made alive in the spirit ;
60003019	in which also he went and preached to the spirits in prison ,
60003020	who formerly did not obey , when the patience of God waited in the days of Noah , during the building of the ark , in which a few , that is , eight persons , were saved through water .
60003021	And corresponding to that , baptism now saves you — not the removal of dirt from the flesh , but an appeal to God for a good conscience — through the resurrection of Jesus Christ ,
60003022	who has gone into heaven and is at the right hand of God , with angels and authorities and powers subject to him .
60004001	Therefore , since Christ has suffered in the flesh , arm yourselves also with the same purpose , because he who has suffered in the flesh has ceased from sin ,
60004002	so as to live the rest of the time in the flesh no longer for human lusts , but for the will of God .
60004003	For you have spent enough time in the past doing what the Gentiles like to do , living in debauchery , lust , drunkenness , orgies , carousing , and lawless idolatry .
60004004	In all this , they are surprised that you do not run with them into the same flood of dissipation , and they abuse you ;
60004005	but they will give account to him who is ready to judge the living and the dead .
60004006	For this reason the gospel was preached even to those who are dead , that though they are judged in the flesh as men , they might live in the spirit according to the will of God .
60004007	The end of all things is near ; therefore be clear minded and sober for your prayers .
60004008	Above all , hold unfailing your love for one another , because love covers a multitude of sins .
60004009	Offer hospitality to one another without grumbling .
60004010	As each one has received a special gift , employ it in serving one another as good stewards of God's varied grace .
60004011	Whoever speaks is to do so as one who is speaking the utterances of God ; whoever serves is to do so as one who is serving by the strength which God supplies ; so that in all things God may be glorified through Jesus Christ . To him belongs the glory and dominion for ever and ever . Amen .
60004012	Beloved , do not be surprised at the fiery ordeal which comes upon you to test you , as though something strange were happening to you .
60004013	But rejoice that you share in the sufferings of Christ , so that you may also be overjoyed when his glory is revealed .
60004014	If you are insulted because of the name of Christ , you are blessed , for the Spirit of glory and of God rests on you .
60004015	But let none of you suffer as a murderer , or a thief , or a wrongdoer , or a troublesome meddler ;
60004016	yet if one suffers as a Christian , let him not be ashamed , but under that name let him glorify God .
60004017	For it is time for judgment to begin with the household of God ; and if it begins with us , what will be the outcome for those who do not obey the gospel of God ?
60004018	And » if it is hard for the righteous to be saved , what will become of the godless man and the sinner ? «
60004019	Therefore , let those who suffer according to God's will do right and entrust their souls to a faithful Creator .
60005001	So I exhort the elders among you , as a fellow elder and a witness of the sufferings of Christ and a partaker in the glory that is to be revealed ,
60005002	shepherd the flock of God that is under your care , serving as overseers — not under compulsion , but voluntarily , according to the will of God ; and not for sordid gain , but with eagerness ;
60005003	not as lording it over those in your charge , but being examples to the flock .
60005004	And when the Chief Shepherd appears , you will receive the unfading crown of glory .
60005005	Likewise you that are younger men be subject to the elders . Clothe yourselves , all of you , with humility toward one another , for » God opposes the proud , but gives grace to the humble . «
60005006	Therefore humble yourselves under the mighty hand of God , that he may exalt you in due time .
60005007	Cast all your anxiety on him , because he cares for you .
60005008	Be sober , be alert . Your adversary the devil prowls around like a roaring lion , seeking someone to devour .
60005009	But resist him , firm in your faith , knowing that the same experiences of suffering are being accomplished by your brethren throughout the world .
60005010	And after you have suffered a little while , the God of all grace , who has called you to his eternal glory in Christ , will himself restore , establish , and strengthen you .
60005011	To him be the dominion for ever and ever . Amen .
60005012	With the help of Silvanus , a faithful brother as I regard him , I have written to you briefly , exhorting you and testifying that this is the true grace of God . Stand fast in it .
60005013	She who is in Babylon , chosen together with you , sends you her greetings , and so does my son Mark .
60005014	Greet one another with a kiss of love . Peace to all of you who are in Christ .
61001001	Simon Peter , a servant and apostle of Jesus Christ , to those who have received a faith of the same kind as ours , by the righteousness of our God and Savior , Jesus Christ :
61001002	grace and peace be multiplied to you in the knowledge of God and of Jesus our Lord .
61001003	His divine power has granted to us everything pertaining to life and godliness , through the true knowledge of him who called us by his own glory and excellence .
61001004	By these he has granted to us his precious and very great promises , so that through them you may escape from the corruption that is in the world because of lust , and become partakers of the divine nature .
61001005	For this very reason , make every effort to add to your faith virtue ; and to virtue , knowledge ,
61001006	and to knowledge , self-control , and to self-control , perseverance , and to perseverance , godliness ,
61001007	and to godliness , brotherly kindness , and to brotherly kindness , love .
61001008	For if these qualities are yours and are increasing , they keep you from being ineffective or unfruitful in the knowledge of our Lord Jesus Christ .
61001009	For whoever lacks these things is blind and shortsighted , and has forgotten that he was cleansed from his old sins .
61001010	Therefore , brethren , be all the more eager to make your calling and election sure . For if you do these things , you will never fall ;
61001011	so there will be an entrance richly provided for you into the eternal kingdom of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ .
61001012	Therefore I will always remind you of these things , even though you know them and are firmly established in the truth you now have .
61001013	I think it right , as long as I am in this body , to stir you up by way of reminder ,
61001014	since I know that the putting aside of my body will be soon , as our Lord Jesus Christ has made clear to me .
61001015	And I will see to it that after my departure you will be able at any time to call these things to mind .
61001016	For we did not follow cleverly devised tales when we made known to you the power and coming of our Lord Jesus Christ , but we were eyewitnesses of his majesty .
61001017	For he received honor and glory from God the Father when the voice came to him by the Majestic Glory , saying , » This is my beloved Son , with whom I am well pleased . «
61001018	We ourselves heard this voice coming from heaven when we were with him on the holy mountain .
61001019	And we have the prophetic word made more sure , and you will do well to pay attention to this as to a lamp shining in a dark place , until the day dawns and the morning star rises in your hearts .
61001020	First of all you must understand this , that no prophecy of scripture is a matter of one's own interpretation ,
61001021	for no prophecy was ever made by the act of human will , but men moved by the Holy Spirit spoke from God .
61002001	But false prophets also arose among the people , just as there will also be false teachers among you , who will secretly introduce destructive heresies , even denying the Master who bought them , bringing swift destruction upon themselves .
61002002	And many will follow their licentiousness , and because of them the way of truth will be reviled .
61002003	And in their greed they will exploit you with false words ; from long ago their condemnation has not been idle , and their destruction has not been asleep .
61002004	For if God did not spare angels when they sinned , but cast them into hell and committed them to pits of darkness , to be reserved for judgment ;
61002005	and if he did not spare the ancient world , but preserved Noah , a preacher of righteousness , with seven others , when he brought a flood upon the world of the ungodly ;
61002006	and if he condemned the cities of Sodom and Gomorrah to destruction by reducing them to ashes , having made them an example to those who would live ungodly thereafter ;
61002007	and if he rescued Lot , a righteous man , who was distressed by the filthy lives of lawless men
61002008	( for by what he saw and heard that righteous man , while living among them , felt his righteous soul tormented day after day by their lawless deeds ) ,
61002009	then the Lord knows how to rescue the godly from trial , and to keep the unrighteous under punishment for the day of judgment ,
61002010	and especially those who indulge the flesh in its corrupt desire and despise authority . Bold and willful , they are not afraid to revile the glorious ones ,
61002011	whereas angels , though greater in power and might , do not bring a reviling judgment against them before the Lord .
61002012	But these , like irrational animals , creatures of instinct , born to be caught and killed , reviling in matters of which they are ignorant , will be destroyed in the same destruction with them ,
61002013	suffering wrong for their wrongdoing . They count it a pleasure to revel in the daytime . They are blots and blemishes , reveling in their deceptions , as they carouse with you .
61002014	They have eyes full of adultery , that never cease from sin ; they entice unstable souls . They have hearts trained in greed . Accursed children !
61002015	Forsaking the right way , they have gone astray , having followed the way of Balaam , the son of Beor , who loved the wages of unrighteousness ;
61002016	but he was rebuked for his own transgression by a donkey — a beast without speech — who spoke with a man's voice and restrained the prophet's madness .
61002017	These are springs without water and mists driven by a storm ; for them the blackest darkness has been reserved .
61002018	For speaking out arrogant words of vanity , they entice by fleshly desires , by sensuality , those who barely escape from the ones who live in error .
61002019	They promise them freedom , while they themselves are slaves of corruption ; for whatever overcomes a man , to that he is enslaved .
61002020	For if , after they have escaped the defilements of the world by the knowledge of the Lord and Savior Jesus Christ , they are again entangled in them and are overcome , the last state has become worse for them than the first .
61002021	For it would have been better for them not to have known the way of righteousness , than having known it , to turn away from the holy commandment handed on to them .
61002022	It has happened to them according to the true proverb , » A dog turns back to its own vomit , « and , » A sow , after having washed , returns to wallowing in the mire . «
61003001	This is now the second letter that I have written to you , beloved , and in both of them I have aroused your sincere mind by way of reminder ;
61003002	that you should remember the words spoken beforehand by the holy prophets and the commandment of the Lord and Savior spoken through your apostles .
61003003	First of all you must understand this , that scoffers will come in the last days , with scoffing , following their own lusts
61003004	and saying , » Where is the promise of his coming ? For ever since the fathers fell asleep , all things continue as they were from the beginning of creation . «
61003005	They deliberately ignore this fact , that by the word of God heavens existed long ago , and the earth was formed out of water and by means of water ,
61003006	through which the world at that time was destroyed , being deluged with water .
61003007	But by the same word the present heavens and earth are reserved for fire , being kept for the day of judgment and destruction of ungodly men .
61003008	But do not ignore this one fact , beloved , that with the Lord one day is like a thousand years , and a thousand years like one day .
61003009	The Lord is not slow about his promise , as some count slowness , but is patient toward you , not wishing for any to perish but for all to come to repentance .
61003010	But the day of the Lord will come like a thief , in which the heavens will pass away with a roar and the elements will be destroyed with fire , and the earth and the works that are in it will be burned up .
61003011	Since all these things are to be destroyed in this way , what sort of people ought you to be in holy lives and godliness ,
61003012	looking for and hastening the coming of the day of God , because of which the heavens will be destroyed by fire , and the elements will melt with intense heat !
61003013	But according to his promise we are looking for new heavens and a new earth , in which righteousness dwells .
61003014	Therefore , beloved , since you look for these things , be diligent to be found by him in peace , spotless and blameless .
61003015	And regard the patience of our Lord as salvation ; just as also our beloved brother Paul , according to the wisdom given him , wrote to you .
61003016	He writes the same way in all his letters , speaking in them of these matters . His letters contain some things that are hard to understand , which ignorant and unstable people distort , as they do the other Scriptures , to their own destruction .
61003017	You therefore , beloved , knowing this beforehand , be on your guard so that you are not carried away by the error of lawless men and fall from your own steadfastness .
61003018	But grow in the grace and knowledge of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ . To him be the glory both now and to the day of eternity . Amen .
62001001	That which was from the beginning , which we have heard , which we have seen with our eyes , which we have looked upon , and our hands have touched , concerning the Word of life —
62001002	the life was manifested , and we have seen it , and testify to it , and proclaim to you the eternal life which was with the Father and was manifested to us —
62001003	that which we have seen and heard we proclaim also to you , so that you may have fellowship with us ; and our fellowship is with the Father and with his Son Jesus Christ .
62001004	And we write this that our joy may be complete .
62001005	This is the message we have heard from him and declare to you , that God is light and in him is no darkness at all .
62001006	If we say we have fellowship with him , and walk in darkness , we lie and do not live according to the truth .
62001007	But if we walk in the light , as he is in the light , we have fellowship with one another , and the blood of Jesus his Son cleanses us from all sin .
62001008	If we say we have no sin , we deceive ourselves , and the truth is not in us .
62001009	If we confess our sins , he is faithful and just , and will forgive us our sins and cleanse us from all unrighteousness .
62001010	If we say that we have not sinned , we make him a liar , and his word is not in us .
62002001	My little children , I write this to you so that you may not sin . But if anyone does sin , we have an advocate with the Father , Jesus Christ the righteous .
62002002	And he is the atoning sacrifice for our sins , and not for ours only but also for the sins of the whole world .
62002003	Now by this we know that we know him , if we keep his commandments .
62002004	He who says , » I know him , « but does not keep his commandments , is a liar , and the truth is not in him .
62002005	But whoever keeps his word , truly the love of God is perfected in him . By this we know that we are in him :
62002006	he who says he abides in him ought to walk as he walked .
62002007	Beloved , I am writing you no new commandment , but an old commandment that you had from the beginning . The old commandment is the word that you have heard .
62002008	Yet I am writing you a new commandment , which is true in him and in you , because the darkness is passing away and the true light is already shining .
62002009	He who says he is in the light and hates his brother is in the darkness still .
62002010	He who loves his brother abides in the light , and there is no cause for stumbling in him .
62002011	But he who hates his brother is in the darkness and walks in the darkness , and does not know where he is going , because the darkness has blinded his eyes .
62002012	
62002013	
62002014	
62002015	Do not love the world or the things in the world . If anyone loves the world , the love of the Father is not in him .
62002016	For all that is in the world — the lust of the flesh , and the lust of the eyes , and the pride of life — is not of the Father but is of the world .
62002017	And the world is passing away , and the lust of it ; but he who does the will of God abides forever .
62002018	Little children , it is the last hour ; and as you have heard that the Antichrist is coming , even now many antichrists have come ; by this we know that it is the last hour .
62002019	They went out from us , but they were not of us ; for if they had been of us , they would have continued with us ; but they went out that it might be plain that none of them were of us .
62002020	But you have an anointing from the Holy One , and you all know .
62002021	I write to you , not because you do not know the truth , but because you know it , and because no lie is of the truth .
62002022	Who is the liar but he who denies that Jesus is the Christ ? This is the Antichrist , he who denies the Father and the Son .
62002023	No one who denies the Son has the Father ; whoever acknowledges the Son has the Father also .
62002024	Let that abide in you which you heard from the beginning . If what you heard from the beginning abides in you , then you also will abide in the Son and in the Father .
62002025	And this is what he has promised us — eternal life .
62002026	These things I have written to you about those who try to deceive you .
62002027	But the anointing which you have received from him abides in you , and you do not need that anyone teach you ; but as his anointing teaches you about all things , and is true , and is not a lie , and just as it has taught you , abide in him .
62002028	And now , little children , abide in him , so that when he appears we may have confidence and not be ashamed before him at his coming .
62002029	If you know that he is righteous , you know that everyone who does right is born of him .
62003001	See what love the Father has given us , that we should be called children of God ! And so we are ! The reason why the world does not know us is that it did not know him .
62003002	Beloved , now we are children of God ; and it has not yet been revealed what we shall be , but we know that when he appears , we shall be like him , for we shall see him as he is .
62003003	And everyone who has this hope in him purifies himself , just as he is pure .
62003004	Everyone who commits sin also commits lawlessness ; sin is lawlessness .
62003005	And you know that he appeared to take away our sins , and in him there is no sin .
62003006	No one who abides in him sins . No one who sins has either seen him or known him .
62003007	Little children , let no one deceive you . He who does right is righteous , just as he is righteous .
62003008	He who commits sin is of the devil , for the devil has sinned from the beginning . The reason the Son of God appeared was to destroy the works of the devil .
62003009	No one who is of God practices sin , for God’s seed remains in him ; and he cannot sin , because he has been born of God .
62003010	By this it may be seen who are the children of God , and who are the children of the devil : whoever does not do right is not of God , nor he who does not love his brother .
62003011	For this is the message which you heard from the beginning , that we should love one another ,
62003012	and not be like Cain who was of the evil one and murdered his brother . And why did he murder him ? Because his own deeds were evil and his brother's righteous .
62003013	Do not marvel , my brethren , if the world hates you .
62003014	We know that we have passed from death to life , because we love the brethren . He who does not love abides in death .
62003015	Anyone who hates his brother is a murderer , and you know that no murderer has eternal life abiding in him .
62003016	By this we know love , that he laid down his life for us . And we also ought to lay down our lives for the brethren .
62003017	But if anyone has the world's goods and sees his brother in need , yet closes his heart against him , how does the love of God abide in him ?
62003018	Little children , let us not love in word or tongue but in deed and in truth .
62003019	By this we know that we are of the truth , and shall assure our hearts before him
62003020	whenever our hearts condemn us ; for God is greater than our hearts , and he knows everything .
62003021	Beloved , if our hearts do not condemn us , we have confidence before God ;
62003022	and we receive from him whatever we ask , because we keep his commandments and do what pleases him .
62003023	And this is his commandment : that we should believe in the name of his Son Jesus Christ , and love one another , just as he has commanded us .
62003024	Now those who keep his commandments abide in him , and he in them . And by this we know that he abides in us , by the Spirit whom he has given us .
62004001	Beloved , do not believe every spirit , but test the spirits to see whether they are of God ; because many false prophets have gone out into the world .
62004002	By this you know the Spirit of God : every Spirit that confesses that Jesus Christ has come in the flesh is of God ,
62004003	and every spirit which does not confess Jesus is not of God . This is the spirit of the Antichrist , of which you have heard that it was coming , and now it is in the world already .
62004004	You are of God , little children , and have overcome them , because he who is in you is greater than he who is in the world .
62004005	They are of the world and therefore speak as of the world , and the world listens to them .
62004006	We are of God . Whoever knows God listens to us ; he who is not of God does not listen to us . By this we know the spirit of truth and the spirit of error .
62004007	Beloved , let us love one another , for love is of God ; and everyone who loves is born of God and knows God .
62004008	He who does not love does not know God , for God is love .
62004009	In this the love of God was made manifest among us , that God sent his only Son into the world , so that we might live through him .
62004010	In this is love , not that we loved God but that he loved us and sent his Son to be the atoning sacrifice for our sins .
62004011	Beloved , if God so loved us , we also ought to love one another .
62004012	No one has ever seen God ; but if we love one another , God abides in us and his love is perfected in us .
62004013	By this we know that we abide in him and he in us , because he has given us of his Spirit .
62004014	And we have seen and testify that the Father has sent his Son as the Savior of the world .
62004015	Whoever confesses that Jesus is the Son of God , God abides in him , and he in God .
62004016	So we know and believe the love God has for us . God is love , and he who abides in love abides in God , and God in him .
62004017	In this love is perfected among us , that we may have confidence for the Day of Judgment , because as he is so are we in this world .
62004018	There is no fear in love , but perfect love casts out fear , because fear has to do with punishment . And he who fears is not made perfect in love .
62004019	We love because he first loved us .
62004020	If anyone says , » I love God , « and hates his brother , he is a liar ; for he who does not love his brother whom he has seen , cannot love God whom he has not seen .
62004021	And this commandment we have from him : that he who loves God must love his brother also .
62005001	Everyone who believes that Jesus is the Christ is born of God , and everyone who loves the parent loves the child .
62005002	By this we know that we love the children of God , when we love God and obey his commandments .
62005003	For this is the love of God , that we keep his commandments . And his commandments are not burdensome .
62005004	For whatever is born of God overcomes the world . And this is the victory that has overcome the world — our faith .
62005005	Who is it that overcomes the world but he who believes that Jesus is the Son of God ?
62005006	This is he who came by water and blood — Jesus Christ ; not only by water , but by water and blood .
62005007	And it is the Spirit who bears witness , because the Spirit is the truth .
62005008	There are three witnesses , the Spirit , the water , and the blood ; and these three agree .
62005009	If we receive the testimony of men , the testimony of God is greater ; for this is the testimony of God which he has borne witness of his Son .
62005010	He who believes in the Son of God has the testimony in himself . He who does not believe God has made him a liar , because he has not believed in the testimony that God has given of his Son .
62005011	And this is the testimony : that God has given us eternal life , and this life is in his Son .
62005012	He who has the Son has life ; he who does not have the Son of God does not have life .
62005013	I write these things to you who believe in the name of the Son of God , so that you may know that you have eternal life .
62005014	And this is the confidence which we have in him , that if we ask anything according to his will he hears us .
62005015	And if we know that he hears us , whatever we ask , we know that we have the requests that we have asked of him .
62005016	If anyone sees his brother commit a sin that does not lead to death , he will ask , and God will give him life for those whose sin is not leading to death . There is sin leading to death . I do not say that he should pray about that .
62005017	All wrongdoing is sin , and there is sin that does not lead to death .
62005018	We know that anyone born of God does not sin ; but he who was born of God keeps him , and the evil one does not touch him .
62005019	We know that we are of God , and the whole world is under the power of the evil one .
62005020	And we know that the Son of God has come and has given us understanding , that we may know him who is true ; and we are in him who is true , in his Son Jesus Christ . This is the true God and eternal life .
62005021	Little children , keep yourselves from idols .
63001001	The elder to the chosen lady and her children , whom I love in the truth ; and not only I , but also all who know the truth ,
63001002	because of the truth which abides in us and will be with us forever :
63001003	grace , mercy , and peace will be with us , from God the Father and from Jesus Christ the Father's Son , in truth and love .
63001004	I rejoiced greatly to find some of your children walking in the truth , just as we have been commanded by the Father .
63001005	And now I ask you , lady , not as though I were writing you a new commandment , but the one we have had from the beginning , that we love one another .
63001006	And this is love , that we walk according to his commandments . This is the commandment , just as you have heard from the beginning , that you should walk in love .
63001007	For many deceivers , who do not acknowledge Jesus Christ as coming in the flesh , have gone out into the world . Any such person is the deceiver and the antichrist .
63001008	Watch yourselves , that you do not lose what you have worked for , but that you may receive a full reward .
63001009	Anyone who runs ahead and does not abide in the teaching of Christ does not have God ; he who abides in the teaching has both the Father and the Son .
63001010	If anyone comes to you and does not bring this teaching , do not receive him into your house or give him any greeting ;
63001011	for he who greets him shares in his wicked work .
63001012	Though I have much to write to you , I do not want to use paper and ink , but I hope to come to see you and talk with you face to face , so that our joy may be complete .
63001013	The children of your chosen sister greet you .
64001001	The elder to the beloved Gaius , whom I love in truth .
64001002	Beloved , I pray that you may be in good health and that all may go well with you , even as your soul is getting along well .
64001003	For I greatly rejoiced when some of the brethren arrived and testified to the truth of your life , and how you are walking in truth .
64001004	I have no greater joy than this , to hear that my children are walking in the truth .
64001005	Beloved , you are acting faithfully in whatever you accomplish for the brethren , and especially when they are strangers ;
64001006	and they have testified to your love before the church . You will do well to send them on their way in a manner worthy of God .
64001007	For they went out for the sake of the Name , accepting nothing from the Gentiles .
64001008	Therefore we ought to support such men , so that we may be fellow workers in the truth .
64001009	I wrote something to the church ; but Diotrephes , who loves to be first among them , does not accept what we say .
64001010	So if I come , I will call attention to what he is doing , gossiping against us with evil words . And not satisfied with that , he refuses himself to welcome the brethren , and also stops those who want to welcome them and puts them out of the church .
64001011	Beloved , do not imitate what is evil , but what is good . The one who does good is of God ; the one who does evil has not seen God .
64001012	Demetrius has received a good testimony from everyone , and from the truth itself ; and we add our testimony , and you know that our testimony is true .
64001013	I had much to write you , but I do not want to do so with pen and ink ;
64001014	I hope to see you soon , and we will talk face to face . Peace to you . The friends here send their greetings . Greet the friends there by name .
64001015	
65001001	Jude , a servant of Jesus Christ and brother of James , to those who are called , beloved in God the Father and kept for Jesus Christ :
65001002	may mercy , peace , and love be multiplied to you .
65001003	Beloved , although I was very eager to write you about our common salvation , I felt the necessity to write to you appealing that you contend for the faith which was once for all delivered to the saints .
65001004	For certain persons have crept in secretly , those who were long ago marked out for this condemnation , ungodly persons who turn the grace of our God into licentiousness and deny our only Master and Lord , Jesus Christ .
65001005	Now I desire to remind you , though you were once for all fully informed , that the Lord who saved a people out of the land of Egypt , afterward destroyed those who did not believe .
65001006	And the angels who did not keep their own domain , but abandoned their proper abode , he has kept in eternal chains under darkness for the judgment of the great day ,
65001007	just as Sodom and Gomorrah and the surrounding cities , which likewise acted immorally and indulged in strange flesh , serve as an example by undergoing a punishment of eternal fire .
65001008	Yet in the same way these men in their dreamings defile the flesh , reject authority , and revile the glorious ones .
65001009	But Michael the archangel , when he disputed with the devil and argued about the body of Moses , did not dare pronounce against him a reviling judgment , but said , » The Lord rebuke you ! «
65001010	But these men revile whatever they do not understand ; and the things that they know by instinct , like unreasoning animals do , by these things they are destroyed .
65001011	Woe to them ! For they have gone the way of Cain , and for the sake of gain they have rushed headlong into the Balaam's error , and perished in Korah's rebellion .
65001012	These are the men who are blemishes in your love feasts when they feast with you without fear , caring for themselves ; clouds without water , carried along by winds ; autumn trees without fruit , twice dead , uprooted ;
65001013	wild waves of the sea , casting up their own shame like foam ; wandering stars , for whom the blackest darkness has been reserved forever .
65001014	It was also about these men that Enoch , in the seventh generation from Adam , prophesied , saying , » Behold , the Lord came with many thousands of his holy ones ,
65001015	to execute judgment on all , and to convict all the ungodly of all their ungodly deeds which they have done in an ungodly way , and of all the harsh things which ungodly sinners have spoken against him . «
65001016	These are grumblers , finding fault , following after their own lusts ; they speak arrogantly , flattering people for their own advantage .
65001017	But you must remember , beloved , the predictions of the apostles of our Lord Jesus Christ ;
65001018	they said to you , » In the last time there will be scoffers , following their own ungodly lusts . «
65001019	These are the ones who cause divisions , worldly-minded , devoid of the Spirit .
65001020	But you , beloved , build yourselves up on your most holy faith ; pray in the Holy Spirit ;
65001021	keep yourselves in the love of God ; wait anxiously for the mercy of our Lord Jesus Christ to eternal life .
65001022	And have mercy on some , who doubt ;
65001023	save others , snatching them out of the fire ; and on some have mercy with fear , hating even the garment polluted by the flesh .
65001024	Now to him who is able to keep you from falling and to present you without blemish before the presence of his glory with great joy ,
65001025	to the only God our Savior , through Jesus Christ our Lord , be glory , majesty , dominion , and authority , before all time and now and forever . Amen .
66001001	The revelation of Jesus Christ , which God gave him to show to his servants what must soon take place . And he made it known by sending his angel to his servant John ,
66001002	who bore witness to the word of God and to the testimony of Jesus Christ , even to all that he saw .
66001003	Blessed is he who reads the words of this prophecy , and blessed are those who hear , and who keep what is written in it ; for the time is near .
66001004	John , to the seven churches which are in Asia : grace to you and peace from him who is and who was and who is to come , and from the seven spirits who are before his throne ,
66001005	and from Jesus Christ , who is the faithful witness , the firstborn from the dead , and the ruler of the kings of the earth . To him who loves us and has freed us from our sins by his blood ,
66001006	and has made us a kingdom and priests to his God and Father , to him be glory and dominion for ever and ever . Amen .
